### [1] [Analytical Angle-Finding and Series Expansions for Quantum Signal Processing via Orthogonal Polynomial Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05321)
*Pierre-Antoine Bernard,Nathan Wiebe*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文从正交多项式与双正交多项式理论出发，系统刻画了量子信号处理（quantum signal processing, QSP）协议中可实现的基多项式，给出了包括Hermite、Jacobi和Rogers-Szegő多项式在内的显式旋转角表达式，并建立了与SU(1,1)-QSP及双变量QSP的深层联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子信号处理（QSP）是量子算法中用于哈密顿量模拟及相关应用的核心框架，但其中可实现的多项式基及其与正交多项式理论的关系尚未被充分刻画。本文旨在从正交性与双正交性角度，统一理解QSP协议中编码多项式序列所需的旋转角、逼近效率及多项式可实现的充要条件。

Method: 通过将QSP每一步实现的序列多项式视为关于某一线性泛函（具有积分表示）的正交或双正交基，推导出Hermite、Jacobi和Rogers-Szegő多项式族对应的显式QSP旋转角公式；进而利用Hermite级数展开给出光滑函数块编码（block-encoding）的门复杂度上界；并基于根的性质完整刻画了SU(1,1)-QSP可实现的

Result: 编码上述多项式族至度数n需要2n+2个旋转角；利用Hermite级数展开，光滑函数f的ε-近似块编码仅需O(log(1/ε))个量子门；双正交性在双变量QSP（bivariate QSP）场景下同样成立，导出了一组可实现多项式的必要条件。

Conclusion: 正交多项式与双正交多项式理论与QSP的关联，不仅为求解QSP角度发现问题提供了新方法（显式角度表达式），还为SU(1,1)-QSP中多项式的可实现性提供了基于根的完整刻画，并揭示了双变量QSP中多项式必须满足的双正交性条件。

Abstract: Quantum signal processing is a powerful framework in quantum algorithms, playing a central role in Hamiltonian simulation and related applications. The sequence of polynomials implemented at each step of this protocol provides a polynomial basis for block-encoding any polynomial of a unitary. We characterize the achievable polynomial bases in terms of their orthogonality or biorthogonality with respect to a linear functional admitting an integral representation. Explicit expressions for the quantum signal processing angles are derived for families of polynomial sequences, including Hermite, Jacobi, and Rogers-Szegő polynomials. We show that $2n+2$ rotation angles are required to encode a sequence of polynomials in these classes up to degree $n$. We use this result to show that an $ε$-approximation of a smooth function $f$ can be block-encoded using $O(\log(1/ε))$ gates via its Hermite series expansion. The connections established with the theory of orthogonal and biorthogonal polynomials lead to a new method for solving the quantum signal processing angle-finding problem, yielding explicit expressions for the angles. They also provide a complete characterization of the polynomials achievable by $\mathrm{SU}(1,1)$-QSP in terms of their roots. Biorthogonality properties are shown to hold in the bivariate QSP setting, yielding a set of necessary conditions for achievable polynomials.

</details>


### [2] [Weighted Phase-Space Paths for Exact Wigner Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05764)
*Surachate Limkumnerd,Panat Phanthaphanitkul*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文指出，在相空间（phase space）中表示的量子态通常不是正定随机过程的概率密度，并基于维格纳动力学（Wigner dynamics）系统阐述了这一事实。论文证明了非二次势下维格纳-莫尔生成元（Wigner–Moyal generator）不是福克-普朗克（Fokker–Planck）生成元，因此精确的维格纳函数必须以加权经验测度重建，而非未加权的载子轨迹密度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清量子态在相空间中表示时，其对象通常不是正随机过程的概率密度这一基本事实，并纠正将维格纳动力学等同于经典随机扩散过程的常见误解。

Method: 通过分析维格纳动力学（Wigner dynamics），区分不同条件（仅要求复现玻恩密度 vs. 要求所有外尔有序期望值）下相空间对象的约束程度；引入加权经验测度的随机表示，并定义残差诊断量以量化非经典贡献。

Result: 非二次势下维格纳-莫尔生成元包含高阶符号动量转移项，非正定布朗扩散的福克-普朗克生成元；精确维格纳函数需通过加权经验测度重建；建立了前向-反向路径比的符号因子与维格纳干涉贡献奇偶性（parity）的关联。

Conclusion: 维格纳函数的随机表示需引入符号权重或分支事件来捕获非经典修正；前向-反向路径比中的符号因子记录的是维格纳干涉的奇偶性，而非热力学熵产生（thermodynamic entropy production）。

Abstract: A quantum state can be written in phase space, but the resulting object is not generally the probability density of a positive stochastic process on ordinary phase space. We spell this out for Wigner dynamics. If a positive phase-space process is required only to reproduce the Born density after integrating over momentum, the requirement fixes only an integrated current; the local drift and diffusion remain underdetermined. If one instead requires all Weyl-ordered expectation values, the phase-space object is fixed to be the Wigner function. For non-quadratic potentials the Wigner--Moyal generator contains higher-order, signed momentum-transfer terms, so it is not the Fokker--Planck generator of a positive Brownian diffusion. The exact Wigner function must therefore be reconstructed, in a stochastic representation, as a weighted empirical measure \[ \FW(\z,t)=\E_{\Pp}[W_tδ(\z-\z_t)], \qquad \z=(q,p), \] rather than the unweighted density of sampled carrier trajectories. With classical Hamiltonian flow as the carrier, all nonclassical correction beyond classical transport sits in the Moyal residual and can be represented by signed weights or branching events. The same split defines a residual diagnostic that vanishes for quadratic Hamiltonians and measures what classical carrier transport misses in anharmonic dynamics. The formulation also gives a forward--reverse relation for signed Wigner path measures. The ratio of forward and reversed contributions separates into a positive magnitude factor and a sign factor. This sign records the parity of the Wigner interference contribution; it is not a thermodynamic entropy production.

</details>


### [3] [Quantizing gravitational fields with an entropy-corrected action principle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05239)
*Jianhao M. Yang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文基于扩展的平稳作用量原理，发展了一套引力场量子化的变分框架。通过引入相对熵修正项，在不依赖正则动量算符化的前提下重建了惠勒-德维特方程，从而避免了正规量子化中的算符排序歧义问题。该框架进一步应用于引力场与无质量标量场的耦合系统，利用引力场的速率方程定义涌现时间参数，恢复出带有量子修正项的薛定谔方程，并探讨了相对熵与量子引力中全息对偶的可能联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典正则量子化（canonical quantization）中，将正则动量提升为算符的操作会引发算符排序（operator ordering）的歧义性，这一问题长期困扰引力场的量子化。本文旨在发展一种避免上述歧义的新变分框架，以实现引力场的一致量子化。

Method: 方法包含三个核心步骤：(1) 基于信息论动机，在经典平稳作用量原理中加入由场涨落相对熵（relative entropy）构成的修正项；(2) 在超空间（superspace）上构建系综形式，纳入该熵修正；(3) 进一步精细化该形式，实现量子化与约束的统一处理，从而解决量子化与约束约化之间的排序歧义。随后将该框架应用于引力场与无质量标量场的耦合系统。

Result: 在不进行正则动量算符化的前提下，恢复了引力波泛函的惠勒-德维特方程（Wheeler-DeWitt equation）。对于耦合系统，利用引力场速率方程定义的涌现时间参数，得到了标量场波泛函的薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation），并附带一个在 $G\hbar^2$ 量级被压低的额外量子修正项。

Conclusion: 该变分框架为引力场的量子化提供了一条避开算符排序歧义的新路径。研究还指出，文中使用的相对熵概念可能与量子引力中的全息对偶（holographic dualities）存在潜在联系，为进一步的理论探索提供了方向。

Abstract: A variational framework for the quantization of gravitational fields is developed based on an extension of the stationary action principle. Within this framework, the Wheeler-DeWitt equation for the gravitational wave functional is recovered without assuming operator promotion of the canonical momentum, thus avoiding the ambiguity of operator ordering in canonical quantization. The derivation is based on three main ingredients. First, motivated by information-theoretic considerations, the classical stationary action principle is generalized by incorporating a correction term constructed from the relative entropy associated with field fluctuations. Second, an ensemble formulation on superspace is enhanced to incorporate this entropy correction. Third, the formalism is further refined to provide a unified treatment of quantization and constraints, thereby addressing the long-standing ambiguity concerning the ordering of quantization and constraint reduction. The framework is then applied to gravitational fields coupled to a massless scalar field. Using an emergent time parameter defined via the rate equation of the gravitational fields, a Schrodinger equation for the scalar-field wave functional is recovered, supplemented by an additional quantum correction term suppressed at order $G\hbar^2$. Finally, we comment on possible connections between the notion of relative entropy employed here and holographic dualities in quantum gravity.

</details>


### [4] [Krylov Dynamics and Operator Growth in Time-Dependent Systems via Lie Algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05290)
*András Grabarits,E. Medina-Guerra,Adolfo del Campo*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在Krylov空间中建立了含时哈密顿量（time-dependent Hamiltonian）量子动力学与李代数结构（Lie-algebraic structure）之间的直接联系，提出了一个统一框架，并引入了一种新的量子速度极限（quantum speed limit）来刻画含时生成元（time-dependent generator）下的复杂度增长速率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 含时量子系统的动力学在Krylov空间中的结构尚不清晰，尤其是在底层李代数结构如何决定Krylov动力学方面缺乏统一理解。

Method: 通过建立Krylov子空间（Krylov subspace）动力学与哈密顿量的李代数结构（Lie algebra）之间的直接联系，利用阶梯算子（ladder operators）生成含时Krylov动力学，并嵌入$\mathfrak{sl}(2,\mathbb{C})$子代数作为最小条件。框架还扩展到振荡子代数（oscillator algebra）及nilpotent Heisenberg–Weyl代数的推广。

Result: 识别了精确含时Krylov动力学由相互作用绘景哈密顿量（interaction-picture Hamiltonian）自然决定的最小条件；证明了时间演化算子的单指数表示（single-exponential representation）可导出时不变的Krylov动力学；提出了一个新的量子速度极限，其函数形式在含时与不含时情形下保持一致；发现该速度极限的饱和强烈受时间驱动影响，仅当哈密顿量在不同时刻自对易时才能保持。

Conclusion: 该工作为含时量子系统中算子增长（operator growth）与Krylov复杂度（Krylov complexity）的描述建立了一个统一的理论框架，揭示了李代数结构在其中的核心作用。

Abstract: We study quantum dynamics generated by time-dependent Hamiltonians in Krylov space, the minimal subspace in which the evolution takes place. We establish a direct link between dynamics in the time-dependent Krylov subspace and the underlying Lie-algebraic structure of the Hamiltonian. We develop a general framework in which the dynamics in the time-dependent Krylov subspace is generated by ladder operators of the associated Lie algebra. In particular, we identify the minimal conditions under which the exact time-dependent Krylov dynamics is naturally determined by the interaction-picture Hamiltonian and governed by an embedded $\mathfrak{sl}(2,\mathbb{C})$ subalgebra. We further show that an exact single-exponential representation of the time-evolution operator gives rise to a distinct time-independent Krylov dynamics in a unitarily related basis, from which the exact time-dependent Krylov dynamics can nevertheless be recovered. We also extend the framework to the oscillator algebra as the simplest extension of the nilpotent Heisenberg--Weyl algebra, and provide further examples, including the translated and dilated harmonic oscillator, systems governed by closed Virasoro subalgebras, a spin in a rotating magnetic field, and higher-dimensional generalizations for multi-level systems. In addition, we introduce a new quantum speed limit to the complexity growth rate generated by a time-dependent generator and show that, for evolutions governed by a Lie algebra, it retains the same functional form as in the time-independent case. Remarkably, saturation of this bound is strongly affected by temporal driving and persists only when the Hamiltonian commutes with itself at different times. These results establish a unified framework for characterizing operator growth and Krylov complexity in time-dependent quantum systems with underlying Lie-algebraic structures.

</details>


### [5] [Entanglement generation in a two-body Schrödinger--Newton model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06577)
*Marcin Płodzień,Julia Osęka-Lenart,Maciej Lewenstein,Michał Eckstein*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个双体薛定谔-牛顿模型（two-body Schrödinger-Newton model），分离了非线性自局域化与不可分离的牛顿对势，通过解析和数值方法研究了两种机制对量子纠缠产生的影响，发现初始空间构型和质量比敏感地决定纠缠动力学，且色散高斯初始态会显著放大纠缠效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 薛定谔-牛顿方程（Schrödinger-Newton equation）为描述大量子系统的自引力演化提供了半经典框架，但其中非线性自场与牛顿对势（Newtonian pair potential）在纠缠产生中的各自作用尚未被清晰分离和理解。

Method: 提出一个双体薛定谔-牛顿模型，将非线性自局域化与不可分离的牛顿对势明确分离，并在一维正则化几何（regularized one-dimensional geometry）下进行数值模拟。

Result: 非线性自场（nonlinear self-field）保持施密特谱（Schmidt spectrum）不变，而直接纠缠产生来自不可分离的牛顿对势；纠缠产生对初始空间构型和质量比（mass ratio）敏感；高度局域的自束缚波包在散射过程中纠缠增长极小，而空间离域化（delocalization）和动力学色散（kinetic dispersion）会放大对势的纠缠能力。

Conclusion: 质量不对称的色散高斯初始态会碎裂较轻粒子，产生维格纳负性（Wigner negativity）和快速纠缠增长；稳态SN轮廓（stationary SN profiles）能显著抑制这一效应，孤立出裸对势贡献，而色散高斯初始态则将其膨胀放大。

Abstract: The Schrödinger--Newton (SN) equation provides a semiclassical framework for the evolution of self-gravitating of massive quantum systems. We propose a two-body Schrödinger--Newton model that separates local nonlinear self-localization from the nonseparable Newtonian pair potential. Analytically, we show that the nonlinear self-field preserves the Schmidt spectrum, whereas direct entanglement generation arises from the nonseparable pair potential. Using numerical simulations in a regularized one-dimensional geometry, we find that entanglement generation depends sensitively on the initial spatial configuration and on the mass ratio. Highly localized, self-bound wavepackets experience minimal entanglement growth during scattering. Spatial delocalization and kinetic dispersion broaden the interaction region, amplifying the entangling power of the pair potential and exciting higher-order spatial modes. For dispersive Gaussian initial states, mass asymmetry shatters the lighter particle, producing Wigner negativity and rapid entanglement growth, whereas stationary SN profiles strongly suppress this effect. Stationary SN profiles isolate the bare pair-potential contribution; dispersive Gaussian initial states inflate it.

</details>


### [6] [Machine Learning Approaches to Building Quantum Circuits for Sets of Matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06633)
*Matvei Fedin,Andrei Morozov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用可解释机器学习方法，构建了适用于任意大小对角矩阵的通用最短路解析量子算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习已成为众多学科中的有用工具，本文旨在借助可解释机器学习来设计量子算法。

Method: 通过研究机器学习算法中的参数，构建通用的最短路解析量子算法。

Result: 成功构建了适用于任意大小对角矩阵的通用最短路解析量子算法（universal shortest analytic quantum algorithm）。

Conclusion: 可解释机器学习（interpretable machine learning）能够有效辅助量子算法的构造，为任意规模的对角矩阵提供了统一的最短路解析方案。

Abstract: Machine learning nowadays becomes a useful instrument in many subjects. In this paper we use interpretable machine learning to build quantum algorithm. By studying the parameters of the machine learning algorithm we were able to construct universal shortest analytic quantum algorithm for arbitrary diagonal matrix of any size.

</details>


### [7] [Systematic construction of quantum many-body scars in frustrated Rydberg arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05297)
*Jean-Yves Desaules,Aron Kerschbaumer,Marko Ljubotina,Maksym Serbyn*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本篇论文引入图论框架，在任意晶格上发现了两种量子多体疤痕（quantum many-body scars）机制（I型和II型），并在六角晶格上数值验证了指数量级的疤痕轨迹，表明疤痕是Rydberg原子阵列超越一维的通用现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前Rydberg原子阵列中的量子多体疤痕仅在二分晶格（bipartite lattices）上被观测到，尚不清楚在有阻挫（frustration）的晶格上疤痕是否存在、如何存续，以及合适的初始态是什么。

Method: 采用图论（graph-theoretic）框架，在任意晶格上寻找适合产生疤痕的候选态。通过该框架预测了两种不同机制：I型疤痕推广了二分晶格情形，利用局域纠缠态（locally entangled states）克服弱阻挫；II型疤痕则利用强阻挫固定部分晶格，使剩余部分自由振荡。

Result: 数值演示了两种疤痕机制，并在六角晶格（hexagonal lattice）上发现了一个指数家族的疤痕轨迹（exponential family of scarred trajectories）；这些轨迹可以编码免受热化（thermalization）保护的信息。

Conclusion: 研究表明，量子疤痕是Rydberg系统超越一维的通用特征，并为在量子模拟器中系统性地探测非热动力学（non-thermal dynamics）提供了实验可行的途径。

Abstract: Quantum many-body scars in Rydberg atom arrays have thus far only been observed on bipartite lattices, leaving open the question of whether and how they survive frustration, and what the appropriate initial states are that lead to nonthermal dynamics. We introduce a graph-theoretic framework to find suitable candidates for scarring on arbitrary lattices. Our framework predicts two distinct mechanisms: type-I scars generalize the bipartite case by using locally entangled states to overcome mild frustration, while type-II scars exploit strong frustration to pin part of the lattice, leaving the remainder to oscillate freely. We numerically demonstrate both mechanisms and uncover an exponential family of scarred trajectories on the hexagonal lattice that can encode information protected from thermalization. Our results establish scarring as a generic feature of Rydberg systems beyond one dimension and provide an experimentally accessible route to systematically probing non-thermal dynamics in quantum simulators.

</details>


### [8] [Universal Neural Propagator: Learning Time Evolution in Many-Body Quantum Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05299)
*Zihao Qi,Christopher Earls,Yang Peng*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出通用神经传播子（Universal Neural Propagator, UNP），一种在全自监督方式下训练的单一统一模型，能够同时跨驱动协议函数空间和指数级大希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）的初始态预测量子多体动力学，在二维驱动伊辛模型（Ising model）上验证了其准确性与可迁移性，并支持在大系统规模下的微调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统量子多体动力学模拟方法每次改变哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）或初始态都需重新计算，而现有基础模型仅能跨哈密顿量或跨初始态之一迁移，无法同时兼顾两者。本文旨在构建一个单一统一模型，实现同时跨驱动协议与初始态的动力学预测。

Method: 引入通用神经传播子（Universal Neural Propagator, UNP），该模型以全自监督方式学习从驱动协议到时间演化传播子（time-evolution propagator）的函数映射。模型训练完成后，可同时预测跨越驱动协议函数空间与指数级大希尔伯特空间初始态的动力学。

Result: 在二维驱动伊辛模型上，UNP在乘积态（product states）与纠缠初始态（entangled initial states）上均表现出准确性与可迁移性；对分布内（in-distribution）与分布外（out-of-distribution）驱动协议同样有效；在超出精确对角化（exact diagonalization）能力的系统尺寸上仍保持精度，并能通过可观测量数据在所有初始态上高效微调。

Conclusion: 通过将学习对象从量子态（quantum states）转向算子（operators），本文为驱动量子物质的可迁移模拟开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Conventional approaches to simulating quantum many-body dynamics produce a single trajectory: if the Hamiltonian or the initial state is changed, the computation must be re-performed. Recent efforts toward foundation models have begun to address this limitation, yet existing methods transfer across either Hamiltonians or initial states, but not both. In this work, we introduce the Universal Neural Propagator (UNP), a single, unified model that learns the functional mapping from driving protocols to time-evolution propagators. Trained in an entirely self-supervised way, a single UNP model predicts dynamics across a function space of driving protocols and an exponentially large Hilbert space of initial states simultaneously. We benchmark on a two-dimensional driven Ising model and demonstrate the UNP's accuracy and transferability across product and entangled initial states, as well as for both in- and out-of-distribution driving protocols. The UNP remains accurate at system sizes beyond exact diagonalization, and can be efficiently fine-tuned across all initial states using observable data. By shifting the object of learning from quantum states to operators, this work opens a route toward transferable simulation of driven quantum matter.

</details>


### [9] [Signature structure of quadratic response under Zeno-Schur coarse graining in open quantum systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05417)
*Ansgar Pernice*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在 Gorini–Kossakowski–Sudarshan–Lindblad (GKSL) 框架下，研究了量子二次响应张量（quadratic response tensor）在 Zeno 粗粒化下的重整化机制，发现 Schur 补结构会导致响应张量的正定性（positive definiteness）不再保持，并提出了一个描述该机制的最小有效流（minimal effective flow），揭示了签名扇区（signature sector）的涌现与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二次响应张量（quadratic response tensor）自然出现在量子动力学描述中，例如量子线性玻尔兹曼方程（quantum linear Boltzmann equation, QLBE），但其在监测诱导粗粒化（monitoring-induced coarse graining）下的修正机制尚不明确。本文旨在探讨该结构如何在 Zeno 消除快自由度过程中发生改变。

Method: 基于 Gorini–Kossakowski–Sudarshan–Lindblad (GKSL) 框架，引入时间尺度分离（time-scale separation），利用 Zeno 消除（Zeno elimination）处理快自由度，得到具有 Schur 补结构（Schur-complement structure）的减式重整化（subtractive renormalization）。进一步构建最小有效流（minimal effective flow）以刻画该机制。

Result: 响应张量的正定性（positive definiteness）在粗粒化后不再保持：慢自由度与快阻尼扇区（rapidly damped sector）之间的耦合可诱导出负方向（negative direction），即使微观张量严格正定。Schur 补压缩（Schur-induced compression）与各向异性扰动（anisotropic perturbation）的竞争将动力学组织为不同的签名扇区（signature sector）。该结构在所考虑的模型类中具有鲁棒性，且在适当参数区间可能可实验观测。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一个通用框架，说明 QLBE 型动力学中的二次响应结构如何在 Zeno 诱导粗粒化（Zeno-induced coarse graining）下被动态重组，为理解开放量子系统中响应张量的粗粒化行为提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Quadratic response tensors arise naturally in quantum kinetic descriptions, such as the quantum linear Boltzmann equation (QLBE), where they encode the coupled structure of drift and fluctuations beyond simple positive-definite forms. Motivated by this class of systems, we investigate how such response structures are modified under monitoring-induced coarse graining.
  Within the Gorini--Kossakowski--Sudarshan--Lindblad (GKSL) framework and under time-scale separation, Zeno elimination of fast degrees of freedom generates a subtractive renormalization with Schur-complement structure. As a result, positive definiteness of the response tensor is not preserved: coupling between slow and rapidly damped sectors can induce negative directions even when the microscopic tensor is strictly positive.
  We formulate a minimal effective flow capturing this mechanism and show that the competition between Schur-induced compression and anisotropic perturbations organizes the dynamics into distinct signature sectors. The resulting structure appears to be robust within the class of models considered and, in appropriate regimes, may be experimentally accessible.
  Our results establish a general framework for how quadratic response structures, as encountered in QLBE-type dynamics, are dynamically reorganized under Zeno-induced coarse graining.

</details>


### [10] [Temporal Coarse-Graining as the Origin of Macroscopic Friction in Quantum Spin Chains via Data-Driven Liouvillian Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05604)
*Seiki Saito*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过集成广义扩展动态模态分解（gEDMD）与Mori-Zwanzig投影方法，从混沌XXZ自旋链的严格幺正动力学中直接提取纳维-斯托克斯流体动力学系数，揭示了宏观耗散（摩擦系数和粘滞系数）并非系统的绝对属性，而是依赖于观测者时间粗粒化分辨率的涌现现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解可逆的幺正量子多体动力学如何涌现出宏观不可逆的流体动力学行为是一个基本挑战。传统方法常将自旋密度动力学强制纳入纯扩散模型，掩盖了压力、自旋电流与局域摩擦之间的微观相互作用；此外，如何将真正的不可逆性与严格的幺正演化相协调，引发了关于观测者时间分辨率作用的基本问题。

Method: 提出一种基于广义扩展动态模态分解（generalized Extended Dynamic Mode Decomposition, gEDMD）并集成Mori-Zwanzig投影的完全数据驱动框架。通过扩展可观测量字典以显式包含自旋电流，从混沌XXZ自旋链中直接提取纳维-斯托克斯（Navier-Stokes）流体动力学系数，并考察不同时间粗粒化尺度下的行为。

Result: 无约束提取揭示了一个深刻的物理二分性：力学弹性系数（$c^2$）内禀地源自精确的幺正动力学，保持了严格的微观可逆性；而宏观摩擦系数（$γ$）和运动粘滞系数（$ν$）在精确导数极限下净耗散为零，围绕零快速振荡。只有在有限时间粗粒化（$Δt_{\rm cg} > 0$）下，系统才经历一个明显的交叉时间尺度，这些可逆波动被平均掉，建立起严格为正的摩擦和粘滞系数的中间功能区间。

Conclusion: 孤立量子系统中的宏观摩擦并非绝对属性，而是根本上由观测者时间分辨率决定的涌现现象。没有有限的时间粗粒化，真正的宏观输运无法建立。

Abstract: Understanding the emergence of macroscopic irreversible hydrodynamics from the reversible unitary dynamics of isolated quantum many-body systems remains a fundamental challenge. Conventional approaches often force spin density dynamics into purely diffusive models, obscuring the microscopic interplay of pressure, spin current, and local friction. Furthermore, reconciling true irreversibility with strictly unitary evolution raises profound questions about the role of the observer's temporal resolution. In this paper, we introduce a fully data-driven framework based on generalized Extended Dynamic Mode Decomposition (gEDMD) integrated with the Mori-Zwanzig projection. By expanding the observable dictionary to explicitly include spin currents, we directly extract the Navier-Stokes hydrodynamic coefficients from a chaotic XXZ spin chain across varying temporal coarse-graining scales. Our unconstrained extraction reveals a profound physical dichotomy: the mechanical elasticity ($c^2$) is intrinsically derived from the exact unitary dynamics, preserving strict microscopic reversibility. In stark contrast, the macroscopic friction ($γ$) and kinematic viscosity ($ν$) exhibit zero net dissipation, oscillating rapidly around zero in the exact-derivative limit. We demonstrate that genuine macroscopic transport cannot be established without finite temporal coarse-graining. By introducing a finite observation timescale ($Δt_{\rm cg} > 0$), the system passes through a distinct crossover timescale where these reversible fluctuations average out, establishing an intermediate functional regime that yields strictly positive friction and viscosity. Our results clearly demonstrate that macroscopic friction in isolated quantum systems is not an absolute property, but fundamentally an emergent phenomenon dictated by the temporal resolution of the observer.

</details>


### [11] [Dynamical Signatures of Floquet Topology in Wave Packet Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05608)
*Xin Shen,Bing Lu,Yan-Qing Zhu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在扩展希尔伯特空间中发展了Floquet微扰理论，通过波包质心（CoM）动力学揭示Floquet拓扑相变的多频率Zitterbewegung振荡特征，为实验探测非平衡拓扑不变量提供了可操作的协议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Floquet系统为设计静态系统中不存在的拓扑相提供了平台，但如何在动力学上表征这些非平衡（non-equilibrium）拓扑不变量仍是一个挑战。

Method: 在扩展希尔伯特空间（extended Hilbert space）中发展Floquet微扰理论（Floquet perturbation theory），解析描述波包的质心动力学，并将其应用于驱动的Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）模型。

Result: 质心表现出多频率的Zitterbewegung振荡，其频谱成分和相位与Floquet能带结构直接相关；拓扑相变处的能带反转在质心动力学中留下显著特征，包括低频模式的涌现和振荡轨迹的相移。

Conclusion: 质心动力学可作为探测Floquet拓扑不变量的一种简单且实验可及的探针，适用于高频和强驱动两种区域。

Abstract: Periodically driven quantum systems, known as Floquet systems, provide a versatile platform for engineering novel topological phases absent in static settings. However, dynamically characterizing these non-equilibrium topological invariants remains a challenge. Here, we develop a Floquet perturbation theory in the extended Hilbert space to analytically describe the center-of-mass (CoM) dynamics of a wave packet. When applied to the driven Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model, our theory reveals that the CoM exhibits multi-frequency Zitterbewegung oscillations, whose spectral composition and phase are directly tied to the system's Floquet band structure. Crucially, we find that band inversions at topological phase transitions imprint distinct signatures in the CoM dynamics, including the emergence of low-frequency modes and phase shifts of the oscillatory trajectory. These dynamical signatures offer a practical protocol for detecting Floquet topological invariants, which we demonstrate for both high-frequency and strongly driven regimes. Our work establishes CoM dynamics as a simple and experimentally accessible probe for exploring topological phase transitions in Floquet systems.

### [12] [Pontus-Mpemba effect in cavity quantum electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05827)
*Stefano Longhi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出在腔量子电动力学（cavity QED）系统中，利用带有光子损耗的Jaynes-Cummings模型实现量子Pontus-Mpemba效应，即通过两步演化协议使量子系统比单次非猝灭弛豫更快地达到平衡，并在光学和电路QED平台上具有实验可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子Pontus-Mpemba效应是一种反直觉现象，系统通过两步演化协议反而比单次弛豫更快地达到平衡。现有研究尚未在腔QED这类可控实验平台中实现该效应，因此需要寻找易于实现的物理系统来探索该效应。

Method: 采用Jaynes-Cummings模型（Jaynes-Cummings model），描述一个两能级原子（two-level atom）与单个有损腔模（lossy cavity）之间的相干相互作用。将分析限制在单激发子空间（single-excitation sector），并通过对腔衰减率（cavity decay rate）实施突然的量子淬火（sudden quench）来产生不同的弛豫轨迹。

Result: 弱耗散下动力学表现为阻尼真空拉比振荡（damped vacuum Rabi oscillations），强耗散下转变为近似指数型原子衰变。原子激发态显示出非单调、加速的衰变行为：淬火耗散轨迹比固定损耗演化弛豫得更快，证实了量子Pontus-Mpemba效应的存在。

Conclusion: 该效应源于相干原子-光子交换（coherent atom-photon exchange）与腔耗散（cavity dissipation）之间的竞争关系，为量子Pontus-Mpemba效应在光学腔QED和电路QED（circuit QED）平台上提供了清晰且实验可实现的实现方案。

Abstract: The quantum Pontus-Mpemba effect is a counterintuitive phenomenon in which a quantum system relaxes faster through a two-step evolution protocol than through a single, unquenched relaxation. This work proposes its realization in cavity quantum electrodynamics using the Jaynes-Cummings model with photon loss. The model captures the coherent interaction between a two-level atom and a single quantized mode of a lossy cavity, providing a minimal yet realistic setting to explore dissipative quantum dynamics. Restricting the analysis to the single-excitation sector, the dynamics feature damped vacuum Rabi oscillations for weak dissipation that transition to near-exponential atomic decay under strong dissipation. A sudden quench of the cavity decay rate generates distinct relaxation trajectories from the same initial atom-cavity state. The atomic excitation then displays a non-monotonic, accelerated decay, where a trajectory with a quenched dissipation relaxes faster than fixed-loss evolution. The effect originates from the interplay between coherent atom-photon exchange and cavity dissipation, establishing a clear and experimentally accessible realization of the quantum Pontus-Mpemba effect in both optical and circuit QED platforms.

### [13] [Macroscopic entanglement between two magnon modes via two-tone driving of a superconducting qubit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06297)
*Rong-Can Yang,Gang Liu,Gen Li,Jie Li*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用腔介导的钇铁石榴石（YIG）球中磁振子（magnon）与超导量子比特（superconducting qubit）之间的耦合，通过双音驱动（two-tone driving）量子比特，实现两个YIG球中两个磁振子模式的纠缠（entanglement），并给出了可行的参数与实验验证方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在已实验实现的磁振子-超导量子比特耦合平台基础上，进一步探索其在制备宏观量子纠缠态方面的潜力，目标是在两个毫米级YIG球中的巨量自旋（超过10^18个自旋）之间实现可验证的宏观纠缠。

Method: 基于YIG球中磁振子与超导量子比特的腔介导（cavity-mediated）耦合系统，通过对量子比特施加双音驱动场（two-tone field），并适当选择两个驱动场的频率和强度，来诱导两个YIG球中磁振子模式之间的纠缠。

Result: 在完全可行的实验参数条件下，可以实现两个磁振子模式之间强纠缠（strong entanglement）；文中还给出了实验上验证该纠缠的探测方案（detection scheme）。

Conclusion: 利用当前可用的实验参数，可以在两个毫米级YIG球的磁振子模式间实现宏观纠缠（涉及超过10^18个自旋），这为宏观量子力学（macroscopic quantum mechanics）及非传统退相干理论（unconventional decoherence theories）等基础研究提供了有前景的应用平台。

Abstract: The cavity-mediated coupling between magnons in an yttrium-iron-garnet (YIG) sphere and a superconducting qubit has recently been demonstrated as a new platform for preparing macroscopic quantum states. Here, based on this system, we propose to entangle two magnon modes in two YIG spheres by driving the qubit with a two-tone field and by appropriately choosing the frequencies and strengths of the two driving fields. We show that strong entanglement can be achieved with fully feasible parameters. We further provide a detection scheme for experimentally verifying the entanglement. Our results indicate that macroscopic entanglement between two magnon modes in two millimeter-sized YIG spheres, involving more than $10^{18}$ spins, can be realized using currently available parameters, which finds promising applications in fundamental studies, such as macroscopic quantum mechanics and the test of unconventional decoherence theories.

### [14] [Microsopic Theory of Spin Polarons in Chern Ferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05292)
*Qiang Gao,Eslam Khalaf*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文发展了SU(2)陈铁磁体中带电激发的微观理论，构建了可绑定任意数量自旋翻转的电荷-$e$自旋极化子态系列，给出了闭式波函数。在理想陈-1能带中，这些极化子是哈密顿量的精确本征态；在非理想情形下，引入尺寸参数和几何信息驱动的单粒子缀饰，将其推广为变分族。波函数有两种等价表示：Weierstrass函数相对动量的Jastrow因子比值，或粒子-空穴波函数的反对称化双子乘积。在最低朗道能级中，单自旋翻转变分态与精确对角化重叠度≥99%，多自旋翻转能量平滑过渡到大尺度（斯格明子）区域。几何非均匀性会破坏极化子，但抑制色散时极化子可在非均匀区域保持稳定。结果为莫尔平台掺杂陈铁磁体分析提供了微观基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 陈铁磁体（Chern ferromagnet）中掺杂引发的带电激发（如自旋极化子和斯格明子）是理解量子霍尔效应和莫尔平台相关现象的关键，但目前缺乏一个可处理任意数量自旋翻转的微观波函数框架。本文旨在填补这一空白，构建从单粒子到多粒子、从小尺度到大尺度激发态的统一变分描述。

Method: 在SU(2)对称陈铁磁体中，基于正常序接触相互作用（normal-ordered contact interaction）的哈密顿量，构造可绑定任意数量自旋翻转的电荷-$e$自旋极化子波函数。在理想陈-1能带中证明其为精确本征态；在非理想情形下，引入单个尺寸参数和基于量子几何的单粒子缀饰函数，将波函数推广为变分族。波函数可等价表示为Weierstrass函数相对动量的Jastrow因子比值，或粒子-空穴波函数的反对称化双子乘积（antisymmetrized geminal product）。

Result: 在最低朗道能级（lowest Landau level）基准测试中，单自旋翻转变分态与精确对角化的重叠度≥99%，并准确捕获了结合能。多自旋翻转能量平滑地过渡到大尺度斯格明子（skyrmion）区域。对于量子几何可调谐的陈能带，相互作用产生的单粒子色散在几何足够非均匀时会迅速破坏自旋极化子；但抑制色散后，极化子在非均匀区域仍保持稳定，结合能缓慢下降，束缚态随几何集中而增大。

Conclusion: 本文为莫尔（moiré）平台中掺杂陈铁磁体的微观分析提供了基础，并建立了描述多极化子激发和相态的变分波函数基础框架。

Abstract: We develop a microscopic theory of charged excitations in an SU(2) Chern ferromagnet and obtain closed-form wavefunctions for a hierarchy of charge-$e$ spin polaron states binding an arbitrary number of spin flips. In an ideal Chern-$1$ band with a normal-ordered contact interaction, we show that these polarons are exact eigenstates of the Hamiltonian with the same energy as single-hole excitations. Away from this ideal limit, we promote these states to a variational family by introducing a single size parameter and a geometry-informed single-particle dressing. Our momentum-space wavefunctions admit two equivalent representations: a ratio of Jastrow factors of Weierstrass functions of relative momenta or an antisymmetrized geminal product of particle-hole wavefunctions. The latter enables efficient evaluation of overlaps and expectation values for large system sizes and many spin flips. Benchmarking in the lowest Landau level, the single-spin-flip ansatz achieves $\gtrsim 99\%$ overlap with exact diagonalization and accurately captures binding energies, while the multi-spin-flip energies interpolate smoothly toward the large-texture (skyrmion) regime. For Chern bands with tunable quantum geometry, we find that interaction-generated single particle dispersion quickly destabilizes the spin polarons once quantum geometry becomes sufficiently non-uniform. When such dispersion is suppressed, however, the bound states persist deeper into the non-uniform regime, with the binding energy slowly decreasing and the bound state becoming larger as the quantum geometry becomes more concentrated. Our results provide a microscopic foundation for analyzing doped Chern ferromagnets in moiré platforms and lay the groundwork for variational wavefunctions of multi-polaron excitations and phases.

</details>


### [15] [Galois Solvability of Finite-Size Bethe Solutions in the Heisenberg Chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05589)
*Oliver R. Bellwood,William J. Munro*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过坐标Bethe假设（coordinate Bethe ansatz）研究了自旋-1/2海森堡反铁磁链（spin-1/2 Heisenberg antiferromagnetic chain）的精确基态代数结构，发现在八格点以上Bethe根（Bethe-roots）出现伽罗瓦不可解性（Galois unsolvability），而基态波函数系数和能量在十格点以上亦不可解，表明量子可积模型（quantum integrable model）也可能因代数复杂性而缺乏显式解析可处理性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管自旋-1/2海森堡反铁磁链是标准可积量子多体模型（integrable quantum many-body model）且可通过Bethe假设精确求解，但其有限尺寸下的显式解通常只能通过Bethe ansatz方程的数值计算获得。本文旨在从代数结构层面分析精确基态的解析可处理性及其随系统尺寸的变化规律。

Method: 采用坐标Bethe假设（coordinate Bethe ansatz）对最多十个格点的自旋链进行精确符号基态分析，系统考察基态波函数、Bethe根及能量的代数复杂度随系统尺寸的增长行为。

Result: 基态波函数和Bethe根的代数复杂度随系统尺寸增长，但增长速度不同。对于八个或更多格点的链，Bethe根呈现伽罗瓦不可解性；对于十个或更多格点的链，基态波函数系数和能量也呈现不可解性。

Conclusion: 量子可积模型虽然原则上可通过Bethe假设精确求解，但由于代数复杂性的存在，其有限尺寸基态在解析层面仍可能缺乏显式可处理性（explicit analytic tractability）。

Abstract: The spin-1/2 Heisenberg antiferromagnetic chain is the canonical example of an integrable quantum many-body model. Despite its exact solvability, explicit finite-size solutions are typically only accessible via numerical evaluation of the Bethe ansatz equations. Here, we analyse the algebraic structure of the exact, symbolic ground states for chains up to ten sites using the coordinate Bethe ansatz. We show that both the ground state wavefunction and the Bethe-roots rapidly develop algebraic complexity with respect to system size, but at different rates. The Bethe-roots appear to become Galois unsolvable for chains of eight or more sites, whereas the ground state wavefunction coefficients and energy appear to become unsolvable for ten or more sites. This demonstrates a lack of explicit analytic tractability in a quantum integrable model due to algebraic complexity.

</details>


### [16] [Field-Induced Local Excitations Causing Zero-Magnetization Plateaus in Antiferromagnets of Antiferromagnetic Spin Dimers Under Magnetic Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05516)
*Myung-Hwan Whangbo,Hyun-Joo Koo,Nikita V. Astakhov,Peter S. Berdonosov,Olga S. Volkova*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过理论分析和实验测量，研究了由反铁磁自旋二聚体（antiferromagnetic spin dimers）构成的材料在零磁化平台（zero-magnetization plateau）现象中的物理机制，发现即使单离子各向异性（single-ion anisotropy）可忽略，该现象仍然存在，并基于反铁磁链的能谱分析和氯化铜钾的比热测量进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 某些由反铁磁自旋二聚体构成的材料在磁场中表现出零磁化平台（zero-magnetization plateau），但其磁性离子的单离子各向异性（single-ion anisotropy）几乎可以忽略，该现象的产生原因尚不明确，因此需要从能谱和热力学角度进行探索。

Method: 理论部分分析了由两个自旋-1/2（spin-half）离子构成的反铁磁自旋二聚体（antiferromagnetic spin dimers）在反铁磁链（antiferromagnetic chain）中受磁场影响的能谱变化；实验部分在2 K温度下测量了氯化铜钾（potassium copper chloride）在不同磁场下的比热（specific heat）。

Result: 研究表明，尽管单离子各向异性可忽略，但反铁磁自旋二聚体链在磁场中仍可出现零磁化平台；此外，比热测量结果与理论能谱分析相互印证，揭示了该现象的微观机制。

Conclusion: 反铁磁自旋二聚体材料中的零磁化平台可以不依赖于单离子各向异性，而是由二聚体链的能谱特性在磁场中的变化所导致。比热测量为这一理论解释提供了实验支持。

Abstract: Certain antiferromagnets composed of antiferromagnetic spin dimers exhibit a zero-magnetization plateau despite that the single-ion anisotropy of their magnetic ions is negligible. The cause for this observation was investigated by analyzing how a magnetic field affects the energy spectrum of an antiferromagnetic chain composed of antiferromagnetic spin dimers made up of two spin-half ions and by carrying out specific heat measurements for potassium copper chloride as a function magnetic field at 2 K.

### [17] [Pro-Tensor Network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06661)
*Gen Yue,Ansi Bai,Linqian Wu,Tian Lan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出“原张量网络（pro-tensor network）”——张量网络（tensor network）的一种范畴化（categorification）版本，作为研究众多多体理论（即“多-多体理论（many-many-body theory）”）的严格且图形直观的框架，并展示了其在Levin-Wen模型、Kitaev-Kong结果推广、广义对称性与拓扑全息术（topological holography）等方面的应用，且不依赖于半单性（semisimplicity）、有限性（finiteness）与刚性（rigidity）等假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有张量网络框架在处理众多多体理论时缺乏足够的严谨性与普适性，尤其是受限于半单性、有限性和刚性等假设，难以探索更广泛的物理系统。

Method: 通过范畴化（categorification）将张量网络提升为“原张量网络（pro-tensor network）”，并建立一套支持图形化计算的综合工具（toolbox）。

Result: 成功将Levin-Wen模型重构为“均匀（uniform）”原张量网络；将Kitaev-Kong的结果推广为将粒子刻画为原单子（promonad）上的模（module）；并将弦网（string-net）原张量网络解释为对称张量网络（symmetric tensor network）的空间，从而适用于广义对称性和拓扑全息术研究。

Conclusion: 该框架去除了半单性、有限性和刚性等传统假设，为在更宽松条件下探索多体物理提供了新的严谨工具。

Abstract: We introduce the pro-tensor network, a categorification of the tensor network, as a fully rigorous yet graphically transparent framework for studying the collection of many many-body theories, which we dub many-many-body theory. We provide a comprehensive toolbox for the graphical calculations using pro-tensor networks. As applications, we recover the Levin-Wen model as a "uniform" pro-tensor network and generalize a result of Kitaev and Kong by characterizing particles as modules over promonads. One can also interpret the string-net pro-tensor network as the space of symmetric tensor networks, thus our framework also applies to the study of generalized symmetry and topological holography. Notably, our generalization dispenses with the assumptions of semisimplicity, finiteness, and rigidity, potentially facilitating the exploration of many-body physics beyond these constraints.

</details>


### [18] [Topological spin freezing in frustrated quantum materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06069)
*U. Jena,M. Barman,A. Pradhan,P. Khuntia*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文系统综述了阻挫量子材料中非常规玻璃态自旋动力学的涌现现象，通过热力学、核磁共振（NMR）、μ子自旋旋转（μSR）及中子散射等多种实验手段，识别了拓扑自旋玻璃行为的特征信号，并提出了包含流体动力学自旋模式和自旋堵塞态的统一理论框架，以理解源于拓扑效应的非常规自旋冻结行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阻挫量子材料中竞争相互作用、非平庸电子能带拓扑、量子涨落及涌现自由度之间的复杂耦合可产生多种奇异现象。玻璃态动力学（glassy dynamics）虽然最初在非晶材料和生物系统中被研究，但近年来在量子凝聚态领域，特别是与自旋集体行为、准粒子激发和拓扑自旋织构（topological spin textures）相关的问题中引起了广泛关注。本文旨在系统理解此类系统中非常规玻璃态自旋动力学的涌现机制。

Method: 采用一套综合性的实验探测手段，包括热力学测量（thermodynamic measurement）、核磁共振（nuclear magnetic resonance, NMR）、μ子自旋旋转（muon spin rotation, μSR）以及中子散射（neutron scattering），对阻挫量子材料中自旋冻结行为的特征信号进行识别与分析。

Result: 上述互补实验技术揭示了非常规自旋动力学、短程自旋关联（short-range spin correlations）、涌现低能激发（emergent low-energy excitations）以及具有拓扑起源的玻璃态行为，从而将这些状态与传统的自旋玻璃（spin glass）和无序磁体（disordered magnets）区分开来。此外，讨论了流体动力学自旋模式（hydrodynamic spin modes）在主导玻璃态动力学中的作用，以及在阻挫晶格中自旋堵塞态（spin-jam states）的涌现。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了一个统一的理论框架，用于理解源于拓扑效应的非常规自旋冻结现象，并桥接了实验观测与理论模型。这些见解有助于推动对竞争相互作用、拓扑缺陷、集体激发、量子纠缠（quantum entanglement）及对称性约束所引发的集体多体现象的理解，可能促进新型量子材料的发现与设计，并对未来量子技术具有潜在影响。

Abstract: Competing interactions, non-trivial electronic band topology, quantum fluctuations, and the interplay between emergent degrees of freedom in frustrated quantum materials can give rise to a wide range of exotic phenomena. Glassy dynamics, originally studied in amorphous materials and biological systems, has recently attracted considerable interest in quantum condensed matter, particularly in relation to the collective behavior of spins, quasiparticle excitations, and topological spin textures. Here, we investigate the emergence of unconventional glassy spin dynamics in a broad class of frustrated quantum materials, where spin freezing exhibit distinct signatures in both thermodynamic and microscopic measurements. Using a comprehensive set of experimental probes, including thermodynamic, NMR, ($μ$SR), and neutron scattering, we identify characteristic signatures of topological spin-glass behavior and these complementary techniques reveal unconventional spin dynamics, short-range spin correlations, emergent low-energy excitations, and glassy behavior of topological origins, distinguishing these states from conventional spin glasses and disordered magnets. Furthermore, we discuss the role of hydrodynamic spin modes in governing glassy dynamics and the emergence of spin-jam states in frustrated lattices, providing a unified framework for understanding unconventional spin freezing of topological origin and bridging experimental observations with theoretical models. This review aims to advance our understanding of collective many-body phenomena arising from competing interactions, topological defects, collective excitations, quantum entanglement, and symmetry constraints. Such insights may facilitate the discovery and design of novel quantum materials and help address fundamental questions in contemporary condensed matter physics, with potential implications for future quantum technologies.

</details>


### [19] [Dominant Role of Sulphur divacancy in Charge Trapping Dynamics in MoS$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06109)
*Srest Somay,Sitangshu Bhattacharya,Krishna Balasubramanian*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，揭示了单层二硫化钼（monolayer MoS₂）中不同空位缺陷对载流子俘获与复合的主导机制：硫双空位（Sulphur divacancy）因晶格强弛豫效应产生高效多声子俘获，俘获系数比硫单空位高出七个数量级，从而主导非辐射复合；而钼空位与硫反位缺陷尽管能级较深，但俘获系数很小，在n型器件中影响有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维半导体中的本征缺陷（intrinsic defects）决定了载流子俘获与复合行为，但缺陷依赖的俘获动力学的微观机制尚不明确。本文旨在从第一性原理出发，揭示不同空位缺陷如何影响载流子俘获系数及其物理根源。

Method: 以单层二硫化钼（monolayer MoS₂）为原型体系，采用第一性原理（first principles）方法计算空位缺陷的载流子俘获系数（carrier capture coefficient）。

Result: 硫单空位（single Sulphur vacancy）形成浅能级缺陷，俘获系数约为 10⁻¹⁶ cm³/s；硫双空位（Sulphur divacancy）尽管能级仅中等深度，但俘获系数高达约 10⁻⁹ cm³/s，比单空位高出七个数量级。该增强源于强晶格弛豫（lattice relaxation）导致的高效多声子俘获（multiphonon capture）。钼空位（molybdenum vacancy）与硫反位（Sulphur antisite）虽属深能级缺陷，但俘获系数很小。

Conclusion: 单空位对载流子俘获贡献微弱，而硫双空位主导非辐射复合（nonradiative recombination）并降低量子产率（quantum yield）。钼空位和硫反位在n型器件中作用有限。

Abstract: Intrinsic defects govern carrier trapping and recombination in two-dimensional semiconductors, yet the microscopic origin of defect-dependent capture dynamics remains unclear. Here, we compute carrier capture coefficients of vacancy defects, treating monolayer MoS$_2$ as a prototype, from first principles. We find that the single Sulphur vacancy forms a shallow defect with a small capture coefficient of $\sim 10^{-16}\ \mathrm{cm}^3/\mathrm{s}$, whereas the Sulphur divacancy exhibits a capture coefficient larger by seven orders of magnitude, $\sim 10^{-9}\ \mathrm{cm}^3/\mathrm{s}$, despite being only moderately deeper in energy. This enhancement originates from strong lattice relaxation enabling efficient multiphonon capture. Consequently, single vacancies contribute weakly to trapping, while Sulphur divacancies dominate nonradiative recombination and reduce quantum yield. In contrast, molybdenum vacancies and Sulphur antisites, although deep, show much smaller capture coefficients, indicating a limited role in carrier trapping in n-type devices.

</details>


### [20] [Quantum Electron Quasicrystal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06302)
*Pierre-Antoine Graham,Filippo Gaggioli,Liang Fu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文基于均匀电子气（homogeneous electron gas）中的强关联相，针对近年来神经网络变分蒙特卡洛（neural-network variational Monte Carlo）计算发现的宽带量子阱中30度扭转的双层Wigner晶体电子准晶（electronic quasicrystal）相，发展了一个解析理论框架，证明零点能（zero-point energy）修正使得经典蜂巢态失稳而选择准晶态，从而将零点运动（zero-point motion）确立为稳定该电子准晶的微观机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 均匀电子气的强关联相是多体凝聚态物理（many-body condensed matter physics）的基本词汇，在半导体中有自然实现。近期神经网络变分蒙特卡洛计算发现了宽量子阱中一种出乎意料的量子物相——由30度扭转的双层Wigner晶体构成的电子准晶（electronic quasicrystal），该相违背经典预期且出现在量子涨落主导的区域，但其起源尚缺乏解析理解。

Method: 作者发展了一个解析理论框架，通过计算双层Wigner晶体构型的零点能（zero-point energy）修正来揭示电子准晶的起源。该方法在经典能量之上引入量子涨落修正，从而重新评估不同晶格构型的相对稳定性。

Result: 计算表明，量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）定性上重塑了能量景观（energetic landscape），使经典蜂巢态（classical honeycomb state）失稳，并在广泛参数范围内选择30度准晶态作为基态。

Conclusion: 研究结果确定了零点运动（zero-point motion）是稳定该电子准晶的机制，并建立了一条由多体量子效应驱动的自发莫尔物理（spontaneous moiré physics）路径。

Abstract: The strongly correlated phases of the homogeneous electron gas constitute the vocabulary of many-body condensed matter physics and find a natural realization in semiconductors. In this setting, recent neural-network variational Monte Carlo calculations discovered an unexpected quantum phase of matter in wide quantum wells: an electronic quasicrystal formed by a bilayer Wigner crystals with a 30-degrees twist. This state defies classical expectations and emerges in a regime dominated by quantum fluctuations. Here, we develop an analytical framework to reveal its origin. By computing zero-point energy corrections to bilayer Wigner crystal configurations, we show that quantum fluctuations qualitatively reshape the energetic landscape, destabilizing the classical honeycomb state and selecting the 30-degrees quasicrystalline ground state over a broad parameter range. Our results identify zero-point motion as the mechanism stabilizing the electronic quasicrystal and establish a route to spontaneous moiré physics driven by many-body quantum effects.

### [21] [Superconducting and correlated phases of an effective Hubbard model on the BCC lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06422)
*Theja N. De Silva*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过两种理论方法研究了体心立方晶格上有效Hubbard模型的电子相，揭示了超导不稳定性中的一级正常-超导相变，以及在强耦合区中费米液体、反铁磁和Mott绝缘相之间的一级相变与竞争关系，为碱掺杂富勒烯体系中的超导与关联驱动现象提供了统一视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受碱掺杂富勒烯分子固体（alkali-doped fulleride molecular solids）的启发，旨在理解体心立方晶格上有效Hubbard模型中的电子相行为及其背后的物理机制。

Method: 在中等耦合区，将局域排斥相互作用近似为动量空间中的长程相互作用，得到精确可解的Hatsugai-Kohmoto模型并辅以BCS型配对项；在强耦合区，采用自旋旋转不变奴隶玻色子形式（spin rotationally invariant slave-boson formalism）绘制温度-相互作用相图。

Result: 中等耦合区揭示了一级正常-超导相变（first-order normal-superconducting phase transition），序参量出现不连续跳跃；强耦合区展示了费米液体相（Fermi-liquid phase）、反铁磁相（antiferromagnetic phase）和Mott绝缘相（Mott insulating phase）之间的一级相变，并存在三者竞争的狭窄中间区域。

Conclusion: 所得相图捕捉了三维体系中巡游性、磁序与Mott局域化之间的相互作用，为富勒烯类晶格体系中的超导与关联驱动现象提供了统一的理论视角。

Abstract: We investigate the electronic phases of an effective Hubbard model on the body-centered-cubic lattice, motivated by alkali-doped fulleride molecular solids. The model incorporates renormalized on-site interactions and an effective inverted Hund's coupling originating from electron-phonon interactions. To access complementary interaction regimes, we employ two theoretical approaches. In the intermediate-coupling regime, the on-site repulsive interaction is approximated by a long-range interaction in momentum space, yielding an exactly solvable Hatsugai-Kohmoto model supplemented by a BCS-type pairing term. Within this framework, we analyze the superconducting instability and demonstrate a first-order normal-superconducting phase transition, characterized by a discontinuous jump of the order parameter. In the strong-coupling regime, where pairing fluctuations are suppressed, we apply the spin rotationally invariant slave-boson formalism to map out the temperature-interaction phase diagram. This analysis reveals first-order transitions between a Fermi-liquid phase, an antiferromagnetic phase, and a Mott insulating phase, with a narrow intermediate region where all three phases compete. The resulting phase diagram captures the interplay of itinerancy, magnetic order, and Mott localization in three dimensions and provides a unified perspective on superconducting and correlation-driven phenomena in fulleride-inspired lattice systems.

### [22] [Emergence of a correlated insulating state in bulk 1T-NbSe$_2$ via metal intercalation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06545)
*M. Tomlinson,AKM A. Rahman,S. Devi,R. Tuchikawa,M. Ishigami,D. Le,Md Z. Mohayman,A. Kushima,Y. Nakajima*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究通过电化学嵌入（electrochemical intercalation）锡（Sn）原子，首次在块体（bulk）中实现了原本仅存在于单层极限的1T-NbSe₂多型体（polymorph）。透射电镜直接证实了1T结构的形成，输运测量显示绝缘体行为，与金属性的2H-NbSe₂形成鲜明对比。密度泛函理论（DFT）预测其能带结构为金属性，因此观测到的绝缘态归因于涌现的电子关联效应（emergent electronic correlations）。拉曼光谱还揭示了与锡嵌入和可能的电荷密度波（charge density wave, CDW）有序相关的振动模式。该工作将电化学嵌入确立为稳定热力学难以获得的块体多型体的有效途径，并将块体1T-NbSe₂定位为研究关联电子态的新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 1T-NbSe₂多型体长期以来仅能在单层极限下存在，在块体形式中一直无法获得，这限制了对其本征关联电子性质的深入研究。本研究旨在探索一种能够将1T-NbSe₂稳定在块体形态的有效合成策略。

Method: 采用电化学嵌入（electrochemical intercalation）方法将锡（Sn）原子插入NbSe₂层间，以诱导结构相变。利用透射电子显微镜（TEM）直接表征结构转变，通过输运测量确定电学性质，结合密度泛函理论（DFT）计算预测电子结构，并使用拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）探测振动模式。

Result: 成功实现了块体1T-NbSe₂的合成，透射电镜直接证实了由Sn嵌入诱导的1T结构形成。输运测量表明样品呈现绝缘体行为，与金属性的2H-NbSe₂截然不同。DFT计算预测其能带结构为金属性，暗示绝缘态来源于涌现的电子关联效应。拉曼光谱检测到与Sn嵌入及可能的电荷密度波（CDW）有序相关的振动模式。

Conclusion: 电化学嵌入是一种有效稳定原本无法获得的块体多型体的方法。块体1T-NbSe₂是研究关联电子态（correlated electronic states）的新型平台，其绝缘行为并非来自单电子能带结构，而是源于电子关联效应。

Abstract: The 1T polymorph of NbSe$_2$, long confined to the monolayer limit, has remained inaccessible in bulk. Here, we report the realization of bulk 1T-NbSe$_2$ via electrochemical Sn intercalation. Transmission electron microscopy directly reveals the formation of the 1T structure induced by Sn intercalation. The intercalated samples exhibit insulating transport behavior, in stark contrast to metallic 2H-NbSe$_2$. Density functional theory calculations, however, predict a metallic band structure, highlighting the crucial role of emergent electronic correlations in the observed insulating state. Raman spectroscopy further reveals vibrational modes associated with Sn intercalation and possible charge density wave order. Our results establish electrochemical intercalation as an effective route to stabilize otherwise inaccessible bulk polytypes, positioning bulk 1T-NbSe$_2$ as a new platform for investigating correlated electronic states.

</details>

### [23] [Variational reduction of homogenous Lagrangian systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05517)
*Javier Fernández,Sergio Grillo,Juan Carlos Marrero,Edith Padrón*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文针对具有缩放对称性（scaling symmetries）的拉格朗日系统（Lagrangian systems）定义了一种变分约化（variational reduction）过程，使系统轨迹可通过约化变分原理的临界点（critical points）恢复至求积（quadratures）程度；同时，用缩放版本的拉格朗日–庞加莱方程（Lagrange-Poincaré equations）刻画了临界点，并探讨了齐次拉格朗日系统与赫格洛茨变分原理（Herglotz variational principle）之间的自然联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为具有缩放对称性的拉格朗日系统建立一种变分约化框架，从而简化系统的动力学分析。

Method: 定义了适用于齐次拉格朗日函数（homogenous Lagrangian function）系统的变分约化过程，通过缩放对称性将原变分问题约化至低维空间；提出缩放版本的拉格朗日–庞加莱方程来描述约化后的临界点；并考察了齐次拉格朗日系统与赫格洛茨变分原理之间的关系。

Result: 证明了在该约化框架下，原系统轨迹可通过求积从约化变分原理的临界点重构；给出了刻画临界点的常微分方程组（ordinary differential equations），即缩放版的拉格朗日–庞加莱方程；分析了齐次拉格朗日系统与赫格洛茨变分原理之间是否存在自然关联。

Conclusion: 缩放对称性可用于拉格朗日系统的变分约化，且该约化过程保持了轨迹的可重构性；齐次拉格朗日系统与赫格洛茨变分原理之间的自然关系有待进一步研究。

Abstract: In this paper we show that a variational reduction procedure can be defined for Lagrangian systems subject to scaling symmetries (i.e. Lagrangian systems defined by a homogenous Lagrangian function), in such a way that the trajectories of the system can be reconstructed up to quadratures from the critical points of the reduced variational principle. Also, we characterize the mentioned critical points in terms of a set of ordinary differential equations which are the scaling analogue of the Lagrange-Poincaré equations. Finally, we study if the homogeneous Lagrangian systems are naturally related or not with the Herglotz variational principle.

</details>

# math.CA [[Back]](#toc)

### [24] [Proof of the Holevo-Utkin conjecture on sharp $\ell_p$ norms for zero-sum vectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05243)
*Haonan Zhang*

Main category: math.CA

TL;DR: 本文证明了一个关于 $\ell_p$ 范数与 $\ell_2$ 范数之比在零和约束（sum-to-zero）条件下的极值猜想，该猜想由 Holevo 和 Utkin 提出并仅证明了 $d=3$ 的情况，本文完成了 $d\ge 4$ 所有剩余维度的证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Holevo 和 Utkin 猜想给出了在零和子空间（zero-sum subspace）上 $\ell_p$ 范数与 $\ell_2$ 范数之比的最小值（$0<p<2$）或最大值（$2<q<\infty$）的封闭表达式，但该猜想仅对 $d=3$ 获证，更高维度（$d\ge 4$）的正确性有待验证。

Method: 本文采用数学分析的方法，针对不同参数区间（$0<p\le1$、$1<p<2$ 和 $2<q<\infty$）分别处理，通过构造或分析极值点，严格证明猜想给出的分段表达式在 $d\ge 4$ 时成立。

Result: 对于 $d\ge 4$ 且 $p>0$，论文确认了 Holevo-Utkin 猜想在所有未决情况下的正确性，即零和约束下 $\ell_p/\ell_2$ 范数比的极值表达式完全成立。

Conclusion: 该猜想在 $d\ge 3$ 的所有维度下得到完全证明，为 $\ell_p$ 范数在零和子空间上的极值行为提供了完整刻画，相关结果可能对量子信息论中的某些问题具有应用价值。

Abstract: Let $d\ge 3$ and $p>0$. Let $\|x\|_p$ denote the $\ell_p$ (quasi-)norm of a $d$-dimensional vector $x$. Holevo and Utkin \cite{HU26} conjectured that for $0<p\le 1$, \[ \min \left\{\frac{\|x\|_p}{\|x\|_2}:\vec{0}\neq x\in\mathbb R^d,\ \sum_{i=1}^d x_i=0\right\} =2^{1/p-1/2}; \] for $1<p<2$, \[ \min \left\{\frac{\|x\|_p}{\|x\|_2}:\vec{0}\neq x\in\mathbb R^d,\ \sum_{i=1}^d x_i=0\right\} = \min\left\{2^{1/p-1/2},\left(\frac{(d-1)^{p/2}+(d-1)^{1-p/2}}{d^{p/2}}\right)^{1/p}\right\}; \] and for $2<q<\infty$ \[ \max\left\{\frac{\|x\|_q}{\|x\|_2}:\vec{0}\neq x\in\mathbb R^d,\ \sum_{i=1}^d x_i=0\right\} = \max\left\{2^{1/q-1/2},\left(\frac{(d-1)^{q/2}+(d-1)^{1-q/2}}{d^{q/2}}\right)^{1/q}\right\}. \] They proved the $d=3$ case in \cite{HU26}. In this paper, we confirm the conjecture of the remaining cases $d\ge 4$.

</details>

### [25] [Concurrence of Symmetry Breaking and Nonlocality Phase Transitions in Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04830)
*Yifan F. Zhang,Fangjun Hu,Guangkuo Liu,Mert Okyay,Xun Gao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了现代扩散变换器（diffusion transformers）中两类相变（phase transition）诊断——对称性破缺（symmetry breaking）与非局域性（nonlocality）——的发生时间，发现二者在生成动力学中几乎同时出现，首次在实践中统一了这两种相变概念，为扩散模型依赖条件控制与全局去噪的时机提供了具体诊断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型在生成动力学的一个临界时间窗口（critical time window）中会发生相变，但现有研究分别从对称性破缺（轨迹分叉进入不同语义极小值）和非局域性（局部去噪失效）两个互补视角来描述这种临界行为。此前尚不清楚这两种相变概念在现代扩散变换器中是否同步发生，因而缺乏统一的理论理解。

Method: 通过评估生成轨迹的动力学过程与输出结果，在扩散变换器中分别测量对称性破缺临界时间与非局域性临界时间，并比较二者是否同时出现。

Result: 观察发现，非局域性临界时间与对称性破缺临界时间几乎同时发生（near-simultaneous occurrence），表明两种相变诊断在扩散变换器中是同步的。

Conclusion: 该工作首次在实践中统一了扩散模型中两类相变概念，为判断模型何时依赖于条件控制（conditioning）与全局去噪（global denoising）提供了具体诊断工具。这一发现有助于从原理上评估模型效率，并指导设计避免不必要计算的架构与采样方案。

Abstract: Diffusion models undergo a phase transition in a critical time window during generation dynamics, with two complementary diagnoses of criticality. The symmetry breaking picture views the critical window as when trajectories bifurcate into different semantic minima of the energy landscape, whereas the nonlocality picture views the critical window as when local denoising fails. We study whether two notions of such phase transitions are concurrent in modern diffusion transformers. By evaluating the dynamics and outcomes of the generation trajectory, we observe a near-simultaneous occurrence of the non-locality and symmetry breaking critical times. Our work is the first to unify the two notions of phase transitions in practice: it provides a concrete diagnostic for when and why diffusion models rely on conditioning and global denoising, enabling principled evaluation of model efficiency and guiding the design of architectures and sampling schemes that avoid unnecessary computation.

</details>

### [26] [Mixed Global Dynamics of the Forced Vibro-Impact Oscillator with Coulomb Friction and its Symplectic Structure, KAM Tori, and Persistence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05605)
*Abdoulaye Thiam*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文对Gendelman等人(2019)发现的受迫振动-碰撞振子（forced vibro-impact oscillator）中哈密顿稳定岛与耗散吸引子共存的现象提供了完整的数学分析，证明了系统的辛结构（symplectic structure）与KAM环面（KAM tori）的存在性，并揭示了正恢复缺陷（restitution defect）或粘性阻尼（viscous damping）对保守结构的破坏作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gendelman等人(2019)发现受迫振动-碰撞振子在单一相空间中同时存在哈密顿稳定岛（Hamiltonian stability islands）和耗散吸引子（dissipative attractors），但缺乏完整的数学解释。本文旨在对此现象提供严格的数学分析，纠正先前工作中的普适性声称（universality claim），并揭示系统在不同参数条件下的动力学行为转变。

Method: 本文利用Filippov流（Filippov flow）理论证明系统的全局适定性（global well-posedness），并在覆盖流形（covering manifold）上构造到分段光滑哈密顿系统（piecewise smooth Hamiltonian system）的全局提升（global lift）。通过辛动力学（symplectic dynamics）形式证明最大正向不变非粘着集（maximal forward-invariant non-sticking set）上的时间-T 频闪映射（time-T stroboscopic map）是精确辛的（exact symplectic）。推导对称T周期轨道的闭式存在方程，并运用Moser扭转定理（Moser's twist theorem）证明椭圆非粘着周期轨道附近不变Cantor族（KAM环面）的存在性，同时通过Melnikov分析（Melnikov analysis）获得与Bernoulli移位（Bernoulli shift）共轭的双曲动力学。采用计算机辅助证明（computer-assisted proof）验证特定参数点下非粘着周期轨道的存在性与椭圆性。

Result: 建立了参数依赖的鞍-中心分岔（saddle-center bifurcation）方程f_sc(F,ω,R)，纠正了先前工作中的普适性声称。证明了椭圆非粘着周期轨道附近存在不变Cantor族（KAM环面），鞍点附近存在与Bernoulli移位共轭的双曲动力学。任何正恢复缺陷或粘性阻尼都会破坏保守结构：椭圆周期轨道持续存在但变为渐近稳定（asymptotically stable），哈密顿稳定岛被单一吸引盆地（attracting basin）取代。该方法可推广至具有弹性碰撞的多粒子系统，获得辛结构和高维KAM环面。

Conclusion: 本文对哈密顿稳定性与耗散性在同一相空间共存的现象提供了完整的数学基础，揭示了干摩擦（dry friction）与弹性壁碰撞（elastic walls）耦合系统中保守与耗散动力学之间的精确边界。纠正了先前文献中的不准确结论，并建立了从保守到完全耗散结构的转变机制。该方法框架可推广至更一般的多粒子弹性碰撞系统。

Abstract: The forced vibro-impact oscillator with Amonton-Coulomb friction and elastic walls was shown by Gendelman et al. (2019) to exhibit a coexistence of Hamiltonian stability islands and dissipative attractors in a single phase space. We provide a complete mathematical analysis of this phenomenon. We prove global well-posedness of the associated Filippov flow and construct a global lift to a piecewise smooth Hamiltonian system on a covering manifold. On the maximal forward-invariant non-sticking set, we show that the time-$T$ stroboscopic map is exact symplectic, within the formalism of symplectic dynamics. We derive a closed-form existence equation for symmetric $T$-periodic orbits and establish a parameter-dependent saddle-center bifurcation at $f_{\rm sc}(F,ω,R)$, correcting a universality claim in prior work. Using Moser's twist theorem, we prove the existence of invariant Cantor families (KAM tori) near elliptic non-sticking periodic orbits, while a Melnikov analysis yields hyperbolic dynamics conjugate to a Bernoulli shift near the associated saddle. We further show that any positive restitution defect or viscous damping destroys the conservative structure: elliptic periodic orbits persist but become asymptotically stable, replacing Hamiltonian islands by a single attracting basin. The approach extends to multi-particle systems with elastic collisions, where a symplectic structure and higher-dimensional KAM tori are obtained. A computer-assisted proof verifies the existence and ellipticity of a non-sticking periodic orbit at a specific parameter point.

</details>


### [27] [Integrable perturbations of polynomial Hamiltonian systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06626)
*Dmitry Treschev*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文证明，在实解析哈密顿系统（Hamiltonian system）中，对于原点处的非退化平衡位置，在特定非共振条件下，可通过添加一个在原点处为高阶小量（阶数≥M+1）的实解析扰动项，使得扰动后的哈密顿系统在全局辛空间（ℝ^{2n}, dy∧dx）上完全可积。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究哈密顿系统在平衡位置附近的动力学行为，特别是通过微小扰动实现完全可积性（complete integrability）的可能性。

Method: 选择辛空间（symplectic space）上的实解析哈密顿函数，在原点处存在非退化平衡位置，并在非共振假设（nonresonance assumptions）下构造一个满足条件的实解析函数F，使系统变为完全可积。

Result: 对任意正整数M，存在一个实解析函数F，其在原点处为O(|x|+|y|)^{M+1}的高阶小量，且扰动后的哈密顿系统在ℝ^{2n}上完全可积。

Conclusion: 通过适当的高阶扰动，可使哈密顿系统在非退化平衡点附近实现全局完全可积。

Abstract: We consider a Hamiltonian system on the symplectic space $({\mathbb{R}}^{2n}, dy\wedge dx)$ with a real-analytic Hamiltonian $H : {\mathbb{R}}^{2n}\to {\mathbb{R}}$. We assume that the system has a non-degenerate equilibrium position at the origin. Under some nonresonance assumptions we prove the following.
  For any positive integer $M$ there exists a real-analytic function $F:{\mathbb{R}}^{2n}\to{\mathbb{R}}$ such that
  (1) $F = O\big( (|x|+|y|)^{M+1} \big)$ at the origin,
  (2) the system with Hamiltonian $H+F$ is completely integrable in ${\mathbb{R}}^{2n}$.

</details>

### [28] [A polar-factor retraction on the symplectic Stiefel manifold with closed-form inverse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06399)
*Ralf Zimmermann*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文在辛 Stiefel 流形（symplectic Stiefel manifold）上提出了一种具有闭式逆（closed-form inverse）的新型回缩映射（retraction），并对其关键性质进行阐述，与现有回缩方法进行了数值性能对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在黎曼计算（Riemannian computing）应用中，需要将流形数据映射到欧几里得空间（Euclidean domain）以进行向量空间运算，而回缩映射（retraction map）提供了一阶近似的局部坐标。然而，现有辛 Stiefel 流形上的回缩中，仅 Cayley 回缩（Cayley retraction）具有已知的闭式逆（closed-form inverse），这限制了计算效率与可逆映射的灵活性。

Method: 本文提出了一种新的回缩映射（retraction），该映射定义在辛 Stiefel 流形上，并具有闭式逆（closed-form inverse）。通过理论分析揭示其关键特征，并与若干现有回缩方法进行数值比较。

Result: 所提出的新回缩在辛 Stiefel 流形上具备闭式逆，这是除 Cayley 回缩外首个具备该性质的已知回缩。数值对比展示了其相对于现有方法的性能差异。

Conclusion: 该新回缩为辛 Stiefel 流形上的黎曼计算提供了另一种具备闭式逆的可行映射方案，有望提升相关应用的数值计算效率。

Abstract: In Riemannian computing applications, it is crucial to map manifold data to a Euclidean domain, where vector space arithmetic is available, and back. Classical manifold theory guarantees the existence of such mappings, called charts and parameterizations, or, collectively, local coordinates. When computational efficiency is of the essence, practitioners usually resort to retraction maps to define local coordinates. Retractions yield first-order approximations of the Riemannian normal coordinates. This work introduces a new retraction on the symplectic Stiefel manifold that features a closed-form inverse. We expose essential features and compare the numerical performance to a selection of existing retractions. To the best of our knowledge, prior to this work, the so-called Cayley retraction was the only retraction on the symplectic Stiefel manifold with known closed-form inverse.

</details>

### [29] [Superconductivity mediated by nematic fluctuations -- the dispersion of collective modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05433)
*Kazi Ranjibul Islam,Andrey Chubukov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文分析了由长程向列涨落（long-range nematic fluctuations）介导的超导体中集体模的谱。研究发现，该系统的对 susceptibility（pair susceptibility）在纵向（幅度）和横向（相位）通道中的解析结构（analytic structure）与 BCS 超导体存在质的区别，从而导致相位模和幅度模具有高度非传统的色散关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有实验和理论研究指出该类超导体的能隙（superconducting gap）具有高度各向异性并在费米面上形成四个弧（arcs），但其超导相内部的集体激发行为尚不明确，需要深入分析。

Method: 推导了超导相深处有限动量 $\mathbf{q}$ 和频率 $\Omega$ 下的对 susceptibility $\chi(\mathbf{q},\Omega)$ 表达式，并分析了其谱函数 $\operatorname{Im}\chi(\mathbf{q},\Omega)$ 在横向（相位）和纵向（幅度）通道中的极点结构（pole structure）。

Result: 该系统的对 susceptibility 在两个通道中的解析结构与常规 BCS 超导体存在本质差异，由此产生高度非传统的相位和幅度集体模色散关系。

Conclusion: 长程向列涨落介导的超导体中，集体模的行为与 BCS 超导体定性不同，表明该类系统中集体激发具有非传统特征。

Abstract: We analyze the spectrum of collective modes in a superconductor in which pairing is mediated by long-range nematic fluctuations. Previous experimental and theoretical studies have found that the superconducting gap in such a system is highly anisotropic and, at any finite $T<T_c$, vanishes on four arcs of the Fermi surface, even when the pairing symmetry is $s$ wave ($s^{+-}$ between hole and electron pockets). We derive the expression for the pair susceptibility $χ(\mathbf{q},Ω)$ at finite momentum $\mathbf{q}$ and frequency $Ω$ deep in the superconducting phase. We analyze the spectral function, $\operatorname{Im}χ(\mathbf{q},Ω)$, and its pole structure in the transverse (phase) and longitudinal (amplitude) channels, and compare the results with those of a conventional $s$-wave superconductor. We find that the analytic structure of the pair susceptibility in both channels is qualitatively distinct from that in a BCS superconductor. This gives rise to a highly unconventional dispersion of phase and amplitude collective modes.

</details>


### [30] [Enhancement of $J$$_c$ by Proton Irradiation in HgBa$_2$Ca$_2$Cu$_3$O$_8$$_+$$_δ$ Single Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05800)
*Wenjie Li,Ran Guo,Xin Zhou,Qiang Hou,Mengqin Liu,Longfei Sun,Yuhang Zu,Wenshan Hong,Yuan Li,Sheng Li,Yue Sun,Zhixiang Shi,Tsuyoshi Tamegai*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过3 MeV质子辐照实验在HgBa₂Ca₂Cu₃O₈₊δ单晶中引入钉扎中心，显著提升了临界电流密度。在2 K自场下，临界电流密度从5.5 MA/cm²提升至26 MA/cm²（剂量为1×10¹⁶/cm²时达到最大值）；77 K下所有辐照样品的自场临界电流密度均超过0.1 MA/cm²。辐照后观察到临界电流密度对磁场的幂律依赖关系，幂指数α接近1，并观察到归一化磁弛豫率的单调磁场依赖行为。通过辐照前后钉扎力密度的分析，观察到钉扎机制的明确转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临界电流密度（critical current density）是超导实际应用的关键参数。本研究旨在通过质子辐照引入钉扎中心（pinning centers），探究其对HgBa₂Ca₂Cu₃O₈₊δ（Hg1223）单晶临界电流密度的增强效果及相关物理机制。

Method: 对HgBa₂Ca₂Cu₃O₈₊δ单晶进行了3 MeV质子辐照实验，通过控制辐照剂量引入钉扎中心。测量了辐照前后不同温度与磁场条件下的临界电流密度、归一化磁弛豫率（normalized magnetic relaxation rate）以及钉扎力密度（pinning force density），并分析了相关标度行为。

Result: 辐照后临界电流密度显著增强，在2 K自场下，临界电流密度从辐照前的5.5 MA/cm²提升至辐照后的26 MA/cm²（最高剂量1×10¹⁶/cm²）。在77 K下，所有辐照样品的自场临界电流密度均超过0.1 MA/cm²。辐照后观察到临界电流密度对磁场的幂律依赖关系（power-law dependence），幂指数α接近1。归一化磁弛豫率呈现单调的磁场依赖关系，可能归因于Hg1223单晶的大各向异性（anisotropy）导致的低不可逆场（irreversibility field）。

Conclusion: 质子辐照可有效引入钉扎中心并显著增强Hg1223单晶的临界电流密度。辐照前后钉扎力密度的分析表明，钉扎机制发生了明确转变（clear mechanism change）。

Abstract: Critical current density is the key parameter for the practical application of superconductivity. In this study, 3 MeV proton irradiation experiments were conducted on HgBa$_2$Ca$_2$Cu$_3$O$_8$$_+$$_δ$ single crystals to introduce pinning centers. The critical current density is found to be strongly enhanced after the irradiation with its maximum at a dose of 1$\times$10$^{16}$/cm$^2$, where the self-field critical current density at 2 K is enhanced from 5.5 MA/cm$^2$ to 26 MA/cm$^2$. At 77 K, the self-field critical current density for all irradiated crystals is over 0.1 MA/cm$^2$. The power-law dependence of the critical current density on the magnetic field is observed after irradiation, with a large power-law exponent $α$ close to 1. A monotonic magnetic field dependence of the normalized magnetic relaxation rate is observed, which could be attributed to the low irreversibility field caused by the large anisotropy in Hg1223 single crystals. Through the analysis of the pinning force density of the crystal before and after irradiation, a clear mechanism change has been observed.

</details>


### [31] [Massive Mitigation of Transport AC Losses in Superconducting Hybrid CORC-TSTC Cables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05981)
*Hasan N. Al-Ssalih,Antonio Badía-Majós,Harold S. Ruiz*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过全三维电磁模型，系统研究了电流注入策略对混合型高温超导电缆（CORC-TSTC）内部电动力学行为及交流损耗的影响，揭示了非绝缘馈电导致强电流重新分布、波形畸变和高损耗，而绝缘馈电（独立供电）可抑制导体间电流交换，将交流损耗降低高达90%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高电流超导电缆是下一代电力传输系统的关键技术，但其部署受限于传输交流损耗（transport AC losses）。混合型CORC-TSTC超导电缆虽具高电流容量与紧凑结构优势，但其在传输电流工况下的电动力学响应，尤其是电流注入条件如何控制内部电流再分布，尚不明确。

Method: 采用先前已在等效电缆磁化实验中得到验证的全三维电磁模型（fully-3D electromagnetic model），在自场（self-field）条件下，对比两种电流注入策略：一是通过CORC与TSTC导体的公共连接注入总电流（非绝缘馈电，non-insulated feeding），二是对每个导体独立供电（绝缘馈电，insulated feeding）。

Result: 非绝缘馈电设计中，电耦合（electrical coupling）导致强电流重新分布、显著波形畸变（waveform distortion）以及CORC层接近磁饱和时的高交流损耗。绝缘馈电则抑制导体间电流交换，稳定电流波形，且在实用工作电流下，传输交流损耗相比传统馈电方案降低高达90%。

Conclusion: 电流注入策略是决定混合超导电缆内部电动力学与能量耗散的核心因素；在馈电端将各组成导体进行电学解耦（electrical decoupling），是实现超高效率电力电缆的一种简单且可扩展的途径。

Abstract: High-current superconducting cables are emerging as key enablers for next-generation power transmission systems; however, their deployment is often limited by transport AC losses. Hybrid superconducting cables combining Conductor-on-Round-Core (CORC) and Twisted Stacked-Tape Conductor (TSTC) architectures have recently been proposed as a promising route toward cables with high current capacity and compact form factors. However, their electrodynamic response under transport current operation remains poorly understood, particularly regarding how current injection conditions govern internal current redistribution. Here, we employ a fully-3D electromagnetic model, previously validated against magnetisation experiments in equivalent cables, to investigate the influence of current injection strategy on the electrodynamics of hybrid CORC-TSTC cables under self-field conditions. By comparing configurations in which the total current is either injected through a common connection between the CORC and TSTC conductors (non-insulated feeding) or supplied independently to each conductor (insulated feeding), we show that electrical coupling in non-insulated designs leads to strong current redistribution, pronounced waveform distortion and elevated AC losses once the CORC layers approach magnetic saturation. In contrast, independent current feeding suppresses inter-conductor current exchange, stabilises the current waveforms, and exhibits an outstanding reduction in transport AC losses of up to 90% at practical operating currents, compared with conventional feeding schemes. These findings reveal the central role of the current injection strategy in governing the internal electrodynamics and energy dissipation of hybrid superconducting cables, and identify the electrical decoupling of the constituent conductors at the feeding point as a simple and scalable route toward ultra-efficient power cables.

### [32] [Josephson spectroscopy study of kagome superconductors toward the deep point-contact regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06150)
*Hailang Qin,Xiao-Yu Yan,Hanbin Deng,Mu-Wei Gao,Guowei Liu,Yuanyuan Zhao,Jia-Xin Yin*

TL;DR: 本文通过将约瑟夫森扫描隧道显微镜（JSTM）推进至深点接触区，发现零偏置电导对正常态电导的二次依赖关系被打破并出现饱和现象，该饱和源于电路串联电阻，并对极小接触电阻下Majorana零模等研究中零偏置电导信号的解释提出警示；同时，确定了JSTM作为原子尺度探针研究低超导转变温度材料中配对密度波态的最佳工作区间。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究将JSTM结推至深点接触（deep point-contact）区，使正常态结电阻降至仅0.15 $h/2e^2 \simeq 2~{\rm k}\Omega$，以kagome超导体为实验体系，测量零偏置电导随正常态电导变化的偏离行为及饱和特征。

Result: 实验发现，进入深点接触区后，零偏置电导（zero-bias conductance, ZBC）对正常态电导的二次依赖关系被打破；此外，观测到零偏置电导出现显著的饱和现象。分析表明该饱和由电路中的串联电阻（series resistance）引起。

Conclusion: 零偏置电导饱和现象对极小尖端-样品结电阻下探索Majorana零模（Majorana zero modes）等奇异物理中零偏置电导信号的解释提出了谨慎警示；同时，研究确定了JSTM可作为原子尺度探针，用于研究低超导转变温度材料（如AV3Sb5 kagome超导体）中的配对密度波（pair-density wave）态，并给出了实现这一目标的最佳工作区间。

Abstract: Josephson scanning tunneling microscopy (JSTM) has emerged as an important technique for probing the superconducting order parameter at the atomic scale. However, the Josephson current in JSTM may behave quite differently when the coupling strength varies. Here, we push the junction to the deep point-contact regime, reaching a normal-state junction resistance of only 0.15 $h/2e^2 \simeq 2~{\rm k}Ω$. We demonstrate, using kagome superconductors, that the zero-bias conductance, a key characteristic of the Josephson current, deviates strongly from the quadratic dependence on the normal-state conductance upon entering the deep point-contact regime. Furthermore, we observe a striking saturation of the zero-bias conductance, which we show arises from the series resistance in the circuit. This also serves as a cautious reminder when interpreting zero-bias conductance saturation or quantization in studies of exotic physics such as that of Majorana zero modes if the tip-sample junction resistance is extremely small. Finally, we identify an optimum regime where JSTM can be used as an atomic-scale probe for studying pair-density wave states in materials with low superconducting transition temperature, such as AV3Sb5 kagome superconductors.

### [33] [Pair-Breaking and Dimensionality in Spin-Orbit Coupled Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06514)

Method: 采用多机制Kharitonov-Feigel'man框架，对LaBi2薄膜进行厚度依赖性超导分析；通过解析薄极限（thin-limit）下场增强超导现象，分别估算自旋交换散射（spin exchange scattering）、顺磁效应（paramagnetic effects）和轨道效应（orbital effects）的贡献。

Result: 在薄极限下观测到场增强超导现象，并据此估算了自旋交换散射在退配对中的作用；明确了不同退配对通道（顺磁与轨道效应）的相对贡献。

Conclusion: 该分析重新界定了临界温度（critical temperature）和Pauli极限（Pauli limit）等基本物理量的定义方式，改变了二维超导体中散射时间（scattering times）的诠释图景。

Abstract: The response of ultra-thin superconducting materials under parallel magnetic fields is often leveraged to obtain insight into the nature of the condensate, including features attributable to unconventional forms of pairing. Despite there being multiple competing mechanisms responsible for suppressing superconductivity, it is common for these analyses to overlook certain depairing channels. Here we report an analysis of thickness dependent superconductivity in thin films of \ce{LaBi2} using the multi-mechanism Kharitonov-Feigel'man framework . By resolving field-enhanced superconductivity in the thin-limit, we obtain an estimate the role of spin exchange scattering, in addition to paramagnetic and orbital effects. Our analyses offer insight into how fundamental quantities such as the critical temperature as well as Pauli limit are defined, recasting the landscape for how scattering times in two-dimensional superconductors can be interpreted.
