### [34] [Charge Scrambling in Strong-to-Weak Spontaneous Symmetry Breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05288)
*Jong Yeon Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究强到弱自发对称性破缺（SWSSB）与荷涨落之间的静态关系，证明连续对称性下长程Rényi-1关联子迫使子系统荷不确定性具有广泛下界，并引入扭结重叠关联子（twist overlap correlator）统一理解非线性SWSSB序、局域荷不确定性及相干荷涨落。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强到弱自发对称性破缺（strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking, SWSSB）虽可通过非线性关联子诊断，但其对守恒荷涨落（charge fluctuations）的直接静态含义并非自动成立，需要澄清两者之间的条件与界限。

Method: 通过理论分析建立Rényi-1关联子长程行为与子系统荷方差（block-charge variance）之间的定量关系；构造退相超流（dephased superfluids）和稀疏固定荷投影子（sparse fixed-charge projectors）等反例；引入扭结重叠关联子（twist overlap correlator），将其分解为强对称性和弱对称性通道，并与Wigner-Yanase偏斜信息（skew information）建立联系。

Result: 连续对称性下，长程Rényi-1关联子及其足够快的渐进收敛迫使子系统荷方差具有广延下界，即截断对称性期望具有广延曲率。退相超流在Rényi-1尾部过慢时可保持SWSSB但荷方差仅为次广延；稀疏固定荷投影子具有广延荷方差但无局域荷转移Rényi-1序或长程条件互信息。弱对称性通道可分离出相干荷涨落。

Conclusion: 这些结果统一了非线性SWSSB序、局域荷不确定性及相干荷涨落的静态理解，为刻画荷置乱（charge scrambling）提供了精确的涨落足迹。

Abstract: Strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking (SWSSB) is diagnosed by nonlinear correlators, but its direct static implication for conserved charge fluctuations is not automatic. We show that, for continuous symmetries, long-range Rényi-1 correlator, together with a sufficiently rapid approach to its nonzero asymptotic value, forces subsystem charge indefiniteness: the block-charge variance has an extensive lower bound; equivalently, the truncated symmetry expectation has extensive curvature. This gives a precise static fluctuation footprint of charge scrambling. We construct examples to show that the implication is conditional and non-reversible: dephased superfluids retain Rényi-1 SWSSB with subextensive charge variance when the Rényi-1 tail is too slow, while sparse fixed-charge projectors have extensive charge variance but no local charge-transfer Rényi-1 order or long-range conditional mutual information. Finally, we introduce a \emph{twist overlap} correlator, which serves as an analogue of charge variance applicable to both discrete and continuous symmetries. This naturally decomposes local block-charge fluctuations into strong- and weak-symmetry channels. We found that the weak-symmetry channel isolates coherent charge fluctuations and is directly related to the Wigner--Yanase skew information. Taken together, these results give a unified understanding for distinguishing nonlinear SWSSB order, local charge indefiniteness, and coherent charge fluctuations.

</details>


### [35] [Measurement-induced phase transitions in disordered fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05306)
*Yunxiang Liao,Max Matheussen,Xinghai Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 通过推导有效场论，证明无序（disorder）不会改变非相互作用费米子系统中测量诱导相变（measurement-induced phase transition）的存在性：d>1时存在面积×对数律相与面积律相之间的转变，d=1时仅呈现面积律相且无相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有大量数值研究，淬火无序（quenched disorder）如何影响测量诱导相变（measurement-induced phase transitions）尚不清楚。本文旨在澄清无序对这一非平衡相变的作用。

Method: 研究一个d维非相互作用费米子系统，同时施加淬火无序和局域粒子密度的连续测量（continuous monitoring），推导描述其长时间普适行为的有效场论（effective field theory）。

Result: 发现该系统受控于与洁净（clean）监测费米子相同的非线性sigma模型（nonlinear sigma model），无序仅通过修改模型参数进入。在d>1时，系统在面积×对数律相（area × log law phase）与面积律相（area law phase）之间存在相变；在d=1时，仅存在面积律相，无相变。数值结果进一步表明，足够大尺寸下的一维洁净与无序自由费米子均呈现面积律行为。

Conclusion: 无序的引入不影响测量诱导相变的存在与否，结论依赖于空间维度。

Abstract: Measurement-induced phase transitions are nonequilibrium transitions between phases characterized by distinct entanglement scaling behaviors, driven by the competition between unitary dynamics and measurements. Despite recent numerical efforts, how quenched disorder affects these transitions remains unclear. In this work, we study a $d$-dimensional noninteracting fermionic system subject to both quenched disorder and continuous monitoring of the local particle density, and derive an effective field theory describing its long-time universal behaviors. We find that the system is governed by the same nonlinear sigma model as in the case of clean monitored fermions, with disorder entering only through a modification of model parameters. This result suggests that the presence or absence of a measurement-induced phase transition is unaffected by the introduction of disorder: in spatial dimensions d>1, a transition occurs between an area x log law phase and an area law phase, whereas in d=1, the system exhibits only an area law phase and no transition. Numerical results further demonstrate that both clean and disordered one-dimensional free fermions exhibit area-law behavior when the system size is large enough.

</details>


### [36] [Frustrated Fields: Statistical Field Theory for Frustrated Brownian Particles on 2D Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05366)
*Igor Halperin*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个统计场论（statistical field theory）来描述二维紧致黎曼流形上具有淬火随机配对相互作用的布朗粒子系统的大N极限。通过粒子模拟支持下的环状鞍点解和Born-Oppenheimer分离，低能动力学被约化为实射影平面上的非线性sigma模型（nonlinear sigma model, NLSM），并用单个低能常数——旋转扩散系数（rotational diffusion coefficient）——复现了多个独立诊断量的行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解具有淬火随机配对相互作用的布朗粒子体系在二维紧致流形上的大N极限行为，特别是其集体动力学和维度约化机制，建立从微观粒子模拟到低能有效场论（effective field theory）之间的定量联系。

Method: 首先构建一个描述该体系的统计场论——受挫场（Frustrated Fields, F2）模型，该模型包含局域与非局域（空间和时间上）的自相互作用，具有自旋玻璃（spin-glass）动力学特征。然后通过粒子模拟发现S^2上密度集中于缓慢进动的大圆环，其取向构成一个指向子（director）。基于这一鞍点解，采用Born-Oppenheimer分离将慢变取向与具有能隙的密度涨落分开，利用对称性将低能动力学约化为(0+1)维实射影平面上的非线性sigma模型（the ℝℙ² NLSM）。

Result: 粒子模拟支持了绝热维度约化（adiabatic dimension reduction）现象：在S^2上密度集中于缓慢进动的大圆环。从模拟中测量得到旋转扩散系数D_rot和静态环剖面f_0后，推导出的有效理论无需额外可调参数即可复现多个独立的取向扇区和密度扇区诊断量。

Conclusion: 该系统在大N极限下的低能动力学可由一个(0+1)维ℝℙ²非线性sigma模型精确描述，展现了从微观粒子模型到低能场论的可检验、无自由参数的约化过程。

Abstract: We develop a statistical field theory that describes the large-N limit of a system of Brownian particles with quenched random pairwise interactions on a compact two-dimensional Riemannian manifold. The resulting Frustrated Fields (F2) model is a non-linear field theory for a smooth self-interacting density field $ρ$ on the manifold, with local and non-local (in space and time) self-interactions characteristic of spin-glass dynamics. Particle simulations show \emph{adiabatic dimension reduction}: on $S^2$, the density concentrates on a slowly precessing great-circle ring whose orientation is a director ($\hat{\mathbf{n}} \sim -\hat{\mathbf{n}}$, even profile). Conditioned on this simulation-supported ring saddle and on a Born-Oppenheimer separation between the slow orientation and the gapped density fluctuations, symmetry fixes the low-energy dynamics to be the nonlinear sigma model (NLSM) on the real projective plane $S^2/\mathbb{Z}_2 = \mathbb{RP}^2$ (the $\mathbb{RP}^2$ NLSM on the projective rotor space) in $(0+1)$ dimensions, governed by a single low-energy constant, the rotational diffusion coefficient $D_{\text{rot}}$. With $D_{\text{rot}}$ and the static ring profile $f_0$ measured from particle simulations, the resulting effective theory reproduces multiple independent orientation- and density-sector diagnostics with no further adjustable parameters.

</details>


### [37] [A transition in the hole probability at finite temperature for free fermions in $d$ dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05431)
*Giuseppe Del Vecchio Del Vecchio,Pierre Le Doussal,Gregory Schehr*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了自由费米气体中空穴概率（hole probability）从高温泊松统计到低温费米排斥统计的交叉行为，通过映射到有效库仑气体（Coulomb gas）精确计算了任意维度下的标度函数，并发现了一个普适的临界相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解自由费米气体中粒子数涨落从高温经典统计到低温量子统计的交叉行为，具有重要的理论和实验意义。

Method: 将空穴概率问题映射到一个有效库仑气体模型，通过求解该模型精确计算出标度函数；辅以Fredholm行列式的数值计算进行验证。

Result: 低温下空穴概率呈标度形式，标度函数在临界点 u_c=2/π 处发生阶数为 3/2(d+1) 的相变，对应库仑气体最优密度中宏观间隙（gap）的涌现。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了自由费米气体中稀有涨落机制在临界点处的突变，理论预测与数值结果吻合良好。

Abstract: In a free Fermi gas at temperature $T$ much higher than the Fermi temperature one expects that the fluctuations of the number of particles in a given region has Poissonian/classical statistics. On the other hand at low temperature the Pauli exclusion principle leads to non trivial counting statistics. It is of great interest from a theoretical and experimental point of view to characterize the crossover between these two limits. Here we focus on the hole probability $P(R,T)$, i.e. the probability that a region of size $R$ is devoid of particles, in dimension $d$, and on the case of a spherical region of large radius $R$. We show that at low temperature it takes the scaling form $P(R,T)\sim \exp\big[-(k_F R)^{d+1}Φ_d(u=2R\,T/k_F)\big],$ where $k_F$ is the Fermi momentum. By mapping the problem to an effective Coulomb gas, we compute exactly the scaling function $Φ_d(u)$ in any dimension. Remarkably, it exhibits a transition of order $\tfrac{3}{2}(d+1)$ at the universal critical value $u_c=2/π$, signaling a sharp change in the mechanism of rare fluctuations, associated with the emergence of a macroscopic gap in the optimal density of the associated Coulomb gas. Our analytical predictions are supported by precise numerical evaluations of the corresponding Fredholm determinants.

</details>


### [38] [Thermodynamics and emergent thermomechanical response of a quantum ring with nonminimal spin--orbit coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05533)
*João A. A. S. Reis,L. Lisboa-Santos,Edilberto O. Silva*

TL;DR: 本文研究了局域在一维量子环上的费米子（fermions）在非最小耦合反对称张量场诱导的有效自旋-轨道相互作用（spin-orbit interactions）下的热力学与涌现热力学性质，发现耦合参数 ξ 会形变角动量分支、重组低能谱，并在内能、熵、热容及自旋-轨道响应函数中留下清晰信号。巨正则系综中费米统计显著增强响应，产生耦合依赖的不稳定性与符号反转；基于自由能指数重求和（exponential resummation）的唯象相互作用拓展显示集体效应可锐化热力学响应并诱发反常热收缩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非最小耦合反对称张量场诱导的有效自旋-轨道相互作用对一维量子环中费米子热力学与涌现热力学性质的影响，旨在揭示谱形变、有限尺寸热力学与涌现力学行为之间的联系。

Method: 采用伴随工作中获得的精确能谱（exact spectrum），建立正则系综与巨正则系综（canonical and grand-canonical ensembles）描述；通过将环周长视为准静态热力学变量（quasi-static thermodynamic variable）构建有效热力学描述；引入基于自由能指数重求和（exponential resummation）的唯象相互作用拓展。

Result: 耦合参数 ξ 形变角动量分支并重组低能谱，在内能、熵、热容和自旋-轨道响应函数中留下清晰特征；巨正则系综中费米统计显著增强响应，产生耦合依赖的不稳定性和符号反转，类似介观 de Haas-van Alphen 振荡；相互作用拓展显示集体效应可锐化热力学响应并诱发反常热收缩（anomalous thermal contraction）。

Conclusion: 自旋-轨道活性量子环中，谱形变、有限尺寸热力学与涌现力学行为之间存在内在关联，耦合参数可调控热力学响应及稳定性，集体效应能引入新的热力学行为。 

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic and emergent thermomechanical properties of fermions confined to a one-dimensional quantum ring with effective spin--orbit interactions induced by nonminimal couplings to antisymmetric tensor fields. Using the exact spectrum obtained in the companion work, we develop canonical and grand-canonical descriptions and show that the coupling parameter~$ξ$ deforms the angular-momentum branches, reorganizing the low-energy spectrum and leaving clear signatures in the internal energy, entropy, heat capacity, and spin--orbit response functions. We also formulate an effective thermomechanical description by treating the ring circumference as a quasi-static thermodynamic variable. This leads to a pressure-like quantity and associated response coefficients, directly linked to the microscopic spectrum. In the grand-canonical ensemble, Fermi statistics strongly enhance the response, producing coupling-dependent instabilities and sign changes reminiscent of mesoscopic de~Haas--van Alphen oscillations. Finally, we introduce a phenomenological interacting extension based on an exponential resummation of the free energy, showing that collective effects can sharpen the thermomechanical response and induce anomalous thermal contraction. Our results connect spectral deformation, finite-size thermodynamics, and emergent mechanical behavior in spin--orbit-active quantum rings.

### [39] [Finite-Time Optimal Control by Noisy Traps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06424)
*Luca Cocconi,Henry Alston,Thibault Bertrand*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发现，当控制器本身具有耗散性时，平衡态被动系统的最优控制不再遵循准静态（quasistatic）无限时长协议，而是会出现有限时长的最优协议，该时长在临界涨落强度以上归零；端点约束会消除这一相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为被动系统（passive system）在平衡态下的最优控制通常偏向于准静态（quasistatic）无限时长协议；本文旨在探究控制器自身具有耗散性（dissipative）时这一最优性是否会被打破。

Method: 研究一个由谐波势阱（harmonic trap）约束的布朗粒子（Brownian particle），该势阱的刚度（stiffness）受随机涨落（stochastically fluctuating）控制，并由外部协议驱动。分析在涨落违反细致平衡（detailed balance）时探针-控制器耦合（probe-controller coupling）与系统之间的连续功交换，并基于平均功泛函（mean work functional）的短时展开（short-time expansion）直接观测相变。

Result: 当控制器涨落违反细致平衡时，最优协议具有有限时长，该时长在高于临界涨落强度时消失为零；引入端点约束（endpoint constraint）后，零时长相变消失，有限时长协议在所有涨落强度下始终保持最优。

Conclusion: 在非平衡控制（nonequilibrium control）下，被动系统可以涌现出有限时长最优性，打破了传统准静态最优的认知。

Abstract: The optimal control of passive systems in equilibrium typically favours quasistatic (infinite-time) protocols. We show that a breakdown of quasistatic optimality occurs when the controller itself is dissipative. Concretely, we study a Brownian particle confined by a harmonic trap with stochastically fluctuating stiffness, driven by an external protocol. When these fluctuations violate detailed balance, the probe-controller coupling continuously exchanges work with the system, altering the optimisation landscape. In this regime, optimal protocols are characterised by a finite duration which vanishes above a critical fluctuation strength. This transition can be directly observed in a short-time expansion of the mean work functional. When imposing an endpoint constraint, the transition to zero duration disappears and finite duration protocols remain optimal for all values of the controller fluctuations. These results demonstrate that finite-time optimality can emerge in passive systems under nonequilibrium control.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物流、金融、能源和调度中的组合优化问题常涉及多态决策变量（multi-state decision variables）。Ising机（Ising machine, IM）需通过二进制展开（binary expansions, 如独热编码 one-hot encoding）来编码此类变量，而Potts机（Potts machine, PM）能原生表示它们。因此PM被认为应在多态问题上优于IM，但据作者所知，尚无系统性研究验证这一预期。

Method: 对五种代表性PM模型与一种参考IM进行基准测试（benchmark），采用Max-3-Cut和Max-4-Cut两个问题，使用800顶点的GSet图（GSet graphs）和最多50顶点的随机图（random graphs）作为测试数据集。

Result: 参考IM在所有测试场景下仍优于每一种PM；IM的优势从Max-3-Cut到Max-4-Cut显著扩大。当前PM动力学（dynamics）在性能上低于二进制方法（binary approaches），即使在PM被认为有优势的领域也是如此。

Abstract: Combinatorial optimization problems in logistics, finance, energy, and scheduling routinely involve multi-state decision variables. Ising machines (IMs) require binary expansions (e.g., one-hot encoding) to encode such variables, whereas Potts machines (PMs) represent them natively. By doing so, PMs are expected to outperform IMs on multi-state problems. To the best of our knowledge, no systematic study of PM models has yet assessed whether this expectation holds. We therefore benchmark five representative PMs against a reference IM on Max-3-Cut and Max-4-Cut, using 800-vertex GSet graphs and random graphs of up to 50 vertices. Surprisingly, the reference IM still outperforms every PM, and the IM supremacy increases significantly in going from Max-3-Cut to Max-4-Cut. These results provide clear evidence that current PM dynamics underperform relative to binary approaches, even in regimes where they are presumed advantageous. We provide a way forward by quantifying the underperformance of current PMs, as well as by identifying three dynamical properties that correlate strongly with their performance ranking. Our work stresses the need for more systematic assessments of algorithmic performance in order to guide the design of more effective Potts machines.

Abstract: Instabilities in thermodynamic systems are often undesirable, as they can lead to loss of control or even catastrophic behavior. Yet, the same mechanisms can also generate rich nonequilibrium behavior and may play a constructive role in living systems. We introduce a theoretical framework, inspired by Rayleigh's analysis of thermoacoustic instabilities, to study the emergence of mechanical activity. In particular, we derive Rayleigh-like criteria governing the onset of activity and the generation of rotational motion in a slow Newtonian probe coupled to driven chemical processes, described by Markov jump processes. ### [42] [Lack of self-averaging of the critical internal energy in a weakly-disordered Baxter model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05915)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 对于g₀的正负两种符号，临界内能的相对方差均随系统尺寸L增大而增大，并在L→∞时趋于有限常数。这表明临界内能和自由能的涨落始终保持有限，不随系统增大而被平均掉，即缺乏自平均性（self-averaging）。数值结果还确认了先前关于无序伊辛模型中临界内能缺乏自平均性的理论预言。

Conclusion: 在弱无序二维Baxter八顶点模型中，无论四自旋耦合强度g₀的符号如何（从而无论比热临界指数如何），临界内能和自由能均不满足自平均性，因此可靠估计这些物理量需要对大量无序实现进行系综平均。该结论扩展了对无序系统中涨落相关性的理解。

Abstract: We investigate the first two moments of the critical internal energy $E$ in a weakly disordered two-dimensional Baxter eight-vertex model as a function of the system size $L$, evaluated at the pseudo-critical point. Disorder is introduced via an equivalent representation of the pure eight-vertex model in terms of two ferromagnetic Ising models coupled by a four-spin interaction of strength $g_0$, where the Ising couplings consist of a uniform ferromagnetic part $J>0$ supplemented by weak Gaussian spatial disorder. In the critical regime, the model is formulated in terms of interacting Grassmann-Majorana spinor fields with quartic interactions and analyzed, for small positive $g_0$, using a combination of replica and renormalization-group methods. We also run extensive numerical simulations measuring the critical internal energy. Our results show that its relative variance increases with $L$ and approaches a finite constant as $L \to \infty$ for both $\pm g_0$. Hence, fluctuations remain relevant independently of the sign of $g_0$ (and thus of the specific-heat exponent), implying a lack of self-averaging of both the critical internal energy and the free energy. Consequently, reliable estimates of these quantities require averaging over many disorder realizations. In addition, we numerically confirm earlier predictions concerning the absence of self-averaging of the critical internal energy in the disordered Ising model.

### [44] [Large Deviation Functions for Open Quantum Systems with a Strong Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06244)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在具有强对称性（strong symmetry）的开放量子系统中，全局尺度累积生成函数（SCGF）通常呈现非解析性，导致Gärtner-Ellis定理无法直接推导出真实的大偏差率函数（large-deviation rate function）。为此，需要一种新的方法来解决这一理论障碍。

Method: 提出将Gärtner-Ellis定理应用于系统算子空间（operator space）的各个分块（block）中：首先在每个块内通过该定理获得局部率函数（local rate function），再通过极小化（minimization）操作恢复全局率函数。该方法的合理性由耗散冻结（dissipative freezing）现象提供支持。

Result: 在一个解析模型和一个三自旋XX相互作用（XX interaction）模型中验证了该方案的有效性。在后一模型中，发现退相干（dephasing）作用下全局SCGF的非解析点消失，表现为一种回避“能级”交叉（avoided “level” crossing）行为，并利用简并微扰论（degenerate perturbation theory）对该行为进行了定量刻画。

Conclusion: 所提出的分块化Gärtner-Ellis定理方法可有效解决强对称性开放量子系统中全局SCGF非解析导致的大偏差问题，耗散冻结现象为此方案提供了理论依据，解析和数值模型均验证了其可行性。

Abstract: In open quantum systems with strong symmetries, the global scaled cumulant generating function (SCGF) is generally nonanalytic, so the Gärtner-Ellis theorem cannot directly yield the genuine large-deviation rate function. To address this issue, we propose that the theorem remains valid within blocks of the systems' operator space: we first obtain local rate functions for each block via the theorem and then recover the global one by minimization. This approach is justified by the dissipative freezing phenomenon in such systems. We demonstrate the scheme in an analytical model and a three-spin model with XX interaction. In the latter, we find that the vanishing of a nonanalytic point in the global SCGF under dephasing appears as an avoided ``level'' crossing, and we quantify this behavior using a degenerate perturbation theory.

### [45] [Criticality around the Spinodal Point of First-Order Quantum Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06436)

Method: 构建微观理论：在量子自旋临界点附近，共振局域激发（resonant local excitations）动态退耦出一个具有涌现离散平移对称性（emergent discrete translational symmetry）的希尔伯特子空间。将原始哈密顿量投影到该子空间上，得到一个有效哈密顿量，该哈密顿量表现出真正的二阶量子相变及基布尔-祖雷克标度律。在打破Z₂对称性的倾斜伊辛链（tilted Ising chain）中进行验证，并推广至交错场PXP模型（staggered-field PXP model）。

Abstract: Universality and scaling are hallmarks of second-order phase transitions but are generally unexpected in first-order quantum phase transitions (FOQPTs). We present a microscopic theory showing that quantum criticality can emerge around the quantum spinodal point of FOQPTs where metastability disappears. We demonstrate that, at this instability, resonant local excitations dynamically decouple a Hilbert subspace characterized by an emergent discrete translational symmetry. Projecting the original Hamiltonian onto this subspace yields an effective Hamiltonian that exhibits a genuine second-order quantum phase transition (SOQPT) and the Kibble-Zurek scaling. We validate this framework in the tilted Ising chain which breaks Z_2 symmetry, and predict the absence of criticality in the staggered-field PXP model. This work indicates that the FOQPT dynamics is usually governed by an emergent critical point around the quantum spinodal point. Our study establishes a bridge between the dynamics of the FOQPT and SOQPT, and thus sheds new light on the long-standing conundrum of the dynamics of the FOQPT.

*Jan Hauke,Julian B. Voits,Ulrich S. Schwarz*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文利用生成函数（generating functions）和递归关系（recursion relation）推导了一般批次到达-降解模型（batch arrival-degradation model）的完整含时概率分布精确解，揭示了囊泡介导分泌中随机释放动力学与下游激活时序之间的透明联系，并证明激活动力学对到达事件的时间统计、批次大小变异及降解过程高度敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 囊泡介导的离子或分子分泌（如神经递质释放或激素分泌）是细胞通讯的核心机制，但这些事件本质上是随机的（stochastic），且动力学因自发爆裂与持续降解的相互作用而破坏了时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）。已有方法未能解析地刻画这一非平衡随机过程的全时概率分布，从而缺乏对下游激活时序的精确理论理解。

Method: 采用生成函数和递归关系推导了一个通用批次到达-降解模型的含时概率分布的精确解；利用首次通过时间（first-passage time）框架分析到达浓度阈值（代表下游激活）的动力学；并讨论扩展到囊泡耗竭（vesicle depletion）的情形。

Result: 激活动力学并非仅由平均动力学决定，而是敏感地依赖于到达事件的时间统计、批次大小变异性以及降解过程。具体而言，具有相同平均速率的不同到达过程可能导致性质上截然不同的首次通过行为，这反映了时间不对称涨落（time-asymmetric fluctuations）的作用。

Conclusion: 该框架在囊泡介导的信号传导中建立了随机释放动力学与激活时序之间的透明理论联系，强调了涨落的时间不对称性和批次大小变异性等非平均因素在激活动力学中的关键作用。

Abstract: Vesicle-mediated secretion of ions or molecules is a central mechanism of cellular communication, for example in processes such as neurotransmission or hormone release. These events are inherently stochastic: vesicle fusions lead to bursts of variable sizes, releasing discrete packets of transmitters that are subsequently cleared or degraded. The dynamics break time-reversal symmetry due to the interplay of spontaneous bursts and continuous degradation. Using generating functions and a recursion relation, we derive an exact solution for the full time-dependent probability distribution of a general batch arrival-degradation model. This framework also enables a full analysis of first-passage times to a concentration threshold representing downstream activation. We show that activation kinetics are not determined by mean dynamics alone, but depend sensitively on the temporal statistics of arrival events, batch-size variability, and degradation. In particular, different arrival processes with identical mean rates can lead to qualitatively distinct first-passage behavior, reflecting the role of time-asymmetric fluctuations. We also discuss extensions incorporating vesicle depletion. Our results provide a transparent link between stochastic release dynamics and activation timing in vesicle-mediated signaling.

</details>

### [47] [Constraints on the inflationary vacuum and reheating era from NANOGrav](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05310)
*Debtosh Chowdhury,Rounak Nath,Sudipta Show*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本研究利用 NANOGrav 15 年数据，假定随机引力波背景（SGWB）源自暴胀（inflation），约束了张量谱指数（n_t）、张量标量比（r）以及再加热参数（ω_re, T_re）；进一步检验非 Bunch-Davies 原初真空对引力波谱的修正，发现数据偏好 alpha-真空，并大幅缩小了参数 α 的范围；提出频率依赖的 α 参数化可缓解蓝谱倾斜问题，未来引力波实验可检验该频率依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing array, PTA）实验探测到的随机引力波背景（SGWB）可能具有暴胀（inflation）起源，但现有模型在解释观测数据时面临“蓝倾斜”（blue-tilted）张量谱等问题；同时，以往计算通常假设 Bunch-Davies 真空，而原初真空的本质尚不明确，亟需探索非标准真空对引力波谱（GW spectrum）的影响。

Method: 基于 NANOGrav 15 年数据集，采用贝叶斯推断方法约束暴胀参数（n_t, r）及再加热相参数（ω_re, T_re）；引入非 Bunch-Davies 真空（alpha-真空）修正引力波谱，并对真空参数 α 进行统计推断；进一步提出频率依赖的 α 参数化以缓解蓝倾斜问题。

Result: 得到极端蓝倾斜的张量谱指数 n_t=2.20^{+0.36}_{-1.2}，以及类似辐射的再加热状态方程 ω_re=0.33^{+0.14}_{-0.36}；数据偏好 alpha-真空而非 Bunch-Davies 真空，且将 α 参数限制在狭窄范围内；频率依赖的 α 参数化能够有效缓解蓝倾斜问题。

Conclusion: NANOGrav 数据倾向于支持非 Bunch-Davies 真空（alpha-真空）及蓝倾斜张量谱的暴胀起源；频率依赖的真空参数提供了一种解决蓝倾斜问题的途径，未来引力波实验可对此进行检验。

Abstract: NANOGrav and various pulsar timing array experiments recently reported evidence for a common red noise signal across millisecond pulsars. This signal exhibits Hellings-Downs inter-pulsar correlation patterns, providing compelling evidence for a stochastic gravitational wave background (SGWB) signal. In general, such a background can come from several astrophysical and cosmological phenomena. Assuming such SGWB has an inflationary origin, we use latest NANOGrav 15-year dataset to constrain the inflationary parameters e.g., tensor spectral index ($n_t$), tensor-to-scalar ratio ($r$), and explore the implications for the reheating phase through constraints on the reheating equation of state ($ω_{\text{re}}$) and reheating temperature ($T_{\text{re}})$. We find the preference for an extremely blue-tilted tensor spectrum $n_t=2.20^{+0.36}_{-1.2}$ and the radiation-like reheating scenario $ω_{\text{re}}=0.33^{+0.14}_{-0.36}$. Despite having no concrete evidence for the nature of the primordial vacua, the computation of gravitational wave (GW) sourced by tensor perturbations assumes the inflationary vacuum to be a Bunch-Davies vacuum. In this work, we examine modifications to the GW spectrum originating from the non-Bunch-Davies primordial vacuum. We find that NANOGrav observations favour a specific type of non-Bunch-Davies vacuum, known as the alpha-vacuum. Furthermore, our analysis demonstrates that the observations strikingly narrow down the range of the parameter $α$ characterizing the vacua. On top of that, we find that a frequency-dependent parametrization of the vacuum parameter $α$ beyond a threshold frequency can yield a minimal solution to alleviate the blue-titled issue. Finally, we highlight the possibility of testing such frequency dependence of $α$ by probing the GW spectrum through future GW experiments.

</details>


### [48] [Backreaction and the Role of Spatial Curvature in the Cosmic Neighborhood](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05454)
*Marco Galoppo,Thomas Buchert,Pierre Mourier*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本研究利用Cosmicflows-4++重建和协变标量平均形式，首次直接计算了局域宇宙中空间平均的动力学量（包括密度、膨胀率、空间曲率和运动学反作用），发现平均空间曲率在所有探测尺度上贡献约10%的能量预算，而运动学反作用贡献很小（最多约1%），且在该尺度范围内未观测到向全局ΛCDM背景的收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 局域宇宙中空间平均的动力学量此前未被直接计算，而协变标量平均形式为检验宇宙学原理和平均场假设提供了工具。

Method: 采用Cosmicflows-4++重建得到的局域宇宙数据，结合协变标量平均形式（covariant scalar averaging formalism），在银河系周围以共动半径延伸至300 Mpc/h的宇宙学相关区域上，提取域平均密度、膨胀率、空间曲率（spatial curvature）和运动学反作用（kinematical backreaction）。

Result: 域平均能量预算呈现随尺度变化的非平凡结构，反映局域宇宙的嵌套结构；平均空间曲率在所有探测尺度上贡献约10%的能量预算；运动学反作用在最小尺度（30 Mpc/h）上最大贡献约1%；在30–300 Mpc/h范围内未观测到向全局ΛCDM背景的收敛。

Conclusion: 局域宇宙中平均空间曲率的显著贡献表明，在数百Mpc尺度上仍需考虑对标准宇宙学背景的偏离；运动学反作用贡献微弱，支持其作为次级效应的预期；局域宇宙的嵌套结构与大尺度空洞壳层（void shell）的物理图像一致。

Abstract: We present the first direct computation of spatially averaged dynamical quantities in the local Universe, employing the Cosmicflows-4++ reconstruction and a covariant scalar averaging formalism. We extract the domain-averaged density, expansion rate, spatial curvature, and kinematical backreaction over cosmologically relevant domains around our Galaxy, extending up to a comoving radius of $300~\mathrm{Mpc}/h$. The resulting domain-averaged present-day energy budget features nontrivial variations with scale that reflect a nested structure within the cosmic neighborhood, including a large-scale void shell encompassing the local cosmic web. Remarkably, we find significant contributions to this energy budget from the average spatial curvature at the $\mathcal{O}(10\%)$ level on all probed scales. By contrast, the kinematical backreaction remains much smaller throughout the surveyed volume, reaching at most a $\mathcal{O}(1\%)$ contribution on the smallest scales considered, i.e., $30~\mathrm{Mpc}/h$. Convergence to the global $Λ$CDM background is not observed within this range of scales.

### [49] [Engineering Quantum Many-Body Scars through Lattice Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05296)
*Erick Parra Verde,Kevin P. Mours,Johannes Zeiher,Ana Hudomal,Jad C. Halimeh*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该论文表明，仅通过改变晶格几何（将一维链变为准一维三角形装饰晶格），即可在PXP模型中诱导和增强量子多体疤痕（quantum many-body scars）现象，使本应热化（thermalizing）的全极化态（fully polarized state）表现出非遍历动力学，并提出在可编程Rydberg原子阵列中的实验实现方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子多体疤痕的稳定通常依赖于精细调控的初始态或设计哈密顿量微扰，缺乏更普适且实验上易行的控制手段。本文旨在探索晶格几何（lattice geometry）本身是否可作为诱导和增强疤痕的有效控制旋钮。

Method: 利用开放边界条件的PXP模型，将一维链结构变换为准一维三角形装饰晶格（triangle-decorated lattice），通过数值模拟分析全极化态的保真度回振（fidelity revivals）、纠缠熵增长以及与弱纠缠本征态塔（tower of weakly entangled eigenstates）的重叠。理论分析表明几何诱导的约束希尔伯特空间（constrained Hilbert space）重新组织，使邻接图（adjacency graph）分解为超立方子图（hypercube subgraphs），从而稳定近似的su(2)代数。

Result: 在三角形装饰晶格上，全极化态展现出显著的保真度回振、缓慢的纠缠熵增长，并与一系列弱纠缠本征态有强重叠。这种非遍历动力学源于几何效应导致约束空间结构改变，形成超立方子图并催生近似的su(2)代数。

Conclusion: 晶格连接性（lattice connectivity）可作为约束量子系统中设计非遍历动力学的通用设计原则。该方案可通过可编程的镊子囚禁Rydberg原子阵列（tweezer-trapped Rydberg atoms）配合空间光调制器（spatial light modulators）实现，并通过激发密度的时间分辨测量探测疤痕动力学。

Abstract: Quantum many-body scars enable persistent non-ergodic dynamics in otherwise thermalizing systems, yet their stabilization typically relies on fine-tuned initial states or engineered Hamiltonian perturbations. Here we show that lattice geometry alone can serve as a powerful and experimentally accessible control knob for inducing and enhancing scarring. By transforming a one-dimensional chain into a quasi-one-dimensional triangle-decorated lattice, we find that the fully polarized state -- normally thermalizing in the PXP model -- exhibits pronounced fidelity revivals, slow entanglement growth, and strong overlap with a tower of weakly entangled eigenstates. We trace this behavior to a geometry-induced restructuring of the constrained Hilbert space, whereby the adjacency graph decomposes into hypercube subgraphs that enforce coherent population transfer and stabilize an emergent approximate $\mathrm{su}(2)$ algebra. We propose a direct implementation in programmable arrays of tweezer-trapped Rydberg atoms, where the triangle-decorated geometry can be realized using spatial light modulators and the resulting scarring dynamics probed via time-resolved measurements of excitation density. Our results establish lattice connectivity as a design principle for engineering non-ergodic dynamics in constrained quantum systems.

</details>


### [50] [Quantum phase diagrams for bosons in hexagonal optical potentials: A continuous-space quantum Monte Carlo study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06171)
*Danilo Nascimento Guimaraes,Laurent Sanchez-Palencia*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本研究通过连续空间精确对角化（continuous-space exact diagonalization）和量子蒙特卡洛模拟（quantum Monte Carlo simulations），系统分析了超冷玻色子在蜂窝状光学晶格（honeycomb lattice）和六方氮化硼（h-BN）晶格中的相图。研究发现，在蜂窝状晶格中，即便在强晶格振幅下，系统也显著偏离标准Bose-Hubbard模型，表现为莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator）瓣的抑制和高阶绝缘相的缺失，这归因于强密度辅助隧穿效应；而h-BN晶格则由于晶格不对称性、相互作用和粒子填充的相互竞争，展现出包含多种子格占据的多重莫特瓣的丰富相图。结果表明，连续空间处理对于捕捉六方几何中玻色量子相的全部复杂性不可或缺。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 六方光学晶格能够模拟石墨烯（graphene）和六方氮化硼（h-BN）结构，为探索强关联量子物质（strongly correlated quantum matter）提供了灵活平台；然而，现有研究多基于格点模型，缺乏对连续空间效应的充分考虑，因此有必要系统理解超冷玻色子在六方几何中的完整相行为。

Method: 采用连续空间精确对角化（continuous-space exact diagonalization）和量子蒙特卡洛模拟（quantum Monte Carlo simulations）两种数值方法，对蜂窝状和h-BN两种六方光学晶格中的超冷玻色子系统进行第一性原理层面的相图计算。

Result: 蜂窝状晶格中，即使增强晶格振幅，系统仍显著偏离标准Bose-Hubbard模型描述，莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator）瓣被抑制且未出现高阶绝缘相，其根源在于强密度辅助隧穿（density-assisted tunneling）效应。h-BN晶格中，晶格不对称性、相互作用与粒子填充三者之间的竞争催生了包含多种子格（sublattice）占据数的多重莫特瓣，呈现丰富得多的相图结构。

Conclusion: 研究结果突显了连续空间处理对于完整捕捉六方几何中玻色量子相复杂性的必要性，也为未来基于超冷原子的实验实现以及进一步的理论研究指明了方向。

Abstract: Hexagonal optical lattices, emulating graphene and hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN) structures, provide a versatile platform for exploring strongly correlated quantum matter. Using continuous-space exact diagonalization and quantum Monte Carlo simulations, we investigate the phase diagrams of ultracold bosons in honeycomb and h-BN lattices. For the honeycomb lattice, we find significant deviations from the standard Bose-Hubbard model even for strong lattice amplitudes. We observe suppressed Mott insulator lobes and the absence of higher-order insulating phases, attributed to strong density-assisted tunneling effects. In the h-BN case, a rich phase diagram emerges, featuring multiple Mott lobes with various sublattice occupations, driven by the interplay of lattice asymmetry, interactions, and particle filling. Our results highlight the necessity of continuous-space treatments for capturing the full complexity of bosonic quantum phases in hexagonal geometries, paving the way for experimental realizations with ultracold atoms and further theoretical work.

</details>


### [51] [The Kubo-Thermalization Correspondence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06666)
*Songtao Huang,Xingyu Li,Jianyi Chen,Alan Tsidilkovski,Gabriel G. T. Assumpção,Pengfei Zhang,Hui Zhai,Nir Navon*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文建立了“久期热化-线性响应对应”（Kubo-Thermalization correspondence），证明了在弱驱动下，一个自旋与热库耦合系统的长期热化磁化强度与短时线性响应谱之间存在精确联系。该对应关系在理论上和实验上（利用超冷费米子实现的有效自旋-1/2杂质）均得到验证，为从平衡响应测量推断强相互作用量子系统中的热化动力学提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子热化（quantum thermalization）描述相互作用量子系统如何弛豫到热平衡，是现代物理学的核心问题。然而，大多数多体系统的实验信息来源于短时跃迁谱学（short-time transition spectroscopy），通常用Kubo线性响应（linear-response）框架解释。这两个视角——长期热化与短时响应——看似根本脱节，因此需要建立二者之间的精确联系。

Method: 作者在理论上提出了Kubo-热化对应（Kubo-Thermalization correspondence），将一个耦合到热库（thermal bath）的自旋系统在弱驱动下的长期热化磁化强度与短时线性响应谱精确联系起来。实验上，利用超冷费米子（ultracold fermions）在两个内态中实现有效自旋-1/2杂质（effective spin-1/2 impurities），并耦合到一个费米海（Fermi sea）来验证该对应关系。

Result: 该对应关系在稳态与初态差异显著、且两区域各自在理论上难以分别描述的情形下仍然成立。实验测量结果确认了理论预测的对应关系。

Conclusion: 该结果为量子热化提供了一个罕见的精确陈述（exact statement），并提供了一种不依赖于系统-库耦合微观细节的新方法，可从强相互作用量子系统中的平衡响应测量推断热化动力学。

Abstract: Quantum thermalization describes how interacting quantum systems relax toward thermal equilibrium, a central problem in modern physics. Yet most experimental information on many-body systems comes from short-time transition spectroscopy, typically interpreted within Kubo's linear-response framework. These perspectives - long-time equilibration versus short-time response - seem fundamentally disconnected. Here we establish an exact link between them: the Kubo-Thermalization correspondence, which connects long-time thermalized magnetization under weak driving to short-time linear-response spectra for a spin coupled to a thermal bath. The correspondence holds even when the steady state differs substantially from the initial state and when each regime is individually difficult to describe theoretically. We experimentally confirm the correspondence using effective spin-1/2 impurities realized with ultracold fermions in two internal states coupled to a Fermi sea. Our results provide a rare exact statement about quantum thermalization and offer a novel route to infer thermalization dynamics from equilibrium response measurements in strongly interacting quantum systems, independent of microscopic details of the system-bath coupling.

</details>

### [52] [Light-Induced Even-Wave Spin Splittings in Nonmagnetic Centrosymmetric Systems with Spin-Orbit Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05316)
*Xiao-Jiao Wang,Dongling Liu,Di Zhu,Zheng-Yang Zhuang,Zhongbo Yan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过圆偏振光在中心对称非磁性体系中动态产生偶宇称自旋分裂，打破了传统自旋分裂中自旋-轨道耦合（奇宇称）与磁交换耦合（偶宇称）的二分法，并实现了s波、d波和g波自旋分裂能带结构，同时发现了陈绝缘体相及相关的自旋与轨道磁化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，自旋分裂（spin splitting）由相对论性自旋-轨道耦合（SOC，奇宇称）和非相对论性磁交换耦合（MEC，偶宇称）两种机制主导，二者受不同对称性约束产生相反宇称的分裂，形成了非磁与磁体系中自旋物理的二分法。本文旨在打破这一二分法，探索在中心对称非磁性体系中通过光驱动动态产生偶宇称自旋分裂的可能性。

Method: 该工作采用圆偏振光（circularly polarized light）作为外场驱动，在中心对称（centrosymmetric）且非磁性（nonmagnetic）的体系中诱导动态自旋分裂。通过分析所诱导分裂的对称性与底层轨道角动量特征（angular character of the underlying orbitals）之间的关系，实现不同波对称性（s-wave、d-wave、g-wave）的自旋分裂能带结构。

Result: 研究成功在中心对称非磁性体系中实现了偶宇称自旋分裂，产生了与铁磁体（ferromagnets）和交变磁体（altermagnets）相同的s波、d波和g波自旋分裂能带结构。此外，这些自旋分裂能带自然支持陈绝缘体相（Chern insulator phase），并伴随相应的自旋磁化（spin magnetization）和轨道磁化（orbital magnetization）。

Conclusion: 该结果在自旋分裂的两种基本机制——自旋-轨道耦合与磁交换耦合——之间建立了一种直接且此前未被认识的概念性联系（conceptual link），为光控自旋物态开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Spin splitting underpins a vast range of spin-dependent phenomena. Traditionally, two primary mechanisms generate such splitting: relativistic spin-orbit coupling (SOC) and nonrelativistic magnetic exchange coupling (MEC). Governed by distinct symmetry constraints, they produce splittings of opposite parity -- odd for SOC and even for MEC -- a dichotomy that underpins the distinct spin physics of nonmagnetic and magnetic systems. In this work, we break this dichotomy by demonstrating the dynamic generation of even-parity spin splitting in centrosymmetric, nonmagnetic systems driven by circularly polarized light. We show that the symmetry of the induced splitting is controlled by the angular character of the underlying orbitals, enabling the realization of s-wave, d-wave, and g-wave spin-split band structures identical to those of ferromagnets and altermagnets. Furthermore, we find that these spin-split bands can naturally host a Chern insulator phase. We also discuss the associated spin and orbital magnetization. Our results establish a direct and previously unrecognized conceptual link between the two fundamental mechanisms of spin splitting.

</details>

Abstract: Understanding the atomic-scale structure and dynamics of amorphous oxide surfaces is essential for interpreting their chemical reactivity, mechanical stability, and interfacial behavior, yet direct experimental characterization remains challenging. We employ Deep Potential (DP) molecular dynamics to generate large-scale, ab initio-quality models of amorphous Al$_2$O$_3$ bulk glasses and melt-quenched free surfaces, enabling a quantitative analysis of both structure and relaxation dynamics with statistical confidence inaccessible to direct ab initio simulation. The trained DP model reproduces experimental liquid and glass structure, captures the cooling-rate dependence of the bulk glass transition, and corrects systematic biases in the polyhedral populations predicted by widely used classical force fields. At the free surface, mass density recovers to bulk values over ~10 $\unicode{x212B}$, while local coordination requires a slightly wider subsurface region to fully converge. Despite this pronounced structural heterogeneity, the surface relaxes on the same timescale as the bulk and exhibits a comparable glass transition temperature, suggesting that the disordered surface is kinetically stable once formed. Together, these results establish a molecular-level picture of amorphous alumina surfaces and demonstrate the capability of machine-learned potentials to resolve structure-property relationships in disordered oxide interfaces.

Abstract: The current work has investigated the effect of co-doping 3Y-Zirconia (3YSZ) with Sc, Mg and Y by wet infiltration. To evaluate the material properties in an application-based perspective, the Knoop hardness, translucency and grain size was measured. We conclude that liquid infiltration is a viable route to perform co-doping of Zirconia with various co-doping elements.

### [55] [MLM: Multi-Layer Moire -- A Python Package for Generating Commensurate Supercells of Twisted Multilayer Two-Dimensional Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05393)
*Anikeya Aditya,Sampad Mohanty*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出并实现了一个名为MLM（Multi-Layer Moire）的开源Python包，用于构建任意层数、任意布拉维格（Bravais lattice）类型的扭曲多层摩尔超晶格（moire superlattice）中的周期超胞，采用求解-舍入（solve-and-round）算法将重合位点搜索从O(N^4)降至O(N^2)复杂度，支持极小扭转角（<1°）和百万原子级超胞，并通过多种二维和氧化物异质结构实例验证其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 层状二维材料间的扭转摩尔超晶格（moire superlattice）为调控量子电子、光学及铁性性质提供了通用平台。对这类体系进行周期性边界条件下的计算建模，需要识别能够精确或在指定容差内再现摩尔周期性的公度超胞（commensurate supercell）。现有代码主要适用于双层体系，对于三层及以上且各层扭转角可独立选择的体系仍面临重大挑战。

Method: MLM包采用求解-舍入（solve-and-round）算法，将重合位点（coincidence-site）搜索转化为每个扭转角下的O(N^2)线性代数问题，相较于传统蛮力枚举（brute-force enumeration）的O(N^4)复杂度显著降低。该算法支持任意布拉维格晶格（Bravais lattice）类型和任意层数的扭转体系，并采用分数坐标原子选择算法，可扩展至包含数百万个原子的超胞。

Result: 在双层石墨烯、双层和三叠层MoS₂、双层SrTiO₃以及PbTiO₃/SrTiO₃氧化物异质结构上进行了验证，成功生成了可直接用于VASP和LAMMPS模拟的结构文件。该算法在所有扭转角下均表现稳健，包括小于1°的极小角度。

Conclusion: MLM为多层扭转摩尔超晶格体系的周期超胞构建提供了一个开源、高效且通用的解决方案，填补了现有代码在多层独立扭转角场景下的空白，为第一性原理和分子动力学计算提供了标准化的结构文件输出。

Abstract: Moire superlattices formed by stacking atomically thin two-dimensional materials with a relative twist angle have emerged as a versatile platform for engineering quantum electronic, optical, and ferroic properties. Computational modelling of such systems with periodic boundary conditions requires the identification of commensurate supercells in which the moire periodicity is reproduced exactly, or within a prescribed tolerance. While several codes exist for bilayer systems, extension to three or more layers with independently chosen twist angles remains a significant challenge. Here we present MLM (Multi-Layer Moire), an open-source Python package that constructs periodic, PBC-compatible moire supercells for an arbitrary number of twisted layers with any Bravais lattice type. The package employs a solve-and-round algorithm that reduces the coincidence-site search to an $O(N^2)$ linear-algebra problem per twist angle, compared to the O(N^4) brute-force enumeration required by conventional approaches. We demonstrate the package on bilayer graphene, bilayer and trilayer MoS$_2$, bilayer SrTiO$_3$, and a PbTiO$_3$/SrTiO$_3$ oxide heterostructure, producing simulation-ready structure files for both VASP and LAMMPS. The fractional-coordinate atom-selection algorithm scales to supercells containing millions of atoms and is robust across all twist angles including very small angles below 1 degree.

### [56] [Band Unfolding via the Quadratic Pseudospectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05423)
*Christopher A. Bairnsfather,Ralph M. Kaufmann,Terry A. Loring,Alexander Cerjan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于伪谱（pseudospectral）方法的能带展开（band unfolding）框架，将传统能带理论推广至缺乏精确周期性的非周期、无序和有限系统，能够揭示准扩展态（approximate extended states）在能量与晶体动量中的特征，并利用附加算符抑制边界态贡献，从而分离出纯体态行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统能带理论（band theory）依赖于精确的平移对称性（translational symmetry），这使其无法适用于包含缺陷、无序、非公度调制（incommensurate modulations）或大单胞的系统。需要一种能够推广到非周期和有限系统的框架，以预测动量分辨（momentum-resolved）的材料响应。

Method: 采用伪谱方法（pseudospectral approach）识别系统哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）和平移算符（translation operators）的近似联合本征向量（approximate joint eigenvectors），从而生成展开能带结构。在有限系统中，通过引入附加算符抑制边界局域态（boundary-localized states）的贡献，系统性隔离纯体态（bulk-only）谱现象。

Result: 在一维和二维的代表性系统上验证了该方案，包括斐波那契链（Fibonacci chain），该方法能够揭示色散包络（dispersive envelope），同时保留底层谱间隙（spectral gaps）的层级结构。

Conclusion: 该伪谱框架可望为传统能带方法不适用的非周期、无序和有限系统提供一种预测动量分辨材料响应的通用方法（broad framework）。

Abstract: Band theory provides the foundation for understanding electronic structure in crystalline materials, but its reliance on exact translational symmetry limits its applicability to systems with defects, disorder, incommensurate modulations, or large unit cells. Here, we introduce a band unfolding framework that directly generalizes traditional band theory to systems where exact periodicity is absent, and which remains well-defined for both aperiodic and finite systems. To do so, we employ a pseudospectral approach to identify approximate joint eigenvectors of a system's Hamiltonian and translation operators, thereby yielding an unfolded band structure whose features are directly connected to the manifestation of approximate extended states simultaneously localized in energy and crystalline momentum. To reveal bulk-only spectral phenomena in finite systems, we further show that this pseudospectral framework naturally accommodates additional operators that suppress contributions from boundary-localized states, enabling the systematic isolation of intrinsic bulk behavior. We benchmark the scheme on several representative systems in one and two dimensions, including a Fibonacci chain, where our approach is able to both reveal a dispersive envelope while preserving the underlying hierarchy of spectral gaps. Looking forward, this pseudospectral approach may yield a broad framework for predicting momentum-resolved material responses in aperiodic, disordered, and finite systems where conventional band-theoretic methods are not applicable.

### [57] [Strain-Dependent Ionic Transport in Li3YCl6 Solid Electrolytes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05603)
*Wei-Fan Huang,Jin Dai,Jiahui Pan,Mingjian Wen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固态电池中的电解质需在电池运行的力学环境下维持高离子电导率，而晶格应变（lattice strain）会显著影响Li+传输，但其与扩散机制的耦合关系尚不明确。

Method: 基于第一性原理数据训练原子簇展开（Atomic Cluster Expansion, ACE）机器学习原子间势（interatomic potential），并驱动大规模分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟。

Result: Li3YCl6中Li+扩散呈现双区Arrhenius行为，在临界温度Tc处从低温一维跳跃（1D hopping）转变为高温三维协同扩散（3D cooperative diffusion）；拉伸应变增强而压缩应变抑制扩散率，但Tc保持不变；低温下应变通过改变激活能垒（activation barrier）主导扩散效率，高温下则通过修正指前因子（pre-exponential factor）发挥关键作用。

Conclusion: 晶格应变可作为调控Li3YCl6固态电解质离子电导率的设计杠杆（design lever），其作用机制随温度区间不同而迥异。

Abstract: Solid-state batteries require electrolytes that sustain high ionic conductivity under the mechanical environment of a functioning cell. Lattice strain, arising from stack pressure, thermal cycling, or lattice mismatch at interfaces, can either enhance or suppress Li+ transport in solid electrolytes, yet how it couples to the underlying diffusion mechanism remains poorly understood. Using Li3YCl6 halide superionic conductor, we address this with large-scale molecular dynamics simulations driven by an Atomic Cluster Expansion (ACE) machine learning interatomic potential trained on first-principles data. The ACE model faithfully reproduces experimental and \textit{ab initio} structural, mechanical, and transport properties of Li3YCl6. We find that Li+ diffusion in Li3YCl6 follows a two-regime Arrhenius behavior, crossing over at a critical temperature $T_c$ from one-dimensional hopping at low temperature to three-dimensional cooperative diffusion at high temperature. Strain substantially modulates diffusivity: tensile strain enhances it while compressive strain suppresses it, yet leaves $T_c$ invariant, indicating that strain tunes diffusion efficiency without reshaping the underlying transport framework. In each regime, the mechanistic origin differs: altered activation barriers dominate at low temperature, while modified pre-exponential factors become critical at high temperature. These results establish lattice strain as a design lever for ionic conductivity in Li3YCl6 solid-state electrolytes.

Abstract: The stoichiometric antiferromagnetic insulator EuTiO$_3$ is proximate to a ferroelectric phase. Here we report a detailed study of the charge transport and magnetic properties of metallic, oxygen-vacancy-doped EuTiO$_{3-δ}$. Using CaH$_2$ as an oxygen getter to achieve a higher carrier concentration than previously reported, we find that the phase diagram of the oxygen-vacancy-doped system is distinct from that obtained via cation doping. In particular, we uncover a change from antiferromagnetic to ferromagnetic order in the metallic state, with a maximum Curie temperature of TC $\approx$ 11 K at the highest carrier concentration of n $\approx$ 10$^{21}$ cm$^{-3}$. These findings are supported by density functional theory calculations, which indicate a significant change in the nearest-neighbor magnetic exchange constant with increasing electron doping. Finally, we report specific heat measurements that confirm the magnetic transition temperatures deduced from magnetization measurements and corroborate the lattice dynamics picture inferred from the diffuse scattering data.

### [59] [Physics-Grounded Understanding of Thermal Boundary Conductance between Ga$_2$O$_3$ and SiC from a Feedforward Neural Network Potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05620)
*Nuohao Liu,Chen Shen,Yue Cao,Song Xue,Pingfan Wu,Zongfang Lin,Masood Mortazavi,Liang Peng,Izabela Szlufarska,Jiechen Wang*

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一个统一的前馈神经网络势（feedforward neural network potential），用于模拟Ga₂O₃/SiC异质集成界面的热边界导纳（TBC）。非平衡模拟表明，TBC随输运长度减小而下降、随温度升高而增大，且(̄201)取向界面的导纳始终高于(100)取向界面。这一方法克服了第一性原理计算成本过高和经典分子动力学势可迁移性不足的问题，为大规模输运预测和热边界导纳的机理理解提供了有效工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ga₂O₃/SiC异质集成在超宽禁带功率电子学领域具有重要应用前景，但界面热边界导纳（TBC）是散热的主要瓶颈。现有实验难以直接获取原子尺度的本征界面输运信息，第一性原理模拟在相关时空尺度上计算成本过高，而经典分子动力学（MD）势在氧化物和碳化物键合环境中往往缺乏可迁移性。

Method: 开发了一个统一的前馈神经网络势（feedforward neural network potential），并针对密度泛函理论（DFT）数据、体相声子色散关系以及β-Ga₂O₃和SiC中各向异性热导率趋势进行了验证。基于该势开展非平衡分子动力学模拟，研究不同界面取向和温度条件下的TBC行为。

Result: 非平衡模拟显示：TBC随输运长度增加而下降、随温度升高而增大；Ga₂O₃(̄201)/SiC(0001)界面的TBC始终高于Ga₂O₃(100)/SiC(0001)界面。上述趋势可归因于长平均自由程载流子的衰减、在基本不变的谱通道内增强的非相干和非谐界面交换，以及(̄201)界面更强的键合与振动耦合。

Conclusion: 单一可迁移的前馈神经网络势能够实现大规模输运预测，并提供基于物理机制的热边界导纳理解。相关代码已在公开仓库中发布。

Abstract: Ga$_2$O$_3$/SiC heterointegration is attractive for ultra-wide-bandgap power electronics, but interfacial thermal boundary conductance (TBC) remains a major heat-removal bottleneck. Direct experimental access to intrinsic atomistic interfacial transport remains limited, particularly for ideally synthesized materials with defect-free interfacial contact. First-principles simulations are too expensive at relevant length and time scales, while empirical Molecular Dynamics (MD) potentials often lack transferability across oxide and carbide bonding environments. We develop a unified feedforward neural network potential and validate it against density-functional data, bulk phonon dispersions, and anisotropic thermal-conductivity trends in both $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ and SiC. Nonequilibrium simulations show that TBC decreases with transport length, increases with temperature, and is consistently higher for Ga$_2$O$_3$$(\bar{2}01)$/SiC(0001) than for Ga$_2$O$_3$(100)/SiC(0001). These trends are explained by attenuation of long-mean-free-path carriers, enhanced incoherent and anharmonic interfacial exchange within broadly unchanged spectral channels, and stronger bonding and vibrational coupling at the $(\bar{2}01)$ interface. The results show how a single transferable feedforward neural network potential can enable large-scale transport prediction and physics-grounded mechanistic understanding of thermal boundary conductance. Code for NEP training and simulation workflows is available at the project repository https://github.com/knowhow07/TBC_Ga2O3_SiC.git

</details>


### [60] [Si/SiGe multi-channel superlattice structure epitaxial growth with segmented temperature control for Next-Generation Logic Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05667)
*Wenlong Yao,Zhigang Li,Guobin Bai,Jianfeng Gao,Jiahan Yu,Junfeng Li,Xiaolei Wang,Jun Luo*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过降低锗扩散系数（降至650°C时的5.6–7%）抑制Ge-Si互扩散并保持赝晶应变，成功实现了4+4通道堆叠结构，其XRD卫星峰清晰、应变处于完全相干状态、界面过渡区宽度仅为1.5–2.6 nm且均方根粗糙度低至0.08 nm。定量分析表明，底部通道因长时间高温暴露导致界面展宽及Ge浓度从20%下降至18.5%，而顶部堆叠仍保持设计目标。该工作为多通道超晶格中的热预算效应提供了工艺-物理理解，并为2 nm节点以下的先进逻辑器件奠定了高质量材料基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在先进逻辑器件中堆叠多层Si/SiGe通道面临严重的热预算累积（thermal budget accumulation）问题，这通过Ge-Si互扩散（interdiffusion）和应变弛豫（strain relaxation）导致界面退化。因此，需要一种策略来抑制互扩散并保持赝晶应变（pseudomorphic strain），从而提升多通道超晶格的材料质量。

Method: 通过降低锗扩散系数（Ge diffusion coefficient）至650°C时的5.6–7%（基于阿伦尼乌斯估算，Arrhenius estimate），抑制Ge-Si互扩散并维持赝晶应变。采用4+4通道堆叠结构，利用X射线衍射（XRD）、倒易空间映射（reciprocal space mapping）等手段表征结构完整性，并对底部到顶部的Ge浓度与界面宽度进行定量分析。

Result: 所制备的4+4通道堆叠结构展现出清晰的XRD卫星峰、完全相干的应变状态、1.5–2.6 nm的界面过渡区宽度以及0.08 nm的低均方根粗糙度（RMS roughness）。定量分析显示，底部界面因长时间高温暴露而展宽，Ge浓度从20%下降至18.5%，而顶部堆叠仍满足设计目标。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了对多通道超晶格中热预算效应（thermal budget effects）的工艺-物理理解（process-physics understanding），并为2 nm节点以下的先进逻辑器件建立了高质量的材料基础。

Abstract: Stacking multiple SiSiGe channels in advanced logic devices faces severe thermal budget accumulation, which degrades interfaces via Ge-Si interdiffusion and strain relaxation.This strategy lowers the Ge diffusion coefficient to 5.6-7% of its value at 650C (Arrhenius estimate), suppressing interdiffusion and preserving pseudomorphic strain. The 4 + 4 channel stack exhibits clear XRD satellite peaks, fully coherent strain state (reciprocal space mapping), sharp interfaces (1.5-2.6 nm transition width) and low RMS roughness (0.08 nm). Quantitative analysis from bottom to top reveals that prolonged high-temperature exposure broadens bottom interfaces and dilutes Ge concentration (from 20% to 18.5%), while the top stack maintains design targets. This work provides a process-physics understanding of thermal budget effects in multi-channel superlattices and establishes a high-quality material foundation for advanced logic devices beyond 2 nm node.

### [61] [A Scalable Translationally Invariant Variational Theory of Ab Initio Polarons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05675)
*Moritz K. A. Baumgarten,Hamlin Wu,Tong Jiang,Joonho Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种可扩展、具有平移不变性的从头算极化子变分理论，通过动量投影（momentum-projected）Toyozawa型波函数与电子-声子核的低秩分解（low-rank factorization），实现近线性计算规模，适用于从弱耦合到强耦合的全部耦合区间，无需使用超胞（supercell）。在Fröhlich模型、LiF和TiO₂（锐钛矿和金红石）上的基准测试表明该方法能准确给出极化子结合能、热力学极限能带结构及实空间极化子延展度。与第一性原理图解蒙特卡洛（DiagMC）的对比显示，在LiF弱耦合电子极化子中结果一致，但在强耦合空穴极化子上发现DiagMC存在显著偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从头算极化子（ab initio polaron）研究面临耦合强度跨越弱耦合到强耦合的挑战，现有方法（如超胞方法）在计算效率和适用范围上存在局限，亟需一种可在热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下系统改进且不依赖超胞的变分方法。

Method: 将动量投影Toyozawa型波函数与电子-声子核的低秩分解相结合，使得计算复杂度随k点数量呈近线性增长（near-linear scaling），同时能够同时描述离域（delocalized）和自陷（self-trapped）载流子。

Result: 在Fröhlich模型、LiF以及锐钛矿和金红石TiO₂上获得了准确的极化子结合能（polaron binding energy）、热力学极限能带结构以及实空间极化子延展度测量。对于LiF，在弱耦合电子极化子基态和能带结构上与DiagMC结果吻合良好；但在强耦合空穴极化子中，发现DiagMC存在显著偏差（significant bias）。

Conclusion: 动量投影变分波函数为在实际材料中进行热力学极限极化子研究提供了一条可系统改进的路径，可推广应用于不同耦合强度的真实材料体系。

Abstract: We introduce a scalable, translationally invariant variational theory for ab initio polarons that remains applicable across coupling regimes without resorting to supercells. Our approach combines a momentum-projected Toyozawa-type wavefunction with a low-rank factorization of the electron-phonon kernel, enabling near-linear scaling with the number of $\mathbf{k}$-points while capturing both delocalized and self-trapped carriers. Benchmarks for the Fröhlich model, LiF, and anatase and rutile TiO$_2$ yield accurate polaron binding energies, thermodynamic-limit band structures, and transparent real-space measures of polaron extent. For LiF, comparison with first-principles diagrammatic Monte Carlo (DiagMC) reveals close agreement for the weak-coupling electron-polaron ground state and band structure. However, in the hole-polaron of LiF, which is in the strong-coupling regime, we found a significant bias in DiagMC results. These results establish momentum-projected variational wavefunctions as a systematically improvable route to thermodynamic limit studies of polarons in real materials.

### [62] [Polarizable atomic multipoles for learning long-range electrostatics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05746)
*Dongjin Kim,Daniel S. King,Yoonjae Park,Roya Savoj,Sebastien Hamel,Xiaoyu Wang,Bingqing Cheng*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种半局域框架（semi-local framework），利用可极化原子多极子（polarizable atomic multipoles）从能量和力中学习静电相互作用，通过局域等变描述符（local equivariant descriptors）预测潜在单极子、偶极子和四极子，并采用非自洽线性响应（non-self-consistent linear response）捕捉残余的非局域电荷转移与极化。该框架在四个基准和四种短程机器学习原子间势（MLIP）架构上系统性地提升了势能面精度，并恢复了具有物理意义的电学响应，包括Born有效电荷张量、极化率、红外光谱和拉曼光谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长程静电相互作用和极化效应是机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potentials, MLIPs）应用于离子体系、极性体系和界面体系的主要障碍。现有MLIPs难以从标准能量和力标签中学习与极化相关的可观测物理量。

Method: 方法包括：（1）局域等变描述符预测环境依赖的潜在单极子、偶极子和四极子；（2）通过非自洽线性响应在诱导电荷和诱导偶极中捕捉非局域电荷转移与极化效应；（3）将多极子层次（multipole hierarchy）与响应项集成到四种短程MLIP架构中。

Result: 多极子层次和响应项系统性地提升了势能面精度，在长程效应重要的体系中增益最大。学习到的潜在变量恢复了物理上有意义的电学响应：准确的Born有效电荷张量、涌现的极化率、与实验高度一致的红外光谱，以及体相水和杂化MAPbI₃钙钛矿的半定量拉曼光谱。

Conclusion: 该框架具有系统可改进性（systematically improvable）和物理透明性（physically transparent），使得在标准能量和力标签上训练的MLIPs能够预测极化敏感的可观测物理量。

Abstract: Long-range electrostatics and polarization remain central obstacles to extending machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) to ionic, polar, and interfacial systems. Here, we introduce a semi-local framework for learning electrostatics from energies and forces using polarizable atomic multipoles. Local equivariant descriptors predict environment-dependent latent monopoles, dipoles, and quadrupoles, while residual non-local charge transfer and polarization are captured by non-self-consistent linear response in induced charges and dipoles. Across four diverse benchmarks and four short-range MLIP architectures, the multipole hierarchy and response terms systematically improve potential energy surface accuracy, with the largest gains in systems where long-range effects are essential. More importantly, the learned latent variables recover physically meaningful electrical responses: accurate Born effective charge tensors, emergent polarizabilities, infrared spectra in close agreement with experiments, and semi-quantitative Raman spectra for bulk water and hybrid MAPbI$_3$ perovskite. This systematically improvable, physically transparent framework enables MLIPs trained on standard energy and force labels to predict polarization-sensitive observables.

### [63] [A Comparative Study of Projected and Unprojected Schemes for Micromagnetic Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05858)
*Changjian Xie*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文从连续性方程（continuity equation）推导微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulation）中磁化强度（magnetization）模长守恒的数学基础，并比较了隐式高斯-赛德尔（implicit Gauss-Seidel）与半隐式BDF1两种无投影（projection-free）时间离散策略在不同耗散系数（dissipation coefficient）下的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在微磁模拟中，磁化强度的模长需保持恒定，现有方法通常依赖投影步骤（projection step）来施加该约束，但这一步骤可能引入额外数值误差或增加计算成本。摘要旨在探索无需投影步骤、仅靠方程自身即可维持模长守恒的离散格式。

Method: 基于连续性方程推导磁化强度模长守恒条件；对时间离散采用两种一阶半隐式策略：隐式高斯-赛德尔法和半隐式BDF1法；分别在有投影和无投影条件下进行对比模拟。

Result: 当耗散系数较大时，无投影的隐式高斯-赛德尔法与有投影版本在稳态和畴壁运动（domain wall motion）上存在显著差异；若耗散系数适当，二者差异缩小。对于BDF1，无论耗散系数大小，有无投影的结果均高度一致，能有效模拟畴壁运动。

Conclusion: BDF1方法在无投影条件下即可可靠模拟微磁动力学过程，稳定性优于隐式高斯-赛德尔法；而隐式高斯-赛德尔法的无投影性能受耗散系数影响较大。

Abstract: In micromagnetic simulations, the constant magnitude of the magnetization can be derived from the continuity equation. Since the time evolution of the magnetization in the continuity equation is perpendicular to the plane determined by the magnetization and the effective field, taking the inner product of both sides of the model with the magnetization shows that the evolution rate of the magnitude of the magnetization is zero, thus keeping the magnitude constant. From this perspective, the equation itself can maintain the constraint of constant magnetization magnitude. We discretized the continuity equation and compared two first-order semi-implicit strategies in time: one is the implicit Gauss-Seidel method, and the other is the semi-implicit Backward Differentiation Formula (BDF) method. We considered the comparison between these two schemes with and without the projection step. The results of micromagnetic simulations show that when the dissipation coefficient is large, the implicit Gauss-Seidel method without the projection step has significant differences from the method with the projection step in both the achieved steady state and domain wall motion. When an appropriate dissipation coefficient is selected, the difference between the two narrows, and both the steady state and domain wall motion can be simulated. For the other method, BDF1, whether the dissipation coefficient is large or small, the results with and without the projection step are quite consistent, and it can effectively simulate the domain wall motion.

</details>


### [64] [Fermi energy Weyl nodes in $\mathbf{AM}$Te$_4$ ($\mathbf{A}$=Ta, Nb, $\mathbf{M}$=Ir, Rh)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05879)
*Shivam Parasar,Jeroen van den Brink,Rajyavardhan Ray*

Abstract: Key aspects of the quantum oscillations and magnetoresistance in Weyl semimetals $AM$Te$_4$ ($A$=Nb,Ta, $M$=Rh, Ir) persist as open questions, obscuring the link between their topological electronic structure and practical implementations. Employing a generalised search procedure, we carry out a comprehensive scan of WPs accounting for all the subbands close to the Fermi energy, and show that this dramatically alters the WP landscape in these compounds. In particular, we predict these compounds to feature WPs within a few meV of the Fermi energy which significantly influence their properties. Remarkably, most of the considered compounds host WPs of more than one type, including NbRhTe$_4$ which hosts type-I, II and III Weyl points. Our comparative analysis of structure and fidelity of computational parameters/models not only provides a detailed mapping of the complex electronic structure in these compounds, but also clarifies quantum oscillations and magnetoresistance observations in this family, bridging the gap between theory and experiments and offering a framework for precise tunability of WPs.

### [65] [Unraveling the Origin of Ferrimagnetic Signatures in (Fe,Mn,Ga)2O3 Bixbyites: The Role of Structurally-Undetectable Spinel Impurities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05885)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 合成了三种不同 Mn:Fe:Ga 比例的 Fe₂₋ₓMnₓO₃:Ga 固溶体及一个无 Ga 的 Fe₂₋ₓMnₓO₃ 参考样品。采用能量色散 X 射线能谱（energy-dispersive X-ray spectroscopy, EDX）、粉末 X 射线衍射（powder X-ray diffraction, XRD）和 X 射线吸收谱（X-ray absorption spectroscopy, XAS）分析化学组成和晶体结构；利用磁强计（magnetometry）和穆斯堡尔谱（Mössbauer spectroscopy）研究磁性态。

Result: 低温磁异常更符合自旋玻璃（spin-glass-like）冻结行为而非传统长程反铁磁有序（antiferromagnetic ordering）。虽然磁性行为随组分和合成冷却速率有所变化，但这些因素不足以解释文献中报道的巨大差异。一个样品中表现出的室温亚铁磁性（ferrimagnetism）是外在的，归因于痕量尖晶石型（spinel-type）杂质相，磁化强度和电子自旋共振（ESR）测量支持这一结论。

Conclusion: 文献中关于 Fe₂₋ₓMnₓO₃ 磁性性质分歧的根本原因在于样品的化学纯度，并在很大程度上取决于所采用的合成技术。

Abstract: The cubic Fe2-xMnxO3 is an intriguing material that has recently been investigated for various applications, including lithium-ion battery anodes, catalysts, energy storage media, humidity sensors, and photocatalysts. Despite its wide range of promising applications, the magnetic properties of Fe2-xMnxO3 remain controversial, with different sources reporting conflicting information regarding the type of magnetic ordering, phase transition temperature, and magnetic moment of this compound. This work presents a study of the magnetic state of three Fe2-xMnxO3:Ga solid solutions with varying Mn:Fe:Ga ratios, along with one gallium-free Fe2-xMnxO3 reference sample. We performed a detailed analysis of the actual chemical composition and crystal structure of the synthesized samples using energy-dispersive X-ray spectroscopy (EDX), powder X-ray diffraction (XRD), and X-ray absorption spectroscopy (XAS) to evaluate compositional differences. The magnetic states of the three Fe2-xMnxO3:Ga samples and the gallium-free Fe2-xMnxO3 were investigated using magnetometry and Mossbauer spectroscopy. The low-temperature magnetic anomalies were found to be more consistent with spin-glass-like freezing than with conventional long-range antiferromagnetic ordering. Although variations in magnetic behavior were observed and found to depend on composition and the cooling rate during synthesis, our results demonstrate that these factors do not account for the drastically different magnetic properties reported for similar bixbyite-type oxides. Instead, the apparent room-temperature ferrimagnetism observed in one sample is most likely extrinsic and can be attributed to a trace spinel-type impurity phase, as supported by magnetizations and ESR measurements. Thus, the origin of these discrepancies lies primarily in the chemical purity of the samples and, to a significant extent, in the synthesis technique employed.

### [66] [Transformation-mediated twinning governs plasticity in body-centered cubic nanocrystals under extreme loading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06114)
*Jan Očenášek,Jesper Byggmästar,Guanying Wei,F. Javier Dominguez-Gutierrez,Jorge Alcalá*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BCC纳米晶体的塑性行为通常与极端加载条件下的孪晶成核（twin nucleation）相关，但传统剪切驱动孪生模式在高压下受到抑制，现有理论无法解释观察到的非常规塑性路径。本文旨在揭示晶体塑性（crystal plasticity）与结构相变（structural phase transitions）交叉区域中的新型孪生机制。

Method: 通过分析BCC Fe、Ta、Nb、Mo和W纳米晶体在不同压力条件下的塑性变形行为，结合能量景观（energy landscapes）分析，系统比较了竞争性纳米孪生模式的激活机制。

Result: 在弹性刚度适中的BCC Fe、Ta、Nb中，塑性由弹性失稳（elastic instability）触发，通过亚稳态或稳态六方密堆积（hexagonal close-packed, HCP）相介导的双重滑移（dual-shuffle）过程启动，该路径与特征{112}孪晶界面（twin boundary planes）无关，由压缩驱动。在弹性刚度较大的BCC Mo和W中，塑性通过由高度畸变面心立方（face-centered cubic, FCC）相介导的剪切驱动弹性失稳路径进行。

Conclusion: 相变介导的孪生（transformation-mediated twinning）在BCC纳米晶体中普遍存在，其激活机制取决于材料的弹性刚度，打破了金属塑性必须由特定晶面上的剪切应力（shear stresses）驱动的传统范式，为理解纳米尺度金属塑性提供了统一框架。

Abstract: Plasticity in body-centered cubic (BCC) nanocrystals is often associated with twin nucleation phenomena under extreme loading conditions. Here, we reveal unconventional twinning pathways that operate at the intersection of crystal plasticity and structural phase transitions. We show that the classical shear-driven twinning mode becomes progressively suppressed with increasing pressure, giving rise to transformation-mediated twinning pathways involving transient HCP or FCC phases. In BCC Fe, Ta, and Nb nanocrystals of moderate elastic stiffness, plasticity is consistently initiated by an elastic instability that triggers a dual-shuffle process mediated by stable or metastable hexagonal closed-packed (HCP) phases. This pathway operates independently of the characteristic {112} twin boundary planes and is driven by compression, challenging the conceptual paradigm for metal plasticity in which plastic deformation arises from shear stresses resolved on specific planes. By contrast, in the archetypal elastically stiffer BCC Mo and W nanocrystals, plastic deformation proceeds via two alternative twinning pathways associated with shear-driven elastic instabilities mediated by highly-distorted face-centered cubic (FCC) phases. Comprehensive analyses of the energy landscapes to the competing nanoscale twinning modes provide mechanistic insight into their activation, establishing a unified framework for transformation-mediated twinning in BCC nanocrystals across a broad range of loading conditions.

</details>


### [67] [Charge-Transfer Induced Reactivity in sp Carbon Atomic Wires: Towards 0-D sp-sp2 Nanostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06186)
*Marco Agozzino,Eleonora Moroni,Yifan Zhang,Valeria Russo,Carlo Spartaco Casari*

Abstract: Carbon Atomic Wires (CAWs) are finite linear chains of sp-hybridized carbon atoms. Here the electrochemical reduction of CAWs in the form of polyynes (i.e. with alternated single-triple bonds) is reported. Upon applying a reducing potential to a solution containing polydispersed hydrogen-capped polyynes, the formation of a black precipitate was observed. Electronic absorption spectroscopy confirmed the irreversible reaction of the carbon chains while excluding degradation or side reactions. Subsequent analyses revealed that the precipitate consisted of amorphous carbon nanoparticles with tunable diameters. This control over particle size is attributed to the modulation of growth kinetics through restricted mass transport toward the solid-liquid interface. Raman spectroscopy showed that the resulting material exhibits an amorphous sp-sp2 character, with a retained sp fraction exceeding 60%. Smaller nanoparticles displayed reduced disorder within the sp2 domains and a broader distribution of sp-chain lengths preserved in the amorphous matrix. Additional experiments on size-selected polyynes suggest that this synthesis method allows to better preserve the starting chain length in the final structure. Unlike previously reported amorphous sp-sp2 carbon networks, the nanoparticles produced in this study show remarkable stability under ambient conditions, retaining their sp character for times in excess of six months. These findings pave the way for future applications, particularly as further diameter tuning may enable access to the quantum-dot regime.

### [68] [Disentangling magnetic and optical contributions in ultrafast dynamics of antiperovskite non-collinear antiferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06233)
*J. Kimak,Tomas Ostatnicky,M. Nerodilova,F. Johnson,O. Faiman,T. Trejtnar,D. Boldrin,F. Rendell-Bhatti,J. Zemen,B. Zou,A. P. Mihai,X. Sun,F. Yu,E. Schmoranzerova,L. Nadvornik,L. F. Cohen,P. Nemec*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过泵浦-探针实验研究了反钙钛矿非共线反铁磁金属Mn₃NiN和Mn₃GaN薄膜的超快自旋动力学，利用偏振分辨测量和光学建模分离磁性与非磁性贡献，发现Mn₃NiN中由压磁矩导致的磁畴再分布产生类似Kerr效应的磁光信号，而Mn₃GaN中无此效应；温度依赖测量揭示Mn₃NiN从单步到两步淬灭动力学的转变，与Mn₃Sn及铁磁金属的退磁行为形成对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非共线反铁磁体（non-collinear antiferromagnet）是一类无需净磁化即可产生贝利曲率驱动现象（如反常霍尔效应AHE）的自旋极化反铁磁体，对其超快自旋动力学的研究有助于理解此类材料中自旋-晶格耦合与磁光响应的微观机制。

Method: 采用泵浦-探针实验（pump-probe experiment），结合探测偏振分辨测量和基于Yeh形式（Yeh's formalism）的全光学建模，定量分离磁性与非磁性贡献；同时进行温度依赖测量以分析淬灭动力学变化。

Result: 在Mn₃NiN（Γ₄g相，具有显著AHE）中，非零入射角下磁光信号呈现强烈的外磁场依赖，来源于压磁矩（piezomagnetic moment）驱动磁畴分布重新分布，通过类似Kerr效应的磁光效应检测；Mn₃GaN（Γ₅g相，无AHE）则无此磁场依赖。Mn₃NiN的温度依赖测量显示从单步到两步淬灭动力学的转变，与几乎温度无关的Mn₃Sn及金属铁磁体中的I型至II型退磁交叉类似。

Conclusion: Mn₃NiN与Mn₃GaN的对比表明，非共线反铁磁体的磁光响应与晶体对称性（Γ₄g vs Γ₅g）及压磁性质密切相关；Mn₃NiN中的两步淬灭动力学暗示其超快退磁机制可能与铁磁体存在共性，值得进一步研究。

Abstract: Non-collinear antiferromagnets are a class of spin-polarized antiferromagnets in which chiral spin textures give rise to Berry-curvature-driven phenomena, such as the anomalous Hall effect (AHE), without net magnetization. We investigate the properties of thin films of antiperovskite non-collinear antiferromagnetic metals Mn3NiN and Mn3GaN using pump-probe experiments. In both materials, we observe a strong dependence of pump-polarization-independent dynamics, induced by femtosecond laser pulses, on the angle between the sample normal and the direction of probe propagation. In Mn3NiN, where the presence of a sizable AHE indicates the Γ4g phase, the measured magnetooptical (MO) signals acquire an additional, strong dependence on the external magnetic field when the probe pulses are incident at nonzero angles. In contrast, in Mn3GaN, where the absence of AHE indicates the Γ5g phase, the measured signals do not depend on the magnetic field. Using probe-polarization-resolved measurements combined with full optical modeling based on Yeh's formalism, we quantitatively separate magnetic and non-magnetic contributions to the measured signals. We show that in Mn3NiN, the observed magnetic field dependence results from field-controlled redistribution of magnetic domain populations, enabled by their piezomagnetic moments and detected by a Kerr-like MO effect, while this effect is absent in Mn3GaN. Temperature-dependent measurements reveal a change from single-step to two-step quenching dynamics with increasing temperature in Mn3NiN. This behavior contrasts with the nearly temperature-independent quenching dynamics reported for the non-collinear antiferromagnetic Heusler compound Mn3Sn, but resembles the crossover from type-I to type-II demagnetization dynamics in metallic ferromagnets.

Conclusion: 这些结果提供了此前缺失的CrI₃磁振子谱信息，并进一步巩固了其自旋激发具有拓扑性质（topological nature）的结论。

Abstract: Two-dimensional honeycomb lattice ferromagnet chromium tri-iodide (CrI$_3$) has attracted tremendous interest because it retains ferromagnetism down to the monolayer limit and hosts intriguing topological magnons. As a prototypical van der Waals magnet, CrI$_3$ provides an ideal platform for exploring the interplay between reduced dimensionality, magnetic order, and nontrivial spin excitations. Here, using inelastic neutron scattering together with improved sample quality, we uncover the magnon winding feature around the $K$-point of the hexagonal Brillouin zone, a key signature of Dirac magnons. In addition, we find that the magnon energy follows a $T^2$-renormalization behavior at elevated temperatures, consistent with magnon-magnon interactions. This phenomenon is a manifestation of resonance coupling of incident photons with continuum states (Fano resonance). Hpwever, precise mechanism of appearence of the resonance and of related conductivity - surface hydrogenation or specific type of surface reconstruction - remains debatable. We present detailed analysis of infra-red spectra of nanodiamonds of different sizes (2.6-30 nm) possessing the "transmission window" and show that the C-H stretch vibrations of adsorbed functional groups cannot be responsible the the Fano resonance. At the same time, it is suggested that a bending mode of monohydride termination on nanodiamond (111) face may couple with diamond optical phonon, explaining the Fano resonance in some cases. ### [72] [Molecular dynamics simulation study of mechanical properties of 3C-SiC with extended defects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06574)
*Serhii Shmahlii,Andrey Sarikov*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过大规模分子动力学模拟，采用Vashishta势和解析键序势（ABOP），系统考察了扩展缺陷（包括Shockley不全位错终止堆垛层错、双位错复合体与三位错复合体）对立方碳化硅（3C-SiC）弹性性质的影响，发现材料刚度随缺陷密度增加而下降，弹性模量最大降幅可达约4%–6%，表明扩展缺陷网络可显著改变3C-SiC的弹性响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展缺陷（如位错与堆垛层错）对碳化硅等结构材料的力学性能具有重要影响，但现有研究缺乏对立方碳化硅（3C-SiC）中不同扩展缺陷构型如何定量改变其弹性常数的系统理解。本研究旨在填补这一空白，为材料设计与应用提供参考。

Method: 采用大规模分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，分别使用Vashishta势（Vashishta potential）和解析键序势（analytic bond-order potential, ABOP）描述原子间相互作用。构建包含Shockley不全位错（Shockley partial dislocations）终止堆垛层错（stacking faults）以及双位错复合体（double dislocation complexes）和三位错复合体（triple dislocation complexes）的体系，通过改变缺陷浓度量化独立弹性刚度常数C11、C12和C44的变化，并基于这些常数计算有效体模量（bulk modulus）、剪切模量（shear modulus）和杨氏模量（Young's modulus）。模量评估同时沿特定晶向和采用Voigt-Reuss-Hill平均（Voigt-Reuss-Hill averaging）以获取取向无关的总体表征。

Result: 结果呈现一致趋势：Shockley不全位错及位错复合体的密度增加会导致材料刚度下降。在Vashishta势下，平均弹性模量最大降幅约6%；在ABOP下，最大降幅约4%。三位错复合体引起的扰动相对较小。不同缺陷构型对弹性常数的影响程度存在差异。

Conclusion: 扩展缺陷网络能够可测量地改变3C-SiC的弹性响应，在进一步的科学研究和实际应用中应予以考虑。两种势函数的结果在趋势上一致，但定量值有所差异，提示势函数选择对预测精度的重要性。

Abstract: In this study, large-scale molecular dynamics simulations with the Vashishta potential and the analytic bond-order potential (ABOP) were performed to investigate the effect of extended defects on the elastic properties of cubic silicon carbide (3C-SiC). Specifically, we focused on systems containing Shockley partial dislocations terminating stacking faults, along with double and triple dislocation complexes. The changes in the independent elastic stiffness constants C11, C12 and C44 upon varying the mentioned extended defects concentrations were quantified. Using the values of these constants, the effective bulk, shear, and Young's moduli were calculated for different defect types and concentrations. The moduli were calculated along particular crystallographic directions aligned with the mentioned defect configurations as well as evaluated using Voigt-Reuss-Hill averaging to provide overall orientation-independent characterization of the defect-altered lattice. The obtained results reveal a general trend of diminishing the material's stiffness with increasing densities of Shockley partial dislocations and dislocation complexes. Depending on the defect configuration, the average elastic moduli decrease by up to approximately 6 % with the Vashishta potential and up to about 4 % using the analytic bond-order potential. At this, triple dislocation complexes induce smaller perturbations. These findings demonstrate that extended defect networks can measurably modify the elastic response of 3C-SiC and should be considered in further scientific research and practical applications of this material.

### [73] [Moire based strain analysis in wurtzite GaAs -- rock-salt (Pb,Sn)Te core-shell nanowires grown by molecular beam epitaxy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06603)
*Maciej Wojcik,Sania Dad,Piotr Dziawa,Slawomir Kret,Wojciech Pacuski,Janusz Sadowski*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究纤锌矿GaAs核与(Pb,Sn)Te拓扑晶体绝缘体壳组成的核/壳纳米线异质结构的界面结构，并探寻估算拓扑绝缘体壳层中应变的替代方法。

Method: 采用两套分别专用于III-V族和IV-VI族半导体的分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy, MBE）系统生长纳米结构；使用高分辨透射电子显微镜（high resolution transmission electron microscopy, HRTEM）、扫描透射电子显微镜（scanning transmission electron microscopy, STEM）和几何相位分析（geometric phase analysis, GPA）表征界面结构。

Result: 在核与壳材料之间的晶格失配（lattice mismatch）直接导致观察到失配位错（misfit dislocations）和莫尔条纹（moiré fringes）；利用这些特征估算了结晶性拓扑绝缘体壳层中的应变。

Conclusion: 莫尔条纹分析（moiré patterns analysis）可作为一种估算核/壳纳米线结构中应变的替代方法。

Abstract: We investigate core/shell GaAs/(Pb,Sn)Te nanowire nanoheterostructures with wurtzite (wz) GaAs cores and (Pb,Sn)Te topological crystalline insulator shells. The nanostructures have been grown by molecular beam epitaxy using two distinct MBE systems dedicated to III-V, and IV-VI semiconductors. The interface structure of wz-GaAs/(Pb,Sn)Te nanowires is investigated using high resolution transmission electron microscopy, scanning transmission electron microscopy and geometric phase analysis. Misfit dislocations and moiré fringes are observed as a direct result of the lattice mismatch between the core and the shell materials, and used to estimate strain in crystalline topological insulator shells. Our results point to a possibility of using moiré patterns analysis as an alternative, for estimating strain in the core-shell nanowire structures.
