### [74] [Wick Renormalized Parabolic Stochastic Quantization Equations on Rough Metric Measure Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05442)
*Hongyi Chen,Yifan,Yang*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 论文在短时间次高斯热核行为（sub-Gaussian heat kernel behavior）的度量度量空间上，给出了求解Wick重整化随机量化方程（Wick renormalized stochastic quantization equations）的充分条件，并建立了不变测度，适用于巴洛-木上型分形等粗糙空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Wick重整化随机量化方程的求解推广到具有粗糙局部几何（rough local geometry）的度量度量空间（metric measure spaces），例如巴洛-木上型分形（Barlow–Kigami type fractals）及其笛卡尔积，从而为量子场论（quantum field theory）和统计力学（statistical mechanics）在非整数维度中的严格化提供可能。

Method: 利用短时热半群（short-time heat semigroup）构建完整的分析框架，以满足粗糙局部几何带来的技术挑战；基于热核的Hausdorff维数$d_h$、游走维数$d_w$和最大空间Hölder正则性$\Theta$等参数，给出局部解与全局解的充分条件。

Result: 得到了局部解存在的充分条件，该条件依赖于$d_h$、$d_w$和$\Theta$以及非线性项的幂次；对于全局解，需满足基于相同参数的更严格条件；对所有全局解，构造了Markov过程的不变测度（invariant measure）。

Conclusion: 所得结果适用于包括巴洛-木上型分形及其笛卡尔积在内的多种粗糙空间，为在非整数维度上严格建立量子场论和统计力学的相关结构开辟了可能性。

Abstract: On metric measure spaces with sub-Gaussian heat kernel behavior in small time, we obtain a sufficient condition to solve Wick renormalized stochastic quantization equations with polynomial interaction. Given the power of the nonlinearity, the local solution condition depends on the Hausdorff dimension $d_h$, the walk dimension $d_w$, and the maximal spatial Hölder regularity of the heat kernel $Θ$. A slightly more restrictive condition based on the same parameters is required for a global solution. For all global solutions, we construct an invariant measure for the Markov process defined by the solution. Our results apply to many rough spaces such as Barlow--Kigami type fractals as well as their Cartesian products and open up the possibility of making rigorous various structures in quantum field theory and statistical mechanics in non-integer dimensions. In the process, we build entirely from the short-time heat semigroup the necessary analytic framework that accommodates the issues which come with allowing rough local geometry.

</details>


### [75] [Wandering Exponents and the Free Energy of the High-Dimensional Elastic Polymer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05631)
*Gerard Ben Arous,Pax Kivimae*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了弹性聚合物（elastic polymer）在高维连续高斯随机环境中的渐近行为，给出了自由能的显式渐近公式，刻画了低温与高温相的特征，并发现游走指数（wandering exponent）从扩散性（diffusive）到超扩散性（superdiffusive）的转变与复本对称破缺（replica symmetry breaking, RSB）从一步到全步的转变精确重合，严格验证了Mézard与Parisi的物理学结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维极限下研究定向聚合物（directed polymer）在空间相关、时间独立的高斯随机环境中的行为，并严格验证Mézard与Parisi关于复本对称破缺（replica symmetry breaking）的物理学预测。

Method: 通过给出自由能（free energy）的显式渐近公式（asymptotic formula），该公式依赖于两个采样构型内积（inner product）的分布；进而利用该内积分布的隐式公式，刻画低温与高温相。

Result: 当空间相关函数（spatial correlation function）呈指数或幂律衰减时，给出了游走指数（wandering exponent）的渐近形式；弱相关或短程相关下模型为渐近扩散性（asymptotically diffusive），强长程相关下则为渐近超扩散性（asymptotically superdiffusive）；该转变与从一步复本对称破缺（one-step replica symmetry breaking）到全步复本对称破缺（full-step replica symmetry breaking）的转变精确重合。

Conclusion: 该工作严格确认了物理学文献中Mézard与Parisi [53]关于弹性聚合物模型中相变与复本对称破缺类型的多项发现。

Abstract: We study the behavior of the elastic polymer, a model of a directed polymer in a continuous Gaussian random environment that is independent in time and correlated in space, as the dimension of the environment is taken to infinity. We give an explicit asymptotic formula for the free energy, which is given in terms of the distribution of the inner product of two sampled configurations, which we also obtain an implicit formula for. From this, we provide an explicit characterization of both the low- and high-temperature phases of this model in terms of the spatial correlation function of the environment. We find asymptotics for the wandering exponent when the spatial correlation function is either an exponential or a power-law decay. Our results show that when the correlations are either suitably weak or short ranged, the model is asymptotically diffusive. On the other hand, for suitably strong long ranged correlations, the model is asymptotically superdiffusive. Moreover, we show that this transition coincides exactly with another transition where the model goes from being one-step replica symmetry breaking to full-step replica symmetry breaking. This rigorously confirms many of the findings of Mezard and Parisi [53] in the physics literature.

</details>


### [76] [$\mathsf{GL}_N(\mathbb{C})$ Brownian motion and stochastic PDE on entire functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06429)
*Theodoros Assiotis,Zahra Sadat Mirsajjadi*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文构造了一般线性群GL_N(C)上布朗运动奇异值的完整边缘标度极限，证明极限路径满足带对数相互作用的无穷随机微分方程（SDE）系统并具有吉布斯重采样性质，且极限重整化逆向特征多项式满足含非线性乘性噪声和线性漂移的随机偏微分方程（SPDE）。在特殊初始条件下，该线系与Ahn构造的随机矩阵乘积奇异值的通用标度极限一致，并对Hua-Pickrell和Bessel随机zeta函数为平稳测度的两个模型给出了类似结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究一般线性群上布朗运动奇异值的边缘标度极限，旨在理解该非交换随机过程的普适行为，并建立与随机矩阵乘积、随机zeta函数等经典模型的内在联系。

Method: 通过构造完整边缘标度极限，将极限路径描述为带对数相互作用的无穷维随机微分方程系统；利用吉布斯重采样性质与指数布朗桥关联；将极限重整化逆向特征多项式转化为随机偏微分方程；通过与Ahn构造的线系比较进行验证。

Result: 极限路径求解了带对数相互作用的无穷SDE系统，具有吉布斯重采样性质；极限重整化逆向特征多项式满足含非线性乘性噪声和线性漂移的SPDE；特殊初始条件下，所得线系与Ahn的通用标度极限在取对数坐标后一致；对Hua-Pickrell和Bessel随机zeta函数模型得到类似结果。

Conclusion: GL_N(C)布朗运动的奇异值标度极限具有丰富的随机结构，可与随机矩阵乘积的通用极限对应，并扩展至其他随机zeta函数模型。

Abstract: We construct the full edge scaling limit of the singular values of Brownian motion on the general linear group $\mathsf{GL}_N(\mathbb{C})$ starting from general conditions. We show that the limiting paths solve an infinite system of SDE with log-interaction and have a Gibbs resampling property with exponential Brownian bridges. Moreover, we show that the evolution of the limiting rescaled reverse characteristic polynomial solves a stochastic partial differential equation with a non-linear multiplicative noise and linear drift. From a special initial condition the resulting line ensemble coincides, in logarithmic coordinates, with a line ensemble constructed by Ahn which arises as a universal scaling limit of singular values of products of random matrices. We prove some analogous results on the evolution of limiting characteristic polynomials for two models whose stationary measures are given by the Hua-Pickrell and Bessel stochastic zeta functions respectively.

### [77] [Two-mode geometry controls multiscale organization in bipartite systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06208)
*Ottavia Falconi,Giulio Cimini,Pablo Villegas*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于拉普拉斯算子的重整化框架，可直接作用于二分网络（bipartite networks）的双模结构，在保持角色分离（role separation）的前提下进行尺度变换，揭示了系统中普遍性与几何结构的分离，并通过实证网络分析发现了非平凡的多尺度层级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多复杂系统具有互补角色并自然表现为二分网络，但其多尺度结构难以揭示——因为粗粒化（coarse-graining）过程必须保持角色分离，而标准方法通过单模投影（one-mode projection）破坏了这种分离。

Method: 引入一种基于拉普拉斯算子（Laplacian）的重整化（renormalization）框架，直接作用于二分网络的原始双模结构；通过临界态下的受控二分系综进行分析，并应用于实证二分网络。

Result: 结构不平衡性（structural imbalance）系统性地重塑了不同尺度下的组织方式，但保持标度性质不变，表明普遍性（universality）与几何结构（geometry）之间存在分离。在实证网络中发现了两种角色的非平凡多尺度层级；而单模投影后的重整化（截断扩散路径至最近邻）则产生了性质不同的结构。

Conclusion: 双模几何结构（two-mode geometry）是揭示具有角色分离的系统之多尺度组织的基本约束条件。

Abstract: Many complex systems are organized around complementary roles and naturally described as bipartite networks. Unveiling their multiscale structure presents a fundamental challenge because coarse-graining procedures must preserve role separation, whereas standard approaches collapse it via one-mode projections. Here we introduce a Laplacian-based renormalization framework that operates directly on the bipartite architecture, enabling scale transformations while retaining role differentiation. Using controlled bipartite ensembles at criticality, we show that structural imbalance systematically reshapes organization across scales while leaving scaling properties invariant, revealing a separation between universality and geometry. Applying the coarse-graining framework to empirical bipartite networks, we uncover nontrivial multiscale hierarchies for both roles. In contrast, renormalization performed after one-mode projection -- which truncates diffusion paths to nearest neighbors -- yields qualitatively different structures. Our results identify two-mode geometry as a fundamental constraint for revealing multiscale organization in systems with role separation.

### [78] [What You Don't Know Won't Hurt You: Self-Consistent Hierarchical Inference with Unknown Follow-up Selection Strategies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06636)
*Reed Essick,Amanda M. Farah*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文证明在天文巡天数据的后续观测（follow-up）中，无需显式建模复杂的候选源选择过程，仅通过层次贝叶斯推断（hierarchical Bayesian inference）即可自洽地推断天体源的内在群体（intrinsic population）属性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 天文巡天（astronomical surveys）会触发大量后续观测，但候选源被选中进行后续观测的决策过程难以建模，导致从有偏且不完整的观测样本中推断源群体的内在属性面临挑战。

Method: 利用层次贝叶斯推断（hierarchical Bayesian inference）框架，证明即使后续观测的选择决策与感兴趣的潜在参数（latent parameters）强相关，也无须显式建模选择过程即可准确推断内在群体分布。

Result: 通过多个实例展示：（1）后验约束（posterior constraints）的精度取决于后续观测过程本身；（2）若初始巡天选择不完美，则需对污染源（contaminants）群体进行建模。

Conclusion: 该结果可大幅简化涉及多观测者非协调后续观测的群体推断问题，对LSST、Gaia及下一代引力波干涉仪（gravitational-wave interferometers）等巡天项目产生的海量候选源处理具有重要实际意义。

Abstract: Many astronomical surveys prompt follow-up observations, but the decision process through which candidates are selected for follow-up can be difficult to model. This poses a challenge when inferring properties of the intrinsic population of astrophysical sources, rather than those of the set of objects detected by the survey and often-incomplete follow-up observations. We alleviate this problem by demonstrating that explicitly modeling of the follow-up selection process is not required for self-consistent inference of the intrinsic population. Using the framework of hierarchical Bayesian inference, we show that the intrinsic population can be accurately inferred even when the decision to follow up candidates strongly correlates with latent parameters of interest. We provide several worked examples, showing that the precision of posterior constraints can depend on the follow-up process and that one may have to model a population of contaminants if the initial selection is imperfect. Our result could dramatically simplify population inference that incorporates uncoordinated follow-up from multiple observers triggered by the deluge of candidates from surveys like LSST, Gaia, and next-generation gravitational-wave interferometers.

### [79] [Baby Universe in a Coupled SYK Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05291)
*Andrew Sontag,Herman Verlinde*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过分析双标度极限下具有Maldacena-Qi耦合的SYK模型配分函数的三个鞍点，建立了它们与三种不同拓扑时空的全息对偶，并发展出弦图规则（chord rules）来描述这些几何结构；结果发现第三个鞍点对应的Hartle-Hawking弦态中，婴儿宇宙（baby universe）与外部时空之间存在真正的纠缠，为闭宇宙支持非平凡希尔伯特空间提供了证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解双标度极限下SYK模型中三个鞍点的全息对应关系，特别是探索婴儿宇宙（baby universe）的量子纠缠性质及其希尔伯特空间结构。

Method: 通过将有效$G, \Sigma$作用量按耦合$\mathcal{J}$的幂次展开，将配分函数表示为弦图（chord diagram）的加权和；对弦图进行切片操作，在每个鞍点对应的空间切片上生成希尔伯特空间描述。

Result: 三个鞍点分别对偶于三种拓扑不同的时空：一对欧几里得黑洞（两个热圆盘）、热AdS$_2$（圆柱体）、以及带婴儿宇宙的热AdS$_2$（带手柄的圆柱体）。第三个鞍点的Hartle-Hawking弦态中，婴儿宇宙与外部时空存在真正的纠缠（genuine entanglement）。

Conclusion: 闭宇宙可以拥有非平凡的希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space），其量子纠缠性质可通过SYK模型的弦图方法进行描述和计算。

Abstract: We analyze three saddle points of the path integral computing the partition function of the SYK model with a Maldacena-Qi coupling in the double scaling limit. The three saddle points are holographically dual to three topologically different spacetimes: a pair of Euclidean black holes (two thermal disks), a thermal AdS$_2$ (a cylinder), and a thermal AdS$_2$ with a baby universe (a cylinder with a handle). We develop explicit chord rules that span and probe these three bulk geometries. We derive the rules by expanding the effective $G,Σ$ action in powers of the coupling $\mathcal{J}$ and writing the partition function as a weighted sum of chord diagrams. By slicing the diagrams open, we generate a Hilbert space description on a spatial slice for each saddle point. The Hartle-Hawking chord state for the third saddle point has genuine entanglement between the baby universe and the external spacetimes, providing evidence that a closed universe can support a nontrivial Hilbert space.

### [80] [Ultraviolet completion of Starobinsky inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05295)
*Ignatios Antoniadis,Chrysoula Markou,Dimitri V. Nanopoulos*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个包含任意曲率标量函数 $F(R)$ 的 $N=1$ 超引力理论，将其描述为无尺度超引力（no-scale supergravity）中的两个手征超场，并展示了该理论在微扰展开下可得到 Starobinsky 宇宙学模型的微小形变，从而在有效场论框架内解决初始条件问题；此外，一个包含粒子物理标准模型的四维异质弦模型（heterotic string model）可作为该理论的微观实现示例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将 $F(R)$ 引力推广到超引力框架，并构建一个具有任意 $F(R)$ 函数形式的 $N=1$ 超引力作用量，同时希望该理论能在有效场论层面解决 Starobinsky 宇宙学模型的初始条件问题，并与弦论（string theory）所预测的沼泽地距离猜想（swampland distance conjecture）保持自洽。

Method: 利用无尺度超引力中的两个手征超场（chiral superfields）来描述该 $F(R)$ 超引力：其中一个超场包含标量场（scalaron），扮演 Starobinsky 暴胀子（inflaton）角色；另一个包含在暴胀平台上因自发超对称破缺（spontaneously broken supersymmetry）产生的高德斯通费米子（goldstone fermion）。该理论在标量曲率 $R$ 的幂级数微扰展开下，得到 Starobinsky 模型的微小形变。

Result: 该理论中的（复）标量分量在弦论膨胀子（string dilaton）存在下获得非快子质量（non-tachyonic mass），并可被设为零；同时标量场的赝标量伙伴也可被设为零，从而使标量势约化为 $F(R)$ 引力的形式。微扰展开得到的形变解决了有效场论中的初始条件问题，且其有效性尺度低于沼泽地距离猜想所预言的塔状态（tower of states）能标。此外，一个四维异质弦模型可作为该理论的微观实现。

Conclusion: 本文构建的 $F(R)$ 超引力理论不仅统一了 $F(R)$ 引力与超对称，还通过微扰形变改进了 Starobinsky 宇宙学的初始条件问题，并与弦论中的沼泽地猜想自洽。该工作为将修改引力理论嵌入超弦理论（superstring theory）提供了具体的构造路径。

Abstract: We construct an $N=1$ supergravity action whose bosonic part contains an arbitrary function of the scalar curvature, the so-called $F(R)$ gravity. As in $R+R^2$ supergravity, it can be described in terms of two chiral superfields of no-scale supergravity: one contains the scalaron which plays the role of the Starobinsky inflaton and the other contains the goldstone fermion of spontaneously broken supersymmetry during the inflation plateau. Its (complex) scalar component acquires a non-tachyonic mass in the presence of the string dilaton and can be set to zero, together with the pseudoscalar partner of the scalaron, so that the scalar potential is reduced to the one of $F(R)$ gravity. In a perturbative expansion in powers of $R$, one obtains a small deformation of the Starobinsky cosmological model that solves the problem of initial conditions within the validity of the effective field theory, below the scale of tower of states predicted by the swampland distance conjecture. We also show that a particular example of an underlying microscopic theory with such properties is provided by a four-dimensional heterotic string model containing the Standard Model of particle physics.

### [81] [Positivity of the gravitational path integral implies the axionic weak gravity conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05305)
*Gabriele Di Ubaldo,Luca V. Iliesiu,Henry W. Lin,Cynthia Yan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过引力路径积分（gravitational path integral）分析内积正定性（positivity of inner products）对与轴子（axion）耦合的引力理论施加的约束，指出若轴子具有精确的平移对称性（shift symmetry），含特定虫洞（wormholes）的构型会违反正定性条件，从而要求虫洞存在非微扰不稳定性以破缺平移对称性，导出了包含精确数值系数的轴子弱重力猜想（axion weak gravity conjecture）的尖锐版本，并讨论了与沼泽地猜想（swampland conjectures）的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力路径积分可计算开宇宙与闭宇宙不同态之间的内积，但为保证希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）良定义，这些内积需满足正半定性（positive semi-definite），这在低能有效理论中并不显然。因此，本文旨在分析内积正定性对耦合轴子的引力理论施加的约束。

Method: 在低能有效理论框架下，假定轴子具有精确平移对称性，研究包含特定虫洞的构型对闭宇宙与开宇宙联合正定性条件的影响，进而推导正定性条件对虫洞稳定性及对称性破缺的要求。

Result: 在温和假设下，当包含某些虫洞时，闭宇宙与开宇宙的联合正定性约束被违反。若这些虫洞在微扰论意义下稳定，正定性要求虫洞具有非微扰不稳定性以破缺平移对称性，从而导出包含精确数值常数的轴子弱重力猜想的尖锐版本。

Conclusion: 所得约束与沼泽地猜想的可能推广相关，特别是距离猜想（distance conjecture）的虚数延拓（imaginary continuation）；该约束适用于弦理论中的轴子，并具有现象学意义。

Abstract: The gravitational path integral can compute inner products between different states of open and closed universes. To have a well-defined Hilbert space, these inner products should be positive semi-definite, which is not manifest in the low-energy effective theory. In this letter, we analyze the constraints that the positivity of inner products imposes on gravitational theories coupled to axions. If the axion has an exact shift symmetry, we show that, under mild assumptions, a combined positivity constraint on closed and open universes is violated when one includes certain wormholes. In low-energy effective theories where these wormholes are perturbatively stable, positivity requires that the wormholes have a non-perturbative instability that breaks the shift symmetry. This leads to a sharp version of the axion weak gravity conjecture, including precise numerical constants. We relate the bound to possible extensions of other swampland conjectures, arguing for an imaginary continuation of the distance conjecture. We comment on how the bound applies to axions in string theory and discuss phenomenological implications.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 高化学势h下出现非均匀相，a粒子束缚态发生凝聚；在大N极限下该相表现为周期性振荡的手征凝聚（chiral condensate）。原有动力学生成标度Λ被两个新标度Λ_n和Λ_c取代，分别控制中性激发和带电激发的质量间隙，以及大N下平均场的振荡轮廓。

Abstract: We study the crystalline phase of the $O(2N)$ Gross--Neveu model with a chemical potential for $a \leq N-2$ of the fermions. We analyze the problem in three independent ways: using perturbative QFT methods, a semiclassical large $N$ analysis, and integrability techniques (both at finite and large $N$). The resulting picture is consistent across all three approaches: at sufficiently large chemical potential $h$, an inhomogeneous phase emerges in which $a$-particle bound states condense and which, at large $N$, corresponds to a periodically oscillating chiral condensate. In this phase, the usual dynamically generated scale $Λ$ is replaced by two new dynamically generated scales $Λ_{\rm n}$ and $Λ_{\rm c}$. These two scales govern the multiple nonperturbative effects in the theory, corresponding in particular to the mass gaps of neutral and charged excitations on top of the inhomogeneous vacuum, respectively. They also control the nonperturbative corrections to observables such as the free energy and provide the parameters characterizing the oscillatory profile of the mean field at large $N$. In this paper, we provide the necessary details of each of the three methods, thereby complementing the results announced in a previous, shorter publication.

Abstract: The no-boundary wavefunction for slow-roll inflation on the 3-sphere exponentially favors a small universe, in sharp disagreement with observations. We show that this problem is resolved by changing the spatial topology to the 3-torus.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构造包含模依赖的规范动能函数阈值修正（threshold corrections）和超势中非微扰效应的有效理论；利用 Wilson 线的退化极限区分不同扇区，并确定尖点形式（cusp forms）在阈值修正中的组合；通过计算标量势（scalar potential）并分析其极值点来得出一般性结论。

Result: 证明了 Sp(4,ℤ) 的不动点（fixed points）是势的极值点；推导了 genus-2 版本的德西特真空不可能定理（no-go theorems）；展示了在通过 Kähler 势的非微扰贡献沿胀子方向破缺超对称后，可出现正能亚稳极小值（positive-energy metastable minima）。

Abstract: We study moduli stabilization in 4D effective field theories with Sp(4,$\mathbb{Z}$) self-duality inspired by heterotic orbifold compactifications with Wilson lines. The target-space duality group of these theories is enhanced from SL$(2,\mathbb{Z})$ to Sp$(4,\mathbb{Z})$, making Siegel modular forms the appropriate language to formulate the effective supergravity action. We construct the corresponding effective theory including moduli-dependent threshold corrections to the gauge kinetic function and nonperturbative effects in the superpotential. The degeneration limit of the Wilson lines distinguishes different sectors and dictates which combination of cusp forms appears in threshold corrections. We compute the resulting scalar potential and prove several general statements about its extrema. In particular, we show that the fixed points of Sp$(4,\mathbb{Z})$ are extrema of the potential, and derive genus-2 analogues of no-go theorems for de Sitter vacua. Finally, we show how positive-energy metastable minima can arise once supersymmetry is broken in the dilaton direction by nonperturbative contributions to the Kähler potential.

Method: 用稳定因果性和过去反射性替代全局双曲性，用广义第二定律替代零能量/曲率条件，在此较弱假设下推导奇点定理。

Result: 证明了在较弱的因果条件和广义第二定律下，半经典引力中的奇点定理仍然成立；进而得出蒸发黑洞的标准模型必然是奇异的，即存在零测地线不完备性。

Abstract: We prove a singularity theorem in semiclassical gravity without assuming global hyperbolicity or the null energy/curvature condition; the former is replaced by the weaker causality conditions of stable causality and past reflectivity, and the latter is replaced as is standard by the Generalized Second Law. ### [86] [Towards Wedge Construction of Four-Dimensional Non-Supersymmetric Theories and Torsion Classes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05333)
*Keshav Dasgupta,Radu Tatar*

TL;DR: 本文研究带有 G_2 结构的七维流形上的 M-理论紧致化，通过扭结 K3 纤维化构造，分析了扭类（torsion classes）如何描述七维流形的挠率及其引发的四维超对称破缺，并探讨了该体系在两种不等价约化下与 Type 0A 和 Type 0 杂化弦理论的联系。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用一个形变的 K3 纤维化（deformed K3 fibration）作为七维流形的结构，在 Morrison–Vafa 极限下将形变 K3 局部描述为一个非平凡环面纤维化；通过指定双谱分解（doubled-spectrum decomposition）和局部扭结结构（local pinched structure），利用 G_2 扭类（G_2 torsion classes）表征七维流形的挠率。

Result: 扭结形变（pinching deformation）位于 G_2 的 27 维表示中；在两种不等价约化下，该形变分别被分配到对应 SU(3) 结构的 W_2 和 W_3 扭类中。在超对称极限下且满足适当假设时，两种约化后的理论可能互为 U-对偶（U-dual）。

Conclusion: G_2 扭类为描述七维流形挠率和四维超对称破缺提供了自然高效的框架；SU(3) 扭类为约化后的非 Kähler 流形提供了恰当的数学描述。远离超对称极限时，两种理论之间的对偶性需谨慎对待。

Abstract: Motivated by recent proposals relating non-supersymmetric Type 0A theory to M-theory compactified on a singular wedge geometry, we study an M-theory compactification on a seven-manifold with G_2 structure, realized as a deformed K3 fibration over a compact three-manifold. In the Morrison--Vafa limit, the deformed K3 may be described locally as a non-trivial torus fibration over a base that is itself a pinched circle fibered over an interval. Once the doubled-spectrum decomposition and the local pinched structure are specified, we show that the G_2 torsion classes provide a natural and efficient way to characterize both the torsion of the seven-manifold and the resulting supersymmetry breaking in four dimensions. Reducing the system to ten dimensions in two inequivalent ways leads respectively to Type 0A and Type 0 heterotic theories compactified on two different non-Kahler manifolds, for which the SU(3) torsion classes furnish the appropriate mathematical description. In particular, we argue that the pinching deformation lies in the 27 of G_2, and that under the two reductions it is distributed differently into the W_2 and W_3 torsion classes of the corresponding SU(3) structures. In the supersymmetric limit, and under suitable assumptions, the two resulting theories may become U-dual to one another. Away from that limit, however, we argue that any such duality should be treated with considerable caution.

### [87] [Carroll fermions from null reduction: A case of good and bad fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05334)
*Sucheta Majumdar,Aditya Sharma,Sourav Singha*

TL;DR: 本文利用零约化（null reduction）方法从 Bargmann 时空导出 Carroll 费米子作用量，揭示了 Dirac 旋量在光锥分解下的“好”与“坏”费米子分别对应磁和电 Carroll 扇区，并构建了相应的 Clifford 代数、规范对称性、正则结构及两点函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用零约化方法：从洛伦兹光锥（light-cone）表述出发，将 Dirac 旋量分解为动力学和约束自由度（即“好”与“坏”费米子）；通过将 Carroll 流形嵌入环境 Bargmann 流形来构建 Clifford 代数（Clifford algebra），并在单个 Bargmann 不变 Dirac 作用量中同时获得电（electric）和磁（magnetic）两类 Carroll 费米子作用量。

Result: 磁 Carroll 扇区由母理论的动力学模式主导，电扇区则由约束模式产生；对 Bargmann 时空进行形变后约束被解除，“坏”费米子转变为描述电 Carroll 费米子的动力学模式。两类理论均满足 Carroll 变换不变性，且两点函数（two-point functions）展现预期行为。

Abstract: We derive Carrollian fermionic actions using the null reduction method from Bargmann spacetimes. In the Lorentzian light-cone formulation, the Dirac spinor naturally decomposes into dynamical and constrained degrees of freedom $-$ the so-called `good' and `bad' fermions $Ψ_{(\pm)}$. These light-cone projections are intrinsically adapted to the null frame and, unlike the chiral decomposition into left- and right-handed spinors $Ψ_{L(R)}$, are valid in arbitrary spacetime dimensions, both even and odd. As in the case of bosons, the magnetic Carroll sector for fermions is governed by the dynamical modes of the parent theory, while the electric sector arises from the constrained modes. Upon deforming to a Bargmann spacetime, these constraints are removed, promoting the `bad' fermions to dynamical modes that describe the electric Carroll fermions. We construct the Clifford algebra on the Carroll manifold through its embedding in the ambient Bargmann manifold, and obtain both electric and magnetic Carroll fermion actions from a \textit{single} Bargmann-invariant Dirac action. We analyze the canonical structure of both theories, establish their invariance under Carroll transformations, and compute the corresponding two-point functions, which exhibit the expected behavior in both sectors. We conclude with some comments on the quantization of these Carrollian theories.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析虫洞效应推导出理论耦合常数在虚数方向上的解析延拓上限（即虚数距离界限）；在弦论实例中寻找使低能理论在该界限处或之前失效的具体效应，以此验证界限的普遍性。

Conclusion: 虫洞效应导致理论耦合常数的虚数方向存在一个不可超越的上限，弦论通过低能理论的失效来强制执行该界限；该界限与已知的弱引力猜想及复度规条件存在重合，暗示其可能是量子引力的一般约束。

Abstract: Some of the simplest wormhole solutions involve massless scalar fields that take imaginary values. Massless fields can be interpreted as coupling constants in asymptotically flat or asymptotically AdS gravity theories. We argue that wormhole effects imply an imaginary distance bound, an upper limit for the analytic continuation of the theory to imaginary values of these couplings. In string theory examples, we find explicit effects that render the low-energy theory invalid either before or precisely at this wormhole limit. We argue that the existence of such effects enforcing the distance bound is a general feature of string theories containing wormholes. In some cases, the bounds we discuss coincide with the weak gravity conjecture, and with the Kontsevich-Segal-Witten condition on complex metrics.

### [89] [Challenges to Understanding Celestial Holography from the Bottom Up](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05350)
*Adam Tropper*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文通过精确可解的二维 Sinh-Gordon 模型检验了“先变换再展开”与“先展开再变换”两种操作顺序的不对等性，指出在具有渐近弱耦合展开的量子场论中，逐项进行天体变换（celestial transform）的方法可能无效，进而使自底向上的天体对偶性测试变得更加微妙。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在天体全息（celestial holography）的自底向上方法中，通常倾向于在微扰论中逐阶将动量空间振幅变换为天体振幅（celestial amplitude）。本文旨在严格检验这一操作在非微扰意义上的有效性。

Method: 作者以精确可解的二维 Sinh-Gordon 模型为测试平台，利用已知的非微扰 S 矩阵，直接比较两种操作顺序：“先变换再展开”（先对理论进行天体变换再作耦合常数展开）与“先展开再变换”（先在微扰论中逐阶展开再逐项进行天体变换）是否等价。

Result: 两种操作顺序在领头阶非平庸耦合阶上就已经不一致（do not agree），说明在具有渐近弱耦合展开的量子场论中，逐项的天体变换不应被假定为有效。

Conclusion: 该发现对拟议的 CCFT（天体共形场论）对偶有直接后果：若仅通过逐项对微扰体振幅进行天体变换来检验对偶，出现不匹配未必能否定对偶提案。这使得自底向上的天体对偶性测试比预期更为微妙。

Abstract: In the bottom-up approach to celestial holography, it is tempting to define celestial amplitudes by transforming momentum-space amplitudes order by order in perturbation theory. We test this prescription in the exactly solvable two-dimensional Sinh-Gordon model. Because the full non-perturbative S-matrix is known, we can compare two operations directly: first transform and then expand, or first expand and then transform. They do not agree, already at leading nontrivial order in the coupling. More broadly, this suggests that naive term-by-term celestial transforms should not be assumed valid in generic quantum field theories with asymptotic weak-coupling expansions. This has an immediate consequence for proposed CCFT duals: if one tries to test them by taking celestial transforms of perturbative bulk amplitudes term-by-term, a mismatch need not falsify the proposal. This makes bottom-up tests of celestial dualities far more subtle than one might have expected.

### [90] [Small Vacuum Energy and Tunneling in a Modified Bousso-Polchinski Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05357)
*James Halverson,Justin Khoury,Cody Long*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一个弦论通量真空中宇宙学常数的简化模型，受IIB型弦论和F-理论紧致化的启发，该模型在薄片（wafer）而非薄壳（shell）中实现小的真空能间距。将该模型应用于Schöller-Skarke卡拉比-丘四重（Calabi-Yau fourfold）数据库，发现绝大多数参数选择（99.95%）对应的真空能间距小于或等于普朗克单位下的10^{-120}。Brown-Teitelboim膜泡成核（membrane nucleation）转变在薄壁近似下主要由通量空间中的巨跃（giant leaps）主导，且宇宙年龄对Calabi-Yau拓扑的限制在整个数据库中均得到满足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 简化弦论通量真空（flux vacua）中宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）的建模，以克服Bousso-Polchinski模型中实现极小真空能间距的困难，并利用大样本的Calabi-Yau四重数据进行定量检验。

Method: 提出一个基于IIB型弦论和F-理论（F-theory）紧致化的宇宙学常数简化模型，与Bousso-Polchinski模型的区别在于小真空能间距出现在“薄片”而非“薄壳”中。将该模型应用于包含532,600,483组不同Hodge数的Schöller-Skarke卡拉比-丘四重数据库，并使用Brown-Teitelboim膜泡成核机制分析通量真空间的跃迁，采用薄壁近似且忽略引力修正。

Result: 在所选参数条件下，数据库中99.95%的Calabi-Yau四重表现出真空能间距≤10^{-120}（普朗克单位）。膜泡跃迁在通量空间中总是由巨跃主导。宇宙年龄对所有Calabi-Yau拓扑的限制在整个数据库中得到满足。

Conclusion: 该简化模型能够在大规模Calabi-Yau数据库中广泛复现极小的真空能间距，且膜泡动力学不会导致微调问题，宇宙学约束也对所有拓扑结构兼容。

Abstract: We propose a simplified model for the cosmological constant in string theory flux vacua motivated by type IIB and F-theory compactifications. Relative to the Bousso-Polchinski model, small vacuum energy spacing occurs in thin wafers rather than thin shells. The model is applied to the entire Schöller-Skarke database of Calabi-Yau fourfolds, which exhibit $532,600,483$ distinct sets of Hodge numbers. The overwhelming majority of those ($99.95\%$ percent for some choices of parameters) exhibit a vacuum energy spacing of~$10^{-120}$ in Planck units or smaller. Brown-Teitelboim membrane nucleation transitions can populate this landscape of flux vacua. In the thin-wall approximation, and ignoring gravitational corrections, we find that the bubble transitions are always dominated by giant leaps in flux space. The age of the universe places a bound on Calabi-Yau topology that is satisfied for the entire Schöller-Skarke database.

### [91] [Celestial dual of conformal gravity MHV amplitudes: an OPE analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05363)

A soft theorem analysis of bulk MHV amplitudes established that this conformal gravity exhibits a chiral $\mathfrak{bms}_4$ symmetry on the celestial sphere with the associated $\mathfrak{sl}(2,\mathbb{R})$ current algebra, which acquires a non-trivial central extension, unlike the Einstein gravity. Here we construct a $2d$ chiral CFT free-field realisation of the relevant chiral $\mathfrak{bms}_4$ algebra in terms of three free scalars ($φ_i$) and three $(β_i,γ_i)$ ghost pairs, and propose vertex operators for the positive-helicity graviton primary $G^{++}_Δ(z,\bar{z})$ as well as the scalar primary $Φ_Δ(z,\bar{z})$, and compute their OPEs. ### [92] [Stochastic modes in postquantum classical gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05375)
*Jonathan Oppenheim,Muhammad Sajjad*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在经典引力量子后理论（postquantum theory of classical gravity）框架下，研究度规的涨落。通过将理论线性化并分解为标量-矢量-张量模式，识别出弥漫于波动方程周围的经典自旋-2场和自旋-0标量场等随机模式，并证明作用量在所有动力学模式上半正定。作者计算了牛顿势涨落的两点函数和功率谱密度，与LISA Pathfinder的过剩噪声进行比较，从而约束了两个无量纲耦合常数的一个组合；同时，FLRW背景下的随机引力波能量密度约束了另一个组合。此外，推导了物质分布的有效作用量，并展示了纯引力理论不同表述之间的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典引力量子后理论要求在数学上自洽地将经典时空与量子物质场耦合，时空必须随机演化。本文旨在系统分析该理论中时空度规的涨落模式，识别其随机自由度，并将理论预测与现有实验观测（如LISA Pathfinder噪声和随机引力波背景）进行对比，从而约束理论参数。

Method: 从经典-量子路径积分（classical-quantum path integral）出发，在闵可夫斯基时空附近线性化，进行标量-矢量-张量分解（scalar-vector-tensor decomposition），识别出随机模式：一个经典自旋-2场和一个自旋-0标量场，两者均在其各自波动方程周围扩散。还存在一个非动力学的矢量场和标量场。利用Onsager-Machlup作用量、Martin-Siggia-Rose形式以及随机微分方程（stochastic differential equations）等多种形式对理论进行交叉验证。

Result: 证明了作用量在所有动力学模式上具有半正定性（positive semi-definite, PSD），这是理论将时空一致地视为经典对象的必要条件。计算了牛顿势涨落的两点函数和功率谱密度，并与LISA Pathfinder的过剩噪声对比，给出了对两个无量纲耦合常数一个组合的约束；在FLRW（Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker）背景下的随机引力波能量密度约束了另一个组合。

Conclusion: 推导了物质分布的有效作用量，发现退相干实验（decoherence experiments）的边界受牛顿势涨落Φ和曲率扰动ψ的约束。展示了纯引力理论的三种不同表述——Onsager-Machlup作用量形式、Martin-Siggia-Rose形式以及随机微分方程形式——之间的一致性。

Abstract: We study fluctuations of the metric in the postquantum theory of classical gravity, a covariant theory which couples a classical spacetime with quantum matter fields. Mathematical consistency requires spacetime to evolve stochastically. Starting from the classical-quantum path integral, we linearize around Minkowski space and perform a scalar-vector-tensor decomposition, identifying the stochastic modes: a classical spin-2 field and spin-0 scalar, both diffusing around their respective wave equations. There is also a non-dynamical vector and scalar field. These are related to the degrees of freedom found in quadratic gravity, but here interpreted as stochastic contributions to spacetime. We show that the action is positive semi-definite (PSD) on all dynamical modes, which is a necessary condition for the theory to consistently treat spacetime classically. We compute the two-point function and power spectral density corresponding to fluctuations of the Newtonian potential, and compare it to the excess noise found in LISA Pathfinder. This sets a bound on one combination of the two dimensionless coupling constants of the theory, while bounds on the stochastic gravitational wave energy density in a FLRW background constrain another combination. We derive the effective action for matter distributions, and find that bounds from decoherence experiments are constrained by fluctuations in the Newtonian potential $Φ$ and the curvature perturbation $ψ$. Finally, we show consistency between different formulations of the pure gravity theory, the Onsager-Machlup form of the action, the Martin-Siggia-Rose form, and that given by stochastic differential equations.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究并讨论共形物质场（conformal matter fields）的量子效应对牛顿势（Newton potential）产生的修正，并比较两种不同理论方法——有效量子引力（effective quantum gravity）和基于共形反常（trace anomaly）的方法——在计算该修正时的差异与协调性。

Method: 采用基于共形反常诱导有效作用量（anomaly-induced effective action）的方法，通过固定量子真空态（quantum vacuum state）来推导Boulware真空态下的反常诱导应力张量（anomaly-induced stress tensor），进而计算经典引力定律的一阶量子修正。

Result: 在Boulware真空态下，通过共形反常方法推导出的牛顿势量子修正，与基于有效量子引力方法类比计算得到的结果不一致。

Conclusion: 要协调两种推导牛顿势领先半经典修正（leading semiclassical corrections）的方法，唯一途径是修改Boulware真空态中能量-动量张量平均值的渐近行为（asymptotic behavior），这一观点近期已在文献中得到讨论。

Abstract: We explore and discuss corrections to the Newton potential from the quantum effects of conformal matter fields. In this special case, one can compare different approaches, including that of effective quantum gravity and another, based on the conformal (trace) anomaly. The comparison of these two methods is the main focus in the present work. Using the anomaly-induced effective action of gravity requires fixing the quantum vacuum state, similar to what is done in the description of black hole evaporation. In the Boulware vacuum state, we compute the anomaly-induced stress tensor and the first-order correction to the classical gravitational law. The quantum correction to the Newton's potential derived in this way, differs from the result calculated in a way analogous to the effective approach to quantum gravity. The only way to reconcile the two approaches for deriving the leading semiclassical corrections to Newtonian potential is to modify the asymptotic behavior of the average of the energy-momentum tensor in the Boulware vacuum state, as has been recently discussed in the literature.

### [94] [Squeezed Gravitons and One-Loop Self-Energy under Light-Cone Smearing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05916)
*Hiroki Matsui*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究引力子（graviton）量子涨落引起的光锥涂抹（light-cone smearing）效应，发现该效应可以正则化量子场论中的紫外发散，且引力子的量子态（真空态、相干态、压缩态）对光锥结构产生不同影响，在暴涨宇宙学背景下可产生有限的可观测修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子引力效应对量子场论（quantum field theory）紫外结构（ultraviolet structure）的影响，特别是引力子量子涨落如何改变光锥的因果结构，以及这种改变能否自然正则化紫外发散。

Method: 将Synge世界函数（Synge's world function）的一阶修正视为算符，计算引力子涨落方差对推迟格林函数（retarded Green's function）的涂抹效应。随后将涂抹后的费曼传播子（smeared Feynman propagator）应用于标量场论的单圈自能计算，包括φ³气泡图（bubble diagram）和φ⁴蝌蚪图（tadpole diagram）。

Result: 真空涨落产生高斯型光锥涂抹（Gaussian smearing）；相干态（coherent state）平移光锥位置；压缩态（squeezed state）调制涂抹宽度。涂抹宽度非零时，单圈自能中的短距离奇异性（short-distance singularities）被正则化。暴涨时期产生的原初引力子对单圈自能贡献约10⁻¹⁰量级的有限修正。

Conclusion: 引力子的量子态可以在量子场论的因果结构和短距离结构上留下有限可观测印记，表明量子引力效应并非必然导致不可探测的普朗克能标物理。

Abstract: We investigate light-cone smearing induced by quantum fluctuations of gravitons and its implications for the ultraviolet structure of quantum field theory. By treating the first-order correction to Synge's world function as an operator, we show that the retarded Green's function is smeared by the variance of graviton fluctuations. The smearing width depends on the quantum state of gravitons: vacuum fluctuations generate a Gaussian smearing of the light cone, coherent states shift the light-cone position, and squeezed states modify the smearing width itself. We then apply the smeared Feynman propagator to one-loop self-energies in interacting scalar field theories. In both the $φ^3$ bubble diagram and the $φ^4$ tadpole diagram, the short-distance singularities responsible for the usual ultraviolet divergences are regularized by a nonzero smearing width. We also estimate the contribution from primordial gravitons generated during inflation and show that it induces a finite correction of order $10^{-10}$ to the one-loop self-energy. Our results suggest that the quantum state of gravitons can leave a finite imprint on the causal and short-distance structure of quantum field theory.

### [95] [Ultraviolet-Finite Perturbative Expansion of Quantum Gravity at Null Infinity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06001)
*Carlos N. Kozameh,Gerardo O. Depaola*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于零曲面表述（Null Surface Formulation, NSF）的渐近平坦真空时空量子引力的微扰论形式，该形式在已计算阶数内逐项紫外有限，无需重整化，并对出射Bondi剪切算子进行了最高至四阶的显式构造。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准协变量子引力的微扰展开存在严重的紫外发散问题，需要复杂的重整化（renormalization）程序。本文旨在建立一个基于零曲面表述的替代性微扰框架，在保持物理可预测性的同时改善紫外行为。

Method: 基于零曲面表述（NSF）构建微扰形式；利用零无穷远（null infinity）处的在壳引力数据递归确定相互作用核（interaction kernels）；将全部积分限制在紧致的天球（celestial sphere）上，从而消除离壳传播子（off-shell propagators），实现逐项紫外有限性。

Result: 出射Bondi剪切算子被显式构造至四阶，该阶数内微扰展开逐项紫外有限；入态与出态之间的映射可在微扰框架下构造，且幺正性（unitarity）在四阶内得到显式验证；出射算子满足与入射算子相同的对易关系，表明变换是正则的（canonical）；共线（collinear）构型产生红外奇点，但不影响已建立的紫外行为；在相干态（coherent states）中，剪切算子的期望值在最低非平庸阶上复现了已知的有限经典引力子散射结果。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个改进紫外行为的量子引力微扰框架，相较于协变方法具有优势；零曲面表述的微扰形式有可能成为研究渐近平坦时空量子引力中散射问题与量子态结构的有力工具。

Abstract: We present a perturbative formulation of quantum gravity for asymptotically flat vacuum spacetimes based on the Null Surface Formulation (NSF), in which the expansion is ultraviolet-finite term by term up to the orders computed, without the need for renormalization. The outgoing Bondi shear operators are constructed explicitly up to fourth order, with interaction kernels determined recursively from on-shell gravitational data at null infinity. Ultraviolet finiteness at each order follows from the on-shell structure of the construction and the restriction of all integrations to the compact celestial sphere, eliminating off-shell propagators. The map between the in and out states admits a perturbative construction, and unitarity is verified explicitly up to fourth order. The outgoing operators satisfy the same commutation relations as the incoming ones, indicating that the transformation is canonical and consistent with the unitary implementation. Collinear configurations give rise to infrared singularities, as expected in massless quantum field theories, but do not affect the ultraviolet behavior established here. In coherent states, the expectation value of the shear reproduces the known finite classical graviton scattering at lowest nontrivial order. These results provide a perturbative framework for quantum gravity with improved ultraviolet behavior relative to the covariant approach.

### [96] [Non-abelian field cohomology, its relation with spontaneous symmetry breaking and Morse's Theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06159)
*V. E. R. Lemes*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 论文证明在SU(2)（可推广至SU(N)）规范场中，自发对称性破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）会改变场的上同调（cohomology），产生一种具有物质场上同调特性的新场。利用这一特性，在Morse泛函极值化框架下构造可重整化幺正规范固定（renormalizable unitary gauge fixing）时，Gribov条件在壳上自动满足，因为特定场组合在 cohomology 上类似物质场，不受Gribov问题影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gribov问题是非阿贝尔规范理论（non-Abelian gauge theory）中规范固定面临的根本困难，尤其在超越微扰论（perturbation theory）的处理中。本文旨在通过揭示自发对称性破缺对场上同调的影响，找到一种自动规避Gribov问题的规范固定方式。

Method: 从SU(2)规范场的上同调分析出发，论证自发对称性破缺会改变场的上同调结构，从而定义出一种具有物质场上同调特性的新场。随后将规范固定问题视为Morse泛函极值化问题，在此框架下引入可重整化幺正规范固定方案。

Result: 发现特定场的组合在 cohomology 上表现为物质场（matter-like），因而天然不受Gribov问题困扰。这使得Gribov条件在壳上自动满足，无需额外约束。

Conclusion: 自发对称性破缺引起的场上同调变化为克服Gribov问题提供了新路径，可重整化幺正规范固定的构造因此成为可能。

Abstract: We show that, for an $SU(2)$ gauge field (the reasoning extends trivially to $SU(N)$), spontaneous symmetry breaking changes the field cohomology. This defines a new field with cohomological properties characteristic of matter fields. Consequently, the construction of a renormalizable unitary gauge fixing, following Morse's problem of functional extremization, leads to the Gribov condition being automatically solved on-shell. This result occurs because a specific combination of fields is cohomologically matter-like and therefore free of the Gribov problem.

</details>


### [97] [Causal self-dual nonlinear electrodynamics from the Born-Infeld theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06193)
*Sergei M. Kuzenko,Jonah Ruhl*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于辅助场（auxiliary field）形式体系的新的自对偶非线性电动力学（self-dual nonlinear electrodynamics, NLED）构造方法，并证明当种子拉格朗日量（seed Lagrangian）取为Born-Infeld理论时，所导出的自对偶NLED模型具有因果性，且满足自对偶方程的一般解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为自对偶非线性电动力学（self-dual NLED）提供一种新的辅助场形式体系，使得通过选择不同的标量势（scalar potential）可以导出多种自对偶模型。

Method: 基于两个要素：（i）种子自对偶理论（seed self-dual theory）$L(F_{\mu\nu}; g)$，其中$F_{\mu\nu}$为电磁场强（electromagnetic field strength），$g$为对偶不变耦合常数（duality-invariant coupling constant）；（ii）标量势（scalar potential）$W(\psi)$。构造拉格朗日量（Lagrangian）$\mathfrak{L}(F_{\mu\nu}; \psi) = L(F_{\mu\nu}; \psi) + W(\psi)$，其中$\psi$为辅助标量场（auxiliary scalar field）。通过运动方程（equation of motion）积分掉$\psi$，得到$\mathsf{U}(1)$对偶不变（duality-invariant）的NLED。

Result: 当种子拉格朗日量选取为Born-Infeld理论时，所导出的自对偶NLED模型是因果的（causal），并且提供了自对偶方程的一般解（general solution）。此外，还阐述了如何将该形式体系与Russo-Townsend形式体系建立联系。

Conclusion: 该辅助场形式体系为构造因果的自对偶NLED模型提供了一般性框架，并且能够与已有的Russo-Townsend形式体系相互关联。

Abstract: Recently we have proposed a new auxiliary-field formulation for self-dual nonlinear electrodynamics (NLED) which makes use of two building blocks: (i) a seed self-dual theory $L(F_{μν};g)$, where $F_{μν}$ is the electromagnetic field strength and $g$ a duality-invariant coupling constant; and (ii) a scalar potential $W(ψ)$. Our formulation is based on the Lagrangian $ \mathfrak{L}(F_{μν};ψ) = L(F_{μν};ψ) + W(ψ)$, where $ψ$ is an auxiliary scalar field. Integrating out $ψ$, using its equation of motion, one obtains a $\mathsf{U}(1)$ duality-invariant NLED. Different self-dual NLEDs are derived by choosing different potentials $W(ψ)$. In the case that the seed Lagrangian defines the Born-Infeld theory, in this paper we demonstrate that the resulting models for self-dual NLED are causal and provide a general solution of the self-duality equation. We also elaborate on the procedure to relate our formulation to that developed by Russo and Townsend.

</details>

Abstract: The massive Majorana field in $1+1$ dimension is employed to investigate the violation of the Bell-CHSH inequality in relativistic Quantum Field Theory. ### [99] [Half-Spacetime Gauging of 2-Group Symmetry in 3d](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06287)
*Davide Bason,Wei Cui,Lorenzo Ruggeri*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在(2+1)维量子场论中构造了一类由2-群对称性的半时空规范（half-spacetime gauging）产生的不可逆对偶缺陷（non-invertible duality defects），并推导了其融合规则，通过具体例子展示了该构造方法。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从具有两个离散阿贝尔0-形式对称性及给定混合反常的母理论（parent theory）出发，分别对其中一个因子进行全局规范（global gauging），从而得到具有2-群对称性或具有非可逆0-形式对称性的理论。当母理论具有三个对称性且满足循环反常结构时，通过半时空规范实现2-群对称性，构造不可逆对偶缺陷，并利用上同调工具（cohomological tools）进行形式化处理。

Abstract: We construct a class of non-invertible duality defects, in (2+1)d quantum field theories, arising from half-spacetime gauging of a 2-group symmetry. Starting from a parent theory with two discrete and Abelian 0-form symmetries and a prescribed mixed anomaly, we show that gauging one factor produces a theory with a 2-group symmetry, while gauging the other yields a theory with a non-invertible 0-form symmetry, whose fusion rules we derive explicitly. When the parent theory possesses three such symmetries with a cyclic anomaly structure, gauging different factors can produce mutually dual theories and the half-spacetime gauging of the 2-group is implemented by a non-invertible duality defect, whose fusion rules we obtain. We illustrate the construction with explicit examples, including a $U(1)\times U(1)\times U(1)$ gauge theory and a general class of product theories. We also include a self-contained pedagogical introduction to the cohomological tools employed throughout the article.

### [100] [Systematic Extraction of Exact Yang-Mills Solutions via Algebraic Tensor Ring Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06379)
*Yu-Xuan Zhang,Jing-Ling Chen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种代数张量环分解框架（algebraic tensor ring decomposition framework），用于将杨-米尔斯理论（Yang-Mills theory）的非线性偏微分方程组（PDEs）映射为可解的微分-代数系统。通过将静态纯规范背景提升为动力学变量，并借助微分-代数商环与代数分岔分析，系统提取了三类精确解：相对论性 SU(2) 色波、动力学 dyonic 通量管以及动力学 SU(3) 构型，揭示了质量间隙生成、指数型屏蔽以及混沌振荡等非微扰现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 杨-米尔斯理论的非线性本质使得提取精确经典解极为困难，而这些解对于理解非微扰真空结构（non-perturbative vacuum structures）至关重要。现有方法缺乏系统性地处理该理论中非线性偏微分方程组的通用框架。

Method: 引入代数张量环分解框架，将杨-米尔斯理论的非线性 PDEs 映射为可处理的微分-代数系统（differential-algebraic systems）。通过将静态纯规范背景（pure-gauge backgrounds）提升为动力学变量，参考态充当几何模板，其 Maurer-Cartan 形式生成稳定非线性自相互作用所需的代数交叉项。利用特定的微分-代数商环（differential-algebraic quotient rings）解析求解微分理想，并通过代数分岔分析（algebraic bifurcation analysis）组织解空间。

Result: 提取了三类精确解：(i) 定义在椭圆商环上的相对论性 SU(2) 色波，微分理想分岔为解耦分支与两个耦合分支，后者展现质量间隙生成（mass gap generation）；(ii) 基于时间依赖螺旋模板的动力学 dyonic 通量管，高斯定律理想将该系统分岔为库仑、Dyonic 和对称 Meissner 三个分支，其中 Meissner 分支的 Artinian 渐近截断产生 Bessel 型指数屏蔽；(iii) 动力学 SU(3) 构型，其高斯定律理想将解空间分岔为四个不同相，非平凡分支迫使振幅动力学映射到广义 x²y² 混沌振荡子。

Conclusion: 该框架为系统表征强耦合规范理论（strongly coupled gauge theories）的经典解空间提供了一种方法化途径，有助于深入理解非微扰真空结构及相关物理现象。

Abstract: The non-linear nature of Yang-Mills theory presents a challenge for extracting exact classical solutions, which are useful for understanding non-perturbative vacuum structures. In this paper, an algebraic tensor ring decomposition framework is introduced to systematically map the non-linear partial differential equations (PDEs) of Yang-Mills theory into tractable differential-algebraic systems. By promoting static pure-gauge backgrounds to dynamical variables, the reference state acts as a geometric template whose Maurer-Cartan forms generate the algebraic cross-terms necessary to stabilize non-linear self-interactions. To analytically resolve the resulting differential ideals, specific differential-algebraic quotient rings are employed as evaluation tools, and the solution space is organized by an algebraic bifurcation analysis. Applying this framework, three distinct classes of exact solutions are extracted: (i) relativistic $SU(2)$ color waves evaluated over an elliptic quotient ring, where the differential ideal bifurcates into a Decoupled Branch and two Coupled Branches, the latter exhibiting mass gap generation; (ii) dynamical dyonic flux tubes obtained from a time-dependent helical template, where the Gauss law ideal bifurcates the system into Coulomb, Dyonic, and symmetric Meissner branches. In the Meissner branch, an Artinian asymptotic truncation yields Bessel-type exponential screening, stabilized by a temporal dominance condition; and (iii) dynamical $SU(3)$ configurations where the Gauss law ideal bifurcates the solution space into four distinct phases. The non-trivial branches enforce a kinetic cancellation mechanism that maps the amplitude dynamics onto a generalized $x^2y^2$ chaotic oscillator. Across these settings, the framework provides a methodical approach to characterize the classical solution space of strongly coupled gauge theories.

### [102] [The Hagedorn Temperature as a Nonequilibrium Dynamical Bottleneck in String Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06497)
*Cesar Damian,Oscar Loaiza-Brito*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从非平衡视角重新审视弦理论的哈格多恩（Hagedorn）区，利用最陡熵增量子热力学（SEAQT）框架，推导了逆温度作为瞬时态依赖量的标量演化方程，发现哈格多恩区可能充当动力学的瓶颈，且该瓶颈强度依赖于态密度的指数增长和代数前因子。研究为哈格多恩行为提供了非平衡解释，并暗示长弦主导、热力学慢化与量子引力中有效描述失效之间的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上弦理论的哈格多恩（Hagedorn）区仅被理解为平衡极限现象——态密度的指数增长使配分函数在哈格多恩温度处发散，而微正则描述中额外能量主要由高激发长弦（long-string）态吸收。本文旨在从非平衡（nonequilibrium）视角重新审视这一区域，探索其动力学特征，而不依赖于全局正则系综的存在。

Method: 采用最陡熵增量子热力学（Steepest-Entropy-Ascent Quantum Thermodynamics, SEAQT）框架，该框架直接在态流形（state manifold）上表述热力学演化，无需全局定义的正则系综。将逆温度（inverse temperature）处理为瞬时态依赖量（instantaneous, state-dependent quantity），推导其精确标量演化方程。在交换极限（commuting limit）下，该动力学由高阶涨落矩（higher-order fluctuation moments）控制。进一步将构造扩展到开放系统，通过系统-热库分割（system-reservoir splitting）SEAQT度量，并对角化哈格多恩评估，分析瓶颈强度。

Result: SEAQT框架下逆温度的演化由高阶涨落矩控制，表明哈格多恩区可能成为有效强度量（effective intensive variable）响应的动力学瓶颈（dynamical bottleneck）。开放系统中，热库耦合可驱动子系统趋向有效的哈格多恩慢化（Hagedorn slowing-down）。对角化哈格多恩评估进一步显示，瓶颈强度不仅依赖于态密度的指数增长，还依赖于其代数前因子（algebraic prefactor）。

Conclusion: 研究为哈格多恩行为提供了一个非平衡解释，揭示了长弦主导、热力学慢化（thermodynamic slowing-down）之间的内在联系，并暗示这一机制可能关联量子引力（quantum gravity）中有效描述（effective descriptions）的失效。

Abstract: The Hagedorn regime of string theory is usually understood as an equilibrium limiting phenomenon: the exponential growth of the density of states makes the canonical partition function singular at the Hagedorn temperature, while in the microcanonical description additional energy is absorbed predominantly by highly excited long-string configurations. In this work we revisit this regime from a nonequilibrium perspective using Steepest-Entropy-Ascent Quantum Thermodynamics (SEAQT), where thermodynamic evolution is formulated directly on the state manifold and does not require a globally well-defined canonical ensemble. The inverse temperature is treated as an instantaneous, state-dependent quantity, and we derive its exact scalar evolution equation. In the commuting limit, this dynamics is controlled by higher-order fluctuation moments, showing that the Hagedorn regime may act as a dynamical bottleneck for the response of the effective intensive variable. We then extend the construction to an open-system setting through a system--reservoir splitting of the SEAQT metric and show that reservoir coupling can drive the subsystem toward effective Hagedorn slowing-down. A diagonal Hagedorn evaluation further shows that the strength of this bottleneck depends not only on the exponential density of states, but also on its algebraic prefactor. These results provide a nonequilibrium interpretation of Hagedorn behavior and suggest a connection between long-string dominance, thermodynamic slowing-down, and the breakdown of effective descriptions in quantum gravity.

Conclusion: 该显式公式为 de Sitter 时空中共形耦合 φ³ 理论的宇宙学波函数计算提供了系统化工具，并揭示了波函数系数与簇代数及四边形多对数之间的深层结构联系。

Abstract: We present an explicit formula for the $n$-site chain graph contribution to the cosmological wavefunction for conformally coupled $φ^3$ theory in de Sitter space. *Joan Elias Miro,Andrea Guerrieri,Mehmet Asim Gumus*

TL;DR: 该工作通过现代数值S矩阵自举（S-matrix bootstrap）方法，进一步收紧了对四维全同标量粒子两两散射振幅的非微扰上下界，并系统分析了边界区域的物理内涵。研究发现，允许区域边界的不同边（edge）展现出截然不同的普适行为，对应于有质量标量粒子在紫外（UV）完成机制上的不同相（phase）分类。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子场论中，散射振幅需要满足幺正性、交叉对称性和解析性等基本公理。现代数值S矩阵自举方法已推导出全同标量粒子两体散射振幅的严格非微扰上下界，刻画出一个具有丰富边界结构（边和顶点）的允许区域。本文旨在进一步收紧该区域，并阐明其边界背后的物理起源，即不同边界特征所对应的紫外物理机制。

Method: 通过分析振幅在Regge极限下的渐近行为（asymptotic Regge behavior）以及共振态（resonance）和虚态（virtual state）的能谱，系统研究S矩阵自举所定义的允许区域边界。通过比较不同边界上S矩阵的普适性质，对边界进行物理分类。

Result: 沿着区域边界上的给定边，S矩阵展现出普适行为，且不同边之间的行为存在显著差异。这表明边界可以被划分为不同的相（phase），每个相对应于一种独特的紫外机制，通过这些机制可以产生一个有质量能隙的标量粒子。

Conclusion: S矩阵自举界定的允许区域边界并非单一结构，而是存在多个具有不同普适行为的边，这些边对应着不同的紫外完成（UV completion）方式。这一分类为理解有质量标量粒子的非微扰散射性质及其紫外起源提供了新的视角。

Abstract: The two-to-two four-dimensional scattering amplitude of identical scalars obeys rigorous two-sided non-perturbative bounds derived via the modern numerical S-matrix bootstrap. These bounds carve out an allowed region with a rich boundary structure, featuring edges and vertices. In this work we further tighten this region and uncover the physics of its boundary by analyzing the asymptotic Regge behavior of the amplitude and the spectrum of resonances and virtual states. We find that the S-matrices along a given edge exhibit universal behavior, sharply contrasting with that on other edges. This reveals a classification of the boundary into distinct phases, corresponding to different UV mechanisms by which a gapped scalar arises.

</details>


### [106] [From Baby Universes to Narain Moduli: Topological Boundary Averaging in SymTFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06653)
*Xingyang Yu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种对称张量场论（SymTFT）视角来理解低维全息对偶中的系综平均，指出系综平均等价于对拓扑边界条件的平均，而非对任意局域动力学的平均，并在Marolf–Maxfield模型和Narain模型中进行具体阐释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低维全息对偶（low-dimensional holography）中常出现系综平均（ensemble averaging）现象，但其微观起源尚不清晰。本文旨在利用对称张量场论（SymTFT）框架，为这种平均操作提供一种统一且具有拓扑起源的解释。

Method: 核心操作是固定SymTFT和物理边界条件（physical boundary condition），而对SymTFT“平板”另一端的拓扑边界条件（topological boundary conditions）进行平均。每个拓扑边界条件对应同一个相对理论（relative theory）的一种绝对完备化（absolute completion），从而将系综平均重新解释为对拓扑完备化（topological completions）的平均，而非对任意局域动力学的平均。该构造通过帽子泛函（cap functionals）及其自然群胚（groupoid）或Haar型测度（Haar-type measures）来形式化。

Result: 在Marolf–Maxfield模型的闭弦扇区中，拓扑边界条件由有限集标记，群胚和（groupoid sum）复现了泊松/贝尔多项式矩（Poisson/Bell-polynomial moments）。在Narain模型中，$\mathbb{R}$-值BF SymTFT的紧致拓扑边界条件与极大迷向子群（maximal isotropic subgroups）一一对应，拓扑边界平均等价于带有Zamolodchikov测度（Zamolodchikov measure）的标准Narain模空间平均。

Conclusion: 该SymTFT框架为低维全息中的系综平均提供了拓扑起源的统一理解，并有望推广至JT引力（JT gravity）、随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）、Virasoro T(Q)FT以及三维引力（3D gravity）等情形。

Abstract: We propose a SymTFT interpretation of ensemble averaging in low-dimensional holography. The central operation is to keep fixed both the SymTFT and the physical boundary condition, while averaging over topological boundary conditions at the other end of the SymTFT slab. Each such boundary condition gives an absolute completion of the same relative theory, so the ensemble is interpreted as an average over topological completions rather than over arbitrary local dynamics. We formulate this construction in terms of cap functionals and their natural groupoid or Haar-type measures, and illustrate it in two examples. In the closed-string sector of the Marolf--Maxfield model, topological boundary conditions are labelled by finite sets, and the groupoid sum reproduces the Poisson/Bell-polynomial moments. In the Narain case, compact topological boundary conditions of an $\mathbb{R}$-valued BF SymTFT are identified with maximal isotropic subgroups, so that topological-boundary averaging becomes the usual Narain moduli average with Zamolodchikov measure. We also discuss possible extensions to JT gravity, random matrix theory, Virasoro T(Q)FT, and 3D gravity.

</details>

### [107] [Geometric Means and Lebesgue-type Decomposition of Completely Positive Maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06019)
*Rui Okayasu*

Main category: math.OA

TL;DR: 本文基于Pusz–Woronowicz正半双线性型理论，在冯·诺依曼代数上引入了完全正（CP）映射的几何平均与平行和，建立了其块矩阵特征刻画、AM–GM–HM不等式，并通过Choi–Jamiołkowski对应在有限维情形与Kubo–Ando几何平均兼容，进而应用于子因子论中的条件期望指数不等式及CP映射的Lebesgue型分解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将正算子（positive operator）上的几何平均与平行和理论推广到冯·诺依曼代数（von Neumann algebra）上的完全正（completely positive, CP）映射框架中，从而为量子信道的插值、子因子论中的指数型不等式以及CP映射的Lebesgue型分解提供统一的算子理论工具。

Method: 基于Pusz–Woronowicz正半双线性型（positive sesquilinear form）理论，通过块矩阵正定性（block matrix positivity condition）条件给出CP映射的几何平均与平行和的具体刻画；在有限维情形下，利用Choi–Jamiołkowski对应（Choi–Jamiołkowski correspondence）将CP映射的几何平均转化为其Choi矩阵的Kubo–Ando几何平均。

Result: 建立了CP映射的几何平均与平行和的基本性质，包括CP序（CP order）下的AM–GM–HM不等式；在有限维情形下证明了与Kubo–Ando几何平均的兼容性；获得了子因子论（subfactor theory）中条件期望（conditional expectation）的指数型不等式；给出了CP映射的Lebesgue型分解（Lebesgue-type decomposition）。

Conclusion: 本文构建的CP映射几何平均与平行和框架，同时推广了Ando关于有界正算子的分解和Kosaki关于冯·诺依曼代数上正规正泛函（normal positive functional）的分解，为算子代数和量子信息论提供了统一的数学工具。

Abstract: We introduce the geometric mean and the parallel sum of completely positive (CP) maps on von Neumann algebras, based on the Pusz--Woronowicz theory of positive sesquilinear forms. We provide a concrete characterization via a block matrix positivity condition and establish their fundamental properties, including the AM--GM--HM inequality with respect to the CP order.
  In finite-dimensional settings, our construction is compatible with the Choi--Jamiolkowski correspondence, under which the geometric mean of CP maps corresponds to the Kubo--Ando geometric mean of their Choi matrices. This yields a natural operator-theoretic framework for interpolating quantum channels.
  As an application, we obtain index-type inequalities for conditional expectations in subfactor theory.
  Finally, we establish a Lebesgue-type decomposition of CP maps via a parallel sum construction, thereby providing a unified framework that simultaneously generalizes Ando's decomposition of bounded positive operators and Kosaki's decomposition of normal positive functionals on von Neumann algebras.

### [108] [Hugoniot Relation for Multi-Temperature Euler Equations of Compressible Plasma Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06131)
*Zhifang Du,Aleksey Sikstel*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过经典Courant–Friedrichs分析，推导了多温度欧拉方程（multi-temperature Euler equations）中两种不同的Hugoniot关系，揭示了激波结构（shock structure）的内在非唯一性，并指出Hugoniot关系无法仅由宏观偏微分方程唯一确定，而必须依赖外部微观物理信息（如实验或第一性原理模拟）来消除歧义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多温度欧拉方程的激波解因模型降阶（model reduction）中微观物理细节的丢失以及非守恒项（non-conservative terms）的出现而天然存在歧义（ambiguous），需要从理论上澄清激波结构的可容许性条件与唯一性问题。

Method: 采用经典的Courant–Friedrichs分析方法，分别针对一般多温度情形和双温度等离子体流（two-temperature plasma flows）情形推导了两种不同的Hugoniot关系，并将这些解与现有数值格式（结构保持方法（structure preserving approach）和消失黏性方法（vanishing viscosity approach））进行对比。

Result: 两种Hugoniot关系均满足可容许性条件（admissibility conditions），证明激波结构存在根本性的非唯一性（non-uniqueness）。Hugoniot关系无法由宏观偏微分方程（macroscopic PDEs）唯一确定，而必须从外部来源（如实验或第一性原理模拟）补充。

Conclusion: 微观物理学在解决激波歧义中具有关键作用，该研究为不连续等离子体流（discontinuous plasma flows）的建模提供了理论基础，并为构建和评估不连续数值近似（discontinuous numerical approximations）提供了有物理依据的参考。

Abstract: Shock solutions for multi-temperature Euler equations are inherently ambiguous due to the loss of microscopic physical detail during model reduction and occurrence of non-conservative terms. This paper presents a detailed analytical study of shock structures in such models. We derive two distinct Hugoniot relations, each corresponding to a physically admissible shock solution: one for the general multi-temperature case and one for two-temperature plasma flows. Through classical analysis à la Courant--Friedrichs, we demonstrate that both satisfy admissibility conditions, revealing a fundamental non-uniqueness in shock structures. By relating these solutions to existing numerical schemes, the structure preserving and vanishing viscosity approaches, we provide physically justified references for constructing and evaluating discontinuous numerical approximations. In particular, we emphasize that the Hugoniot relation is not uniquely determined by the macroscopic PDEs alone, but must be supplied from external sources such as experiments or first-principles simulations. This insight demonstrates the essential role of microscopic physics in resolving shock ambiguity and contributes to the theoretical foundation for modeling discontinuous plasma flows.

</details>

### [109] [Inflation driven by repulsive-like primordial black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05232)
*Konstantinos Dialektopoulos,Theodoros Papanikolaou,Vasilios Zarikas*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种由具有类排斥行为的原初黑洞（primordial black holes, PBHs）驱动的新型自然暴胀机制，在“瑞士奶酪”宇宙学框架下，发现PBHs可以引发早期准德西特膨胀相；轻质量PBHs能够产生具有优雅退出机制和再加热过程的指数暴胀，而特定质量和丰度的PBHs可以作为早期暗能量成分，缓解哈勃张力（Hubble tension）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有暴胀模型多依赖标量场（scalar field），但其微调问题及与量子引力的自然衔接尚存争议。论文试图探索一种由原初黑洞这一更自然的宇宙学实体驱动的暴胀机制，同时借助该机制解释哈勃张力的起源。

Method: 采用“瑞士奶酪”宇宙学框架，假设宇宙填充具有类排斥行为度规的原初黑洞，分别考察轻质量PBHs（m < 5×10⁸ g，在大爆炸核合成前蒸发）以及中等质量PBHs（m ∼ 10¹² g，在物质-辐射相等期附近丰度0.107 < Ω^{eq}_{PBH} < 0.5）的宇宙学演化。

Result: 轻质量PBHs可产生指数暴胀相（exponential inflationary phase），且具备优雅退出（graceful exit）机制，再加热（reheating）通过PBH蒸发完成；中等质量PBHs在特定丰度范围内可充当早期暗能量（early dark energy）成分，从而自然缓解哈勃张力。

Conclusion: 原初黑洞的类排斥行为能够在“瑞士奶酪”框架下同时解释早期宇宙暴胀与哈勃张力问题，为无需标量场的自然暴胀机制提供了一种新的可能性。

Abstract: We review a new natural inflationary mechanism operated by repulsive-like primordial black holes (PBHs). In particular, working within the ``Swiss - Cheese" cosmological framework, we find that a Universe filled with PBHs, whose spacetime metric presents a repulsive-like behaviour, is characterised by an early quasi-de-Sitter cosmic expansion phase. Notably, for light PBHs with $m < 5 \times 10^8 \mathrm{g}$, evaporating before Big Bang Nucleosynthesis (BBN), one is met with an exponential inflationary phase with graceful exit and reheating proceeding through PBH evaporation. Furthermore, one finds as well that PBHs with $m \sim 10^{12}\mathrm{g}$ and abundances $0.107 < Ω^\mathrm{eq}_\mathrm{PBH} < 0.5$ near matter-radiation equality can act as an early dark energy component, easing in this way naturally the Hubble tension.

Method: 利用Gauss-Bonnet定理（Gauss-Bonnet theorem）应用于等离子体中的光学几何，推导出光线偏转角（deflection angle）的修正表达式，并结合灰体因子分析能量发射谱的修正。

Abstract: We study the deflection of light in a homogeneous plasma medium around a BTZ-ModMax black hole, focusing on the effects of the ModMax nonlinear electrodynamics parameter and the cosmological constant. Using the Gauss-Bonnet theorem applied to the corresponding optical geometry in plasma, we derive a modified expression for the deflection angle and examine how plasma dispersion alters the gravitational lensing behavior. The influence of the ModMax parameter in the presence of homogeneous plasma is compared with its vacuum counterpart, as well as with the charged and static BTZ black hole cases, revealing distinct signatures arising from nonlinear electrodynamics. This work highlights the combined impact of homogeneous plasma, spacetime curvature, and nonlinear field dynamics on light deflection in lower-dimensional black hole geometries. We further study the greybody factor and analyze how the presence of homogeneous plasma and the ModMax parameter modifies the energy emission spectrum of the black hole. Our results demonstrate that both plasma effects and nonlinear electrodynamics significantly influence the transmission probabilities and emission rates, providing deeper insight into wave propagation and observational signatures in lower-dimensional black hole geometries.

### [112] [Extended thermodynamics and $P-v$ Criticality of Kalb-Ramond black hole coupled with nonlinear electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05281)
*D. V. Singh,S. Upadhyay,P. Paul,K. Myrzakulov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在反德西特（AdS）时空中构造了一个与非线性电动力学（NLED）耦合的Kalb-Ramond场精确黑洞解，分析了其几何结构和热力学性质，发现Lorentz破坏参数和非线性电动力学效应导致温度非单调、熵偏离面积定律、比热为负等丰富热力学行为，并验证了扩展相空间中的第一定律和Smarr关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Lorentz破坏效应与非线性电动力学（NLED）对反德西特（AdS）时空黑洞几何与热力学性质的影响，揭示其与Kalb-Ramond场耦合所导致的新奇热力学行为。

Method: 通过精确求解Einstein方程获得AdS时空中与非线性电动力学耦合的Kalb-Ramond场黑洞解；计算Hawking温度、熵、比热、Gibbs自由能等热力学量，并在扩展相空间中推导第一定律与Smarr关系。

Result: 该解存在内外两个视界，在临界磁单极荷时简并为退化视界；NLED源导致Hawking温度出现非单调行为与局部极值，熵偏离标准面积定律，比热可呈负值，Gibbs自由能呈现燕尾结构（swallow-tail structure）指示一级相变；扩展相空间中的第一定律和Smarr关系均成立。

Abstract: We present an exact black hole solution in anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetime with a Kalb-Ramond field coupled to nonlinear electrodynamics (NLED), characterized by mass, magnetic monopole charge, and Lorentz-violating parameters. The geometry admits two horizons (inner and outer) that coalesce into a degenerate horizon at a critical monopole charge. Beyond this critical point, no black hole solutions exist. In the limit of vanishing Lorentz-violating parameters, the solution reduces to the modified Kalb-Ramond and Bardeen black holes, while suitable parameter choices reproduce the Reissner-Nordström-AdS and Schwarzschild-AdS geometries. We analyze the thermodynamics of the solution by computing the Hawking temperature, entropy, specific heat, and Gibbs free energy. The NLED source introduces nontrivial modifications: the Hawking temperature displays nonmonotonic behavior with possible local extrema, the entropy deviates from the standard area law, and the specific heat may assume negative values, signaling thermodynamic instabilities. The Gibbs free energy exhibits swallow-tail structures, indicative of first-order phase transitions. Furthermore, we derive the first law of black hole thermodynamics in the extended phase space, together with the Smarr relation, and confirm their validity for the Kalb-Ramond black holes with NLED sources. Our findings highlight the rich thermodynamic structure induced by Lorentz-violating effects and nonlinear electrodynamics in AdS black hole backgrounds.

### [113] [Canonical quantization of all minisuperspaces with consistent symmetry reductions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05311)
*Poula Tadros,Ivan Koář,Otakar Svítek*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文实现了爱因斯坦-希尔伯特拉格朗日量所有对称性约化的量子化，这些约化正确再现了约化后的爱因斯坦场方程，并基于对称临界性原理。研究涵盖了多种时空对称性，推导了哈密顿量与超空间度规的共形对称性（条件对称性），将其提升为算符，并在有无施加这些对称性的情况下求解了惠勒-德威特方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子引力（quantum gravity）研究中，完整量子化爱因斯坦-希尔伯特（Einstein–Hilbert）拉格朗日量面临巨大困难。本文旨在通过对满足对称临界性（principle of symmetric criticality）的对称性约化进行量子化，从而在简化模型中正确再现约化的爱因斯坦场方程，为量子宇宙学（quantum cosmology）和量子黑洞物理提供严格的约化框架。

Method: 首先识别并选取所有满足对称临界性原理的无穷小群作用，这些作用对应于多种时空对称性（spacetime symmetries）。随后推导哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）以及超空间度规（superspace metrics）的共形对称性，即条件对称性（conditional symmetries），并将其提升为量子算符。最后在施加与不施加这些对称性的两种情形下，求解惠勒-德威特方程（Wheeler–DeWitt equation）。

Result: 成功实现了多种经典对称性约化（如球/双曲/平面施瓦西-陶布-NUT度量、Bianchi I/II/VIII/IX时空、近极端克尔几何、漩涡宇宙、FLRW宇宙学等）的量子化。得到了相应的哈密顿量算符与条件对称性算符，并在两种情形下获得了惠勒-德威特方程的解。

Conclusion: 本文建立的量子化方案适用于一大类具有重要物理意义的对称性约化时空，为在量子引力框架下研究宇宙学与黑洞物理提供了统一的量子化路径。条件对称性在求解惠勒-德威特方程中发挥了关键作用。

Abstract: We present the quantization of all symmetry reductions of the Einstein--Hilbert Lagrangian that correctly reproduce the reduced Einstein's field equations -- i.e., characterized by the infinitesimal group actions obeying the principle of symmetric criticality. These correspond to the spacetime symmetries of spherical/hyperbolic/planar Schwarzschild/Taub--NUT, BI/BII/BIII-metrics, near-horizon extreme Kerr geometry, swirling universe, closed/open/flat FLRW cosmologies, other FLRW-type metrics, and Bianchi type I, II, VIII, and IX spacetimes. We derive the Hamiltonian and the conformal symmetries of the superspace metrics (the conditional symmetries), promote them to operators, and solve the Wheeler--DeWitt equation with and without imposing these symmetries.

</details>


### [114] [Perturbations in the parametrized wormhole spacetime and their related quasinormal modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05352)
*Shauvik Biswas,Sayan Chakrabarti*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究参数化静态球对称虫洞时空的电磁扰动与准正则模，聚焦Damour-Solodukhin和弦世界几何及其星系扩展。通过Bronnikov-Konoplya-Pappas参数化方法，利用远场和近喉部参数刻画时空，并将其扩展至嵌入Hernquist暗物质晕的星系虫洞。利用Sgr A*阴影观测约束参数，采用转移矩阵法计算准正则模频率，发现阻尼率对星系致密性更敏感，振荡频率则相对稳定。该方法为无视界致密天体的强场检验提供了观测一致的参数化描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为超越黑洞模型、探索虫洞等无视界致密天体（horizonless compact objects）的强场引力效应，需要建立可观测检验的参数化框架。现有虫洞模型缺乏与观测约束（如阴影）的系统连接，亟需一种能够统一描述几何参数化、阴影约束和动力学响应的方法。

Method: 采用Bronnikov-Konoplya-Pappas参数化方法，通过紧致化径向坐标将度规函数表示为远场后牛顿系数和近喉部连分式展开。将框架扩展至嵌入Hernquist暗物质晕的星系Damour-Solodukhin虫洞，利用Sgr A*阴影观测边界约束星系致密性和变形参数。采用转移矩阵法（transfer matrix method）计算基模准正则模频率，并分析时域环信号（ringdown signals）。

Result: 非多项式度规函数可能限制近喉部展开的收敛性及截断表示的精度。在阴影允许的参数空间内，阻尼率对星系致密性更敏感，振荡频率则相对稳定。谱偏移在阴影允许区域内较小。

Conclusion: 建立了观测一致的参数化虫洞扰动描述，为强场检验无视界致密天体提供了系统性工具，将几何参数化、阴影约束与动力学响应三者联系起来。

Abstract: We study electromagnetic perturbations and the associated quasinormal modes (QNMs) of parametrized static, spherically symmetric wormhole spacetimes, focusing on Damour-Solodukhin and braneworld geometries as well as their galactic extensions. Using the Bronnikov-Konoplya-Pappas parametrization, we express the metric functions in terms of a compactified radial coordinate and characterize the spacetime through far-field and near-throat parameters. The far-field coefficients govern the asymptotic structure and post-Newtonian behaviour, while the near-throat continued-fraction expansion captures the strong-field geometry near the throat. We first apply the parametrization to isolated wormholes and identify its range of validity, showing that non-polynomial metric functions can limit the convergence of the near-throat expansion and hence the accuracy of a truncated representation. We then extend the framework to a galactic Damour-Solodukhin wormhole embedded in a Hernquist dark matter halo. Imposing observational bounds from the shadow of Sgr A$^*$, we constrain the galactic compactness and deformation parameters and obtain an observationally viable parametrized metric. Within the allowed parameter space, we compute the fundamental QNM frequencies using the transfer matrix method and analyze the corresponding time-domain ringdown signals. We find that the damping rate is more sensitive to galactic compactness, whereas the oscillation frequency remains comparatively stable. Although the spectral shifts are small within the shadow-allowed region, the framework provides a systematic link between geometric parametrization, shadow constraints, and dynamical response. Our results establish an observationally consistent parametrized description of wormhole perturbations for strong-field tests of horizonless compact objects.

Abstract: Extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs), with their long-lived and highly relativistic orbital evolution, can probe strong-field spacetime geometry and provide an important means to test general relativity. In this work, we investigate EMRI waveforms in a Schwarzschild-like black hole spacetime arising in bumblebee gravity, where Lorentz symmetry breaking (LSB) is characterized by a dimensionless parameter $\ell$. We construct EMRI waveforms within the Augmented Analytic Kludge (AAK) framework using the modified orbital frequencies and fluxes. We find that $\ell$ significantly affects the orbital evolution and thereby modifies the waveform. These modifications grow with increasing $\ell$ and are further enhanced for more eccentric orbits. Furthermore, using Bayesian analysis, we obtain the posterior distributions of EMRI with the parameter $\ell$ included. Our results show that all injected source parameters are recovered within their $1\,σ$ credible intervals. Abstract: In this work, we present an exact static spherically symmetric vacuum solution of the New General Relativity (NGR) field equations. Unlike the Schwarzschild solution in General Relativity (GR), this solution is characterized by two parameters. ### [117] [Testing General Relativity with Individual Supermassive Black Hole Binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05512)
*Qinyuan Zheng,Bjorn Larsen,Ellis Eisenberg,Chiara M. F. Mingarelli*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个统一的框架，用于通过来自超大质量双黑洞（SMBHBs）的连续引力波（CWs）在纳赫兹频段检验超出广义相对论（GR）的引力理论，涵盖额外极化态、修正色散关系和宇称破缺双折射三类偏离，并通过注入-恢复模拟验证了该框架的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力检验多聚焦于引力波背景（GWB）或爆发事件，而连续引力波（CW）——特别是来自超大质量双黑洞（SMBHBs）的长寿命、近单色纳赫兹信号——因其相干相位演化和跨脉冲星关联能够保留GR偏离的精细信息，但缺乏一个统一的检验框架。

Method: 针对三类超越GR的偏离（额外极化态、修正色散关系、宇称破缺双折射），分别推导了脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）中的跨脉冲星互关联、修正的天线响应函数以及传播诱导的脉冲星项相位延迟。通过注入-恢复模拟，对呼吸模式和巨引力子信号进行了当前观测极限下的验证。

Result: 对于非张量极化，CW的互关联在超越GR模式次主导时与替代极化振幅呈线性标度（区别于GWB的二次标度）。PTA在修正色散关系方面具有竞争力，低频增强天线模式修正和脉冲星项相位延迟；双折射在纳赫兹频段对大多数宇称破缺理论被抑制。纯GR模板在存在超越GR物理时仍能无显著偏倚地恢复源参数。

Conclusion: 该框架支持两阶段分析策略：先在GR假设下识别CW候选体，再检验超越GR的偏离。连续引力波为引力检验提供了独特且互补于引力波背景的探测途径。

Abstract: We develop a unified framework for testing gravity beyond General Relativity (GR) with continuous gravitational waves (CWs) from individual supermassive black hole binaries (SMBHBs). These long-lived, nearly monochromatic nanohertz signals offer unique strengths for precision tests of gravity, since their coherent phase evolution and inter-pulsar correlations in pulsar timing arrays (PTAs) retain detailed information about departures from GR over cosmological propagation distances. We consider three representative classes of deviations from GR: additional polarization states, modified dispersion relations, and parity-violating birefringence. For each, we derive the inter-pulsar cross correlation, the modified antenna response, and the propagation-induced pulsar-term phase delay. For non-tensorial polarizations, the CW cross correlation scales linearly in the alternative-polarization amplitude, compared to the quadratic scaling of the gravitational-wave background (GWB), provided the beyond-GR modes are sub-dominant. PTAs are also competitive for modified dispersion relations, where low frequencies enhance both the antenna-pattern modification and the pulsar-term phase delay. Birefringence, by contrast, is suppressed at nanohertz frequencies for most parity-violating theories. We validate the framework with injection-and-recovery simulations for breathing-mode and massive-graviton signals at current observational limits, recovering the injected beyond-GR parameters and distinguishing the CW signal from both correlated and uncorrelated background models. We further show that a pure-GR CW template recovers source parameters without significant bias when beyond-GR physics is present in the data, supporting a two-stage analysis strategy: identify candidates under GR, then test for deviations.

### [118] [Implications of the LISA stochastic signal from eccentric stellar mass black hole binaries in vacuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05537)
*Ran Chen,Rohit S. Chandramouli,Federico Pozzoli,Riccardo Buscicchio,Enrico Barausse*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文分析恒星质量双黑洞（sBBHs）的轨道偏心率对随机引力波背景（SGWB）的影响，开发了改进的SGWB模型，并利用贝叶斯框架证明高偏心率分布可被稳健区分，且偏心率建模对于LISA观测的天体物理解读至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 恒星质量双黑洞（stellar-mass binary black holes, sBBHs）的天体物理形成通道可能导致其早先旋进阶段存在显著的轨道偏心率（orbital eccentricity），而现有随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational-wave background, SGWB）模型多假设准圆轨道。该研究旨在量化偏心率对未解析sBBHs产生的SGWB的影响，并为未来LISA观测提供准确的理论预测。

Method: 提出一个改进的SGWB模型，首先针对理想化的狄拉克δ偏心率分布（Dirac-delta eccentricity distribution）进行建模，随后扩展至更符合天体物理实际的热分布（thermal distribution）。采用完全贝叶斯框架（fully Bayesian framework）进行分析，并考虑环境效应（如动力学摩擦，dynamical friction）与真空演化的区分。

Result: 若所有双星初始偏心率e₀≳0.9（在轨道频率f_orb=10⁻⁴ Hz处），其SGWB可与准圆sBBHs背景稳健区分。热分布下，当双星形成于f_orb=10⁻⁵ Hz时，SGWB与圆模型一致；但若形成于f_orb=10⁻⁴ Hz，则导致显著系统偏差。环境效应仅在气体密度ρ≳10⁻⁷ g cm⁻³的足够致密环境中可被区分。LISA探测sBBH SGWB可对地面探测器频段内的最大偏心率施加上限。

Conclusion: 将偏心率纳入SGWB建模对于LISA观测的准确天体物理解读至关重要。该研究凸显了偏心率效应在SGWB模型中的重要性，并指出偏心率建模将直接影响地面引力波探测器的模板建模（template modeling）与数据分析。

Abstract: Astrophysical formation channels of stellar-mass binary black holes (sBBHs) can induce significant orbital eccentricities in their early inspiral. We analyze the implications on the stochastic gravitational-wave background (SGWB) from unresolved sBBHs, which can be detected with the Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA). We develop an improved SGWB model for the case of an idealized Dirac-delta eccentricity distribution, and extend it to the more astrophysical case of a thermal distribution. Using a fully Bayesian framework, we find that, if all binaries have a high initial eccentricity $e_0 \gtrsim 0.9$ at an orbital frequency of $f_{\rm orb} = 10^{-4}\,\mathrm{Hz}$, the resulting SGWB can be robustly distinguished from a background of quasi-circular sBBHs. For a thermal eccentricity distribution, the SGWB is consistent with a circular model when binaries form at $f_{\rm orb} = 10^{-5}\,\mathrm{Hz}$, but leads to significant systematic biases if formation occurs at $f_{\rm orb} = 10^{-4}\,\mathrm{Hz}$. We also show that, when eccentricity is properly accounted for, environmental effects such as dynamical friction can be distinguished from vacuum evolution, but only for sufficiently dense environments with gas densities $ρ\gtrsim 10^{-7}\,\mathrm{g\,cm^{-3}}$. Finally, we show that a LISA detection of the sBBH SGWB would place an upper bound on the maximum eccentricity of the sBBH population in the band of ground-based detectors, with direct implications for template modeling and data analysis. Our results highlight the importance of incorporating eccentricity in SGWB modeling to enable accurate astrophysical interpretation of LISA observations.

Abstract: We investigate the optical appearance of rotating black holes embedded in dark matter environments through a phenomenological ray-tracing framework. Instead of focusing on a single dark-matter-dressed geometry, we use a comparative setting in which a regular Einasto-type dark-matter-sourced black hole and a cored-NFW halo black hole are promoted to effective rotating backgrounds. This allows us to separate profile-dependent effects from generic Kerr-like rotational features. We construct observer-screen images by numerical backward ray tracing and analyse the shadow boundary, lensing bands, transfer maps, and synthetic intensity distributions produced by semi-analytic accretion prescriptions. Particular attention is paid to the possible degeneracy between spin and the dark matter parameters, and to whether higher-order lensed images can provide stronger signatures than the primary shadow size alone. For the representative parameters considered here, the Einasto-supported geometry remains close to Kerr, while the cored-NFW case produces a larger apparent image scale and more visible deviations in the lensed structure. The framework developed in this work is lightweight and extensible, and can be used as a first step toward future radiative-transfer and low-resolution accretion-flow studies of rotating dark-matter-dressed black holes.

### [120] [Scalar-Field Reconstruction of Ricci--Gauss--Bonnet Dark Energy in Hořava--Lifshitz Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05663)
*Surajit Chattopadhyay*

TL;DR: 本文在Hořava-Lifshitz宇宙学框架下提出了一个Ricci-Gauss-Bonnet (RGB)暗能量模型，并进行了标量场重构。在幂律尺度因子的平坦FRW背景中，导出了宇宙学参数、标量场动能项和重构势的解析表达式。重构的状态方程(EoS)参数在合适的模型参数选择下，于晚期平滑过渡到类宇宙学常数区域。通过声速平方分析了经典稳定性并识别出稳定参数区域，同时在表观视界处验证了广义第二热力学定律，表明总熵变非负。该模型在特定参数范围内提供了对晚期加速膨胀的理论自洽描述。
