  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有暗能量模型在理论自洽性与观测符合方面仍存在不足，需要构建基于修正引力理论的新暗能量模型。本文尝试在Hořava-Lifshitz宇宙学框架中引入Ricci-Gauss-Bonnet修正，以期获得对晚期宇宙加速膨胀的理论自洽描述。

Method: 采用平坦FRW背景并假设幂律尺度因子，在Hořava-Lifshitz宇宙学框架下构建RGB暗能量模型。通过标量场重构技术将有效暗能量部分映射为标量场理论，导出其动能项和势函数的解析表达式。使用声速平方分析经典稳定性，并基于表观视界处的热力学分析检验广义第二热力学定律。

Result: 重构的状态方程(EoS)参数在适当模型参数下于晚期平滑过渡至类宇宙学常数行为。声速平方分析识别出参数空间中的经典稳定区域。广义第二热力学定律在表观视界处成立，即总熵变化保持非负。

Conclusion: 该RGB暗能量模型在特定模型参数范围内提供了对晚期宇宙加速膨胀的理论自洽描述，且在物理上具有可行性。

Abstract: This paper reports a Ricci-Gauss-Bonnet (RGB) dark energy model within the framework of Hořava-Lifshitz cosmology and presents a scalar-field reconstruction of the effective dark energy sector. In a spatially flat FRW background with a power-law scale factor, we derive analytical expressions for cosmological parameters, scalar field kinetic term, and the reconstructed potential. The reconstructed EoS parameter exhibits smooth transition toward a cosmological-constant-like regime at late times for suitable choices of the model parameters. The classical stability of the model is analyzed through the squared sound speed, and stable regions of the parameter space are identified. Finally, the generalized second law of thermodynamics is investigated at the apparent horizon, and it is shown that the total entropy variation remains non-negative in this model. From these results it can be concluded that the model provides a theoretically consistent description of late-time acceleration, with physical viability maintained within a specific range of the model parameters.

</details>


### [121] [Classical General Relativity as a Non-Conservative Action-Dependent Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05817)
*Callum Bell,David Sloan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文将标度对称性（scaling symmetries）从奇异拉格朗日量描述的经典场论推广到广义相对论的一阶形式化（first-order formulation）中，表明希尔伯特作用量（Hilbert action）的动力学内容可用共形时空几何（conformal spacetime geometry）与一个耗散扇区（dissipative sector）共同描述；线性化分析给出自由波动方程，而二阶引力反作用（gravitational backreaction）动力学由一阶扰动的二次项驱动，但具有非保守性（non-conservative）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前已有研究针对奇异拉格朗日量描述的经典场论考察了标度对称性，本文旨在将这些结果应用于广义相对论的一阶形式化，以探讨其标度不变性结构。

Method: 将先前的标度对称性分析框架应用于广义相对论的一阶形式化；通过对希尔伯特作用量进行数学重构，将其分解为共形几何部分与耗散补偿部分；进一步对运动方程进行线性化与二阶展开分析。

Result: 希尔伯特作用量的动力学内容可由共形时空几何与一个用于补偿标度概念消除的耗散扇区共同表述；一阶度规扰动（first-order metric perturbations）满足自由波动方程（free wave equation）；二阶动力学描述引力反作用，其源项为一阶扰动的二次组合，但该动力学由于作用扇区与几何自由度之间的耦合项而表现出非保守性。

Conclusion: 广义相对论的一阶形式化在标度对称性框架下可自然分解为共形几何部分与非保守的耗散部分，后者源于标度自由度（共形因子）的消除；二阶引力反作用动力学具有非保守特征，表明标度对称性在引力系统的能量-动量交换中扮演重要角色。

Abstract: Scaling symmetries have previously been examined for classical field theories described by singular Lagrangians; in this article, we apply these results to the first-order formulation of General Relativity. It is shown that the dynamical content of the Hilbert action may be formulated in terms of the conformal spacetime geometry, together with a dissipative sector, which is required in order to compensate the elimination of the notion of scale encoded by the conformal factor. Further, we consider the linearisation of the equations of motion of the scale-invariant action, demonstrating that the first-order metric perturbations satisfy a free wave equation, as expected. The second-order dynamics, describing gravitational backreaction, are found to be sourced by quadratic combinations of the first-order perturbations. However, these dynamics are non-conservative, as is made manifest by the presence of terms which couple the action sector with the geometrical degrees of freedom.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法主要局限于四维时空中的准正则模式计算，对于高维Kerr时空（尤其是具有紧致额外维度的情况）缺乏通用的计算框架。

Method: 基于双自旋子（two-spinors）构造向量，发展出一种多自旋子形式体系，该体系在结构上类比四维时空中的Newman-Penrose形式体系，并以此推导高维Teukolsky方程及准正则模式。

Result: 成功以六维时空为例，展示了如何利用多自旋子形式体系推导引力扰动（gravitational perturbations）下的Teukolsky方程并计算准正则模式，且该方法可推广至其他维度。

Conclusion: 所发展的多自旋子形式体系为高维Kerr时空中准正则模式的计算提供了一种通用且可推广的途径。

Abstract: The aim of this paper is to present a general way to calculate quasi-normal modes (QNM) of the Teukolsky equation for higher dimensional (d > 4) Kerr spacetime with compactified extra dimensions. In order to do so, we develop a formalism derived from spinors: we call it multispinor formalism. It is based on vectors of two-spinors and permits us to develop a formalism analogous to that of Newman-Penrose in 4d. From this we show how to derive the Teukolsky equation for gravitational perturbations and calculate the QNM. In order to keep calculations simple we fix, as an example, the dimension number to be six, but the work can be readily generalized to other spacetime dimensions.

### [123] [Singularity Resolution in Quantum Cosmology via Page-Wootters Formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06093)
*Vishal,Malay K. Nandy*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在惠勒-德维特（Wheeler-DeWitt, WDW）框架下，利用佩奇-伍特斯（Page-Wootters）形式论研究平面对称Bianchi-I型宇宙中的经典大爆炸奇点问题。通过构建高斯叠加的动量本征态作为WDW方程的全局解，并构造条件概率密度，该密度在体积趋于零时对所有时钟值均消失，表明经典奇点得到了量子消解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子引力框架下处理经典宇宙学中的大爆炸奇点问题，并解决量子宇宙学中长期存在的“时间问题”（problem of time）。

Method: 采用佩奇-伍特斯（Page-Wootters）形式论，通过将全局态条件化于时钟子系统提供关系性动力学；利用米斯纳变量（Misner variables）将WDW方程转化为克莱因-戈登（Klein-Gordon, KG）型方程，并构造高斯叠加的动量本征态作为全局纠缠态。

Result: 条件概率密度在体积趋于零时对所有时钟值均消失，表明经典奇点得到量子消解；概率密度的正定性对允许的时钟值施加了依赖于高斯波包参数的约束。

Conclusion: 量子关联在关系性动力学的涌现中起关键作用，佩奇-伍特斯形式论为量子宇宙学提供了一致且非奇异的概率描述。

Abstract: We investigate the problem of classical big bang singularity in a plane-symmetric Bianchi type-I universe within the Wheeler-DeWitt (WDW) framework of quantum gravity. To address the problem of time, we employ the Page-Wootters formalism, which provides a relational notion of dynamics by conditioning the global state on a clock subsystem. Using Misner variables, the WDW equation assumes a Klein-Gordon (KG) type form. Its general solution is constructed as a Gaussian superposition of momentum eigenstates, resulting in an entangled global state between the clock and the remaining subsystem. Within this relational framework, we construct conditional states and obtain the corresponding probability density consistent with the KG-type inner product. The resulting conditional probability density vanishes in the limit of zero volume for all clock values, indicating quantum resolution of the classical singularity. We further show that positivity of the probability density imposes constraints on the admissible clock values, which depend on the parameters of the Gaussian wavepacket. These results highlight the essential role of quantum correlations in the emergence of relational dynamics, and demonstrate that the Page-Wootters formalism provides a consistent and nonsingular probabilistic description of quantum cosmology.

### [124] [Cosmological Dynamics of a Non-Canonical Generalised Brans-Dicke Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06147)
*Matthew Debono,Jackson Levi Said,Gabriel Farrugia*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在ΛCDM模型面临宇宙学张力的背景下，研究了一种推广的Brans-Dicke理论——包含非最小耦合（non-minimal coupling）和非正则动能项（non-canonical kinetic term）的标量场理论。通过将场方程重构为自治动力系统，利用动力系统方法分析了三种常用势能（常数、幂律、指数势）下的平衡态及其稳定性，并借助有界相图（bounded phase portraits）可视化流形。研究发现，在三种势能下均存在能复现ΛCDM模型背景行为的可行解，且由于非最小耦合和非正则标量场的引入，动力学行为与其它标量-张量模型存在显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高精度宇宙学数据揭示ΛCDM模型存在若干宇宙学张力（cosmic tensions），暗示可能存在动力学暗能量（dynamical dark energy）组分，亟需探索超越标准广义相对论的替代理论框架。

Method: 采用推广的Brans-Dicke理论（Brans-Dicke theory），引入非最小耦合（non-minimally coupled）且具有非正则动能项（non-canonical kinetic term）的标量场（scalar field）。将场方程重新表述为自治动力系统（autonomous dynamical system），运用动力系统方法（dynamical systems method）分析平衡态及其稳定性，并通过有界相图（bounded phase portraits）可视化流形（flow）。

Result: 对于常数势（constant potential）、幂律势（power-law potential）和指数势（exponential potential）三种广泛使用的势能形式，均找到了能在背景层次（background level）复现ΛCDM模型特征的可行解。尽管使用了类似定义的动力学变量，但由于非最小耦合和非正则场的存在，系统的动力学行为与其它标量-张量模型（scalar-tensor models）存在显著差异。

Conclusion: 该推广的Brans-Dicke理论框架可以提供替代ΛCDM的可行宇宙学模型，其独特的动力学行为为解释宇宙学张力提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: The LCDM model has been presented with a number of cosmic tensions in the face of precision cosmological data, suggesting the presence of a dynamical dark energy component. In this context, we investigate the cosmology arising from a generalisation of Brans-Dicke theory, with a non-minimally coupled scalar field characterising deviations from standard general relativity, and having a non-canonical kinetic term. By reformulating the field equations into an autonomous set of dynamical equations, we use the methods of dynamical systems to investigate the equilibrium states of the system and their stability for a set of widely-used potentials, namely the constant, power-law, and exponential potentials, with the flow visualized using bounded phase portraits. Furthermore, we investigate the physical meaning of the critical points, and we find viable solutions that can reproduce the characteristics of the $Λ$CDM model at background level for each of the three potentials. Furthermore, in each case, we observe that the dynamical behaviour differs noticeably from that observed in other scalar-tensor models due to the non-minimal coupling and non-canonical field, despite using similarly defined dynamical variables.

</details>


### [125] [Spin and Quadrupole Sectors in Nonrelativistic Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06410)
*Utku Zorba*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在ADM变量下，利用大$c$展开（large-$c$ expansion）和统一的偶$\omega$展开方法，系统研究了伽利略（Galilean）分支中广义相对论的ADM作用量与场方程，构建了包含自旋、四极矩及其混合效应的弱支和强支稳态真空解，并重建了近似的时空度规，可用于旋转致密天体（如黑洞和中子星）周围时空的研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在ADM（Arnowitt-Deser-Misner）变量下对广义相对论进行大$c$展开，是为了统一处理伽利略极限（Galilean limit）和卡罗尔极限（Carrollian limit），并系统地获取广义相对论在非相对论极限下的高阶修正解。

Method: 采用统一的偶$\omega$展开方法，以ADM表述为共同起点，重点研究伽利略分支；推导到次次领头阶（NNLO）的ADM作用量与场方程，并在弱支与强支中分别构造稳态真空解。

Result: 弱支中得到了次领头阶（NLO）的Kerr型、Hartle-Thorne型及混合型解，并可推广到高质多极矩。次次领头阶中，弱Kerr型与扩展Hartle-Thorne型分别满足方程，但简单叠加不成立；非线性NNLO方程产生了混合的$J^2Q$源项，需额外修正NNLO的lapse和空间张量场，由此给出ADM规范下的混合弱支伽利略解。强支中，Kerr型数据在NNLO均满足方程，Hartle-Thorne型数据在NLO满足方程。最后，ADM数据可重建为包含自旋、四极矩及混合自旋-四极矩效应的近似时空度规。

Conclusion: 该大$c$展开方法能够系统地构建包含高阶自旋和四极矩效应的伽利略分支解，重建后的近似度规对研究黑洞和中子星等旋转致密天体周围的时空结构具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: We study the large-$c$ expansion of general relativity in ADM variables. Using a unified even $ω$-expansion, the ADM formulation gives a common starting point for Galilean and Carrollian limits. We focus on the Galilean branch and derive the ADM action and field equations up to NNLO. We then construct stationary vacuum solutions in weak and strong branches. In the weak branch, we find NLO Kerr-type, Hartle-Thorne-type and mixed-type solutions. The NLO weak equations also allow a simple extension to higher mass multipoles. At NNLO, the weak Kerr-type and extended Hartle-Thorne-type sectors solve the equations separately, but their naive sum is not a solution. The nonlinear NNLO equations generate mixed $J^2Q$ source terms, which require additional corrections to the NNLO lapse and NNLO spatial tensor field. This gives a mixed weak-branch Galilean solution in the ADM gauge. In the strong branch, Kerr-type data solve the equations through NNLO while the strong Hartle-Thorne-type data solve the NLO equations. We also explain how the ADM data can be reconstructed into approximate spacetime metrics. Since these metrics include spin, quadrupole and mixed spin-quadrupole effects, they may be useful for studying the spacetime around rotating compact objects such as black holes and neutron stars.

</details>


### [126] [On the non-radial oscillations of realistic anisotropic neutron stars: Axial modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06418)
*Jose F. Rodriguez-Ruiz,L. M. Becerra,F. D. Lora-Clavijo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了具有各向异性压力（anisotropic pressure）的中子星轴向（axial）非径向振荡模式，发现压力各向异性会直接耦合物质与度规扰动，并通过数值积分表明：随着星体质量增大，低频w-模频率降低、阻尼时间延长；较大各向异性允许更致密的平衡构型，且频率与阻尼时间经质量标度后对星体致密度（compactness）呈近乎普适的二次依赖关系，对状态方程和具体各向异性模型不敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子星的内部组成和相对论结构可通过其非径向振荡模式加以诊断，但此前对轴向模（axial modes）的研究较少，主要因为各向同性极限下物质与度规扰动相互解耦，而实际星体可能具有各向异性压力，需要给出轴向模的一致处理。

Method: 采用参数化的各向异性模型以保证物质扰动处理的一致性；在静态球对称各向异性中子星背景下对轴向模线性化爱因斯坦场方程（linearized Einstein field equations）进行数值积分，并使用多组真实的状态方程（equation of state）。

Result: 随着中子星质量增大，较低w-模频率降低而阻尼时间延长；较软的状态方程通常给出略高的振荡频率；较大的各向异性（切向压力大于径向压力）允许更高质量的平衡构型，进而导致更低的振荡频率和更长的阻尼时间；频率与阻尼时间经质量标度后对星体致密度呈近乎普适的二次依赖关系，对状态方程和各向异性模型不敏感。

Conclusion: 压力各向异性对中子星轴向模的振荡特性有显著影响，但经过质量标度后，频率和阻尼时间与致密度之间呈现普适的二次关系，这一普适性有助于通过引力波观测约束中子星内部结构。

Abstract: Non-radial oscillation modes of neutron stars serve as diagnostics of their internal composition and relativistic structure. In this work, we investigate the perturbations of static and spherically symmetric neutron stars characterized by an anisotropic pressure. Given the background symmetry, perturbations decouple into polar and axial modes. To date, axial modes have remained less explored, primarily because matter and metric perturbations decouple in the isotropic limit. In this work, we provide a consistent treatment of axial modes and demonstrate that pressure anisotropy induces a direct coupling between matter and metric perturbations. We employ parameterized anisotropy models that ensure consistency with the treatment of matter perturbations. We numerically integrate the linearized Einstein field equations for the axial modes, employing a diverse set of realistic equations of state. Our results indicate that as the stellar mass grows, the frequency of the lower $w$-mode generally decreases, while its damping time increases. Softer equation of states typically yield slightly higher oscillation frequencies. Furthermore, larger anisotropy (i.e., when the tangential pressure exceeds the radial pressure) allows for more massive equilibrium configurations, which correspondingly leads to lower oscillation frequencies and prolonged damping times. Finally, we demonstrate that the frequency and damping time, both scaled by the stellar mass, exhibit a nearly universal quadratic dependence on the stellar compactness, remaining largely insensitive to both the underlying equation of state and the specific anisotropy model.

</details>


### [127] [Quasi-homogeneous black hole geometrothermodynamics in Einstein-Maxwell theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06602)
*Hernando Quevedo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该综述建立了几何热力学（geometrothermodynamics, GTD）的数学框架，用于以勒让德不变（Legendre-invariant）的方式描述非广延、准均匀的自引力系统。研究表明黑洞基本方程为准齐次函数，并推导了若干黑洞平衡流形的度规及其曲率奇点，建立了曲率奇点与相变（由热容发散确定）之间的直接对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有实验室热力学的标准欧拉恒等式（Euler identity）对黑洞等自引力系统失效，亟需一个能够处理非广延、准均匀性质的勒让德不变形式体系。

Method: 基于几何热力学（GTD）的数学框架，将黑洞基本方程视为准齐次函数，推导平衡流形的度规，并通过曲率奇点分析检验其与热容发散之间的对应关系。

Result: 推导了Reissner-Nordström、Kerr和Kerr-Newman黑洞的平衡流形度规；发现这些流形的曲率奇点与对应热容（heat capacity）的发散位置一致，建立了曲率奇点与相变之间的直接对应。

Conclusion: 几何热力学（GTD）能够以勒让德不变的方式统一描述非广延自引力系统；黑洞平衡流形的曲率奇点可作为判断相变的几何判据。

Abstract: In this review, we establish the mathematical framework of geometrothermodynamics (GTD) as a formalism capable of describing non-extensive, quasi-homogeneous, self-gravitating systems in a Legendre-invariant manner. We argue that the fundamental equations of black holes are quasi-homogeneous functions, a property that invalidates the standard Euler identity of laboratory thermodynamics. We derive the metrics for the equilibrium manifold and analyze their curvature singularities for the Reissner-Nordström, Kerr, and Kerr-Newman black holes. Furthermore, we establish a direct correspondence between the curvature singularities of the equilibrium space and phase transitions, as determined by the divergences of the corresponding heat capacities.

### [128] [The strange and flavor-singlet axial form factors of the nucleon from lattice QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06559)
*Alessandro Barone,Dalibor Djukanovic,Georg von Hippel,Harvey B. Meyer,Konstantin Ottnad,Hartmut Wittig*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文通过格点量子色动力学（lattice QCD）计算了核子的单态轴矢形状因子（singlet axial form factor）及其奇异夸克贡献，并结合同位旋矢量（isovector）与八重态同位旋标量（isoscalar octet）的结果，提供了跨不同味道通道的核子轴矢结构完整格点QCD测定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核子单态轴矢形状因子是理解核子轴矢结构的关键输入，其在前向极限下与同位旋矢量及八重态同位旋标量通道共同构成质子自旋完整味道分解（flavor decomposition）的基础。

Method: 采用$N_f = 2 + 1$ CLS规范场系综（gauge ensembles）及$O(a)$改进Wilson费米子（$O(a)$-improved Wilson fermions）进行格点QCD计算，并对手征极限、连续极限及无穷体积极限的外推给出了完整的误差预算。特别关注了断开贡献（disconnected contributions）的处理，因其是提取奇异夸克成分的关键要素。

Result: 给出了单态轴矢形状因子$G^{u+d+s}_A(Q^2)$及相关的奇异夸克贡献$G^{s}_A(Q^2)$的格点QCD数值结果。

Conclusion: 结合同位旋矢量与八重态同位旋标量轴矢形状因子的已有测定，本研究提供了跨不同味道通道的核子轴矢结构的全面格点QCD描述。

Abstract: The singlet axial form factor of the nucleon provides essential input for a complete understanding of the nucleon axial structure. Together with the isovector and isoscalar octet channels, in the forward limit it forms the basis for a full flavor decomposition of the proton spin. In this work we present a lattice QCD determination of the singlet axial form factor $G^{u+d+s}_A(Q^2)$ and related strange contribution $G^{s}_A(Q^2)$ using a set of $N_f = 2 + 1$ CLS gauge ensembles with $O(a)$-improved Wilson fermions, with a full error budget for the extrapolation to the chiral, continuum and infinite-volume limits. Particular focus is placed on the treatment of the disconnected contributions, which constitute the crucial element for the extraction of the strange component. Together with determinations of the isovector and isoscalar octet axial form factors, this work provides a comprehensive lattice QCD determination of the nucleon axial structure across different flavor channels.

</details>


### [129] [Lattice fermion formulation via Physics-Informed Neural Networks: Ginsparg-Wilson relation and Overlap fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06022)
*Tatsuhiro Misumi*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于物理信息神经网络（Physics-Informed Neural Networks, PINNs）的机器学习框架来构建格点费米子（lattice fermions），将狄拉克算子（Dirac operator）的构造转化为受物理约束的优化问题，并展示了该框架既能高精度复现现有算子，又能自主发现新的代数字结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 格点费米子构造中，狄拉克算子需同时满足对称性、局域性（locality）和加倍子退耦（doubler-decoupling）等多种物理要求，传统方法依赖解析构造或近似展开，存在灵活性和泛化能力不足的问题。

Method: 将狄拉克算子的构造建模为受物理约束的优化问题，以物理信息神经网络（PINNs）作为求解器：将Ginsparg-Wilson (GW) 关系作为软约束（soft constraint）纳入损失函数进行训练，并在广义多项式Ansatz中通过神经网络自主驱动高阶项归零，从而发现代数字结构。

Result: 训练满足GW关系的神经网络能够高数值精度地复现重叠费米子算子（overlap fermion operator），并学习到有效的符号函数映射（sign-function mapping），无需预设的多项式或有理近似。在广义多项式框架下，网络自主将高阶项推向零，恢复出标准GW关系；改变初始搜索偏向后，同一框架还能找到对应Fujikawa型广义GW关系的不同解。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了机器学习方法不仅可以高精度重现已知的格点费米子构造，还能作为一种代数发现工具，自主探索满足物理约束的算子空间，为格点场论（lattice gauge theory）中的算子设计提供了新的自动化途径。

Abstract: We propose a novel, machine-learning-based framework for constructing lattice fermions using Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs). Our approach treats the formulation of the Dirac operator as an optimization problem guided by physical requirements, such as symmetries, locality and doubler-decoupling conditions. We first demonstrate that, when trained to satisfy the Ginsparg-Wilson (GW) relation as a soft constraint, a neural network reproduces the overlap fermion operator to high numerical accuracy and learns an effective sign-function mapping without explicitly using a prescribed polynomial or rational approximation. Secondly, we extend the framework from operator construction to machine-assisted algebraic discovery. Within a generalized polynomial ansatz, the network autonomously drives higher-order terms to zero and recovers the standard Ginsparg-Wilson relation. Remarkably, by changing the initial search bias, the same framework also finds a distinct solution corresponding to a Fujikawa-type generalized GW relation.

Method: 改编自Y. Foures (Choquet)-Bruhat (1952)的分析技术，在Sobolev型函数空间（Sobolev type spaces）中处理Goursat型拟线性双曲系统的适定性问题。

Conclusion: 本文成功将半线性情形下的Goursat问题推广到超拟线性情形，并为真空Einstein方程在调和规范下的半全局适定性提供了新的理论依据。

Abstract: In this work, we significantly extend the results of D. Houpa, 2006 on the Goursat problem for second-order semi-linear hyperbolic systems to the broader framwork of second-order hyper-quasilinear hyperbolic systems of Goursat type, in which the coefficients of the second-order derivatives depend linearly on the unknown. By adapting techniques inspired by Y. Foures (Choquet)- Bruhat, Acta Mathematica, 1952. we show that in the Sobolev type spaces for the Goursat problem quasilinear hyperbolic of the second order considered, the solution exists and is defined in the vicinity of the meeting characteristic hypersurfaces which carry the initial data. ### [131] [Equidistribution of Eigenfunctions of Quantum Cat Maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06569)
*Robert Koirala*

Main category: math.AP

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证Kim与作者先前数值实验所提示的短周期本征函数的半经典等分布与坐标局域化共存的结论，并与已有文献中观测到的疤痕现象进行对比，以澄清该显式构造族的谱性质。

Method: 对Kim与作者构造的量子猫映射的短周期本征函数进行半经典测度分析，证明其在 $\mathbb{T}^2$ 上等分布；同时通过 $\ell^\infty$-范数的渐近行为证明其对数级大的范数集中于有界个坐标上。

Result: 短周期本征函数在半经典意义下于 $\mathbb{T}^2$ 上等分布；其对数级大的 $\ell^\infty$-范数渐近集中于有界个坐标，表明强坐标局域化与半经典等分布在此族中同时成立。

Conclusion: 该显式族为半经典等分布与强坐标局域化共存提供了严格证明，并与Faure等人报告的短周期疤痕现象形成鲜明对照，拓展了对量子猫映射本征函数微观行为的理解。

Abstract: We prove that the short-period eigenfunctions of quantum cat maps constructed by Kim and the author equidistribute on $\mathbb{T}^2$ in the sense of semiclassical measures. We also show that their logarithmically large $\ell^\infty$-norm is asymptotically concentrated on a bounded number of coordinates. Thus, for this explicit family, strong coordinate localization coexists with semiclassical equidistribution. These results confirm the behavior suggested by earlier numerical evidence of Kim and the author, and contrast with the scarring phenomena for short-period eigenfunctions observed by Faure, Nonnenmacher, and De Bièvre.

### [132] [Simplified approach to extracting nucleon transversity in collinear factorization using near-side energy-energy correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28131)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在双强子碎裂机制（dihadron fragmentation framework）下，利用近侧能量-能量关联函数（near-side energy-energy correlators），在共线因子化（collinear factorization）范围内构造横向自旋可观测量。推导了半举深度非弹散射（SIDIS）和正负电子湮灭过程中横向自旋可观测量的领头阶解析结果。

Result: 领头阶解析结果表明，新可观测量的表达式与共线因子化中提取（非）极化部分子分布函数（unpolarized/polarized PDFs）和单强子碎裂函数（single-hadron fragmentation functions）所用的形式高度相似。针对现有及未来实验设施的动力学条件给出了预言，证实了能量-能量关联函数项目提取横向自旋部分子分布函数（transversity PDF）的可行性。

Conclusion: 所提出的能量-能量关联函数（energy-energy correlators）方法为提取横向自旋部分子分布函数（transversity PDF）提供了一条避开传统建模复杂性的新途径，且在现有及未来实验条件下具备可行性。

Abstract: We develop a novel strategy for accessing the transversity parton distribution function (PDF) of the nucleon within collinear factorization using near-side energy-energy correlators in the dihadron fragmentation framework. We show how this removes the complications of previous approaches that must model either intrinsic parton transverse momentum or resonances in the invariant mass distribution of a final-state dihadron. We present leading-order analytical results for transverse-spin observables in semi-inclusive deep-inelastic scattering and electron-positron annihilation, highlighting their close similarity to the expressions one uses in extracting (un)polarized PDFs and (single-hadron) fragmentation functions in collinear factorization. We make predictions for kinematics relevant for existing and future facilities that demonstrate the feasibility of an energy-energy correlator program in extracting the transversity PDF.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过夸克味改变算符（flavor-changing operator）$(\bar{s}γ_μd)(\barχγ^μχ)$ 分析暗物质产生，考虑再加热温度低于QCD crossover时，通过K介子衰变$K\toπχ\barχ$和散射$Kπ\toχ\barχ$过程生成暗物质丰度。

Result: 低再加热温度下，玻尔兹曼抑制（Boltzmann suppression）导致K介子丰度下降，需更大耦合常数以补偿；该物理机制与NA62、KOTO及KOTO II实验对稀有K介子衰变$K^+\toπ^+χ\barχ$和$K_L\toπ^0χ\barχ$的搜索直接关联。

Abstract: We investigate freeze-in production of light dark matter through the quark flavor-changing operator $(\bar{s}γ_μd)(\barχγ^μχ)$ in a low-reheating cosmology. For reheating temperatures below the QCD crossover, kaon decays and scatterings generate the dark matter abundance through $K\toπχ\barχ$ and $Kπ\toχ\barχ$. The same interaction induces the rare kaon decays $K^+\toπ^+χ\barχ$ and $K_L\toπ^0χ\barχ$. This links the freeze-in relic abundance to searches at NA62, KOTO, and KOTO II. We find that lower reheating temperatures require larger couplings to compensate for the Boltzmann-suppressed kaon abundance, making kaon-driven freeze-in dark matter testable at rare kaon decay experiments.

### [134] [The temporal distribution of SN1987A neutrino events](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06401)
*Riccardo Maria Bozza,Vigilante di Risi,Veronica Oliviero,Giulia Ricciardi,Francesco Vissani*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过引入相对时间偏移（RTO）方法，将SN1987A中微子数据的时间精度提升至亚秒级，实现了Kamiokande-II、Baksan与IMB探测器的时间轴精确对齐。分析表明Baksan时间戳需提前30.4秒、Kamiokande-II需延迟约6.4秒，并基于统一时间线对首个Kamiokande-II事件的中子化爆（neutronization burst）起源进行检验，结果支持吸积相电子反中微子解释，似然比约为3–6，证实标准解释（仅探测到逆β衰变事件）并建立了超新星中微子时间学的最严格约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SN1987A中微子数据的解释长期受到显著绝对时间不确定性（absolute timing uncertainties）以及角分布中已知张力的阻碍，需要更精确的时间对齐方法来解决这些核心问题。

Method: 首次使用相对时间偏移（relative time offset, RTO）方法，对Kamiokande-II和Baksan数据与IMB时钟进行定量高精度对齐；通过卡方分析（chi-square analysis）确定各探测器的时间校正量。

Result: Baksan绝对时间戳需要提前30.4秒，Kamiokande-II需要延迟约6.4秒，时间不确定度降低两个数量级至亚秒级（sub-second level）。首个Kamiokande-II事件的中子化爆起源被排除，吸积相（accretion phase）电子反中微子起源的似然比（likelihood ratio）为3–6（依赖于具体MSW振荡情景）。

Conclusion: 分析结果支持标准解释——即仅探测到逆β衰变（inverse beta decay）事件；该框架提供了迄今对SN1987A时间学（chronology）最严格的约束，并为未来银河系超新星观测建立了精度基准。

Abstract: The interpretation of the SN1987A neutrino data continues to be hindered by significant absolute timing uncertainties and a well-known tension in the angular distributions. We perform a quantitative, high-precision alignment of the Kamiokande-II and Baksan data with the IMB clock, using for the first time the relative time offset (RTO) and reducing the temporal uncertainty by two orders of magnitude to the sub-second level. The chi-square analysis shows that Baksan's absolute timestamps require an advancement of 30.4 s, while those of Kamiokande-II require a delay of about 6.4 s. The knowledge of the unified timeline provides a necessary and rigorous basis for testing whether the first Kamiokande-II event arose from the neutronization burst - a possibility motivated by its angular properties. Our analysis favors an accretion phase electron anti-neutrino origin over a neutronization-burst origin, with a likelihood ratio of 3-6, depending on the specific MSW oscillation scenario. This result corroborates the standard interpretation - that only inverse beta decay events were detected. Our framework yields the most stringent constraints to date on the SN1987A chronology and establishes a precision benchmark for future Galactic supernova observations.

</details>


### [135] [Probing unknown nonperturbative effects in $b \to s \ell\ell$ with inclusive and exclusive observables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06567)
*P. Alvarez-Cartelle,B. Capdevila,E. Lunghi,J. Matias*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文从新的视角重新审视了b→sμμ衰变中观测到的分支比系统偏差的起源，通过对比包含衰变（inclusive decay）与遍举衰变（exclusive decay）对非微扰贡献的不同敏感度，构造了可区分新物理（New Physics）与恒定的强子贡献（constant hadronic contribution）的观测量，并基于现有数据给出了倾向于新物理解释的初步证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在解决粒子物理中的一个长期问题：b→sμμ跃迁（$b\to s μμ$ transition）中所有分支比（branching ratios）的系统性亏损，究竟源于新物理（New Physics），还是某种未知的、普适的强子贡献（universal hadronic contribution）在模仿新物理的信号。

Method: 利用非微扰贡献（non-perturbative contributions，尤其是c̄c圈）对包含衰变（inclusive decay）$B\to X_s \ell\ell$和遍举衰变（exclusive decay）$B\to K^{(*)}\ell\ell$的不同影响——包含衰变中的可因子化贡献（factorizable contributions）可由$e^+e^-\to \mathrm{hadrons}$数据精确确定，而遍举衰变中可能存在额外的迷人企鹅贡献（charming-penguin effects）——构造了排除率与包含率之比（ratios of exclusive to inclusive modes）作为区分新物理与恒定强子贡献的观测量，并在高$q^2$区域对包含测量值与遍举通道之和进行了互补性比较。

Result: 基于现有数据对新观测量的初步评估显示，结果倾向于新物理解释（preference for the New Physics interpretation）；高$q^2$下的互补性比较同样不支持恒定强子贡献的解释。

Conclusion: 本文提出的新观测量可直接由LHCb实验测量，无需借助B工厂的$J/ψK^{(*)}$分支比进行归一化（normalisation），并可结合未来LHCb与Belle II的测量数据进一步检验新物理与强子贡献两种可能性。

Abstract: In this paper we revisit, from a different perspective, a long-standing question: ``Is the systematic deficit observed in all branching ratios mediated by a $b\to s μμ$ transition due to New Physics, or to a hypothetical constant unknown universal hadronic contribution that mimics New Physics?'' The key observation that allows us to distinguish between these two possibilities is that non-perturbative contributions associated with $c\bar c$ loops affect inclusive $B\to X_s \ell\ell$ and exclusive $B\to K^{(*)}\ell\ell$ modes differently. In inclusive decays, factorizable contributions are exactly determined from data on $e^+e^-\to \mathrm{hadrons}$, while non-factorizable corrections are described by resolved-photon contributions at low $q^2$ and by local power corrections at high $q^2$. In exclusive decays, by contrast, hypothetical charming-penguin effects, beyond those already included in current uncertainty estimates, could appear, in a worst-case scenario, as a constant, universal contribution that it seems, in principle, indistinguishable from genuine New Physics. We identify two observables, constructed from ratios of exclusive to inclusive modes, that can discriminate between a New Physics contribution and a constant hadronic contribution. Moreover, these ratios can be measured directly by LHCb, as they do not require any normalisation to $J/ψK^{(*)}$ branching fractions from B factories. A preliminary evaluation of these observables with present data shows some preference for the New Physics interpretation. In a complementary test, a comparison between inclusive measurements and the corresponding sum of exclusive modes at high $q^2$ similarly disfavours an explanation based on a constant hadronic contribution. Finally, we provide projections for the new observables based on expected LHCb and Belle II measurements in the near future.

</details>


### [136] [Nonthermal leptogenesis via cosmological gravitational particle production is tested by inflationary gravitational waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05304)
*Tammi Chowdhury,Leah Jenks,Edward W. Kolb,Andrew J. Long,Evan McDonough*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究宇宙暴胀与跷跷板模型中右手中微子产生之间的尺度巧合关系，以解释观测到的宇宙重子不对称性。

Method: 通过分析暴胀模型与右手中微子产生之间的物理关联，并结合下一代宇宙微波背景（CMB）实验的检验能力，构建可同时解释重子不对称性的理论框架。

Result: 暴胀模型能够产生足够丰度的右手中微子，从而解释观测到的宇宙重子不对称性；该模型产生的引力波信号可作为实验检验的探针。

Conclusion: 暴胀与右手中微子产生之间存在有意义的尺度重合，该模型可通过下一代CMB实验及引力波信号得到检验。

Abstract: We explore the coincidence of scales between cosmic inflation and right-handed neutrinos in seesaw models. We show that inflation models, which will be tested by next-generation CMB experiments, can produce right-handed neutrinos in sufficient abundance to explain the observed baryon asymmetry of the universe. The model can be tested by gravitational wave signatures from cosmic inflation and particle production.

</details>


### [137] [On the equivalence of unitarization prescriptions for the Sommerfeld enhancement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05309)
*Barry E. Cimring,Tracy R. Slatyer*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有长程相互作用的自相互作用暗物质（self-interacting dark matter）在低速度下由Sommerfeld效应（Sommerfeld effect）导致的湮灭增强，重点探讨了该增强在近零能共振（near-zero-energy resonances）处可能违反幺正性（unitarity）的问题。通过对比多种正则化方案，发现这些方案在领头阶上一致，并提出了一个与正则化无关（regulator-independent）的幺正化（unitarization）方案，可推广至多态系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自相互作用暗物质在低速度下的Sommerfeld增强在参数空间中的近零能共振点处会导致标准计算结果违反幺正性（unitarity）。近期提出的多种正则化方案——有的引入显式紫外（UV）标度，有的则不引入——引发了这些方案是否一致的疑问，亟需系统比较与统一。

Method: 本文对比了多种已提出的正则化（regulation）方案，包括依赖截断（cutoff-dependent）与不依赖截断的方法，通过解析和数值分析考察其在幺正性修正较大时的行为。在此基础上，推导出一个与正则化无关的幺正化（unitarization）方案，该方案仅使用标准增强因子（standard enhancement factor）、硬湮灭振幅（hard annihilation amplitude）和长程势中的散射S矩阵（S-matrix）来表达修正后的增强。

Result: 即使在名义上依赖截断的方法中，正则化后的Sommerfeld增强截面（cross sections）对紫外（UV）正则化子（regulator）的依赖性极弱，近似独立；当幺正性保持修正（unitarity-preserving corrections）较大时，各种正则化方案在领头阶（leading order）上一致。

Conclusion: 本文给出了一种与正则化无关的幺正化方案，该方案适用于多态系统（multi-state systems），修正后的增强因子可由标准增强因子、硬湮灭振幅以及长程势中的散射S矩阵直接表达，为暗物质Sommerfeld效应的自洽计算提供了统一框架。

Abstract: The annihilation of self-interacting dark matter with long-range interactions can be significantly enhanced at low velocities through the Sommerfeld effect. At special points in parameter space, where near-zero-energy resonances exist in the spectrum of the theory, the standard calculation of this enhancement appears to violate unitarity. Recently, several approaches have been proposed to regulate this behavior, some introducing explicit ultraviolet (UV) scales and others not, raising the question of whether these prescriptions are consistent. In this paper, we compare these approaches and show that even in nominally cutoff-dependent methods, the regulated Sommerfeld-enhanced cross sections are independent of the UV regulator to a good approximation, and that when the unitarity-preserving corrections are large, the regulation schemes coincide to leading order. We use these insights to write down a regulator-independent prescription for unitarization applicable to multi-state systems, where the modified enhancement can be written solely in terms of the standard enhancement factor, the hard annihilation amplitude, and the $S$-matrix for scattering in the long-range potential.

### [138] [First next-to-next-to-leading-order extraction of fragmentation functions for Lambda hyperons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05314)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于蒙特卡洛抽样和神经网络（neural network）参数化的统计框架，在NNLO精度下对共线非极化碎裂函数进行全局拟合。数据来源包括单举电子-正电子湮灭（single-inclusive electron-positron annihilation）以及中性流和带电电流半单举深度非弹性散射（semi-inclusive deep-inelastic scattering）。

Result: 获得了包含七个独立部分子味（parton flavours）的碎裂函数集，首次实现了价夸克（valence-quark）分布的独立确定。该分析为奇异重子（strange baryons）的强子化机制提供了新见解。

Conclusion: MAPFF1.0_Lambda为未来关于Λ超子碎裂函数的唯象学和实验研究建立了基线，并深化了对奇异重子强子化过程的理解。

Abstract: We present MAPFF1.0_Lambda, the first global analysis at next-to-next-to-leading order in perturbative QCD of the collinear unpolarised fragmentation functions of Lambda hyperons. The fit is based on data from single-inclusive electron-positron annihilation, and from both neutral-current and -- for the first time -- charged-current semi-inclusive deep-inelastic scattering. We have adopted a statistical framework based on Monte Carlo sampling and parametrised fragmentation functions in terms of a neural network. The fragmentation function set comprises a total of seven independent parton flavours, allowing for the first independent determination of valence-quark distributions. Our analysis offers new insights into the hadronisation mechanism of strange baryons and establishes a baseline for future phenomenological and experimental investigations.

### [139] [All-loop four-quark Bethe-Salpeter kernel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05349)
*Piotr Bargiela*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用现代散射振幅方法，在大数量夸克风味近似（large number of quark flavors approximation）的次领头阶，解析计算了无质量量子色动力学（Quantum Chromodynamics, QCD）中四夸克Bethe-Salpeter核的全圈裸微扰部分，并通过积分约化和直接积分技术得到主积分基与广义多对数函数结果，同时提供了胶子和夸克传播子，为非微扰构造和未来唯象应用奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Dyson-Schwinger方程（Dyson-Schwinger equations）框架下，截断方案的选择存在歧义性。本文旨在通过大N_f近似下全圈水平的解析计算，提供一种系统可改进且保持渐近自由（asymptotic freedom）的替代路径，从而避免截断方案的歧义。

Method: 采用现代散射振幅方法，在大数量夸克风味近似的次领头阶（subleading order）进行计算；利用积分约化（Integration-By-Parts reduction）技术将洛伦兹标量费曼积分（Lorentz scalar Feynman integrals）约化至最小主积分基（minimal Master Integral basis），并通过直接积分法将其表达为广义多对数函数（Generalized Polylogarithms）。

Result: 解析计算了四夸克Bethe-Salpeter核（Bethe-Salpeter kernel）的全圈（all-loop）裸微扰部分；作为副产品，同时给出了胶子传播子（gluon propagator）和夸克传播子（quark propagator）的结果。

Conclusion: 该计算路径具有系统可改进性，且保持了渐近自由；未来可向非微扰形式化（nonperturbative formulation）方向拓展，并有望应用于唯象学（phenomenology）研究。

Abstract: We analytically calculate the all-loop bare perturbative part of the four-quark Bethe-Salpeter kernel using modern scattering amplitude methods. We work to subleading order in the large number of quark flavors approximation of massless Quantum Chromodynamics, which simultaneously makes an all-loop calculation feasible, is systematically improvable, and preserves asymptotic freedom. It also allows for avoiding the ambiguity of choosing a truncation scheme in Dyson-Schwinger equations. We exploit state-of-the-art methods in Integration-By-Parts reduction of Lorentz scalar Feynman integrals into a minimal Master Integral basis, and direct integration into Generalized Polylogarithms. As a byproduct of our calculation, we also provide the result for the gluon and quark propagators. We discuss a path towards nonperturbative formulation and potential future phenomenological applications.

### [140] [Squeezed Vibrational States in Superfluid Helium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05345)

Method: 通过观测超流氦中由超快激光诱导的双折射振荡（birefringence oscillations），分解其响应为各振动模式的叠加，并分析初始相位与多模干涉的关系。

Conclusion: 该研究首次为超流氦中准粒子对的各向异性量子压缩提供了直接实验证据，并指出多模干涉是理解初始相位及超快响应叠加上位机制的关键。

Abstract: Ultrafast birefringence oscillations observed in superfluid helium provide evidence for anisotropic quantum squeezing of quasiparticle pairs. The measured response is a superposition of contributions from all vibrational modes, with dominant contributions from rotons, maxons, and Pitaevskii's plateau. The nonzero initial phase follows naturally from multimode interference.

### [141] [Exact theory of plasmon reflection and transmission in partially gated two-dimensional system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05504)
*I. M. Moiseenko,D. A. Svintsov*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文发展了一套等离子体激元（plasmon）在二维电子系统（2DES）有栅与无栅区域边界处散射的精确理论。利用Wiener-Hopf技术推导了反射与透射系数的解析表达式，全面考虑了栅极边缘的衰减场（evanescent field）和向自由空间电磁波的辐射损失。结果表明：在非推迟极限（non-retarded limit）且栅极-2DES间距较小时，反射等离子体激元主导总电场，辐射损失可忽略；反射与透射系数的幅值和相位对间距与电导率存在复杂依赖关系。该工作为基于2DES的可调等离子体激元晶体在太赫兹检测与调制中的应用提供了严格理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论对等离子体激元在二维电子系统有栅/无栅边界处的散射行为缺乏精确描述，特别是对栅极边缘衰减场与辐射损失的完整处理尚属空白，限制了可调等离子体激元晶体（tunable plasmonic crystals）的建模。

Method: 运用Wiener-Hopf技术（Wiener-Hopf technique）推导了等离子体激元从界面两侧入射时的复数反射系数与透射系数的解析表达式，并完整纳入栅极边缘衰减场与自由空间电磁波辐射损失。

Result: 在非推迟极限且栅极-2DES间距较小时，反射等离子体激元主导总电场，辐射损失可忽略；反射与透射系数的幅值和相位依赖于2DES-栅极间距与2DES电导率，且对来自两侧的入射呈现复杂关系。

Conclusion: 该严格理论为基于二维电子系统的可调等离子体激元晶体在太赫兹检测与调制（terahertz detection and modulation）中的应用提供了坚实基础。

Abstract: We develop an exact theory of plasmon scattering at the boundary between gated and ungated regions of a two-dimensional electron system (2DES). Using the Wiener-Hopf technique, we derive analytical expressions for the complex reflection and transmission coefficients of plasmons incident from both sides of the interface. The theory fully accounts for evanescent fields at the gate edge and radiative losses into free-space electromagnetic waves. In the non-retarded limit and for small gate-2DES separation, the reflected plasmon dominates the total electric field, while radiative losses are negligible when plasmon scattering. The amplitudes and phases of the reflection and transmission coefficients for plasmons incident from both sides have a complex dependence from 2DES-gate separation and conductivity of 2DES. Our results provide a rigorous foundation for modeling tunable plasmonic crystals based on 2DES for terahertz detection and modulation.

### [142] [The Interplay of Data Structure and Imbalance in the Learning Dynamics of Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06367)
*Flavio Nicoletti,Chenxiao Ma,Enrico Ventura,Luca Saglietti,Stefano Sarao Mannelli*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文通过高维分析框架研究扩散模型（diffusion model）中类别依赖的学习动态，揭示了类别方差决定学习顺序、质心几何起次要作用、采样不平衡可逆转顺序并导致少数类延迟特化（delayed speciation）的层次机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实世界数据集存在固有的异质性（heterogeneity），但按类别的结构差异和采样不平衡如何塑造扩散模型的训练动态——以及可能加剧其中不公平性——仍缺乏理解。现有理论假设数据同质（homogeneous），未考虑类别不平衡和异质性对学习动态的重塑作用。

Method: 构建高维分析框架，研究基于分数的扩散模型（score-based diffusion model）中的类别依赖学习。分析训练于高斯混合（Gaussian mixture）数据上的随机特征模型（random-features model），推导特征协方差谱（feature-covariance spectrum）以刻画每类的泛化和记忆时间。

Result: 揭示了控制学习动态的显式层次：类别方差（class variance）是学习顺序的首要决定因素，稳定偏好高方差类别；质心几何（centroid geometry）仅起次要作用。采样不平衡作为调节因子可逆转该顺序，在强不平衡下迫使少数类在反向扩散中获得独特且延迟的特化时间（speciation time）。扩散模型可能在记忆某些类的同时，其他类仍未能充分学习。

Conclusion: 理论预测通过在Fashion MNIST上训练的U-Net模型得到实证验证。

Abstract: Real-world datasets are inherently heterogeneous, yet how per-class structural differences and sampling imbalance shape the training dynamics of diffusion models-and potentially exacerbate disparities-remains poorly understood. While models typically transition from an initial phase of generalization to memorizing the training set, existing theory assumes homogeneous data, leaving open how class imbalance and heterogeneity reshape these dynamics. In this work, we develop a high-dimensional analytical framework to study class-dependent learning in score-based diffusion models. Analyzing a random-features model trained on Gaussian mixtures, we derive the feature-covariance spectrum to characterize per-class generalization and memorization times. We reveal the explicit hierarchy governing these dynamics: class variance is the primary determinant of learning order-consistently favoring higher-variance classes-while centroid geometry plays a secondary role. Sampling imbalance acts as a modulator that can reverse this ordering and, under strong imbalance, forces minority classes to acquire distinct, delayed speciation times during backward diffusion. Together, these results suggest that diffusion models can memorize some classes while others remain insufficiently learned. We validate our theoretical predictions empirically using U-Net models trained on Fashion MNIST.

</details>

### [143] [Higher-order interactions in ecology can be hidden in plain sight](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06301)
*Violeta Calleja-Solanas,Santiago Lamata-Otín,Carlos Gómez-Ambrosi,Jesús Gómez-Gardeñes,Sandro Meloni*

Main category: q-bio.PE

TL;DR: 该研究指出，高阶Lotka-Volterra动力学在某些场景下可被有效配对模型精确重现，因此高阶相互作用无法仅从时间序列数据中推断；此外，不同的相互作用机制可能生成几乎无法区分的动力学，导致机械可识别性问题，从而产生准确但具有误导性的生态学解释。研究强调需要结合时间序列数据以外的生态信息来可靠推断相互作用结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然高阶相互作用（higher-order interactions）被越来越认为是生态动力学（ecological dynamics）的关键组成部分，但目前尚不清楚能否仅通过时间序列数据（time-series data）可靠地推断出这些相互作用的存在。

Method: 研究通过比较高阶Lotka-Volterra动力学（higher-order Lotka-Volterra dynamics）与拟合自相同丰度时间序列的有效配对模型（effective pairwise models）之间的动力学表现，分析两者在特定场景下是否可相互重现。

Result: 高阶Lotka-Volterra动力学在某些场景下可被有效配对模型准确重现；不同的相互作用机制（interaction mechanisms）可生成几乎无法区分的动力学，即存在机械可识别性（mechanistic identifiability）的根本问题。

Conclusion: 高阶相互作用无法仅从时间序列数据中可靠推断；需要结合时间序列数据以外的额外生态信息（additional ecological information）来可靠推断相互作用结构（interaction structure），否则可能得出准确但具有误导性（accurate yet misleading）的生态学解释。

Abstract: Higher-order interactions are increasingly recognized as a key component of ecological dynamics. However, we show that higher-order Lotka-Volterra dynamics can, in some scenarios, be accurately reproduced by effective pairwise models fitted to the same abundance time series. Consequently, higher-order interactions cannot, in general, be inferred from time-series data alone. We further identify a fundamental problem of mechanistic identifiability, whereby distinct interaction mechanisms generate nearly indistinguishable dynamics, potentially leading to accurate yet misleading ecological interpretations. Our results highlight the need to complement time-series data with additional ecological information to infer interaction structure reliably.

### [144] [Dynamics and Radiative Signatures of Accretion Flows onto a Kerr-like Wormhole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04631)
*Jing-ze Xia,Hong-xuan Jiang,Cheng Liu,Yosuke Mizuno*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过广义相对论磁流体动力学（GRMHD）模拟和广义相对论辐射输运（GRRT）计算，研究了吸积流在类Kerr虫洞（Kerr-like wormhole）上的动力学与成像特征，发现喉部附近发射可在图像中占主导，并在光变曲线中产生准周期性调制，为通过视界尺度观测检验这类奇特致密天体提供了可检验的特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虫洞（wormhole）作为黑洞的一种理论替代模型，为在强引力场中通过视界尺度图像进行观测检验提供了潜在途径。本文旨在通过数值模拟探究类Kerr虫洞的吸积与成像特征，以区分其与标准克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole）的观测差异。

Method: 采用Kerr黑弹度规（Kerr black-bounce metric，喉部参数$\ell = 2.5\,\rm M$），利用二维与三维GRMHD模拟初始化一个磁化几何厚环（magnetized geometrically thick torus）位于虫洞一侧入口，另一侧初始无气体。随后基于GRMHD结果，使用RAPTOR程序在230 GHz进行光线追踪（ray-tracing）成像，并通过高阶光子路径分析视界尺度图像结构。

Result: 自旋参数通过参考系拖曳效应（frame-dragging effects）影响虫洞两侧的动力学性质。GRRT计算显示，喉部附近发射可在图像中占主导，这与克尔黑洞情况不同；该发射提供信号的变分成份，并在光变曲线中引入清晰的准周期性调制（quasi-periodic modulation）。

Conclusion: 上述特征可通过视界尺度观测来确认或排除这类奇特致密天体（exotic compact objects），为区分虫洞与标准黑洞提供了潜在的观测可检验标志。

Abstract: Wormholes are a hypothetical object that connects disparate points in spacetime. It is a theoretically well-motivated black hole alternative and offers a potential observationally testable arena for probing strong-field gravity with horizon-scale images. We perform general relativistic magnetohydrodynamic (GRMHD) simulations and general relativistic radiative transfer (GRRT) calculations of accretion flows onto a Kerr-like wormhole. Adopting a Kerr black-bounce metric with a fixed throat parameter $\ell = 2.5\,\rm M$, we explore the effects of spin using both two- and three-dimensional simulations. The accretion flow is initialized as a magnetized geometrically thick torus near one mouth of the wormhole, while the opposite mouth is initially gas-free. We find that the spin parameter influences the dynamical properties on both sides of the wormhole through the frame-dragging effects. Based on the GRMHD results, we compute ray-traced images at $230\,\mathrm{GHz}$ using \texttt{RAPTOR}, and analyze the horizon-scale image structure through higher-order photon trajectories. Our GRRT calculations show that emissions originating from the immediate vicinity of the throat can dominate, in contrast to the case of a Kerr black hole. It provides the variable component of the signal and imprints a clear quasi-periodic modulation in the light curves. These properties would be useful to either confirm or rule out such exotic compact objects through horizon-scale observations.

</details>


### [145] [No model-independent evidence for a peak in binary black hole spin (mis)alignments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05300)
*Noah E. Wolfe,Salvatore Vitale,Michael Zevin*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究利用LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA第四次引力波瞬变目录的数据分析黑洞自旋倾角（spin tilt）分布，发现自旋倾角峰值缺乏统计显著性和模型独立性，并确认了自旋大小与质量之间的稳健相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞自旋-轨道错位程度（即倾角）是区分孤立双星形成、动力学环境形成以及层级三体（hierarchical triple）形成等不同双星形成机制的重要诊断工具。然而，由于单事件对倾角的约束较差，以及模型设定错误（model misspecification）、数值方差和泊松方差（Poisson variance）的影响，稳健的群体级自旋倾角测量十分困难。

Method: 分析了第四次LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA引力波瞬变目录（gravitational-wave transient catalog）的数据，检验不同黑洞质量下是否有优先自旋取向；同时采用补充方法，在固定质量标度（fixed mass scales）上测量自旋大小和自旋倾角分布。

Result: 发现自旋倾角分布中的峰值并不具有统计显著性（statistically significant）且不具有模型独立性（model independent）。未发现质量与自旋倾角之间存在可靠的相关性，但确认了自旋大小（spin magnitude）与质量之间存在稳健的相关性，这与近期其他分析结果一致。

Conclusion: 当前数据无法基于自旋倾角性质可靠地识别子群体；自旋大小与质量的相关性得到进一步确认，为理解黑洞双星的形成与演化提供了约束。

Abstract: The degree of black-hole spin-orbit misalignment ("tilts") in the astrophysical population could be a powerful diagnostic to distinguish between binary formation in isolation, in dynamical environments, or in hierarchical triples. However, robust population-level spin tilt measurements are complicated by model misspecification as well as numerical and Poisson variance, ultimately owing to poor single-event constraints on tilts. Motivated by reports of a possible peak in the spin tilt distribution, we analyze the fourth LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA gravitational-wave transient catalog to test for preferred spin orientations at different black hole masses. We find that a peak in spin tilts is not statistically significant nor model independent. Since the data cannot be used to reliably identify subpopulations based on their spin tilt properties, we also consider a complementary approach: measuring the spin magnitude and tilt distributions at fixed mass scales. We find no confident correlation between mass and spin tilt, but we do confirm a confident correlation between spin magnitude and mass, corroborating recent analyses.

### [146] [Gravitational Lensing of Gravitational Waves from Astrophysical Sources: Theory, Detection, and Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06321)
*Zhiwei Chen,Youjun Lu*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文综述了引力波透镜效应（gravitational wave lensing），涵盖其理论框架（几何光学与波动光学）、探测率预测、搜索策略以及在天体物理和宇宙学中的应用前景，包括约束暗物质、哈勃常数和其他宇宙学参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波透镜效应能够提供传统电磁波透镜无法获取的信息，有望成为研究基础物理和宇宙学的强有力探针。本文旨在系统梳理该领域的最新进展，为未来的观测与理论研究提供参考。

Method: 基于理论分析，将引力波透镜分为几何光学（geometric optics）和波动光学（wave optics）两个区间：前者产生多像、时间延迟和放大效应；后者导致频率依赖的波形调制。识别方法包括事件对之间的参数重叠以及区别于非透镜信号的特征调制。

Result: 探测率依赖于源和透镜的红移及质量分布，未来观测台站有良好的探测前景。已确认的透镜引力波事件可有效约束暗物质（dark matter）、透镜结构、哈勃常数（Hubble constant）及其他宇宙学参数。

Conclusion: 引力波透镜效应是极具潜力的研究工具，未来观测有望在天体物理和宇宙学领域取得重要突破。本文为后续的探测策略和物理应用提供了全面的理论基础和前景展望。

Abstract: Gravitational waves (GWs) from distant sources such as inspiralling and merging stellar-mass compact binaries, intermediate-mass and supermassive-binary-black-hole can be gravitationally lensed by intervening objects, ranging from stars and primordial black holes to galaxies and clusters. Depending on the GW wavelength relative to the lens scale, lensing occurs in two regimes: geometric optics, producing multiple images with time delays and magnifications, and wave optics, resulting in frequency-dependent waveform modulations. Lensed signals are identified via parameter overlap between event pairs or characteristic frequency-dependent modulations that distinguish them from unlensed signals. Detection rates depend on the redshift and mass distributions of sources and lenses, with promising prospects for future observatories. Once confirmed, lensed GWs will be powerful probes of fundamental physics and cosmology: they can constrain dark matter, lensing structures, the Hubble constant, and other cosmological parameters. In this review, we provide a concise overview of GW lensing, covering the theoretical framework, predicted detection rates, search strategies, and applications. We conclude with prospects and future directions for observing and exploiting lensed astrophysical GW events.

### [147] [Local droplet etching-assisted quantum dot epitaxy for telecom C-band quantum light emitters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05956)

Conclusion: LDE 方法在新材料体系集成方面具有多功能性，为实现具有可调发射性质的量子光源的可扩展制备奠定了基础。

Abstract: Significant progress in quantum light sources for quantum communication applications requires reproducible and symmetric quantum emitters acting as single-photon sources capable of generating entangled photons on demand at specific telecom wavelengths. Here, we propose telecom-emitting epitaxial quantum dots (QDs) fabricated using the local droplet etching (LDE) approach. Precise numerical modeling, combining multiband $\boldsymbol{k} \cdot \boldsymbol{p}$ and configuration-interaction methods, supports the optical characterization and identifies thermal excitation pathways that explain the persistence of emission up to liquid-nitrogen temperatures. These results highlight the versatility of the LDE approach for integrating new material systems and pave the way toward scalable fabrication of quantum light sources with tailored emission properties.

### [148] [Elastic and structural anisotropy in silica thin films for gravitational-wave detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06282)
*Brenda Bracco,Michele Magnozzi,Stefano Colace,Maurizio Canepa,Giulio Favaro,Marco Bazzan,Massimo Granata,David Hofman,Alessandro Di Michele,Laura Silenzi,Gianpietro Cagnoli,Giovanni Carlotti,Paola Sassi,Silvia Corezzi*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文利用布里渊光散射（Brillouin light scattering, BLS）首次实验证明，离子束溅射沉积的SiO2薄膜具有柱状弹性对称性（cylindrical elastic symmetry），即面内各向同性但沿膜法线方向存在约6%的压缩各向异性。该各向异性在500°C热处理后不变，但在900°C下几乎消除；红外反射实验揭示了沿生长轴的氧结构非均匀性。研究表明，通过高温热处理恢复各向同性可软化材料、促进面外膨胀并平滑结构非均匀性，可能对降低热噪声（thermal noise）起关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波探测器中反射镜镀层的热噪声（thermal noise）对材料弹性性质高度敏感，但现有数据分析和理论模型均假设材料是均匀且各向同性的（homogeneous and isotropic），这一假设从未经过实验验证。本文旨在首次实验检验离子束溅射（ion-beam-sputtered, IBS）SiO2薄膜的弹性对称性，澄清其是否真正各向同性，并为未来低热噪声镀层设计提供依据。

Method: 采用布里渊光散射（Brillouin light scattering, BLS）技术直接测量材料在GHz频率下的弹性常数实部（real part），以此检测弹性对称性。同时结合红外反射率实验，揭示沿生长轴方向桥接氧（bridging oxygen）与非桥接氧（non-bridging oxygen）结构的分布非均匀性，以验证各向异性的结构起源。

Result: IBS-SiO2薄膜具有柱状弹性对称性（cylindrical elastic symmetry），面内各向同性但沿膜法线方向存在约6%的压缩各向异性。该各向异性在500°C、10小时热处理后保持不变，但在900°C下几乎完全消除。BLS测得的数据表明，在kHz-GHz频率范围内力学弛豫（mechanical relaxation）的贡献可忽略，因此BLS可替代传统对各向异性不敏感的测量方法获取低频弹性性质。

Conclusion: 通过高温热处理（900°C）恢复各向同性——软化材料、实现超过7%的面外膨胀并平滑结构非均匀性——可能是降低热噪声的关键途径。本研究作为概念验证（proof-of-concept），为未来更广泛镀层材料的设计提供了重要参考，超越了对二氧化硅单种材料的理解。

Abstract: The thermal noise of mirror coatings for gravitational-wave detectors critically depends on the elastic properties of the constituent materials. Data analyses and theoretical models typically assume each material is homogeneous and isotropic, but isotropy has never been explicitly verified. Using Brillouin light scattering (BLS), we demonstrate for the first time that ion-beam-sputtered SiO2 -- a material still viable for future mirror coatings -- exhibits cylindrical elastic symmetry, with in-plane isotropy but a notable 6% compressive anisotropy along the film normal. This anisotropy remains unchanged after the post-deposition heat treatment currently used in ground-based detectors (500 $^\circ$C, 10 h) but is nearly eliminated at 900 $^\circ$C. Infrared reflectivity experiments support these findings by directly revealing heterogeneities in the distribution of bridging and non-bridging oxygen structures along the growth axis. While BLS measures the real part of the elastic constants at GHz frequencies, the data reveal negligible contributions from mechanical relaxations in the kHz-GHz range, making BLS a valid substitute for low-frequency properties obtained from standard anisotropy-insensitive techniques. Our results highlight that restoring isotropy through heat treatment -- by softening the material, enabling more than 7% out-of-plane expansion, and smoothing out structural heterogeneities -- may play a key role in reducing thermal noise. This proof-of-concept study extends beyond silica, providing critical insights for the design of future coatings.

### [149] [Breakdown of Emergent Chiral Order and Defect Chaos in Nonreciprocal Flocks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05448)

TL;DR: 二维非互易混合群落中手性有序性在拓扑缺陷增殖下普遍不稳定，导致时空混沌和有限关联长度，而关联长度在非互易性消失时发散。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验非互易混合系统中手性有序性（chiral order）的稳定性，揭示其在二维系统中的普适行为。

Method: 结合大规模基于智能体的模拟（agent-based simulations）与粗粒化连续描述（coarse-grained continuum description）。

Result: 反称耦合（antisymmetric couplings）产生的旋转手性态（rotating chiral states）被拓扑缺陷（topological defects）的增殖破坏，导致时空混沌；关联长度（correlation length）在非互易性（nonreciprocity）消失时发散；低于该截止尺度时，密度和取向有序涨落呈现标度不变但具有非普适指数（nonuniversal exponents）。

Conclusion: 密度与有序性之间的耦合导致拓扑缺陷成为持续的非线性涨落源，这是该非普适行为的成因。

Abstract: We show that chiral order in two-dimensional nonreciprocal flocking mixtures is generically unstable. Combining large-scale agent-based simulations with a coarse-grained continuum description, we demonstrate that rotating chiral states emerging from antisymmetric couplings are destroyed by the proliferation of topological defects. The resulting dynamics is spatiotemporally chaotic and characterized by a finite correlation length that diverges as nonreciprocity vanishes. On length scales below this cutoff, density and orientational order fluctuations remain scale-free, but the associated scaling exhibits nonuniversal exponents. We attribute this atypical behavior to the coupling between density and order, which causes topological defects to act as persistent sources of nonlinear fluctuations.

### [150] [Solvent-induced memory effects in a model electrolyte](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06293)
*Sleeba Varghese,Benjamin Rotenberg,Pierre Illien*

Method: 将离子和溶剂分子描述为相互作用的布朗粒子，运用随机密度泛函理论推导出离子电荷密度满足的广义朗之万方程，明确纳入溶剂介导的记忆效应。

Result: 在快溶剂与慢离子动力学的明确时间尺度分离条件下，得到了动态电荷结构因子（dynamical charge structure factors）的简洁解析表达式，并通过布朗动力学（BD）模拟验证。对于慢溶剂情形，预测了离子动力学中出现两步弛豫现象。

Conclusion: 该工作为离子-溶剂动力学提供了一种介观层次（mesoscopic approach）的理论方法，并为研究电解质中涨落诱发现象（fluctuation-induced phenomena）开辟了新的途径。

Abstract: The fluctuations of ions in polar solvents remain poorly understood theoretically due to the complex coupling between ionic motion and solvent polarization. Indeed, while all-atom resolution can be achieved in numerical simulations, analytical approaches require suitable levels of coarse-graining. In this work, we describe ions and solvent molecules as interacting Brownian particles and use stochastic density functional theory to derive a generalized Langevin equation for the ionic charge density, explicitly accounting for solvent-mediated memory effects. In the regime where there is a clear timescale separation between fast solvent and slow ion dynamics, we obtain simple expressions for dynamical charge structure factors, which are validated by BD simulations. For slow solvents, we predict an emerging two-step relaxation in ionic dynamics. These results provide a mesoscopic approach for ion-solvent dynamics and open pathways to study fluctuation-induced phenomena in electrolytes.

### [151] [Cooking crystalline candies and the ductile to brittle transition in concentrated suspensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06513)
*Andreia F. Silva,James A. Richards,Fiona Jeffrey,Rory E. O'Neill,Daniel J. M. Hodgson,Christopher Ness,Wilson C. K. Poon*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和模拟，揭示了非布朗悬浮液和膏状物（non-Brownian suspensions and pastes）中存在从韧性到脆性的转变（ductile to brittle transition），并指出该转变由固体颗粒体积分数（solid volume fraction）从摩擦阻塞（frictional jamming）向随机密堆积（random close packing）变化所驱动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管非布朗悬浮液和膏状物在工程应用中广泛存在，其韧性到脆性转变是否存在及其起源仍缺乏充分研究，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 本文通过煮沸糖-奶油-黄油混合物（即“软糖（fudge）”）制备糖晶体悬浮液，通过改变烹饪时间或最终烹饪温度来观察材料行为变化；同时将实验拓展至非布朗方解石（calcite）颗粒悬浮液，并结合基于粒子的模拟（particle-based simulations）探究该现象的机制及其对边界条件（boundary conditions）的敏感性。

Result: 随着烹饪时间或最终温度升高，材料依次从流体（fluid）转变为韧性固体（ductile solid），再转变为脆性固体（brittle solid），后者在压缩中突然断裂。在非布朗方解石颗粒悬浮液中，随着固体分数从摩擦阻塞向随机密堆积移动，也观察到相同的转变序列。

Conclusion: 非布朗悬浮液和膏状物的韧性-脆性转变由固体颗粒体积分数升高驱动；粒子模拟还表明该现象对边界条件敏感。

Abstract: The existence and origin of the ductile to brittle transition in non-Brownian suspensions and pastes is underexplored despite the ubiquity of such materials in practical applications. We demonstrate the phenomenon in candies of sugar crystals in a water-protein-fat matrix prepared by boiling a sugar-cream-butter mixture (known as 'fudge' in some countries). As cooking time or final cooking temperature increases, we observe a transition from a fluid to a ductile solid, then to a brittle solid that abruptly fractures in compression. We propose that this is driven by rising solid sugar crystal volume fraction, and indeed find the same sequence of behaviour in a suspension of non-Brownian calcite particles as the solid fraction moves from frictional jamming to random close packing. Particle-based simulations reveal the sensitivity of the observed phenomenon to boundary conditions.

### [152] [Non-Local Particle Flows Become Local When Considering Dissipative Stress](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06531)
*Martin Trulsson*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过无摩擦稠密悬浮体的二维Kolmogorov流动模拟，证明非均匀剪切流中表现出的非局域性（nonlocality）实际上源于应力测量与平均方式的人为假象，而非局域流变学（local rheology）的本质失效。两种独立机制——引入耗散应力恢复均匀μ(J)定律，以及几何混合长度构造解释残余亚屈服行为——共同支持这一结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稠密颗粒流与悬浮流在非均匀剪切下，局部屈服准则（yield criterion）亚临界区域仍存在持续粒子运动，这一表观非局域性（apparent nonlocality）促使非局域流变学模型（nonlocal rheological models）的发展。本文旨在揭示该现象的真实物理机制。

Method: 采用无摩擦稠密悬浮体（frictionless dense suspensions）的粒子分辨模拟（particle-resolved simulations），在二维Kolmogorov流动（two-dimensional Kolmogorov flow）中进行研究。分别引入剪切率加权耗散应力（shear-rate-weighted dissipative stress）$τ_W=\langle τ\dot γ\rangle/\langle \dot γ\rangle$和几何混合长度构造（geometric mixing-length construction）两种独立方法进行分析。

Result: 耗散应力$τ_W$在整个流动主体中恢复了均匀的μ(J)定律，推断的摩擦系数严格保持在屈服值以上。而采用常规应力的几何混合长度构造，则解释了流动反转处亚直径层（sub-diameter layer）内的残余亚屈服行为（residual sub-yielding）。

Conclusion: 两种方法基于不同哲学与机制，共同表明在该几何构型和无摩擦情形下，表观非局域性很大程度上是应力测量与平均方式的人工假象（artefact），而非局域流变学的内在失效。

Abstract: Dense granular and suspension flows under inhomogeneous shear exhibit persistent particle motion in regions where the local yield criterion is subcritical, an apparent breakdown of locality that has motivated the development of a generation of nonlocal rheological models. Using particle-resolved simulations of frictionless dense suspensions in two-dimensional Kolmogorov flow, we show that two independent considerations together account for this signature. First, replacing the conventional shear stress by a shear-rate-weighted dissipative stress $τ_W=\langle τ\dot γ\rangle/\langle \dot γ\rangle$, which isolates the component of stress that performs irreversible work, restores the homogeneous $μ(J)$ law throughout the bulk of the flow, with the inferred friction remaining strictly above yield. Second, a simple geometric mixing-length construction, applied with conventional stresses and requiring no fluctuation input, accounts for the residual sub-yielding within a sub-diameter layer at flow reversals. Each approach is based on a different philosophy and mechanism, and together they suggest that much of the apparent non-locality in this geometry and frictionless case is an artefact of how stress is measured and averaged rather than an intrinsic breakdown of local rheology.

</details>


<div id='physics.chem-ph'></div>

# physics.chem-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [153] [Density diversity in training data governs thermodynamic transferability of machine learning interatomic potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05733)
*Minwoo Kim,Seungtae Kim,Je-Yeon Jung,Min Young Ha,Won Bo Lee*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在固定计算预算下，对训练构型进行密度多样化（而非温度多样化）是构建热力学可迁移机器学习原子间势（MLIP）的最有效策略；密度多样性可同时解决液态和气态条件下的失效模式，其物理根源在于局域配位拓扑对密度比对温度更敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potentials, MLIPs）虽能以降低的计算成本提供第一性原理精度，但其在不同热力学状态之间的可迁移性（transferability）仍存疑，尤其对于局域环境远离晶体平衡的流体系统，现有模型在气态等极端条件下表现不佳。

Method: 通过对比固态数据库与分子数据库训练的基础MLIP在不同密度和温度条件下的表现，采用从头训练（from-scratch training）和知识蒸馏（distillation）实验控制变量，系统研究密度多样性与温度多样性对模型迁移性的影响，并利用配位数分析（coordination number analysis）揭示物理机制。

Result: 基于固态数据库训练的基础MLIP能准确描述液态密度但无法处理气态条件，而基于分子数据库训练的模型则表现相反；密度多样化数据集能同时解决这两类失效模式，温度多样化数据集则无法弥补缺失的密度区间；配位拓扑（local coordination topology）对密度的敏感性高于温度。

Conclusion: 密度多样性应作为构建热力学可迁移MLIP的设计原则，并提供了评估基础模型与从头训练模型热力学覆盖范围的验证框架，从而支持跨多种操作条件的流体相过程可靠原子模拟。

Abstract: Machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) offer first-principles accuracy with reduced computational cost, but their transferability across different thermodynamic states remains questionable, particularly for fluid systems where molecules experience local environments far from crystalline equilibrium. Here, we demonstrate that diversifying the density of training configurations, rather than temperature, is the most effective strategy for building thermodynamically transferable MLIPs within a fixed computational budget. We first show that foundation MLIPs trained on solid-state databases accurately describe liquid-like densities but fail at gas-like conditions, while molecular-database-trained models exhibit the opposite behavior. Controlled from-scratch training and distillation experiments confirm that density-diverse datasets resolve both failure modes, whereas temperature-diverse datasets cannot compensate for missing density regimes. Coordination number analysis reveals the physical origin of this behavior: local coordination topology is more susceptible to density than temperature, leading to further structural diversity. These results establish density diversity as a design principle for thermodynamically transferable MLIPs and provide a validation framework for assessing the thermodynamic coverage of both foundation and from-scratch models, enabling reliable atomistic simulation of fluid-phase processes across diverse operating conditions.

</details>

### [154] [Frustrated Dynamics of Distance Matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05376)
*Igor Halperin*

Main category: nlin.PS

TL;DR: 本文提出受挫距离矩阵（Frustrated Distance Matrix, FDM）模型，是 Bogomolny-Bohigas-Schmit（BBS）静态距离矩阵系综在球面 S^2 上的动态推广。通过分析 N 个布朗粒子在淬火随机耦合下的成对测地线距离，揭示谱结构在粒子从均匀分布坍缩至一维环并缓慢漂移的过程中的演化规律。研究发现 BBS 静态谱模板在每一时刻得以保留，动态仅表现为谱质量的重分布，并以此设计了可从距离矩阵中提取的结构变化诊断指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 静态 BBS 理论只能从独立同分布（i.i.d.）样本的距离矩阵谱中恢复流形的几何信息，无法捕捉点过程结构随时间的演化。本文旨在引入时间分辨的 FDM 谱，从动态距离矩阵中提取结构变化信息，并建立粒子层面的“真实情况”（ground truth）与谱诊断之间的校准关系。

Method: 通过在球面上引入 N 个布朗粒子，粒子间存在淬火（quenched）随机成对耦合，耦合强度与粒子间的测地线距离呈线性关系，由此构建 FDM 模型。对比静态 BBS 谱模板，利用独立同分布重采样验证体密度自平均（self-averaging）机制，并从中提取可计算的结构变化谱诊断指标。

Result: BBS 静态谱模板在每一时间步保持不变，动态演化为该模板内谱质量的重新分布，这种重分布足够尖锐，足以标记一维环的形成。体密度自平均被确认为谱模板保持不变的机制，通过独立同分布重采样比较得到了验证。

Conclusion: 所提出的谱诊断指标仅需距离矩阵即可计算，可推广至金融相关矩阵、图和网络邻接谱、分子动力学中的相似性矩阵以及参数流形上的动力学等反问题（inverse problem）场景。

Abstract: We introduce the Frustrated Distance Matrix (FDM) model, a dynamic extension of the static distance-matrix ensemble on S^2 analyzed by Bogomolny, Bohigas, and Schmit (BBS). Its entries are pairwise geodesic distances between N Brownian particles on the sphere evolving under quenched random pairwise couplings linear in those distances. Where the static BBS theory recovers geometric information about the underlying manifold from spectra of distance matrices on i.i.d.\ samples, the time-resolved FDM spectrum carries information about structural changes of the underlying point process. The particle dynamics realize one such change: a fast collapse from a uniform configuration onto a one-dimensional ring, followed by slow rotational drift of the ring orientation; the particle-level picture provides the ground truth against which spectral diagnostics are calibrated. We find that the static BBS template is preserved at every time, with the dynamics entering as a redistribution of spectral mass within that template, sharp enough to flag ring formation. We propose self-averaging of the bulk density as the mechanism behind this preservation, verified by an i.i.d.-resample comparison, and extract a small set of spectral diagnostics of the structural change computable from the distance matrix alone. We suggest that our diagnostics can be applied in other similar inverse-problem settings: financial correlation matrices, graph and network adjacency spectra, similarity matrices in molecular dynamics, and dynamics on parameter manifolds.

</details>

### [155] [The General Structure of Trilinear Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05624)
*Takeshi Fukuyama*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文提出三线性（trilinear）结构作为Hirota双线性形式在可积系统中的自然推广，并证明Ernst系统的高阶导数项可由一个普适的三线性核（trilinear kernel）统一描述，为超越双线性层次的可积性提供了新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在可积系统（integrable systems）中，Hirota双线性形式（bilinear formalism）与Grassmannian几何及Plücker关系密切相关，但更高阶的代数结构（如三线性耦合）尚未被充分探索。本文旨在将三线性结构作为双线性形式的自然延拓加以研究，并考察其在爱因斯坦方程（Einstein equations）中的应用。

Method: 将Ernst势（Ernst potential）写成tau函数比（tau-ratio form）形式，将非线性方程分解为包含所有二阶导数项的立方扇区（cubic sector）和一个四次梯度包络（quartic gradient envelope）；将立方扇区识别为YTSF型三线性核（YTSF-type trilinear kernel），并建立了一般的三线性核判据（trilinear kernel criterion）。

Result: 将三线性核判据应用于Tomimatsu–Sato解族，发现δ=3解与δ=2解具有相同的三线性核结构，仅存在一个常系数归一化差异。

Conclusion: 三线性核是Ernst系统最高阶导数扇区的普适结构（universal structure），为超越双线性层次（bilinear hierarchy）的可积性研究提供了新视角。

Abstract: We investigate trilinear structures as a natural extension of the Hirota bilinear formalism in integrable systems. While bilinear equations are associated with Grassmannian geometry and Plücker relations, trilinear equations suggest a higher algebraic structure involving three-slot couplings of tau functions.
  Focusing on the stationary axisymmetric Einstein equations, we show that when the Ernst potential is written in a tau-ratio form, the nonlinear equation decomposes into a cubic sector containing all second-derivative terms and a quartic gradient envelope. The cubic sector is identified with a YTSF-type trilinear kernel.
  We formulate a general trilinear kernel criterion and apply it to the Tomimatsu--Sato solutions. In particular, we demonstrate that the $δ=3$ solution possesses the same trilinear kernel structure as the $δ=2$ case, with a universal normalization up to a constant factor.
  These results suggest that the trilinear kernel represents a universal structure governing the highest-derivative sector of the Ernst system, providing a new perspective on integrability beyond the bilinear hierarchy.

</details>

### [156] [Analysis of Mixed Radiation Fields at the MoEDAL Experiment Based on Real-Time Data from a Timepix Detector Network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05936)
*Benedikt Bergmann,Petr Burian,Josef Janeček,Claude Leroy,Petr Mánek,James Pinfold,Stanislav Pospíšil,Richard Soluk,Michal Suk*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本研究利用Timepix混合硅像素探测器网络（Timepix hybrid silicon pixel detector network）获取的数据，系统测定了大型强子对撞机（Large Hadron Collider, LHC）MoEDAL实验环境中快中子（fast neutrons）、其他强子（hadrons）及高电离粒子（highly ionizing particles）的通量和特性。这些粒子构成了MoEDAL实验中用于搜寻狄拉克磁单极子（Dirac magnetic monopole）径迹的被动核径迹探测器（Nuclear Track Detectors, NTDs）的实验本底。论文展示了辐射场分析结果，重点包括中子和高电离粒子的方向分布，并首次报告了Timepix探测器的空间径迹追踪能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MoEDAL实验使用被动核径迹探测器搜索狄拉克磁单极子的径迹，但环境中存在快中子、强子和高电离粒子等本底粒子，其中部分粒子在NTD中产生的径迹与磁单极子无法区分。因此，需要精确确定这些本底粒子的通量和特性，以支持磁单极子搜索实验的可靠解读。

Method: 研究基于2013年至2018年间作为MoEDAL实验一部分安装和运行的Timepix混合硅像素探测器网络获取的数据。该网络是MoEDAL实验首个也是唯一的有源探测器系统（active detector system），能够实时测量混合辐射场（mixed radiation fields），包括MoEDAL实验区不同区域的辐射组分构成、能谱特性和方向特性。

Result: 论文详细呈现了辐射场分析结果，重点包括中子和高电离粒子的通量、特性及其方向分布。此外，首次报告了Timepix探测器的空间径迹追踪能力，展示了从单个探测器帧中重建粒子方向和能量损失分布（energy-loss profiles）的结果。

Conclusion: 本研究成功利用Timepix有源探测器网络系统地表征了MoEDAL实验环境中的辐射本底，特别是中子和高电离粒子的通量和方向分布。同时验证了Timepix探测器在混合辐射场中实现空间径迹追踪的能力，为MoEDAL实验的磁单极子搜索提供了关键的背景数据支持。

Abstract: The primary objective of this work is the determination of fluences and characteristics of fast neutrons, other hadrons, and highly ionizing particles in the environment of the MoEDAL experiment at the Large Hadron Collider. These particles constitute an experimental background for the passive Nuclear Track Detectors (NTDs) used by MoEDAL to search for tracks potentially produced by Dirac magnetic monopoles, in particular by particles indistinguishable in NTD from monopoles. The study is based on data acquired by the Timepix hybrid silicon pixel detector network, which represents the first and only active detector system installed and operated as part of the MoEDAL experiment from 2013 to 2018. The Timepix detector network enables real-time measurements of mixed radiation fields, including the composition, spectral properties, and directional characteristics of individual radiation components across different regions of the MoEDAL experimental area. The paper presents detailed results of the radiation field analysis with emphasis on neutrons and highly ionizing particles, including their directional distributions. The first results demonstrating the spatial tracking capabilities of the Timepix detectors are also reported, illustrating the reconstruction of particle direction and energy-loss profiles from individual detector frames.

</details>

### [157] [Parameter estimation for kappa distributions using the EM algorithm in the superstatistical framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05428)
*Leonardo Sebastian Herrera,Sergio Davis*

Main category: stat.ME

TL;DR: 本文针对kappa分布不属于指数族、无法直接应用最大似然估计的问题，提出基于数据增广（data augmentation）的期望最大化（EM）算法，通过引入服从伽马分布的逆温度作为隐变量，恢复指数族结构，实现解析封闭形式的参数估计，并在合成数据上验证了收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kappa分布广泛用于空间等离子体物理中建模具有扩展尾部的速度分布函数，但其参数估计存在根本性困难：kappa分布不属于指数族（exponential family），因此无法直接应用解析可处理的最大似然方法（maximum likelihood methods）。

Method: 提出基于数据增广（data augmentation）的解决方案：将逆温度（inverse temperature）β作为服从伽马分布（gamma distribution）的隐变量（latent variable），从而在完整数据似然（complete-data likelihood）中恢复指数族结构；进而实现解析封闭形式的期望最大化（EM）算法，其E步和M步均基于充分统计量（sufficient statistics）导出。该方法对β波动的物理机制保持不可知（agnostic），这也是Beck-Cohen超统计力学框架（superstatistics framework）的核心特征。

Result: 将该方法应用于合成数据（synthetic data），结果表明EM算法收敛到通常的最大似然估计量（maximum likelihood estimators）。

Conclusion: EM算法为存在温度波动的超统计系统（superstatistical systems）中的推断提供了计算高效且概念清晰的替代方案，在保持统计严谨性的同时不损失物理可解释性。

Abstract: Kappa distributions are widely used in space plasma physics to model velocity distribution functions with extended tails. However, parameter estimation in these distributions presents a fundamental challenge: the kappa distribution does not belong to the exponential family, which prevents the direct application of analytically tractable maximum likelihood methods. In this work we propose a solution to this problem based on data augmentation: we introduce the inverse temperature $β$ as a gamma-distributed latent variable, thereby recovering the exponential family structure in the complete-data likelihood. This enables an implementation of the expectation-maximization (EM) algorithm in analytically closed form, with E-step and M-step derived from sufficient statistics. Our approach is agnostic with respect to the underlying physical mechanism generating fluctuations of $β$, which is a central aspect of the Beck-Cohen superstatistics framework, allowing a statistically rigorous treatment without compromising physical interpretability. We demonstrate that the method converges to the usual maximum likelihood estimators by applying it to synthetic data. Our results suggest that EM offers a computationally efficient and conceptually clear alternative for inference in superstatistical systems with temperature fluctuations.

</details>


### [158] [A renormalization-group inspired lattice-based framework for piecewise generalized linear models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05493)
*Joshua C. Chang*

Main category: stat.ME

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类受重整化群（RG）理论启发的分层加性模型，该模型具有可解释的显式分区结构，并利用统计物理中的副本分析（replica analysis）研究了其泛化性质，推导出格点设计和正则化先验的标度律，在公开数据集上取得了与黑盒方法及其他可解释方法相当的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习模型（如ReLU卷积神经网络）虽具有局部线性特性，但其分区结构（partition structure）不透明、难以解释或修改。本文旨在设计一种兼具表达力与内在可解释性的模型，其分区结构显式、可解释且易于约束或调整。

Method: 基于重整化群（renormalization group, RG）理论，构建输入空间的多维格点（lattice）分区，每个维度对应一个可能影响统计量的属性。参数以分层加性展开（additive hierarchical expansion）形式表达，每个高阶项捕捉相对于较低（更粗糙）相互作用尺度的变化。该模型等价于分段广义线性模型（piecewise GLM）、分层混合效应回归（hierarchical mixed-effects regression）或带结构化参数共享的回归树（regression tree）。采用副本分析（replica analysis）研究以Watanabe-Akaike信息准则（WAIC）为代理的泛化损失。

Result: 理论分析得到两个实用结果：(i) 根据数据集大小和预测变量维度设计格点的指导原则；(ii) 添加高阶展开项时正则化先验（regularization prior）的标度律（scaling law），使得增加模型复杂度不必然增加泛化损失。公开数据集上的实验表明，该方法与黑盒方法及其他内在可解释方法性能相当。

Conclusion: 受RG启发的分层加性模型在保持显式可解释性的同时，通过统计物理分析方法提供了实用的正则化策略，在泛化性能上可与黑盒方法竞争。

Abstract: We formally introduce a class of models inspired by renormalization group (RG) theory, built on additive hierarchical expansions analogous to those appearing in functional ANOVA and mixed-effects models. Like ReLU convolutional neural networks, they are almost everywhere locally linear; unlike ReLU networks, their partition structure is explicit, interpretable, and easy to modify or constrain. In these models, one defines a multidimensional lattice partition of the input space and uses it to scaffold variations in regression parameters. Each dimension of the lattice corresponds to an attribute by which the statistics of the problem may vary. The parameters are themselves expressed in the form of an expansion, where each term captures variations relative to a lower (coarser) interaction scale. These models admit multiple equivalent interpretations: as piecewise GLMs, as hierarchical mixed-effects regressions, or as regression trees with structured parameter sharing. Since RG motivates the design of these models, we use techniques from statistical physics -- specifically replica analysis -- to study their generalization properties. Specifically, we analyze the behavior of the Watanabe-Akaike Information Criterion (WAIC) as a proxy for generalization loss. This analysis yields two practical results: (i) guidance on the lattice design as a function of dataset size and predictor dimensionality; and (ii) a principled scaling law for the regularization prior when adding higher-order terms to the expansion so that one can increase model complexity without an expected increase in generalization loss. We evaluate the methodology on public datasets and find performance competitive against both blackbox methods and other intrinsically interpretable approaches.

</details>

# q-bio.BM [[Back]](#toc)

### [159] [Enhancing Cryo-EM Density Map Segmentation in Phenix for Improved Atomic Model Building](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05259)
*Chenwei Zhang*

Main category: q-bio.BM

TL;DR: 本文提出了 PhenixCraft，一个用于从冷冻电镜密度图（cryo-EM density maps）构建原子模型的全自动流程，通过整合 AlphaFold 预测提升了模型构建中的图谱分割精度，并在 TM-scores 和序列准确度上显著优于传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 冷冻电镜（cryo-EM）密度图中的噪声和伪影（artifacts）传统上会阻碍 Phenix 软件中模型构建时的图谱分割步骤，导致效率低下和局限性。为解决这一问题，作者旨在开发一个全自动流程来提升原子模型构建的性能。

Method: PhenixCraft 采用全自动流水线，通过整合 AlphaFold 预测来增强 Phenix 模型构建过程中的图谱分割（map-segmentation）步骤，从而应对传统方法难以处理的噪声和伪影挑战。

Result: 实验结果表明，PhenixCraft 在 TM-scores（模板建模分数）和序列准确度（sequence accuracy）方面均表现出更优性能，显著改进了传统 Phenix 模型构建的限制和低效问题。

Conclusion: PhenixCraft 作为一种全自动流程，能够有效利用 AlphaFold 预测提升冷冻电镜密度图向原子模型构建的准确性和效率，优于传统方法。

Abstract: We introduce PhenixCraft, a fully automated pipeline for building atomic models from cryo-EM density maps. By integrating AlphaFold predictions, we enhance the map-segmentation step in Phenix during model building, addressing challenges posed by noise and artifacts that traditionally hinder this step. Our results demonstrate PhenixCraft's superior performance in TM-scores and sequence accuracy, significantly improving upon the limitations and inefficiencies of traditional model building using Phenix.

</details>
