### [160] [Competing nonlinearities, criticality, and order-to-chaos transition in deep networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05294)
*Omri Lesser,Debanjan Chowdhury*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出一种统计混合激活函数（statistical mixture of activations）机制，通过每个神经元独立随机地从双组分分布中抽取激活函数，实现了深度神经网络初始化信号传播的连续相变。以 Tanh 和 Swish 的混合为例，在临界混合比例 $p_c$ 处网络获得尺度不变性（scale invariance），且不牺牲平滑性，解决了此前仅非光滑 ReLU 族可实现尺度不变传播的长期矛盾。实验表明，测试性能在 $p_c$ 附近达到最优，且淬火激活无序（quenched activation disorder）起到结构正则化作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度神经网络的表达能力源于非线性激活函数（nonlinear activation functions），其在初始化时的信号传播有效场论揭示了几种不同的普适类（universality classes），展现出不同的深度标度行为。如何在分析可控的条件下调控这些普适类目前仍是一个开放问题，这构成了本文的核心动机。

Method: 提出统计混合激活函数机制：每个神经元独立随机地从双组分分布（如 Tanh 与 Swish 的混合）中以混合比例 $p$ 抽取激活函数。通过方差传播、平行与垂直磁化率（parallel and perpendicular susceptibilities）以及 Lyapunov 指数（Lyapunov exponents）等方法表征该相变。

Result: 该机制引发了一个关于预激活（preactivation）方差深度标度的连续相变（continuous phase transition），分离出方差坍缩（variance-collapsing）与方差膨胀（variance-inflating）两个相；在临界点 $p_c$ 处网络实现统计尺度不变性（statistical scale invariance），方差与深度无关且保持平滑性。在真实数据集上训练多层感知机时，测试性能随 $p$ 呈现非单调变化，最优值出现在理论预测的 $p_c$ 附近。

Conclusion: 统计激活混合为穿越深度网络普适类相图提供了一种可控工具。淬火激活无序充当结构正则化器（structural regularizer），在抑制记忆损坏标签的同时保持泛化能力。初始化层面的相变直接影响了学到的表征。

Abstract: Deep neural networks owe their expressive power to nonlinear activation functions. The effective field theory of signal propagation at initialization reveals a few distinct universality classes of activations that exhibit different depth scaling. Tuning across these, especially with analytical control, is an open problem. We show that a statistical mixture of activations, where each neuron independently and randomly draws its activation from a two-component distribution with mixing fraction $p$, provides a new mechanism for a continuous phase transition. Applied to a mixture of Tanh and Swish, the transition is sharp in the depth scaling of the preactivation variance, separating a variance-collapsing from a variance-inflating phase; at $p_c$, the network acquires statistical scale invariance, with depth-independent variance, without sacrificing smoothness. This resolves a longstanding tension, where scale-invariant propagation has previously required the non-smooth ReLU family, rendering such networks ill-suited to curvature-based optimizers, physics-informed architectures, and neural-network quantum states. We corroborate the transition through variance propagation, parallel and perpendicular susceptibilities, and Lyapunov exponents. Training multilayer perceptrons on real datasets reveals non-monotonic test performance as a function of $p$, with an optimum near the theoretically predicted $p_c$, confirming that the initialization-level transition has direct consequences for learned representations. The quenched activation disorder acts as a structural regularizer, suppressing memorization of corrupted labels while preserving generalization. Our framework establishes statistical activation mixtures as a controlled tool for navigating the phase diagram of deep network universality classes.

</details>


### [161] [Resonance Proliferation Across Localization Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05445)
*Carlo Vanoni,David M. Long,Anushya Chandran*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文针对多体局域化（many-body localization, MBL）模型在有限尺寸下向退局域化缓慢漂移的现象，发展了一种基于统计雅可比近似（statistical Jacobi approximation, SJA）的统计方法，通过推导共振态频率分布的流方程，预测了表征共振密度的幂律指数θ(w)，并成功在多个随机矩阵模型和MBL实空间模型中与数值结果吻合，为解释MBL中的有限尺寸漂移提供了理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多体局域化（many-body localization, MBL）模型在中间无序强度下随着系统尺寸增大，会数值上缓慢地向退局域化漂移，但尚无令人满意的理论解释这一现象。数值结果表明，这种漂移由多体共振（many-body resonances）的增殖驱动。

Method: 采用统计雅可比近似（statistical Jacobi approximation, SJA），推导描述共振态在频率尺度w下密度的幂律指数θ(w)的流方程（flow equation）。该方法捕捉了大频率尺度上的共振形成如何随后影响低频率尺度上共振形成的过程。

Result: 局域化相由一条θ(w)>0的固定点线（line of fixed points）描述，而流的失稳则标志着共振增殖和热化（thermalization）的开始。预测的θ(w)在随机正则图（random regular graphs）上的安德森模型（Anderson model）和Lévy-Rosenzweig-Porter随机矩阵系综（random matrix ensemble）中与数值结果吻合，并在MBL实空间模型的中间无序强度下与数值测量一致。

Conclusion: 该研究通过建立共振频率分布的流方程，将共振增殖、特征态性质（如参与率 participation ratio）和动力学可观测量（如返回概率 return probability）联系起来，对解释MBL中观测到的有限尺寸漂移迈出了重要一步。

Abstract: Models of many-body localization (MBL) exhibit slow numerical drifts towards delocalization with increasing system size, for which no satisfactory theory exists. Numerics indicates that these drifts are driven by the proliferation of many-body resonances at intermediate disorder strengths. We develop a statistical method to predict the distribution of resonance oscillation frequencies which captures how the formation of resonances at larger frequency scales subsequently affects the formation of resonances at lower frequencies. Working within the statistical Jacobi approximation (SJA), we derive a flow equation for a power-law exponent $θ(w)$ characterizing the density of resonances at frequency scale $w$. A localized phase is described by a line of fixed points with $θ(w)>0$, while an instability of the flow signals resonance proliferation and the onset of thermalization. The predicted $θ(w)$ matches numerics on the Anderson model on random regular graphs and the Lévy-Rosenzweig-Porter random matrix ensemble, both of which host resonance-driven delocalization transitions. We further connect the flow to eigenstate properties such as the participation ratio and to dynamical observables such as the return probability. The predicted $θ(w)$ also matches what is numerically measured in real-space models of MBL at intermediate disorder strengths, representing a significant step towards explaining the finite-size drifts observed in MBL.

</details>


### [162] [Lecture Notes on Statistical Physics and Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06394)
*Olaf Hohm*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文以经典统计物理（classical statistical physics）为核心，系统介绍了与神经网络（neural networks）和深度学习（deep learning）相关的统计力学概念，包括玻尔兹曼-吉布斯分布（Boltzmann-Gibbs distribution）、相变（phase transition）、重整化群（renormalization group）以及基于伊辛自旋（Ising spins）和自旋玻璃（spin-glass）模型的Hopfield网络（Hopfield networks）、玻尔兹曼机（Boltzmann machines）和受限玻尔兹曼机（restricted Boltzmann machines），并延伸到现代深度学习与大型语言模型（large language models）的描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 使没有物理学背景的读者也能理解统计物理的核心概念（如相变和重整化群），并将这些概念与神经网络和深度学习联系起来。

Method: 将统计物理视为概率论或统计学的一个分支；在有限配置空间（finite configuration space）上引入玻尔兹曼-吉布斯分布和热力学势（thermodynamic potentials），以伊辛自旋和自旋玻璃模型为例；将相变定义为晶格点数趋于无穷时出现的不连续（discontinuity）；通过Hopfield网络和玻尔兹曼机连接自旋玻璃模型与机器学习，并在受限玻尔兹曼机的学习算法中使用类似重整化群的隐变量积分方法。

Result: 阐述了统计物理与神经网络之间的形式对应关系，表明受限玻尔兹曼机的学习算法与重整化群有内在联系，并指出早期深度学习的部分发展受限于玻尔兹曼机多层架构的启发。

Conclusion: 经典统计物理为理解神经网络和深度学习提供了概率论框架，尤其是相变、重整化群等概念在机器学习模型（如玻尔兹曼机和大型语言模型）中具有重要的理论解释意义。

Abstract: These lecture notes introduce some topics of classical statistical physics, particularly those that are relevant for neural networks and deep learning. Statistical physics is treated as a branch of probability theory or statistics, with the goal of making concepts such as phase transitions and the renormalization group accessible to readers without prior knowledge of physics. We introduce the Boltzmann-Gibbs distribution and the thermodynamic potentials on a finite configuration space, notably for Ising spins and spin-glass models on a lattice, and then define phase transitions as discontinuities that arise in the limit that the number of lattice points goes to infinity. We further introduce Hopfield networks and Boltzmann machines, which are governed by the same energy function as spin-glass models, and discuss the learning algorithm for restricted Boltzmann machines. In this algorithm hidden neurons are integrated out as in the renormalization group. Finally, modern deep learning is introduced, whose early developments were in part motivated by restricted Boltzmann machines in that they carry many layers of hidden neurons. A description of large language models is given.

</details>


### [163] [Probing critical phases in quasiperiodic systems via subsystem information capacity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06075)
*Huaijin Dong,Long Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过子系统信息容量（SIC）这一新诊断工具，系统地研究了准周期系统的纠缠动力学，发现临界相具有明显的空间异质性，表现为信息容量的阶梯式斜坡和亚区域回波，从而有效区分扩展相、局域相和临界相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在识别能够清晰区分准周期系统中扩展相、临界相和局域相的动力学印记（dynamical signatures），特别是找到明确将临界相与其他两相区分开的诊断方法。

Method: 以扩展哈珀模型（extended Harper model）为研究对象，将半链纠缠熵（half-chain entanglement entropy）与空间分辨的子系统信息容量（subsystem information capacity, SIC）相结合进行分析。

Result: 临界相表现出扩展相和局域相所缺乏的显著空间异质性；稳态SIC呈现随子系统尺寸变化的阶梯式斜坡，反映了链的碎片化；动力学上出现亚区域回波（subregion echoes），其周期与亚区域长度成比例，与受限准粒子反射的准粒子图像定量吻合；将碎片化归因于哈密顿量非对角跃迁项中的不可公度分布零点（incommensurately distributed zeros, IDZs）。

Conclusion: SIC作为一种强大的实空间探针（real-space probe），能够通过稳态轮廓、初始位点灵敏度和亚区域回波的存在性，清晰区分迁移率边和临界相等不同场景，揭示支撑临界相多分形结构（multifractal structure）的瓶颈连接性。

Abstract: We systematically investigate the entanglement dynamics of quasiperiodic systems across their extended, critical, and localized phases, aiming to identify dynamical signatures that can clearly distinguish the critical phase from the other two. Focusing on the extended Harper model, we complement the half-chain entanglement entropy with the spatially resolved subsystem information capacity (SIC) and demonstrate that the critical phase exhibits a pronounced spatial heterogeneity that is absent in the extended and localized phases. In the steady state, the SIC reveals a stepwise ramp as a function of subsystem size, reflecting an underlying fragmentation of the chain into weakly connected subregions. Dynamically, information initially localized within such a subregion can undergo coherent long-lived oscillations, dubbed subregion echoes, whose period scales with the subregion length, in quantitative agreement with a quasiparticle picture of confined quasiparticle reflections. We trace this internal fragmentation to the incommensurately distributed zeros (IDZs) in the off-diagonal hopping terms of the Hamiltonian. To establish the generality of the SIC as a diagnostic tool, we further apply it to a mobility-edge phase with coexisting extended and localized states and to a critical phase that does not originate from IDZ fragmentation, and show that the SIC can cleanly distinguish these scenarios through their distinct steady-state profiles, initial-site sensitivities and the presence of subregion echoes. Our results establish the SIC as a powerful real-space probe for diagnosing critical phases and for uncovering the bottlenecked connectivity that underlies their multifractal structure.

</details>


### [164] [Floquet-induced suppression of thermalization in a quasiperiodic Ising chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06089)
*Biswajit Paul,Nilanjan Roy,Tapan Mishra*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文证明，在适当的周期性驱动（periodic driving）协议下，多体局域化（many-body localized, MBL）系统可以抵抗热化，并转变为一种非遍历扩展相——多体临界相（many-body critical, MBC phase）。通过研究 kicked 准周期伊辛链，发现中等驱动频率下 MBL 相被完全抑制，MBC 相在参数空间中扩散。该工作将 Floquet 驱动确立为稳定非遍历扩展多体相的有效途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知周期性驱动系统中多体局域化（MBL）系统会发生热化，本文试图寻找一种驱动方案来抵抗这种热化，从而探索 MBL 之外的新型非遍历相态。

Method: 采用 kicked 准周期伊辛链（kicked quasiperiodic Ising chain）作为模型，通过准能量统计（quasienergy statistics）、Floquet 本征态（Floquet eigenstates）、自关联动力学（autocorrelation dynamics）和纠缠增长（entanglement growth）等多种方法表征相图。

Result: 高频驱动下，遍历相、MBL 相与 MBC 相共存；而在中等驱动频率下，MBL 相被完全抑制，MBC 相在参数空间中扩散。非单调特征揭示了非遍历相的丰富性。

Conclusion: Floquet 驱动提供了一种超越传统 Floquet-MBL 范式、稳定非遍历扩展多体相的有效途径。

Abstract: Many-body localized (MBL) systems are known to thermalize in periodically driven systems. In this work, we demonstrate that under proper driving protocol, this thermalization this thermalization can be resisted such that the MBL phase turns into a non-ergodic extended phase, known as the many-body critical (MBC) phase. Considering a kicked quasiperiodic Ising chain, we show that while at high-frequency driving the ergodic, MBL, and the MBC phases coexist, at moderate driving frequencies the MBL phase is completely suppressed and the MBC phase proliferates in the parameter space. Using quasienergy statistics, Floquet eigenstates, autocorrelation dynamics, and entanglement growth, we characterize the emergent phases and identify non-monotonic signatures revealing richness of the nonergodic phases. Our results establish Floquet driving as a powerful route to stabilizing nonergodic extended many-body phases beyond the conventional Floquet-MBL paradigm.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文针对 IceCube Upgrade 的暗物质探测能力进行敏感性预测，评估其在 3–500 GeV 质量范围内通过太阳核心与银河系中心暗物质湮灭产生中微子通量的探测潜力，表明仅需三年数据即可对部分暗物质模型实现领先限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: IceCube Upgrade 作为 IceCube 中微子天文台（IceCube Neutrino Observatory）的扩展，设计用于增强对 1–500 GeV 能量区间中微子的探测能力，从而提升对低质量暗物质（low-mass dark matter）场景的灵敏度。本研究旨在量化该升级对暗物质湮灭产生的中微子通量的探测前景。

Method: 研究通过投射敏感性分析（sensitivity projection），评估 IceCube Upgrade 对来自太阳核心（core of the Sun）和银河系中心（Galactic Center）的暗物质湮灭（dark matter annihilation）产生的中微子通量（neutrino fluxes）的探测能力，重点关注暗物质质量在 3–500 GeV 范围内的情形。

Result: 投射结果表明，IceCube Upgrade 能够对这一参数空间中的暗物质施加严格限制，仅需三年数据采集即可在某些暗物质模型上实现领先的探测灵敏度（leading sensitivities）。

Conclusion: IceCube Upgrade 将在低质量暗物质探测方面显著提升 IceCube 的实验能力，为未来暗物质间接探测（indirect dark matter detection）提供强有力的实验约束。

Abstract: The IceCube Upgrade, an extension designed to enhance the IceCube Neutrino Observatory's detection of neutrinos with energies between 1 GeV and 500 GeV, will markedly improve IceCube's sensitivity to low-mass dark matter scenarios. In this study, we present sensitivity projections for the IceCube Upgrade to neutrino fluxes arising from dark matter annihilation. In particular, we consider dark matter with masses between 3 GeV to 500 GeV from both the core of the Sun and the Galactic Center. These projections indicate that the IceCube Upgrade will enable stringent limits on dark matter in this parameter space, achieving leading sensitivities to some dark matter models with only three years of data taking.

</details>

### [166] [Equivariant 2-Poisson Algebra Bundles over Configuration Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05398)
*Hai Châu Nguyên*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在配置空间（configuration spaces）的等变向量丛（equivariant vector bundles）框架下，构造了诱导等变函子及其与限制函子的伴随关系，定义了Hadamard和张量积（Hadamard and Cauchy tensor products）并证明其构成对称2-幺半结构（symmetric 2-monoidal structure），进而构造了自由交换2-代数丛（free commutative 2-algebra bundle），并证明斜对称丛映射可诱导该2-代数丛上的相容泊松括号（Poisson bracket）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究带对角的配置空间（即 $M^n/\mathfrak{S}_n$ 轨道折叠商空间（orbifold quotient））上的等变向量丛，旨在建立其张量代数结构并探索泊松几何性质。

Method: 采用等变向量丛的等价语言，构造诱导等变函子（induced-equivariance functor）并证明其与限制函子（restriction functor）之间的伴随关系。定义Hadamard积与Cauchy张量积并证明它们构成对称2-幺半结构。在此基础上构造张量代数丛与对称代数丛，并证明对于局部向量丛（local vector bundle）$V \rightarrow M$，$\mathbf{S}^{\boxtimes} \big( \mathbf{S}^{\otimes}(V) \big)$ 是由 $V$ 生成的自由交换2-代数。

Result: 建立了诱导等变函子与限制函子的伴随关系；证明了Hadamard积与Cauchy张量积构成对称2-幺半结构；构造了自由交换2-代数丛 $\mathbf{S}^{\boxtimes} \big( \mathbf{S}^{\otimes}(V) \big)$；证明了任意斜对称丛映射 $k : V \boxtimes V \rightarrow \mathbf{I}_{\otimes}$ 可在此2-代数丛上诱导相容的泊松括号。

Conclusion: 该工作为配置空间上的等变向量丛建立了系统的2-代数与泊松结构框架，为进一步研究相关几何与代数结构提供了基础。

Abstract: We study equivariant vector bundles over configuration spaces with diagonals included, viewed as orbifold quotients $M^n/\mathfrak{S}_n$ by permutation groups. Working in the equivalent language of equivariant vector bundles, we construct an induced-equivariance functor and prove its adjunction with restriction. We then define Hadamard and Cauchy tensor products and show that they form a symmetric $2$-monoidal structure. We construct the corresponding tensor and symmetric algebra bundles and prove that, for a local vector bundle $V \rightarrow M$, the bundle $\mathbf{S}^{\boxtimes} \big( \mathbf{S}^{\otimes}(V) \big)$ is the free commutative $2$-algebra generated by $V$. Finally, we show that any skew-symmetric bundle map $k : V \boxtimes V \rightarrow \mathbf{I}_{\otimes}$ induces a compatible Poisson bracket on this $2$-algebra bundle.

</details>


### [167] [Accessory Parameter of Confluent Heun Equations, Voros Periods and classical irregular conformal blocks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06079)
*Kohei Iwaki,Hajime Nagoya,Ayato Shukuta*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过Voros周期导出了Heun微分方程及其所有合流方程的辅参数形式级数展开，并将这些展开与经典共形块（classical conformal blocks）进行比较，验证了二者之间的Zamolodchikov型猜想在包含不规则奇点（irregular singularities）情形下的成立。此外，作为先前工作的推广，给出了如何在谱曲线（spectral curve）上选取环路以得到与经典共形块对应的Voros周期的详细方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用Voros周期（Voros periods）推导Heun方程及其所有合流方程（confluent equations）的辅参数形式级数展开；将这些展开与Bonelli–Shchechkin–Tanzini近期获得的经典共形块进行对比；在谱曲线上为Voros周期选取特定环路，从而建立与经典共形块的对应关系。

Result: 得到了Heun方程及其合流方程的辅参数的Voros周期形式级数展开，验证了这些展开与对应经典共形块之间满足Zamolodchikov型猜想，包括在不规则奇点情形下的成立。

Conclusion: 本文在Mironov–Morozov、Piatek–Pietrykowski以及Lisovyy–Naidiuk等前人工作的基础上，提供了在谱曲线上选择环路的详细方案，使得所得Voros周期通过辅参数与经典（规则或不规则）共形块相对应，从而系统性地建立了辅参数级数展开与共形块理论之间的联系。

Abstract: For the Heun differential equation and all of its confluent equations, we derive formal series expansions of the accessory parameters using the Voros periods. We then compare these expansions with the classical conformal blocks recently obtained by Bonelli--Shchechkin--Tanzini, and examine the Zamolodchikov-type conjecture expected to hold between them, allowing for irregular singularities. In particular, as an extension of the previous works of Mironov--Morozov, Piatek--Pietrykowski and Lisovyy--Naidiuk, we provide a detailed prescription for choosing cycles on the spectral curve that yield the Voros period which corresponds to the classical (regular or irregular) conformal blocks through the accessory parameter.

### [168] [Non-relativistic limit of generalized relativistic Pauli operators by Feynman-Kac formulae](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06099)
*Soichiro Sakamoto*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了在约束条件2α=γβ+γ²下，广义相对论性Pauli算子的非相对论极限（c→∞），利用Feynman-Kac表示证明了热半群$e^{-tH_c^{S,α}}$强收敛到$e^{-tH^{S,α}}$，极限生成元为$\frac{α}{2m^{\frac{2}{α}-1}}(σ·(-i∇-a))²+V$，并同样研究了广义相对论性Schrödinger算子的非相对论极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非相对论量子力学中，Pauli算子描述了带自旋粒子在磁场中的运动；其相对论性推广及非相对论极限的严格数学分析对理解从相对论到经典力学的过渡至关重要，但目前对于广义形式（基于Bernstein函数）下该极限的收敛性尚未充分研究。

Method: 采用Feynman-Kac表示方法，将热半群$e^{-tH_c^{S,α}}$表示为布朗运动（Brownian motion）、子ordinators（subordinator）和泊松过程（Poisson process）的路径积分形式，进而分析c→∞时半群的强收敛性。

Result: 证明当光速c趋于无穷时，广义相对论性Pauli算子的热半群$e^{-tH_c^{S,α}}$强收敛到$e^{-tH^{S,α}}$，极限生成元为$\fracα{2m^{\frac{2}{α}-1}}(σ·(-i∇-a))²+V$；类似结果对广义相对论性Schrödinger算子同样成立。

Conclusion: 通过路径积分方法严格建立了广义相对论性Pauli算子在约束条件下的非相对论极限，为Bernstein函数框架下的相对论量子算子的经典极限提供了数学依据。

Abstract: The non-relativistic limit of a generalized relativistic Pauli operator\[H_c^{S,α}=\left(2c^β\bigl(σ\cdot(-i\nabla-a)\bigr)^2+(mc^γ)^{2/α}\right)^{α/2}-mc^γ+V\]on $L^2(\mathbb{R}^3;\mathbb{C}^2)$ is investigated under the constraint$2α=γβ+γ^2$.This operator generalizes the relativistic Pauli operator within the framework of Bernstein functions.The associated heat semigroup $e^{-tH_c^{S,α}}$ admits a Feynman--Kac representation involving Brownian motion, a subordinator, and a Poisson process.Using this representation, we prove that the semigroup $e^{-tH_c^{S,α}}$ converges strongly to $e^{-tH^{S,α}}$ as $c\to\infty$, where the limiting generator is given by\[H^{S,α}=\fracα{2m^{\frac{2}α-1}}\bigl(σ\cdot(-i\nabla-a)\bigr)^2+V.\]The non-relativistic limit of a generalized relativistic Schrödinger operator is also investigated.

</details>


### [169] [Dynamical cooling driven by self-similar fronts in the 2D nonlinear Schrödinger model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06396)
*Jason Laurie,Simon Thalabard,Sergey Nazarenko*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过直接模拟、波动力学方程（WKE）和四阶微分近似模型（DAM），分析了散焦二维非线性薛定谔模型中的部分热化与随后的冷却动力学过程，发现谱演化中存在多个自相似区间，并通过自相似前沿驱动有效动力冷却，指向形式上的零温平衡态——类似于经典波系统中的紫外灾变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解散焦二维非线性薛定谔（nonlinear Schrödinger）模型中从部分热化到冷却的动力学机制，揭示谱演化中的自相似行为以及向零温平衡态趋近的物理过程。

Method: 采用直接数值模拟（direct simulations），并结合波动力学方程（wave-kinetic equations, WKE）与四阶微分近似模型（fourth-order differential approximation model, DAM）进行理论分析。

Result: 发现演化中的WKE谱呈现两个不同的自相似区间（similarity ranges）——准热核心（quasi-thermal core）与紫外尾（ultraviolet tail）；而在DAM中，额外出现了一个红外自相似区间（infrared self-similarity）。通过拉伸准热区域，自相似前沿驱动了向形式零温平衡态的有效动力冷却过程。

Conclusion: 该动力学冷却过程在形式上对应于一个温度为零但定义不明确的平衡态，其行为类似于经典波系统中的紫外灾变（ultraviolet catastrophe）。

Abstract: We analyze the dynamics towards partial thermalization and subsequent cooling in the defocusing two-dimensional nonlinear Schrödinger model, using direct simulations and insights from the wave-kinetic equations (WKE) and a fourth-order differential approximation model (DAM). We show that the evolving WKE spectrum exhibits two distinct similarity ranges--the quasi-thermal core and the ultraviolet tail--whereas in the DAM, an additional range of infrared self-similarity appears. By stretching the quasi-thermal region, the self-similar fronts drive an effective dynamical cooling process towards the formal but ill-defined equilibrium state at vanishing temperature--analogous to an ultraviolet catastrophe in a system of classical waves.

</details>

Conclusion: 该充要条件完善了对薛定谔算子谱阈值处零能态性质的理解，并为后续相关研究提供了更一般的理论基础。

### [171] [Tunable Interlayer Charge-transfer States in MoSe$_2$/WS$_2$ Moiré Superlattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05571)
*Zheyu Lu,Jiahui Nie,Tianle Wang,Rwik Dutta,Ruishi Qi,Jingxu Xie,Can Uzundal,Jianghan Xiao,Ziyu Wang,Yibo Feng,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,James R. Chelikowsky,Archana Raja,Steven G. Louie,Mit H. Naik,Michael P. Zaletel,Feng Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算与光学反射光谱相结合，系统研究了电子掺杂的MoSe₂/WS₂莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattice）中出现的莫尔激子态（moiré excitonic states）和层间电荷转移态（interlayer charge-transfer states），揭示了掺杂电子的局域化行为，并通过垂直电场调控实现了从Type-I到Type-II的能带对齐切换与可调谐的Fermi-Hubbard模型，预测了整数及分数填充下的多种关联电荷有序态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过渡金属二硫属化物（transition metal dichalcogenide, TMD）异质双层形成的莫尔超晶格为研究强关联电子（strongly correlated electrons）、激子（excitonic）和拓扑现象提供了多功能平台，特别是角度对齐的MoSe₂/WS₂异质双层在零垂直电场下具有Type-I能带对齐，包含丰富的关联自旋与电荷物理，亟需对其光学激发与关联态进行全面理解。

Method: 采用大规模第一性原理计算（large-scale first-principles calculations）与光学反射光谱（optical reflection spectroscopy）相结合的方法，对角度对齐的电子掺杂MoSe₂/WS₂莫尔超晶格中出现的莫尔激子态和层间电荷转移态进行了系统研究。

Result: 观察到垂直电场将异质结构能带对齐从Type-I切换为Type-II时，出现从n/n₀=1到4的系列层间电荷转移跃迁（其中n₀为莫尔密度）；通过调节垂直电场可精确控制层间电子局域化，在有效蜂巢晶格（effective honeycomb lattice）上实现具有可调谐电荷转移带的Fermi-Hubbard模型。蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulation）进一步预测在整数和分数填充下均会出现多种关联电荷有序态。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了对电子掺杂MoSe₂/WS₂莫尔超晶格中出现的关联电荷转移态与光学激发行为的全面理解，莫尔激子态可作为掺杂电子局域化轮廓的灵敏光学探针，所实现的电场可调Fermi-Hubbard模型为探索强关联物理提供了可控实验平台。

Abstract: Moiré superlattices formed by transition metal dichalcogenide (TMD) heterobilayers provide a versatile platform for studying strongly correlated electronic, excitonic, and topological phenomena in solids. In particular, angle-aligned MoSe$_2$/WS$_2$ heterobilayers, which have a Type-I band alignment at zero vertical electric field, host rich correlated spin and charge physics. Here, combining large-scale first-principles calculations and optical reflection spectroscopy, we report a thorough study of the emergent moiré excitonic states and interlayer charge-transfer states in angle-aligned electron-doped MoSe$_2$/WS$_2$ moiré superlattices. The moiré excitonic states serve as sensitive optical probes to the localization profile of doped electrons. We observe a series of interlayer charge-transfer transitions from n/n$_0$ = 1 to 4 (where n$_0$ denotes the moiré density) when the vertical electric field switches the heterostructure band alignment from Type-I to Type-II. By tuning the vertical electric field, we can precisely control the interlayer electron localization, realizing a Fermi-Hubbard model with a tunable charge-transfer band on an effective honeycomb lattice. Furthermore, Monte Carlo simulation of the doping dependence of the electric-field susceptibility predicts that multiple correlated charge-ordered states appear at both integer and fractional fillings. Our results provide a holistic understanding of the emergent optical excitations and the correlated charge-transfer states in electron-doped MoSe$_2$/WS$_2$ moiré superlattices.

### [172] [Multifrequency Floquet Engineering of Magnon Polaritons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05576)
*L. Hackner,A. R. Myatt,W. Wustmann,N. J. Lambert*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过调制微波腔频率而非磁子频率，实现了腔磁子极化激元（cavity magnon-polaritons）的Floquet工程（Floquet engineering），并引入双频率Floquet调制，展示其能谱与单频调制的定性差异，包括新的反交叉（anticrossings）出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究中通过调制磁子频率实现Floquet工程面临技术困难（如随时间变化的偏置磁场难以实现），因此需要探索更可行、调制深度和带宽更大的替代方案来操控磁子-光子混合系统的能谱。

Method: 采用调制微波腔频率的方法替代调制磁子频率，施加可公度的双频率（commensurate two-frequency）Floquet调制，其中较高频率为较低频率的2倍和3倍，并控制两个驱动分量的相对振幅和相位。

Result: 双频率Floquet调制下，能谱依赖于驱动信号的相对振幅和相位；与单频调制相比，出现定性不同的特征，尤其是原本未耦合的边带（sidebands）之间产生了新的反交叉结构。

Conclusion: 该平台提供了一种替代性方法，可用于操控混合系统中的Floquet准能级（Floquet quasi-energy levels），在实现大调制深度和带宽的同时避免了磁子频率调制的技术难点。

Abstract: Floquet engineering of cavity magnon-polaritons by periodically modulating the magnon frequency has recently attracted much interest as a way to manipulate the energy spectrum of magnon-photon hybrid systems. However, modulating the frequency of magnons by a time-varying bias magnetic field can be challenging. We demonstrate cavity magnon-polariton Floquet engineering by modulating the microwave cavity frequency, allowing large modulation depth and bandwidth. We apply commensurate two-frequency Floquet modulations with the higher frequency at twice and three times the lower frequency, and demonstrate that the resulting spectrum depends on the relative amplitude and phase of the two drive tones. In comparison with single-frequency Floquet modulations, the spectrum has qualitatively different features; in particular, new anticrossings appear between previously uncoupled sidebands. Our platform offers an alternative way to manipulate Floquet quasi-energy levels in hybrid systems.

</details>


### [173] [Collective quantum state at the atomic limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05587)
*Fan Zhang,Yanxing Li,Chengye Dong,Ninad Kailas Dongre,Viet-Anh Ha,Yu-Chuan Lin,Yiyuan Luo,Hyunsue Kim,Joshua A. Robinson,Feliciano Giustino,Fan Zhang,Chih-Kang Shih*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究利用低温扫描隧道显微镜在单层WSe₂的镜像孪晶边界段中直接观测到量子化集体模式，证明Tomonaga-Luttinger液体行为即使在纳米尺度（最短1纳米）的原子级受限体系中仍能存活，并展示了自旋-电荷分离与新的多体量子点现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 集体量子态（collective quantum states）通常与扩展系统相关联，而强关联态能否在原子尺度下存活是一个基础问题。本文旨在探索Tomonaga-Luttinger液体（Tomonaga-Luttinger liquid）这类一维集体量子物质在原子级受限条件下的存在极限与行为。

Method: 采用低温扫描隧道显微镜和扫描隧道谱（low-temperature scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy）技术，对单层WSe₂中原子级受限的镜像孪晶边界（mirror twin boundary）段进行直接成像与谱学测量。

Result: 观察到与分数化自旋和电荷激发（fractionalized spin and charge excitations）相关的不同驻波支，这些模式在最短1纳米的线段中依然存在，确立了Luttinger液体行为的原子尺度受限极限。超短段形成一类新型多体量子点（many-body quantum dots），其离散谱来源于受限集体玻色模式而非单粒子电子态。在有序链中，点间耦合重塑类电子基态，而集体自旋/电荷激发基本保持完整，揭示了涌现多体模式的不同耦合响应。

Conclusion: 集体量子物质可以在原子长度尺度下持续存在并展现根本不同的耦合行为，这为利用原子级受限构建块来工程化强关联量子相（strongly correlated quantum phases）建立了新的平台。

Abstract: Collective quantum states are often associated with extended systems, where spatially extensive degrees of freedom enable emergent many-body behavior; whether such strongly correlated states survive at atomic dimensions remains a fundamental question. Tomonaga-Luttinger liquids provide a paradigmatic example of one-dimensional collective quantum matter characterized by spin-charge separation. Using low-temperature scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy, we directly visualize quantized collective modes in atomically confined mirror twin boundary segments of monolayer WSe2. Distinct standing-wave branches associated with fractionalized spin and charge excitations persist in segments as short as one nanometer, establishing the atomic-scale confinement limit of Luttinger-liquid behavior. These ultrashort segments form a new class of many-body quantum dots whose discrete spectra arise from confined collective bosonic modes rather than single-particle electron states. When assembled into ordered chains, inter-dot coupling reshapes electron-like fundamental states while collective spin/charge excitations remain largely intact, revealing distinct coupling responses of emergent many-body modes. Our results demonstrate that collective quantum matter can persist and exhibit fundamentally distinct coupling behavior at atomic length scales, establishing a novel platform for engineering strongly correlated quantum phases from atomically confined building blocks.

</details>


### [174] [Inter-harmonic ratio structure and saturation of Bernstein modes in graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05655)
*Miguel Tierz*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文推导了石墨烯中伯恩斯坦模式（Bernstein modes, BM）在准经典弹道区间的峰值吸收公式，揭示了其可分解为发射谱、模式分裂、转折点增强和残余介电响应因子四个部分；发现不同谐波间峰值比率仅由谐波阶数决定（$I_n/I_m\simeq m/n$），并受线宽修正影响；该分解框架还能统一描述低功率振幅与非线性饱和行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 石墨烯中的伯恩斯坦模式（Bernstein modes, BM）是有限波矢（finite-wavevector）的磁等离子体激元，由接触近场激发，而普通回旋共振（cyclotron resonance, CR）仅探测$q\approx0$的响应。现有理论对BM谐波间峰值的定量关系及线宽效应缺乏统一刻画，因此需要建立更精确的吸收谱分解框架。

Method: 在准经典弹道（quasiclassical ballistic）输运区间内推导BM峰值吸收公式，将其分解为发射谱（launch spectrum）、伯恩斯坦模式分裂（Bernstein-mode splitting）、转折点增强（turning-point enhancement）和残余介电响应因子（residual dielectric-response factor）的乘积。通过分析固定激发频率下BM高阶泛音（$n\ge2$）的采样动量$q\simeq\omega/v_F$，约化谐波间峰值比率，并进行光滑发射源合成测试及线宽/介电参数敏感性分析。

Result: BM泛音间峰值比率简化至$I_n/I_m\simeq m/n$，光滑发射源和屏蔽因子互相消去，仅保留线宽修正和每对谐波的残余响应比率。合成测试中，带噪声的全波矢谱能有效恢复残余比率；发射源/介电参数误设仅引入约1–2%的偏移，而线宽假设导致约10–30%的偏移。低功率振幅可通过相同分解与非线性和（nonlinear saturation）建立联系。

Conclusion: 若BM谐波共享相同的冷却区域和辐射热（bolometric）读出，则低功率斜率与起始强度的乘积在谐波间保持不变；BM与CR的功率扫描遵循不同标度的归一化饱和曲线，分别具有$Γ^{-1/2}$和$Γ^{-1}$的线宽标度律（linewidth scaling）。该结果强调线宽是影响BM谱定量分析的关键因素，远大于发射源/介电参数的敏感性。

Abstract: Bernstein modes (BM) in graphene are finite-wavevector magnetoplasmons excited by contact near fields, whereas ordinary cyclotron resonance (CR) probes $q\approx0$. We derive the BM peak absorption in the quasiclassical ballistic regime and show that it factorizes into a launch spectrum, Bernstein-mode splitting, turning-point enhancement, and residual dielectric-response factor. At fixed excitation frequency, BM overtones ($n\ge2$) are sampled, to leading order, at the same momentum $q\simeqω/v_F$. Smooth launch and screening factors therefore cancel in inter-harmonic peak ratios, yielding $I_n/I_m\simeq m/n$, modified by linewidth corrections and one residual response ratio for each harmonic pair. In smooth-launcher synthetic tests, noisy full-$q$ spectra recover the residual ratio within errors: moderate launcher/dielectric misspecification within this benchmark family shifts it by only $\sim\!1$--$2\%$, whereas linewidth assumptions shift it by $\sim\!10$--$30\%$. The same factorization connects low-power amplitudes to nonlinear saturation. If BM harmonics share the same cooling region and bolometric readout, the low-power slope times onset intensity is harmonic independent, while BM and CR power sweeps obey distinct normalized saturation curves with linewidth scalings $Γ^{-1/2}$ and $Γ^{-1}$.

### [175] [Nonlinear Hall quantum oscillations to probe topological Brown-Zak fermions in graphene moiré systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05681)
*Jinrui Zhong,Huimin Peng,Yuqing Hu,Qi Feng,Qiuli Li,Shihao Zhang,Qinsheng Wang,Jinhai Mao,Junxi Duan,Yugui Yao*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出并实验验证了石墨烯莫尔系统中的一种新型非线性霍尔效应（NLHE）量子振荡，该振荡源于磁场下主导NLHE机制随布洛赫态重现的交替变化，能够以低至0.5T的起始场灵敏探测Brown-Zak费米子，并在可公度条件下揭示其非线性输运主要由量子几何贡献主导，首次实验探测到Brown-Zak费米子的拓扑性质。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管二阶非线性霍尔效应（second-order nonlinear Hall effect, NLHE）因其与电子布洛赫波函数量子几何（quantum geometry）的深刻联系而备受关注，但磁场下的NLHE研究尚属空白；同时，线性响应区（linear response regime）的量子振荡（quantum oscillations）已被证明是研究电子系统的有力工具，因此探索NLHE中的量子振荡有望为揭示新型准粒子丰富的量子几何性质提供新途径。

Result: 该量子振荡能够灵敏探测Brown-Zak费米子，起始场仅需0.5 T；当可公度条件（commensurability condition）满足时，Brown-Zak费米子的非线性输运主要受量子几何贡献（quantum geometric contributions）支配。

Conclusion: 该发现不仅确立了一种新型量子振荡，还首次实现了对Brown-Zak费米子拓扑性质的实验探测，为探索新型拓扑准粒子（topological quasiparticles）提供了新思路。

Abstract: Due to the deep connection with the quantum geometry of electronic Bloch wavefunctions, the second-order nonlinear Hall effect (NLHE) has been an attractive topic since its proposal. However, studies on NLHE under a magnetic field have been lacking. Given that quantum oscillations in the linear response regime have been proven to be useful tools in investigating electronic systems, searching for quantum oscillations in NLHE is of great interest and is expected to provide new avenues to unveil rich quantum geometric properties of novel quasiparticles. Here, we propose a new type of NLHE quantum oscillations and experimentally probe it in graphene moiré systems. It stems from the alternation of the dominant NLHE mechanisms with recurring Bloch states under magnetic field, which enables sensitive detection of Brown-Zak fermions, giving an onset field as low as 0.5 T. Most importantly, when the commensurability condition is satisfied, the nonlinear transport of Brown-Zak fermions is mainly governed by quantum geometric contributions. Our findings not only establish a new type of quantum oscillations, but also demonstrate the first experimental detection of the topological nature of Brown-Zak fermions, shedding light on the exploration of novel topological quasiparticles.

### [176] [Thermodynamic incompleteness in non-Markovian Majorana transport I: Island dynamics and missing transport statistics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05754)
*Yang Tian*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明，浮动的马约拉纳岛（Majorana island）的非马尔可夫岛态动力学（non-Markovian island-state dynamics）在一般情况下无法完全确定在引线中测量的热力学输运统计量（thermodynamic transport statistics）。作者通过库仑阻塞岛（Coulomb-blockaded island）与结构化库（structured reservoirs）耦合的模型，利用Schrieffer-Wolff变换分析协同隧穿（cotunneling）区，发现岛态记忆核（memory kernel）不足以唯一确定输运中的电子来源、去向及能量交换，并提出热力学完备性判据（thermodynamic completeness criterion）来标识哪些输运信息在岛态动力学中缺失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在非马尔可夫环境下，马约拉纳岛（Majorana island）的岛态动力学是否足以完全确定引线中的热力学输运统计量（thermodynamic transport statistics），即检验岛态信息与输运信息之间的对应关系是否完备。

Method: 以库仑阻塞岛（Coulomb-blockaded island）上M个马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero modes）与结构化库（structured reservoirs）耦合为模型；在协同隧穿（cotunneling）区应用Schrieffer-Wolff变换，得到由马约拉纳双线性算符（Majorana bilinears）驱动的库辅助跃迁；通过迹去库后得到每个双线性对应的记忆核（memory kernel），并以此为基础分析岛态可观测量的可预测性及输运信息的缺失。

Result: 岛态记忆核（memory kernel）在协同隧穿近似（cotunneling approximation）下足以预测所有岛态可观测量，但不足以确定哪个引线或探测器通道提供了电子、吸收了电子或携带了相应的能量交换。这是一种真正的热力学信息丢失，而非岛态方程的误差。基于此提出热力学完备性判据（thermodynamic completeness criterion）：只有当输运可观测量在所有给出相同岛态记忆核的库通道分配上保持不变时，岛记忆方程才能确定该可观测量。

Conclusion: 两个具有结构化库的马约拉纳装置（structured-reservoir Majorana devices）可以拥有完全相同的岛态层析成像（island-state tomography）和弛豫行为，但在引线中测量的电荷噪声（charge noise）、热噪声（heat noise）和混合电荷-能量关联（mixed charge-energy correlations）却可以不同。从库记录到岛核的投影几何以及隧道接触网络的拓扑结构，共同决定了哪些输运信息在岛态动力学中缺失。

Abstract: We show that the complete knowledge of the non-Markovian island-state dynamics of a floating Majorana island does not, in general, determine the thermodynamic transport statistics measured in the leads. We demonstrate this statement in a Coulomb-blockaded island with $M$ Majorana zero modes coupled to structured reservoirs. In the cotunneling regime, a Schrieffer-Wolff transformation gives reservoir-assisted transitions generated by Majorana bilinears. After the reservoirs are traced out, the island state determines the memory kernel associated with each bilinear, and this is enough to predict all island-state observables within the cotunneling approximation. It is not enough to determine which lead or detector channel supplied the electron, absorbed the electron, or carried the corresponding energy exchange. This is a genuine loss of thermodynamic information, not an error in the island equation. We formulate the result as a thermodynamic completeness criterion: an island memory equation determines a transport observable only when that observable is constant over all assignments of reservoir channels that give the same island memory kernel. The criterion gives a measurable prediction. Two structured-reservoir Majorana devices can have identical island-state tomography and relaxation, but different charge noise measured separately in the leads, heat noise, and mixed charge-energy correlations. The geometry of the projection from reservoir records to island kernels and the topology of the network of tunnel contacts identify which transport information is absent from island-state dynamics.

</details>


### [177] [Emergent spin quantum Hall edge states at the boundary of two-dimensional electron gas proximitized by an $s$-wave superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05847)
*M. V. Parfenov,V. S. Khrapai,I. S. Burmistrov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文论证了在量子化磁场下的二维电子气-超导体（2DEG-S）混合结构中，拓扑保护并未丧失，而是体现在自旋输运通道中。该系统属于Altland-Zirnbauer分类中的C类，支持偶数整数量子化的横向自旋电导——即自旋量子霍尔效应。作者提出了通过电学测量探测该拓扑保护的实验方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于Altland-Zirnbauer对称性分类（Altland-Zirnbauer classification），将2DEG-S系统归属于对称类C（symmetry class C），并论证该类支持偶数整数量子化的横向自旋电导（transverse spin conductivity）——即自旋量子霍尔效应（spin quantum Hall effect）。通过理论分析展示该系统中存在拓扑保护的边缘态，携带自旋电流（spin current），其自旋电导（spin conductance）具有偶数整数量子化且对无序具有鲁棒性。

Result: 2DEG-S混合结构中拓扑保护仍然存在，但在自旋输运通道中展现，而非电荷通道。系统呈现出偶数整数量子化的自旋电导，该量子化对无序不敏感。所提出的实验方案可通过电学测量直接验证该拓扑保护，为检测手性Andreev边缘态的C类起源提供了具体路径。

Conclusion: 2DEG-S混合结构中的拓扑保护并未失效，而是转移到自旋输运通道，表现为可观测的自旋量子霍尔效应。这一发现不仅解释了电荷通道中非整数量子化的实验现象，还为通过电学手段探测C类拓扑相提供了可行的实验方案。

Abstract: Hybrid two-dimensional electron gas-superconductor (2DEG-S) structures in a quantized magnetic field offer a promising platform for realizing new topological phases. While recent experiments reveal chiral Andreev edge states, their charge conductance is not integer quantized and is disorder sensitive, raising the question of whether topological protection survives. We argue that it does, but manifests in the spin transport channel. The 2DEG-S system belongs to symmetry class C of the Altland-Zirnbauer classification, which supports an even-integer quantized transverse spin conductivity -- the spin quantum Hall effect, so far unobserved experimentally. We demonstrate that 2DEG-S hybrids host topologically protected edge states carrying a spin current with an even-integer quantized spin conductance robust against disorder. Finally, we propose an experimental setup to probe this protection via electrical measurements, establishing a concrete route to detect the class C origin of the chiral Andreev edge states.

### [178] [Intrinsic Floquet Generation and $1/I$ Quantum Oscillations in a Sliding Charge-Density Wave](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05894)
*Yi Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明均匀滑动的电荷密度波（sliding charge-density wave, CDW）可作为内在的直流-交流转换器，在Floquet形式下精确可解，产生带隙劈裂和边带阶梯。通过精确解揭示弱探针隧穿谱中的1/I振荡源于局域化相干细丝（coherent filament）中的宏观电流输运，为近期在准一维CDW绝缘体中观测到的奇特量子振荡提供了严格的输运解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Floquet形式对孤立滑动CDW问题进行精确求解，得到分立的带隙边缘和Floquet边带阶梯（sideband ladder）；通过弱探针隧穿谱分析逆电流（1/I）振荡；引入分段多端模型（segmented multiterminal model）解释接触附近非弹性相位滑移退相干（inelastic phase-slip dephasing）对振荡可见度的抑制。

Result: 1) 滑动CDW系统在Floquet形式下精确可解，展现带隙劈裂与Floquet边带阶梯；2) 弱探针隧穿谱在固定偏压下呈现1/I振荡，与边带阶梯匹配；3) 宏观电流必须通过高度局域化的相干细丝（coherent filament）渗流，有效通道数远小于几何链数；4) 接触附近的非弹性相位滑移退相干强烈抑制外电压探针上的振荡可见度。

Conclusion: 该工作为近期在准一维CDW绝缘体中观测到的1/I量子振荡提供了严格的输运解释，揭示了绝缘带隙保护Floquet相干性的空间-时间转换（spatial-to-temporal conversion）机制，为内禀驱动量子器件（intrinsically driven quantum devices）提供了新范式。

Abstract: The realization of intrinsic, tunable high-frequency quantum states without external radiation is a major goal in condensed matter physics and quantum device engineering. Here, we demonstrate that a uniformly sliding charge-density wave (CDW) acts as an intrinsic dc-to-ac converter, transforming spatial periodicity into temporal periodicity to realize a unique periodically driven quantum state. We show that the isolated sliding-CDW problem is exactly solvable in Floquet form, yielding split gap edges and a ladder of Floquet sidebands. Using this exact solution, we reveal that weak-probe tunneling spectroscopy naturally yields an inverse-current ($1/I$) oscillation as a fixed-bias cut of the sideband ladder. Matching the observed oscillation period to theory indicates that the macroscopic current must percolate through a highly localized coherent filament, with an effective channel number orders of magnitude smaller than the geometric chain count. Furthermore, using a segmented multiterminal model, we demonstrate that inelastic phase-slip dephasing near the contacts explains the strong suppression of oscillation visibility on outer voltage probes. Ultimately, our results provide a rigorous transport interpretation of the striking $1/I$ quantum oscillations recently observed in quasi-one-dimensional CDW insulators. More broadly, they highlight a universal spatial-to-temporal conversion mechanism where the insulating gap protects Floquet coherence, offering a novel paradigm for intrinsically driven quantum devices.

### [179] [Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction as a coherence diagnostic for chirality-induced spin selectivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06008)
*Vishvendra S. Poonia*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出通过超交换相互作用（superexchange interaction）中的对称性判据，区分手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）的两种机制：相干SU(2)自旋旋转（coherent CISS）与非相干自旋相关滤波（incoherent CISS）。相干CISS产生巨大的Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya（DM）相互作用，比值|D|/JH可达3，而非相干CISS导致D=0。DM相互作用可作为相干序参量，其临界旋转角低于现有输运推断值两个数量级，可通过现有交换谱学（exchange spectroscopy）实验验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）的物理机制——是相干SU(2)自旋旋转还是非相干自旋相关滤波——是分子自旋电子学（molecular spintronics）中一个未解决的核心问题，对不对称化学（asymmetric chemistry）和量子信息（quantum information）等领域具有重要意义。

Method: 通过对手性分子桥（chiral molecular bridge）中介的超交换相互作用（superexchange interaction）施加对称性判据，区分相干CISS（实现为隧穿电子的幺正自旋旋转）与非相干CISS（实现为厄米非幺正但自旋对角的隧穿矩阵）。利用Lindblad方法证明耗散自旋滤波无法修改虚隧穿介导的超交换，并推导闭合形式的角、对映体及灵敏度特征。

Result: 相干CISS产生比值|D|/JH高达3的巨DM相互作用，比Si/SiGe中本征Rashba自旋-轨道耦合（Rashba spin-orbit coupling）大两个数量级；非相干CISS精确产生D=0。临界相干旋转角比当前输运推断值低两个数量级，五种候选分子即使考虑保守的界面放大效应也能超出一个至两个数量级。

Conclusion: DM相互作用可作为相干序参量（coherence order parameter），将长期存在的输运争议转化为一个具有量子振幅分辨能力的二元自旋量子比特（spin-qubit）实验，该实验可利用栅极定义量子点（gate-defined quantum dots）中现有的10 kHz交换谱学（exchange spectroscopy）实现。

Abstract: Whether chirality-induced spin selectivity (CISS) reflects coherent SU(2) spin rotation or incoherent spin-dependent filtering is a central unresolved question in molecular spintronics, with implications ranging from asymmetric chemistry to quantum information. We show that these two scenarios are distinguishable by a sharp symmetry criterion on the superexchange interaction mediated by a chiral molecular bridge. Coherent CISS, implemented as a unitary spin rotation of the tunneling electron, generates a giant Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya (DM) interaction with ratio |D|/JH up to 3, which is two orders of magnitude beyond intrinsic Rashba spin-orbit coupling in Si/SiGe. Incoherent CISS, represented by any Hermitian (non-unitary but spin-diagonal) tunneling matrix, produces D = 0 identically; we prove this as a structural theorem, reinforced by a Lindblad argument that dissipative spin filtering cannot modify virtual-tunneling-mediated superexchange. The DM interaction thus serves as a coherence order parameter, nonzero only when quantum amplitudes for opposite-spin transmission maintain a fixed relative phase. We derive closed-form angular, enantiomeric, and sensitivity signatures and show that the critical coherent rotation angle lies two orders of magnitude below current transport-inferred values and is accessible to existing 10 kHz exchange spectroscopy in gate-defined quantum dots. Five candidate molecules are predicted to exceed this threshold by one to two orders of magnitude even in a conservative interface-amplification scenario. The proposed measurement converts a long-standing transport controversy into a binary spin-qubit experiment with quantum-amplitude resolution.

</details>

Abstract: Understanding the magnetotransport behaviors in topological systems remains alluring, as a lot of intrinsic information could be extracted, e.g., the band structures, Berry phase, Fermi surface, carrier density, and so on. Firstly, we analyze the chemical potential and magnetoconductivity oscillations with the magnetic field and reveal that there exist two distinct oscillation frequencies, which are caused by the characteristic torus Fermi surface and can be regarded as an important experimental signature of nodal-line semimetals. Then we calculate the MR and find that although the MR is nonsaturating with the magnetic field in the low-energy region, the MR ratio is much smaller than that reported in the experiment.

### [181] [Sub-kelvin thermal conductivity of substrates and on-chip routing in quantum integrated systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06146)
*Charles Bon-Mardion,Arnaud Lorin,Edouard Deschaseaux,Céline Feautrier,Daniel Mermin,Jean Charbonnier,Jing Li,Jean-Luc Sauvageot,Candice Thomas*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文实验研究了量子架构中两种基本组件——衬底（substrate）和片上布线（on-chip routing）——在亚开尔文温区的热特性。高阻硅在300 mK下热导率最高（5×10⁻² W/m·K），而低阻硅、硼硅玻璃和蓝宝石的热导率更低（10⁻³–10⁻⁴ W/m·K量级）。通过非平衡格林函数方法提取了声子平均自由程，并发现超导铌布线会增加面内热导，但衬底仍是主要热通路。结果强调了衬底选择与三维集成（3D integration）功能分区在量子系统热管理中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模量子系统日益依赖异质组件（如量子比特、控制电子学和读出电路）的紧密集成，这使得低温热管理成为核心挑战。本研究旨在系统评估衬底材料和片上布线这两种基础构件对量子架构热特性的影响，为优化热设计提供实验依据。

Method: 实验测量了四种衬底材料（高阻硅、低阻硅、硼硅玻璃、蓝宝石）在亚开尔文温区的热导率，并利用有限元非平衡格林函数（finite-element non-equilibrium Green's function）方法评估弹道电导（ballistic conductance），提取声子平均自由程（phonon mean free path）。同时设计专用测试结构，测量超导铌（Nb）布线对系统热导的影响。

Result: 高阻硅在300 mK下热导率最高，为5×10⁻² W/m·K；低阻硅、硼硅玻璃和蓝宝石的热导率依次为8×10⁻⁴ W/m·K、2×10⁻³ W/m·K和2×10⁻³ W/m·K。超导铌布线增加了系统的面内热导（in-plane thermal conductance），但衬底仍然是主导热通路。

Conclusion: 衬底材料的选择对量子系统的热性能具有决定性作用，高阻硅因其高热导率在低温下优势明显。片上布线虽增大热导，但并未改变衬底作为主热通路的地位。研究进一步指出，通过三维集成方法实现功能分区（function partitioning）是提升量子架构热管理效率的关键方向。

Abstract: The development of large-scale quantum systems increasingly relies on the close integration of heterogeneous components such as qubits, control electronics, and readout circuits, making thermal management at cryogenic temperatures a central challenge in such architectures. In this work, we present an experimental thermal study of two building blocks of such systems: the substrate and the on-chip routing. We first investigate the sub-kelvin thermal conductivity of four substrate materials: high-resistivity silicon, low-resistivity silicon, borosilicate, and sapphire. We report that high-resistivity silicon exhibits the highest thermal conductivity among the substrates studied ($5\cdot10^{-2}$~W/m$\cdot$K at 300~mK), while low-resistivity silicon, borosilicate, and sapphire show lower values ($8\cdot10^{-4}$~W/m$\cdot$K, 2$\cdot10^{-3}$~W/m$\cdot$K, and 2$\cdot10^{-3}$~W/m$\cdot$K at 300~mK, respectively). Ballistic conductance evaluation using a finite-element non-equilibrium Green's function approach further allows us to extract the phonon mean free path in each substrate and gives insights into the involved scattering mechanisms. Additionally, we employ a dedicated test vehicle to evaluate the impact of on-chip routing on the thermal conductance of the system. Our measurements with superconducting Nb routing lines reveal that the routing increases the in-plane thermal conductance of the system, but the substrate remains the dominant heat path. These results highlight the critical role of the substrate choice within quantum systems and underscore the importance of function partitioning through 3D integration approaches for more efficient thermal management in quantum architectures.

### [182] [Anomalous Thomson Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06299)
*Ying-Fei Zhang,Zhi-Fan Zhang,Zhen-Gang Zhu,Gang Su*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出反常汤姆孙效应（anomalous Thomson effect, ATE），建立其与反常能斯特效应（anomalous Nernst effect, ANE）的理论关系，并基于Fe3Sn2的狄拉克模型和实验数据证明ATE系数可显著大于ANE系数，尤其CeCrGe3在液氮温区ATC可达ANC的15倍，且该效应可利用现有ANE数据直接验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提出反常汤姆孙效应（ATE）这一新物理效应，揭示其与反常能斯特效应（ANE）的内在联系，并探索其在固态热电制冷中的应用潜力。

Method: 理论推导反常汤姆孙系数（ATC）作为反常能斯特系数（ANC）的函数；采用Fe3Sn2的大质量狄拉克模型（massive Dirac model）刻画由贝里曲率（Berry curvature）驱动的本征输运；利用CoS2、Co3Sn2S2和CeCrGe3的实验ANE数据反推ATC。

Result: ATC相对于ANC普遍增强；低温极限下ATC/ANC比值趋近于3；CeCrGe3在液氮温区（liquid-nitrogen temperature regime）ATC可达ANC的15倍。

Conclusion: 反常汤姆孙效应（ATE）在液氮温区具有显著的热电制冷应用价值，且无需额外设备即可通过现有ANE实验数据直接验证。

Abstract: We propose an effect named the anomalous Thomson effect (ATE), analogous to the anomalous Hall effect and the anomalous Nernst effect (ANE). The anomalous Thomson coefficient (ATC) is derived as a function of the anomalous Nernst coefficient (ANC); hence, the ATC inherits the same mechanisms of the ANC. Specifically, we study a massive Dirac model for Fe3Sn2 to capture intrinsic Berry-curvature-driven transport. Our results show that the ATC is generally enhanced relative to the ANC. In the low-temperature limit, the ratio ATC/ANC approaches three. Since the relation between the ATE and the ANE is model-independent, we utilize experimental ANE data to infer experiment-related ATC for CoS2, Co3Sn2S2, and CeCrGe3. We find that the ATC for CeCrGe3 can be as large as fifteen times the ANC in the liquid-nitrogen temperature regime, making this effect highly attractive for solid-state thermoelectric refrigeration in this temperature range. It is important to emphasize that the proposed ATE can be directly verified using existing ANE data, without the need for additional equipment or measurements.

### [183] [Genus-protected higher-order topological phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06383)
*Shahroze Shahab,Hui Liu,Daniel Varjas,Ion Cosma Fulga*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出不依赖晶格对称性、仅由体带隙、基本对称性（fundamental symmetries）和系统全局拓扑（如亏格genus）保护的高阶拓扑相（HOTPs）构建方案，使边界态（boundary states）免于被纯表面微扰移除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统高阶拓扑相（HOTPs）的保护机制依赖于晶格对称性（lattice symmetries），一旦后者被破坏，边界模式（boundary modes）可在不开辟体带隙（bulk gap）的情况下被移除。因此，需要探索不依赖晶格对称性的更鲁棒的拓扑保护机制。

Method: 提出构造方案，利用体带隙（bulk gap）、基本对称性（fundamental symmetries）以及系统形状的整体拓扑（如亏格genus或孔洞数目）来保护高阶拓扑相，完全独立于任何晶体对称性（crystalline symmetries）。

Result: 只要保持局域基本对称性（fundamental local symmetries）不变，由此构造的边界态（boundary states）无法被任何纯表面微扰（purely-surface perturbation）移除。

Conclusion: 高阶拓扑相的保护机制可超越晶格对称性的限制，拓展至更基本的对称性和全局拓扑来源，提升了高阶边界态的鲁棒性和普适性。

Abstract: Higher-order topological phases (HOTPs) feature protected gapless modes on boundaries of higher codimension, such as the corners or hinges of a crystal. They are understood as being protected by lattice symmetries: If the latter are broken, it becomes possible to remove the boundary modes without closing the bulk gap. In this work, we present construction schemes for HOTPs protected solely by the bulk gap, by fundamental symmetries, and by the global topology of the system shape (its genus, or number of holes), independent of any crystalline symmetries. As long as the fundamental local symmetries are preserved, the resulting boundary states cannot be removed by any purely-surface perturbation.

Abstract: Electron spins in single molecules are a promising platform for quantum information processing. However, their practical implementation as qubits requires reliable control at the single-entity level, including an efficient state initialization. Here, we demonstrate the remote, all-electrical initialization of the electron spin in single molecules: Using electron spin resonance scanning tunneling microscopy, we investigate coupled pairs of S=1/2 molecules (Fe-FePc), where one molecule serves as a readout and pumping unit for the neighboring one. We show that the exchange interaction between them enables angular momentum transfer, which allows for the control of the remote spin state via the direction and magnitude of the spin-polarized tunneling current and the exchange coupling strength. These results establish a general, all-electrical approach for remote spin initialization that is readily transferable to a wide range of spin-based quantum architectures.

Result: 推导出的扩展LLG方程包含两个阻尼项：两者均为空间非局域（spatially nonlocal）和各向异性（anisotropic）的，其中一项还本质上是非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）的，即时间非局域。这些阻尼结构源于快（AMI层中量子磁子）与慢（FI层中经典自旋）局域自旋之间的相互作用，以及非平衡磁子分布的驱动效应。

The bosonic bath is comprised of quantum magnons within a layer of altermagnetic insulator (AMI) that is attached to a conventional FI layer, often one of the key ingredients within spintronic and magnonic multilayers, so that interaction between slow classical (in the FI layer) and fast quantum (in the AMI layer) localized spins ensues. Such a bath, including its driving to produce a nonequilibrium distribution of altermagnetic magnons, generates a rich structure of the SKFT-derived extended LLG equation for classical spins within the FI layer. Our LLG equation contains two damping terms, both of which are spatially nonlocal and anisotropic, while one of them is also intrinsically non-Markovian, i.e., nonlocal in time. We demonstrate how to exploit these terms for tuning spintronic and magnonic effects within the FI layer of AMI/FI bilayers that involve spin wave or domain wall propagation, as well as skyrmion annihilation.

H. MacDonald, Proc. Natl. Acad. Sci. U.S.A. 108, 12233 (2011)]. We take as an example the moiré physics of electrons in twisted bilayer kagomé (TBK) metals near $1/3$ filling where monolayer Dirac cones lie. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统磁存储面临“磁记录三难困境”（magnetic recording trilemma），即信噪比、热稳定性和可写性无法同时优化；而现有的热辅助磁记录（HAMR）依赖激光和等离子体换能器，难以集成至片上或嵌入式架构中，亟需一种全电子化的替代方案。

Method: 通过在插层二维磁体 Ni₁/₄TaSe₂ 中施加低电流密度脉冲，利用焦耳热（Joule heating）将材料加热至居里温度以上，使磁畴在远低于矫顽力（coercive field）的约 2 mT 小磁场下完成写入；读取通过反常霍尔效应实现。

Result: 实验直接证明，电流脉冲可将二维磁体加热至居里温度以上，写入所需磁场仅为约 2 mT，比该材料的矫顽场小约 100 倍，实现了高效的数据写入与电子读取。

Conclusion: 该全电子式方案结合二维磁介质，为能量辅助磁记录（energy-assisted magnetization recording）开辟了新的记录路径，兼具基础创新性与技术应用潜力。

Abstract: The ever-increasing demand for fast, reliable, and energy-efficient information storage continues to push magnetic memory technologies toward their fundamental limits. Conventional scaling strategies, which rely on reducing bit size, inevitably run into the "magnetic recording trilemma," where signal-to-noise ratio, thermal stability, and writability cannot all be optimized simultaneously. Heat-assisted magnetic recording (HAMR) has emerged as the leading solution, enabling high-density storage by transiently heating the medium during the write cycle. However, the reliance on laser optics and plasmonic transducers restricts HAMR primarily to hard-disk drives, limiting its integration with on-chip or embedded architectures. Here, we demonstrate an electronic variant of HAMR in which Joule heating from low-current density current pulses facilitates data writing, while the anomalous Hall effect provides electronic readout. Employing intercalated 2D magnet Ni$_{1/4}$TaSe$_2$, we show direct evidence that current pulses heat the material above its Curie temperature, during which a small magnetic field of ~2mT (100 times smaller than the coercive field) enables efficient data writing. The all-electronic approach combined with the 2D magnetic medium creates timely opportunities to revisit the energy-assisted magnetization recording, enabling new recording schemes that combine fundamental novelty with technological impact.

</details>


### [188] [Colossal Magnetoresistance and Phonon Driven Exchange Dynamics in Eu$_5$Sn$_2$As$_6$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.06649)
*Luke Pritchard Cairns,Kohtaro Yamakawa,Shengzhi Zhang,Youzhe Chen,Bernard Field,Rainer Reczek,Ryan P. Day,Joel E. Moore,Marcelo Jaime,Sinead M. Griffin,Robert J. Birgeneau,James G. Analytis*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究通过测量Eu₅Sn₂As₆的热导率和磁致伸缩，揭示晶格在巨磁阻效应（colossal magnetoresistance）中的关键作用：外场消除自旋构型简并（degeneracy of spin configurations）并抑制磁致应变（magnetostrain），从而增强声子主导的热导率；通过与自旋玻璃绝缘体（spin-glass insulators）对比，指出这种晶格效应并非电子退局域化（electron delocalization）的附带产物，而是其驱动力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 新一代基于Eu²⁺的反铁磁体（antiferromagnets）展现出与钙钛矿锰氧化物（perovskite manganites）及掺杂Eu-硫族化物（Eu-chalcogenides）截然不同的巨磁阻行为，其背后的晶格作用机制尚不明确。

Method: 对代表性Eu₅Sn₂As₆样品进行热导率（thermal conductivity）和磁致伸缩（magnetostriction）测量，分析其随外磁场的变化行为，并与自旋玻璃绝缘体进行对比。

Result: 热导率和磁致伸缩均强烈依赖于外磁场，且与磁化强度（magnetization）同步变化：在Eu²⁺磁矩极化方向饱和。声子主导的热导率在磁场下增强，归因于自旋构型简并的解除；高场下因磁致应变被抑制而趋于饱和。

Conclusion: 晶格通过交换阻挫（exchange frustration）引起的强声子散射（phonon scattering）的抑制，是驱动电子退局域化并产生巨磁阻效应的关键机制，而非该效应的附带现象。

Abstract: The emergence of colossal magnetoresistance in a new generation of Eu$^{2+}$-based antiferromagnets is intriguing given stark contrasts to the archetypal perovskite manganites and doped Eu-chalcogenides. In this study the thermal conductivity and magnetostriction of Eu$_5$Sn$_2$As$_6$ -- one such representative -- have been measured to better understand the role of the crystal lattice. Both properties are strongly field-dependent and mirror the magnetization, saturating once the Eu$^{2+}$ moments are polarized. The field-enhancement of the phonon-dominated thermal conductivity is interpreted through the lifting of a degeneracy of spin configurations, and the subsequent saturation due to quenched magnetostrain in high field. Comparison with spin-glass insulators suggests that this phenomenon is not a byproduct but rather the driver of electron delocalization due to the suppression of strong phonon scattering arising from exchange frustration.

</details>
